Chapter 1 pratijñāsūtra PJS

  1. 1.1viśuddhajñānadehāya trivedīdivyacakṣuṣe |                    śreyaḥprāptinimittāya namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ||
  2. 1.2abhivandya gurūnādau śiṣyadhīpadminīravīn |                    tatprasādāt kariṣye 'haṃ mīmāṃsāślokavārttikaṃ ||
  3. 1.3tadvidvāṃso 'nugṛhṇantu cittaśrotraiḥ prasādibhiḥ |                    santaḥ praṇayivākyāni gṛhṇanti hy anasūyavaḥ ||
  4. 1.4na cātrātiva kartavyaṃ doṣadṛṣṭiparaṃ manaḥ |                    doṣo hy avidyamāno 'pi taccittānāṃ prakāśate ||<4>
  5. 1.5kuto vā gṛhṇate doṣaṃ sūrayo madvidhoktiṣu |                    neṣyate yaḥ parastho 'pi sa svayaṃ gṛhyate katham ||
  6. 1.6nirdoṣatvaikavākyatvaṃ kva vā lokasya dṛśyate |                    sāpavādā yataḥ ke cin mokṣasvargāv api prati ||
  7. 1.7āgamapravaṇaś cāhaṃ nāpavādyaḥ skhaliteṣv apy apodyate |                    na hi sadvartmanā gacchan skhaliteṣv apy apodyate ||
  8. 1.8yathā kathañ cid ārabdhā trayīmārgānusāriṇī |                    vāgvṛttir alpasārāpi śraddadhānasya śobhate ||<5>
  9. 1.9mīmāṃsāśāstratejobhir viśeṣeṇoj jvalīkṛte |                    vedārthajñānaratne me tṛṣṇātīva vijṛmbhate ||
  10. 1.10prāyenaiva hi mīmāṃsā loke lokāyatīkṛtā |                    tāmāstikapathe kartum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kṛto mayā ||
  11. 1.11athāto dharmajijñāsā sūtram ādyam idaṃ kṛtam |                    dharmākhyaṃ viṣayaṃ vaktuṃ mīmāṃsāyāḥ prayojanam ||
  12. 1.12sarvasyaiva hi śāstrasya karmaṇo vāpi kasya cit |                    yāvat prayojanaṃ noktaṃ tāvat tat kena gṛhyate ||
  13. 1.13mīmāṃsākhyā tu vidyeyaṃ bahuvidyāntarāśritā |                    na śuśrūṣayituṃ śakyā prāganuktvā prayojanam ||<6>
  14. 1.14vidyāntareṣu nāpy etad yady abhīṣṭaṃ prayojanam |                    anarthaprāpaṇaṃ tāvat tebhyo nāśaṅkyate kva cit ||
  15. 1.15mīmāṃsāyāṃ tv ihājñāte durjñāte vāvivekataḥ |                    nyāyamārge mahān doṣa iti yatnopacaryatā ||
  16. 1.16tasmāt prayojanaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sūtrakṛtā svayam |                    yat svenoktaṃ vadeyus tad bhāṣyakārādayaḥ katham ||
  17. 1.17siddhārthaṃ jñātasambandhaṃ śrotuṃ śrotā pravartate |                    śāstrādau tena vaktavyaḥ sambandhaḥ saprayojanaḥ ||<7>
  18. 1.18śāstraṃ prayojanaṃ caiva sambandhasyāśrayāv ubhau |                    taduktyantargatas tasmād bhinno noktaḥ prayojanāt ||
  19. 1.19siddhiḥ śrotṛpravṛttīnāṃ sambandhakathanād yataḥ |                    tasmāt sarveṣu śāstreṣu sambandhaḥ pūrvam ucyate ||
  20. 1.20yāvat prayojanenāsya sambandho nābhidhīyate |                    asambaddhapralāpitvād bhavet tāvad asaṃgatiḥ ||
  21. 1.21iha tv ākṣipya sambandhaṃ bhāṣya evābhidhāsyate |                    dharmaprasiddhyasiddhibhyāṃ, tasmān nānyo 'bhidhīyate ||
  22. 1.22na cāpy atrāthaśabdena śāstrasambandha ucyate |                    sambandhaṃ kriyayor hy eṣa brūte śāstrāc ca te pṛthak ||<8>
  23. 1.23yo 'py ayaṃ śāstrasambandho varṇyate kaiś cid āditaḥ |                    kriyānantaryarūpo vā guruparvakramo 'pi vā ||
  24. 1.24sadasadbhāvayos tasya viśeṣo nopalabhyate |                    śrotuvidhau niṣedhe vā jñāne vā śāstragocare ||
  25. 1.25tasmād vyākhyāṅgam icchadbhiḥ sahetuḥ saprayojanaḥ |                    śāstrāvatārasambandho vācyo nānyas tu niṣphalaḥ ||<9>
  26. 1.26loke ityādibhāṣyasya ṣaḍarthān sampracakṣate |                    bhāṣyakārānusāreṇa, prayuktasyāditaḥ pṛthak ||
  27. 1.27sarvavyākhyām upālambhaṃ pratyākhyānaṃ tathā pare |                    parisaṃkhyās tutī kecithaśabdasya dūṣaṇam ||
  28. 1.28sādhāraṇī viśiṣṭā ca sūtravyākhyā dvidhā matā |                    viśiṣṭā pratisūtraṃ yā sarvārthā tv iyam ucyate ||
  29. 1.29pravṛttis tu padeṣv eva nivṛttiḥ sūtrasaṃśrayā |                    vedavākyāviruddheṣu na tu sarveṣu keṣu cit ||<10>
  30. 1.30adhyāhārasya vākyeṣu vyatyāsasya ca sambhavāt |                    tenaiṣām iti sūtrāṇāṃ pārārthye saty api grahaḥ ||
  31. 1.31evaśabdo 'lpavācyatvād, asyāvṛttau tu gauravam |                    prasiddhatvād avācyaṃ cet, na doṣaḥ puṅgirām ayam ||<11>
  32. 1.32vyākhyāṅgatvābhimānena yo 'dhyāhārādyapekṣate |                    svasaṃjñāṃ vāpi tasyedaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ nirūpyate ||
  33. 1.33vṛtyantareṣu keṣāñ cil laukikārthavyatikramaḥ |                    śabdānāṃ dṛśyate teṣam upālambho 'yam ucyate ||
  34. 1.34athāta ity ayaṃ loke nānantarye prayujyate |                    tasmāt tādarthyam etasya paribhāṣādibhir bhavet ||
  35. 1.35prasiddhahāniḥ śabdānām aprasiddhe ca kalpanā |                    na kāryā vṛttikāreṇa sati siddhārthasambhave ||
  36. 1.36sūtrārthe kliśyataś caivaṃ dūre vedārthanirṇayaḥ |                    tatra yatnasya bhāratvaṃ vaktṛśrotroḥ prasajyate ||
  37. 1.37na vyākhyāsyati sūtrāṇi codanārthaparatvataḥ |                    yat tasya parihāro 'yaṃ pratyākhyānena cocyate ||<12>
  38. 1.38prayāso vedavākyeṣu kāryaḥ sūtreṣv anena kim |                    phalavattvāphalatvābhyām, ebhiḥ karaṇasammataiḥ ||
  39. 1.39codanārtha upetavyaḥ, nobhayaṃ yatnagauravāt |                    padārthānāṃ prasiddhatvāt vyākhyeyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
  40. 1.40evaṃśabdādiko granthaḥ pakṣe cāsmin samarthyate |                    padacchedadādyabhāvena pratyākhyānamatis tv iyam ||<13>
  41. 1.41brabīty eva hi sūtrārtham, atiriktādi ceṣyate |                    nanv aśaktam idaṃ sūtraṃ samyak sūtritam ity api ||
  42. 1.42sūtre cāgamakatvādi pratyākhyāne virudhyate |                    na copāyānabhijñena śakyopeyāvadhāraṇā ||
  43. 1.43nānyato vedavidbhyaś ca sūtravṛttikriyeṣyate |                    pratyākhyānasya hetuś ca padārthānāṃ prasiddhatā ||
  44. 1.44yoktā sā vedavākyānaṃ tulyārthatvān nivārayet |                    vākyārthe tatra sandehād vyākhyānaṃ cet pravartate ||
  45. 1.45sūtreṣv api samānatvāt pratyākhyānaṃ na yujyate |                    na vyākhyātavyam ityevaṃ pratyākhyāne ca sidhyati ||<14>
  46. 1.46duṣṭavyākhyā niṣedhena tadapetā na vāryate |                    asya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvāt phalgutvāc cāpi parvayoḥ ||
  47. 1.47madhyame cātidaurjanyāt parisaṃkhyaiva yujyate |                    vaidikaṃ jaiminīyaṃ ca yatra vākyaṃ virudhyate ||
  48. 1.48yathāśrutagṛhīte 'rthe tatredam upadiśyate |                    adhyāhārādibhiḥ sūtraṃ vaidikaṃ tu yathāśrutam ||
  49. 1.49neyam, virodhe 'nyonyasya vaidikānāṃ bhavantu te |                    yathā dharmāvabodhasya pramāṇaṃ vaidikaṃ vacaḥ ||<15>
  50. 1.50tadarthanirṇaye hetur jaiminīyaṃ tathaiva naḥ |                    vākyasāmarthyatulyatvāt tathā padatadarthayoḥ ||
  51. 1.51adhyāhārādibhir muktā vyākhyā sarvatra yujyate |                    asambhavād avaśyaṃ yā virodhe 'nyatarasya tu ||
  52. 1.52anyāyyakalpanā sāpi vikalpena prasajyate |                    prāthamyenāvaruddhatvād upāyavaśato 'tha vā ||
  53. 1.53yathāśrutena sūtreṇa nyāyyāṃ bādheta codanām |                    tena vedāviruddhasya sati sambhava ity ayam ||
  54. 1.54vidhīyate 'rthaḥ, śeṣaṃ tu yathāprāptam anūdyate |                    śeṣabhājāṃ bhavel lopa ity adhyāhārakalpanā ||<16>
  55. 1.55viprakarṣāt paśoś ceti vibhaktiḥ pariṇamyate |                    padena vyavadhānaṃ tu loke saṃniyamād iti ||
  56. 1.56sūtreṇa vyavadhānaṃ tu pānavyāpadi kalpitam |<17>                    paśusāmānyavidhyādau sūtram evānyathā kṛtam ||
  57. 1.57agnayaś ca svakālatvād deyadharmāpayātanam |                    vyākhyānaṃ vākyabhedena, guṇakalpās tv amī kṛtāḥ ||
  58. 1.58autpattikas tu gavyasya tathoṣṇikkakubhor iti |                    darśanāc ca viśeṣasya tathābhyudaya ity api ||<18>
  59. 1.59sūtrakārapraśaṃsā vā loka ityādinocyate |                    prasiddhair abhidhānād dhi na śiṣyāḥ kleśitā yataḥ ||
  60. 1.60bhavitavyaṃ tu teneti prāgasmād ekavākyatā |                    vedādhyayanavākyād vā tenāthety asya dūṣaṇam ||
  61. 1.61prasiddhārthapadaiḥ śakyaḥ sūtrair vedārthanirṇayaḥ |                    na ca so 'sty athaśabdasya vinā te pūrvakarmaṇā ||
  62. 1.62prasiddhārthaṃ padaṃ yuktaṃ tac ca nāstīti dūṣaṇam |                    prasiddho 'py athaśabdādeḥ kiṃpadārtho 'tra varṇyate ||<19>
  63. 1.63pradarśanārtham ity eke, ke cin nānārthavācinaḥ |                    samudāyād avacchidya bhavadāsena kalpitāt ||
  64. 1.64śaktito 'vayavaṃ caiva varṇayantyaṣṭamādivat |                    na cātra codanāvyākhyā gauravaṃ tatra coditam ||
  65. 1.65yad vākṣepo yathoktasya vṛttābhāvād asambhavāt |                    yadi lokaprasiddhārthagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pade ||
  66. 1.66sa nāsty atrāthaśabdasyety adhyāhārādikalpanam |                    vedādhyayanavṛttatvaṃ snānasyotkarṣakalpanā ||
  67. 1.67nāvyākhyāte 'thaśabdārthe jñāyate tena varṇyate |<20>                    anarthake 'tha vānyārthe prasiddhir bādhyate dhruvam ||
  68. 1.68tasmāc chrutārthasiddhyarthaṃ vṛttaṃ kim api gamyate |                    viśiṣṭaliṅgavijñānād viśiṣṭe liṅginīkṣite ||
  69. 1.69sūtreṇāsambhavaṃ matvā naitad ity abravīt paraḥ |                    ānantaryopadeśena taddṛṣṭārthatayāpi ca ||
  70. 1.70vedādhyayanam ākṣiptaṃ kim asūtritacodanā |                    yena vṛttena jijñāsā vinā naivopapadyate ||
  71. 1.71tadānantaryam uktaṃ hi dṛṣṭārtham avakalpate |                    kriyamāṇā ca jijñāsā niyamād yasya kasya cit ||
  72. 1.72kriyetānantaraiveti vyarthaṃ tadupadeśanam |<21>                    saṅkalpādibhir apy eṣā vinā satyaṃ na sidhyati ||
  73. 1.73sādhāraṇyāt tu te 'py atra nopadeśyāḥ kathañ cana |                    tasmād dharmabubhutsāyām asādhāraṇakāraṇam ||
  74. 1.74nirvṛttaṃ sūtrakāreṣṭaṃ tac ca nākhyayanād ṛte |                    anyasyāpīty anenaiva vedapāṭhe prabādhite ||
  75. 1.75prāg apīti hi vaktavyaṃ tatrāpy anyasya sambhavāt |                    pūrveṇaiva hi labdhārthe tādṛśīṃ tv ity anena kim ||
  76. 1.76vakṣyamāṇam anālocya sambhavet paricodanā |                    na tāvat sādhyate 'dyāpi codanā dharmasādhanam ||
  77. 1.77iha vā kāni vākyāni vivariṣyati jaiminiḥ |                    dharmamātrābhidhānād dhi buddhādivacanāny api ||
  78. 1.78paṭhitvā dharmajijñāsety anyasyāpīti codanā |<22>                    yad vā bhavatu nāmedṛk sūtraṃ vedam adhītya tu ||
  79. 1.79jijñāsānantaraṃ kāryety atrāpi dvayam īpsitam |                    nānadhītya na cāpy anyat kṛtvety etan na labhyate ||
  80. 1.80vakṣyamāṇavacobhaṅgyor vākyabhedaprasaṅgataḥ |                    adhītyaiveti hi vidhau snānāder apy anantarā ||
  81. 1.81bhaved dharmasya jijñāsā nānantaryavidhis tadā |                    ānantaryavidhāne tu yā vedādhyayane kṛte ||
  82. 1.82ity evam anuvādatvāt prāg apy eṣā prasajyate |                    buddhavākyādipāṭhasya tādṛśīṃ tv ity apākriyā ||<23>
  83. 1.83prāg apīti ca codyasya, sāmarthyād vedalābhataḥ |                    naivaitayor vacobhaṅgyor eko 'py artho vidhīyate ||
  84. 1.84api cetyādikenoktam, kin tv ityetad vidhīyate |                    ānantaryaṃ parastāc ca nāpi śiṃṣma itīha tu ||
  85. 1.85ke cid adhyāharanti, <24> asya sūtrasyānyaparatvataḥ |                    na vāryate 'nadhītatvaṃ nānantaryaṃ vidhīyate ||
  86. 1.86sāmarthyāsiddhyadṛṣṭārthaprasaṅgāt tena lakṣaṇā |                    ānantaryavacovyaktir āśritaivātra lakṣyate ||
  87. 1.87śrutārthaṃ tv aparityajya lakṣaṇārtho vidhīyate |                    pratītā dharmajiñāsā vedādhyāyād anantarā ||
  88. 1.88tatkālasyāvaruddhatvāt snānābhāvaṃ hi lakṣayet |<25>                    virodho yugapatprāpteḥ, daurbalyaṃ vedabādhanāt ||
  89. 1.89snānasya tena bādhaḥ syād dharmajijñāsayā balāt |<26>                    dṛṣṭārthatvādisaṃyuktaṃ vākyaṃ lakṣaṇayā tv iti ||
  90. 1.90punaruktyā gatārthatvāt tyaktaṃ kaiś cit, tad ucyate |                    yady apy asya bhaved vācyam ānantaryam asaṃśayam ||
  91. 1.91tathāpi pūrvatāmātraṃ lakṣayed avirodhataḥ |                    granthagrahaṇamātre ca kṛte snānaṃ virudhyate ||
  92. 1.92adhītyetyadhigamyeti vyākhyāne tv avirodhitā |                    yas tv evamavirodhitvaṃ kurvannāplavanaṃ vadet ||
  93. 1.93adṛṣṭāyātha vāpy anyaḥ saṃskāraṃ tasya cottaram |                    ihāsnānādiniyamo yaḥ kṛto brahmacāriṇaḥ ||
  94. 1.94avidhitvam anāśritya so 'vasānam apekṣate |                    tato 'pekṣāvaśāt snānam asnānādinivartanam ||
  95. 1.95virodhasāhacaryābhyāṃ dṛṣṭārthatvena lakṣayet |<27>                    tasmād adhyayanasnānajijñāsākramavācinām ||
  96. 1.96dṛṣṭārthatvāya śabdānām evaṃ vyākhyeyam āśritā |                    snātvā jijñāsamāno 'pi nanu vedaṃ na bādhate ||
  97. 1.97tenāvirodhitā tasya, ityevaṃ vadata uttaram |                    yathaivādhyayanāt snānaṃ smaryate samanantaram ||
  98. 1.98tathā tataḥ paro 'py anyaḥ padārtho 'nyaḥ paras tataḥ |                    tataś cāvaśyakartavye bādhe smārtasya kasya cit ||
  99. 1.99yogyatvād āgate kāle prāthamyāt snānabādhanam |                    so 'yaṃ pāṭhakramasyārthād bādha ity avagamyate ||<28>
  100. 1.100guṇapradhānayor vāpi virodhād guṇabādhanam |                    snānopalakṣitā cātra nivṛttir guruveśmanaḥ ||
  101. 1.101virodhitvena bādhyeta na tu madhvādibhakṣaṇam |                    tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhanmadhumāṃsādyavarjayan ||
  102. 1.102jijñāsetāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate |                    gurugehanivṛttyaṃśo yāvac ca na samāpyate ||
  103. 1.103tāvat sakalavācitvān na snānaṃ paryavasyati |                    gurugehādanāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate ||
  104. 1.104tatparatvavidhānāc ca na tāvad dārasaṅgrahaḥ |                    vyākhyāya kīrtitā cātra snāyād iti punaḥ smṛtiḥ ||<29>
  105. 1.105smāvartiṣṭa metyādi smṛter yady apy anantaram |                    viparītārtham ity asmāt tadvākyād apanīyate ||
  106. 1.106athaśabdena yo bādhaḥ purastād upavarṇitaḥ |                    tanmātrasyaiva bādho 'tra dṛṣṭārthatvāt pradarśitaḥ ||
  107. 1.107smṛtiprāptam idānīṃ tu madhumāṃsādyavarjanam |                    pratiṣedhann adṛṣṭārthaṃ sūtrakāro na śobhate ||
  108. 1.108nivṛttya gurugehāc ca jijñāsārthaḥ punar bhavet |                    praveśaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭārtha iti naiveha sūtritaḥ ||
  109. 1.109nirgamo hi kṛtārthasya dṛṣṭārtho guruveśmanaḥ |                    smaryate tasya nārthaḥ syād akṛtārthasya nirgame ||
  110. 1.110athaśabdaprasiddhyaiva vedagrahaṇahetutā |                    ānantaryopadeśitvād ataḥ śabdena kiṃ punaḥ ||<30>
  111. 1.111yogyatvam athaśabdena yady api pratipāditam |                    tad eva hetur atreti nātaḥśabdād vinā bhavet ||
  112. 1.112lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣasyaiva tadā tad dhi prasajyate |                    jijñāsāyāś ca hetutve phalārthatvādi sambhavet ||
  113. 1.113ataḥśabdagṛhītaṃ vā tatrādhyayanam āśritam |                    hetāvakathyamāne hi maṅgalādy apy asau vadet ||<31>
  114. 1.114snānabādhasya vā hetur ata ity ucyate punaḥ |                    yogyasyādhītavedatvān nāvasthātuṃ hi labhyate ||
  115. 1.115sanvācyecchāntaraṃ karma jñānaṃ vyāpnoti tāvatā |                    jñānopasarjanā saiva na tu vidhyādi gamyate ||
  116. 1.116iṣes tu karma bāhyaḥ syād dharmaḥ sā vātha vā dvayam |                    samānakartṛkatvaṃ tu tumunoktaṃ liṅā vidhiḥ ||
  117. 1.117evaṃ viṣayanānātvān na kā cit punaruktatā |                    sūtritecchābhinirvṛttyai dvitīyecchātra sūtritā ||
  118. 1.118prakṛtyā vikṛtir yasmāc caturthyantā samasyate |                    tādarthye yūpadārvādau tenāsminn asamāsatā ||<32>
  119. 1.119sa hi tasyety anenokto dharmasyety eṣa vigrahaḥ |                    dharmāyeti tu tādarthye ṣaṣṭhī vṛtteti kathyate ||
  120. 1.120prāpnoty atra caturthy eva viśeṣaś ced vivakṣitaḥ |                    sāmānyasya vivakṣāyāṃ tādṛśaṃ kathyate katham ||
  121. 1.121sambandhamātra evaiṣā ṣaṣṭhyutpannā tathāpi tu |                    viśeṣaniṣṭhatā tasyā bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
  122. 1.122sādhanābhāsatā cātra pūrvapakṣārthagocarā |                    anyasādhanam anyasya sādhanābhāsa ucyate ||
  123. 1.123kratvarthaṃ puruṣārthasya tadarthaṃ ca krator iti |<33>                    śeṣalakṣaṇaśabdaś ca kṛtsnaśāstravivakṣayā ||
  124. 1.124prasiddhaḥ śakyate jñātum prasiddhatvāt tu neṣyate |                    aprasiddhas tv aśakyatvānnatarām ity ato 'bravīt ||
  125. 1.125jijñāsyaḥ saṃśayād dharmaḥ śreyaskaratayāpi ca |                    asandigdho hy ajijñāsyo yo vā syān niṣprayojanaḥ ||
  126. 1.126svarūpādiṣu dharmasya dvidhā vipratipadyate |                    pūrvaṃ pramāṇarūpābhyām, <34> pādenādyasya nirṇayaḥ ||
  127. 1.127sthite vedapramāṇatve punar vākyārthanirṇaye |                    matir bahuvidāṃ puṃsāṃ saṃśayān nopajāyate ||
  128. 1.128ke cid āhur asāv arthaḥ, ke cin nāsāv ayaṃ tv iti |                    tannirṇayārtham apy etat paraṃ śāstraṃ praṇīyate ||

Chapter 2 codanāsūtra CDS

  1. 2.1dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ codanocyate |                    svarūpādes tataḥ siddhaḥ, <35> svarūpaṃ ceha sūtryate ||
  2. 2.2dvayam ekena sūtreṇa śrutyarthābhyāṃ nirūpyate |                    svarūpe 'pi hi tasyokte pramāṇaṃ kathyate 'rthataḥ ||
  3. 2.3kimādyapekṣitaiḥ pūrṇaḥ samarthaḥ pratyayo vidhau |                    tena pravartakaṃ vākyaṃ śāstre 'smin codanocyate ||
  4. 2.4codanaiva pramāṇaṃ cetyetaddharme 'vadhāritam |                    sākāṅkṣam iti manvāno yuktileśaṃ dvaye 'spṛśat ||<36>
  5. 2.5sambhāvyate pramāṇatvaṃ śabdasyaivaṃvidheṣv api |                    indriyāder asāmarthyaṃ vakṣyamāṇamadīdiśat ||
  6. 2.6atyantāsaty api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi |                    tenotsarge sthite tasya doṣābhāvāt pramāṇatā ||
  7. 2.7codanety abravīc cātra śabdamātravivakṣayā |                    na hi bhūtādiviṣayaḥ kaś cid asti vidhāyakaḥ ||
  8. 2.8indriyādivyudāsena śabdo yāvan na sādhyate |                    tāvac ca tadviśeṣasya kuto vāvasaro bhavet ||
  9. 2.9nimittamātraṃ vocyeta pramāṇaṃ ceha lakṣaṇam |<37>                    pramāṇaṃ tv api śabdo vā tajjñānaṃ vā nirūpyate |
  10. 2.10padārthas tanmatir vā syād vākyārthādhigamo 'pi vā |                    pūrveṣāṃ tu pramāṇatve phalatvaṃ tasya gamyate ||
  11. 2.11jñāne lakṣaṇaśabdo 'yaṃ yadi nāma prayujyate |                    codanoktis tadā kāryaṃ tatkāryaṃ cāpi lakṣayet ||
  12. 2.12nimittamātre śabde ca pramāṇe mukhyavṛttayoḥ |                    sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāc codanālakṣaṇatvayoḥ ||
  13. 2.13dravyakriyāguṇādīnāṃ dharmatvaṃ sthāpayiṣyate |                    teṣām aindriyakatve 'pi na tādrūpyeṇa dharmatā ||
  14. 2.14śreyaḥsādhanatā hy eṣāṃ nityaṃ vedāt pratīyate |                    tādrūpyeṇa ca dharmatvaṃ tasmān nendriyagocaraḥ ||
  15. 2.15pradarśanārtham atroktam indriyaṃ sūtrakāravat |<38>                    nānyat kiñ ceti vācchedaḥ sāmānyārthaḥ prayujyate ||
  16. 2.16tadasāmarthyasiddhyai ca punar indriyakīrtanam |                    kiñ ceti madhyam acchedo hetupraśne prayujyate ||
  17. 2.17yady api tv anumānasyāpy evamādau samarthatā |                    vinā sambandhabodhena na tu tasyodbhavaḥ kva cit |
  18. 2.18na sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ dharmasambandhadarśanam |                    liṅgasya kasya cit siddhaṃ yena syād anumānatā ||
  19. 2.19nanu śabdo 'pi sambandhabodhānnarte pravarttate |                    padaṃ tat, na ca tadvācyo dharmaḥ, vākyārtha eva saḥ ||
  20. 2.20vākyasyāvācakatvaṃ ca, <39> padārthānāṃ ca hetutā |                    sambandhasyānapekṣāṇāṃ vākyārthe sthāpayiṣyate ||
  21. 2.21nityatvāder asiddhatvād, abhyupetyocyate 'tha vā |                    sutarām apramāṇatvaṃ vaktṛprāmāṇyavarjanāt ||
  22. 2.22pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭaṃ hi śabdo 'rthaṃ prāpayet sadā |                    smṛtivac ca svayaṃ tasya prāmāṇyaṃ nopapadyate ||
  23. 2.23nūnaṃ tatrānubhūto 'sāvityāptoktinibandhanā |                    buddhiḥ sākṣād adṛṣṭe 'pi yuktārthe puruṣoktitaḥ ||<40>
  24. 2.24nātmīyād anyadīyād vā pratyakṣāder vinā kva cit |                    vacasaḥ satyatā dṛṣṭā tathā syāc codanāsv api ||
  25. 2.25tena saty api vijñāne pratijñāder yathaiva hi |                    svātantryān na pramāṇatvaṃ tathā vede 'pi dṛśyatām ||
  26. 2.26svargayāgādisambandhaviṣayā codanā mṛṣā |                    pratyakṣādyagatārthatvādīdṛgbuddhādivākyavat ||
  27. 2.27yad vāptenāpraṇītatvād bālonmattādivākyavat |                    vyomādivac ca nityatvāt prāmāṇyasya nirākṛtiḥ ||
  28. 2.28yadi vā puruṣādhīnaprāmāṇyāḥ sarvacodanāḥ |                    svato vā na pramāṇaṃ syur vākyatvāt puruṣoktivat ||
  29. 2.29prāmāṇyaṃ vā narāpekṣaṃ sarvaśabdeṣu gamyatām |                    śabdaiḥ sambandhyamānatvād apramāṇyaṃ tathaiva hi |<41>
  30. 2.30na syād vaktṛguṇānāṃ ced vacaḥ prāmāṇyahetutā |                    taddoṣair apramāṇatvaṃ kim ity asya bhaviṣyati ||
  31. 2.31evaṃ sthite tu vedasya sati vāsati vā nare |                    prāmāṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā nanv ity etadacūcudat |
  32. 2.32tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ buddhavākye 'pi yujyate |                    tato 'pi pratyayotpattes tasmāj jātyuttaraṃ tv idam ||
  33. 2.33sarvavijñānaviṣayam idaṃ tāvat parīkṣyatām |                    pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve svataḥ kiṃ parato 'tha vā ||
  34. 2.34svato 'satām asādhyatvāt ke cid āhur dvayaṃ svataḥ |                    apare kāraṇotpannaguṇadoṣāvadhāraṇāt ||<42>
  35. 2.35svatas tāvad dvayaṃ nāsti, virodhāt, parato na ca |                    niḥsvabhāvatvam evaṃ hi jñānarūpe prasajyate |
  36. 2.36kathaṃ hy anyānapekṣasya viparītātmasambhavaḥ |                    kimātmakaṃ bhavet tac ca svabhāvadvayavarjitam |
  37. 2.37vijñānavyaktibhedena bhavec ced aviruddhatā |                    tathāpy anyānapekṣatve kiṃ kveti na nirūpyate ||<43>
  38. 2.38tasmāt svābhāvikaṃ teṣām apramāṇatvam iṣyatām |                    prāmāṇyañ ca parāpekṣam, atra nyāyo 'bhidhīyate ||
  39. 2.39aprāmānyam avastutvān na syāt kāraṇadoṣataḥ |                    vastutvāt tu guṇais teṣāṃ prāmāṇyam upajanyate ||
  40. 2.40prāmāṇyaṃ hi yadotsargāt tadabhāvo 'tha kṛtrimaḥ |                    tadā svapnādibodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ kena vāryate ||
  41. 2.41matpakṣe kāraṇābhāvāt prāmānyaṃ nopajāyate |                    hetumattvaprasaṅgo 'to na bhaviṣyaty avastunaḥ ||
  42. 2.42indriyādiguṇāś cāsya kāraṇam, tadasad dvidhā |<44>                    duṣṭatvād indriyādīnām abhāve 'nyatamasya vā |
  43. 2.43ata eva ca vo bhrāntir doṣair mithyātvadhīr iti |                    tadvyāptes tu guṇābhāvas tatkṛtā hy apramāṇatā ||
  44. 2.44tasmāt kāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ jñānaprāmāṇyakāraṇam |                    svabhāvato 'pramāṇatvaṃ tadabhāvena lakṣyate |
  45. 2.45anvayavyatirekābhyām aprāmāṇyaṃ na doṣataḥ |                    nājñāne dṛśyate hy etatkāraṇābhāvahetuke ||
  46. 2.46tataś ca puruṣābhāvāt sati vā śuddhyasambhavāt |                    nirmūlatvāt pramāṇatvaṃ codanāyāṃ na yujyate ||<45>
  47. 2.47svataḥ sarvapramāṇānāṃ prāmāṇyam iti gamyatām |                    na hi svato 'satī śaktiḥ kartum anyena śakyate ||
  48. 2.48ātmalābhe ca bhāvānāṃ kāraṇāpekṣatā bhavet |                    labdhātmanāṃ svakāryeṣu pravṛttiḥ svayam eva tu |
  49. 2.49jāte 'pi yadi vijñāne tāvan nārtho 'vadhāryate |<46>                    yāvatkāraṇaśuddhatvaṃ na pramāṇāntarād bhavet ||
  50. 2.50tatra jñānāntarotpādaḥ pratīkṣyaḥ kāraṇāntarāt |                    yāvad dhi na paricchinnā śuddhis tāvad asatsamā ||
  51. 2.51tasyāpi kāraṇe śuddhe tajjñāne syāt pramāṇatā |                    tasyāpy evam itīcchaś ca na kva cid vyavatiṣṭhate ||
  52. 2.52yadā svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ tadānyan naiva gṛhyate |                    nivarttatte hi mithyātvaṃ doṣājñānād ayatnataḥ ||
  53. 2.53tasmād bodhātmakatvena prāptā buddheḥ pramāṇatā |                    arthānyathātvahetūtthadoṣajñānād apodyate ||
  54. 2.54aprāmāṇyaṃ tridhā bhinnaṃ mithyātvājñānasaṃśayaiḥ |                    vastutvād dvividhasyātra sambhavo duṣṭakāraṇāt ||<47>
  55. 2.55avijñāne tu doṣāṇāṃ vyāpāro naiva kalpyate |                    kāraṇābhāvatas tv eva tatsiddhaṃ nastvaduktivat ||
  56. 2.56doṣataś cāpramāṇatve svataḥprāmāṇyavādinām |                    guṇajñānānavasthāvan na doṣeṣu prasajyate ||
  57. 2.57sākṣād viparyayajñānāl laghvyeva tv apramāṇatā |                    pūrvābādhena notpattir uttarasya hi sidhyati ||
  58. 2.58duṣṭakāraṇabodhe tu siddhe 'pi viṣayāntare |                    arthāt tulyārthatāṃ prāpya bādho godohanādivat ||<48>
  59. 2.59tatra doṣāntarajñānaṃ bādhadhīr vā parā na cet |                    tadudbhūtau dvitīyasya mithyātvād ādyamānatā ||
  60. 2.60svata eva hi tatrāpi doṣājñānāt pramāṇatā |                    doṣajñāne tv anutpanne na śaṅkyā niṣpramāṇatā ||<49>
  61. 2.61evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ |                    prārthyate tāvataivaikaṃ svataḥ prāmāṇyam aśnute ||
  62. 2.62śabde doṣodbhavas tāvad vaktradhīna iti sthitiḥ |                    tadabhāvaḥ kva cit tāvad guṇavadvaktṛkatvataḥ |
  63. 2.63tadguṇair apakṛṣṭānāṃ śabde saṃkrāntyasambhavāt |                    yadā vaktur abhāvena na syur doṣā nirāśrayāḥ |
  64. 2.64pauruṣeye dvayaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ doṣābhāvo guṇās tathā |                    prāmāṇyaṃ tatra guṇato naiva syād ity udāhṛtam ||
  65. 2.65tasmād guṇebhyo doṣāṇām abhāvas tadabhāvataḥ |                    aprāmāṇyadvayāsattvaṃ tenotsargo 'napoditaḥ ||<50>
  66. 2.66pratyayotpattihetutvāt prāmāṇyaṃ nāpanīyate |                    doṣābhāvo guṇebhyaś cen nanu saivāsthitir bhavet ||
  67. 2.67tadā tu vyāpriyante hi jñāyamānatayā guṇāḥ |                    doṣābhāve tu vijñeye sattāmātropakāriṇaḥ ||
  68. 2.68tatrāpavādanirmuktir vaktrabhāvāl laghīyasī |                    vede tenāpramāṇatvaṃ nāśaṅkām api gacchati ||
  69. 2.69ato vaktranadhīnatvāt prāmāṇye tadupāsanam |                    na yuktam, apramāṇatve kalpye tatprārthanā bhavet ||
  70. 2.70tataś cāptāpraṇītatvaṃ na doṣāyātra jāyate |                    prayogāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ pratisādhanam ||
  71. 2.71pauruṣeye tu vacane pramāṇāntaramūlatā |                    tadabhāve hi tad duṣyeditaran na kadā cana |<51>
  72. 2.72tenetaraiḥ pramāṇair yā codanānām asaṅgatiḥ |                    tayaiva syāt pramāṇatvam anuvādatvam anyathā ||
  73. 2.73anyasyāpi pramāṇatve saṅgatir naiva kāraṇam |                    tulyārthānāṃ vikalpyatvād ekaṃ tatra hi bodhakam ||
  74. 2.74yatrāpi syāt paricchedaḥ pramāṇair uttaraiḥ punaḥ |                    nūnaṃ tatrāpi pūrveṇa so 'rtho nāvadhṛtas tathā ||
  75. 2.75saṅgatyā yadi ceṣyeta pūrvapūrvapramāṇatā |                    pramāṇāntaram icchanto na vyavasthāṃ labhemahi |<52>
  76. 2.76kasya cit tu yadīṣyeta svata eva pramāṇatā |                    prathamasya tathābhāve pradveṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ ||
  77. 2.77śrotradhīś cāpramāṇaṃ syād itarābhir asaṅgateḥ |                    syāc cet tajjanitenaiva jñānenānyena saṅgatiḥ ||
  78. 2.78vede 'pi śatakṛtvaḥ syād buddhir uccāraṇānugā |                    sādhanāntarajanyā tu buddhir nāsti dvayor api ||
  79. 2.79yathā tv ekendriyādhīnajñānāntaranibandhanā |                    saṅgatiḥ kāraṇaṃ prāptā tathā vede 'pi kalpyatām ||
  80. 2.80tasmād dṛḍhaṃ yadutpannaṃ nāpi saṃvādamṛcchati |                    jñānāntareṇa vijñānaṃ tatpramāṇaṃ pratīyatām ||
  81. 2.81na cānumānataḥ sādhyā śabdādīnāṃ pramāṇatā |                    sarvasyaiva hi mā prāpat pramāṇāntarasādhyatā ||<53>
  82. 2.82nanu pramāṇam ityevaṃ pratyakṣādi na gṛhyate |                    na cetthamagṛhītena vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||
  83. 2.83prāmāṇyaṃ grahaṇāt pūrvaṃ svarūpeṇaiva saṃsthitam |                    nirapekṣaṃ svakāryeṣu gṛhyate pratyayāntaraiḥ ||
  84. 2.84tenāsya jñāyamānatvaṃ prāmāṇye nopayujyate |                    viṣayānubhāvo hy atra pūrvasmād eva labhyate |
  85. 2.85apramāṇaṃ punaḥ svārthagrāhakaṃ syāt svarūpataḥ |                    nivṛttis tasya mithyātve nāgṛhīte parair bhavet ||
  86. 2.86na hy arthasyātathābhāvaḥ pūrveṇārthas tathātvavat |<54>                    tatrāpy arthānyathābhāve dhīr yad vā duṣṭakāraṇe ||
  87. 2.87tāvataiva ca mithyātvaṃ gṛhyate nānyahetukam |                    utpattyavasthaṃ caivedaṃ pramāṇam iti mīyate ||
  88. 2.88ato yatrāpi mithyātvaṃ parebhyaḥ pratipādyate |                    tatrāpy etad dvayaṃ vācyaṃ na tu sādharmyamātrakam ||
  89. 2.89codanārthānyathābhāvaṃ kurvataś cānumānataḥ |                    tajjñānenaiva yo bādhaḥ sa kathaṃ vinivāryate ||
  90. 2.90tanmithyātvād abādhaś cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |                    nānumānād ato 'nyad dhi bādhakaṃ kiñ cid asti te ||
  91. 2.91na cānyair agrahe 'rthasya syād abhāvo rasādivat |                    teṣāṃ jihvādibhir yasmān niyamo grahaṇe 'sti hi ||<55>
  92. 2.92taddhiyaivārthabodhaś cet, tādṛgdharme bhaviṣyati |                    mamāsiddham idaṃ kin tu vedāj jāte 'vabodhane |
  93. 2.93vaktuṃ na dveṣamātreṇa yujyate satyavādinā |                    dveṣād asammatatvād vā na ca syād apramāṇatā ||
  94. 2.94na cātmecchābhyanujñābhyāṃ prāmāṇyam avakalpate |                    agnidāhādiduḥkhasya na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
  95. 2.95na cābhilāpikaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyenāvadhāryate |                    tasmād ālokavad vede sarvasādhāraṇe sati ||
  96. 2.96naivaṃ vipratipattavyam, bauddhāder vakṣyate 'ntaram |<56>                    puruṣāśaktitas tatra sāpavādatvasambhavaḥ ||
  97. 2.97vedasyāpauruṣeyatve siddhā tv evaṃ pramāṇatā |                    kartṛmattve tu vedasya samyaṅmithyātvavādibhiḥ ||
  98. 2.98kartā guṇāś ca doṣāś ca mahājanaparigrahaḥ |                    evamādi vinā yuktyā kalpyam, mīmāṃsakaiḥ punaḥ ||
  99. 2.99idānīm iva sarvatra dṛṣṭān nādhikam iṣyate |                    evambhūtasya vedasya jñānotpattiṃ prakurvataḥ ||
  100. 2.100svarūpaviparītatvasaṃśayau bhāṣyavāritau |                    nivārayiṣyate cāpi duṣṭakāraṇakalpanā ||
  101. 2.101puruṣābhāvatas tena taddvāreṇāpy aśaṅkitau |<57>                    tathā satyatathābhāvo buddhyanutpattim āśritaḥ ||
  102. 2.102tatra vipratiṣiddhatvaṃ bravītītyevamādinā |                    yathādṛṣṭārthavāditvaṃ tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
  103. 2.103indriyeti tu mūlaṃ ced asyāstītyevam abravīt |                    draṣṭṛtvasatyavāditve tac cet pratyayitāditi ||
  104. 2.104dṛśyamānārthavāditve syād anāptoktisatyatā |                    evaṃ tv ekāṅgavaikalyāt pratyudāharaṇasthitiḥ ||
  105. 2.105ekaikābhāvamātre syād āptatvaindriyakatvayoḥ |<58>                    apratyayitapakṣe syād aindriyasyāpy asatyatā ||
  106. 2.106anindriyatvapakṣe vā satpratyayitabhāṣitam |                    vyāhatagranthataivaṃ syāt, tasmāt pūrveṇa satyatā ||
  107. 2.107pareṇa mūlasadbhāva indriyeṇa tu darśitaḥ |                    aprāmāṇyanivṛttyarthaṃ doṣābhāvopavarṇanam ||
  108. 2.108guṇāt prāmāṇyam ityevaṃ tatpūrvaṃ sunirākṛtam |                    pūrvatra pratiṣiddhatvān naitat prāmāṇyakāraṇam ||<59>
  109. 2.109samuccayārtho vāśabdaḥ pūrvasmin, uttaratra ca |                    vikalpenobhayor āha pratyudāharaṇe pṛthak ||
  110. 2.110śakye 'py asatye mithyātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ satye 'py aśaktike |                    nānena vacaneneha sarvajñatvanirākriyā ||
  111. 2.111vacanād ṛta ityevam apavādo hi saṃśritaḥ |                    yadi ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ syāt sarvajñaḥ kena vāryate ||
  112. 2.112ekena tu pramāṇena sarvajño yena kalpyate |                    nūnaṃ sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasādīn pratipadyate ||<60>
  113. 2.113yajjātīyaiḥ pramāṇais tu yajjātīyārthadarśanam |                    bhaved idānīṃ lokasya tathā kālāntare 'py abhūt |
  114. 2.114yatrāpy atiśayo dṛṣṭaḥ sa svārthānatilaṅghanāt |                    dūrasūkṣmādidṛṣṭau syān na rūpe śrotravṛttitā ||
  115. 2.115bhaviṣyati na dṛṣṭaṃ ca pratyakṣasya manāgapi |                    sāmarthyam, nānumānāder liṅgādirahite kva cit ||
  116. 2.116sarvajñakalpanānyais tu vede cāpauruṣeyatā |                    tulyatā kalpitā yena tenedaṃ sampradhāryatām ||<61>
  117. 2.117sarvajño dṛśyate tāvan nedānīm asmadādibhiḥ |                    nirākaraṇavacchakyā na cāsīd iti kalpanā ||
  118. 2.118na cāgamena sarvajñaḥ, tadīye 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt |                    narāntarapraṇītasya prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
  119. 2.119na cāpy evamparo nityaḥ śakyo labdhum ihāgamaḥ |                    nityaś ced arthavādatvaṃ tatpare syād anityatā ||
  120. 2.120āgamasya ca nityatve siddhe tatkalpanā vṛthā |<62>                    yatas taṃ pratipadyante dharmam eva tato narāḥ ||
  121. 2.121yo 'pīndriyārthasambandhaviṣaye satyavāditām |                    dṛṣṭvā tadvacanatvena śraddheye 'rthe 'pi kalpayet ||
  122. 2.122tenāpi pāratantryeṇa bādhitā syāt pramāṇatā |                    prāmāṇyaṃ cet svayaṃ tasya kāpekṣānyendriyādiṣu ||
  123. 2.123yathaivātrendriyādibhyaḥ paricchedāt pramāṇatā |                    śraddheye 'pi tathaiva syān na svātantryeṇa labhyate |
  124. 2.124yathā ca teṣāṃ satyatvaṃ sidhyaty etena hetunā |                    tathānyānavabuddhārthaprāmāṇyābhāvasādhanam |<63>
  125. 2.125aśraddheyārthasatyatvaṃ śraddheye cāpy asatyatā |                    pūrvajñānānuvāditvaṃ dṛṣṭāntavad iheṣyatām ||
  126. 2.126api cālaukikārthatve sati puṃvākyahetukam |                    mithyātvaṃ bauddhavākyānāṃ syād anyonyaṃ sapakṣataḥ ||
  127. 2.127dharmādharmātiriktārthe prāmāṇyaṃ ca prasajyate |                    sāṃkhyādiṣu ca jīvatsu dṛṣṭānto durlabho 'sya ca |
  128. 2.128alaukikārthavācitvaṃ nṛvākyatve satīti ca |                    parasparam apekṣyaiva bauddhādeḥ syān mṛṣārthatā ||
  129. 2.129vaded evaṃ ca yo nāma vādī prathamasaṅgataḥ |                    tasyāpi hetuḥ syād eṣa bhavantaṃ pratyasaṃśayam ||
  130. 2.130buddhādīnām asarvajñam iti satyaṃ vaco mama |                    maduktatvād yathaivāgnir uṣṇo bhāsvara ity api ||
  131. 2.131pratyakṣaṃ ca maduktatvaṃ tvayā sādhyā taduktatā |                    tena hetur madīyaḥ syāt sandigdhāsiddhatā tava ||
  132. 2.132pratyakṣādyavisaṃvādi prameyatvādi yasya ca |                    sadbhāvavāraṇe śaktaṃ ko nu taṃ kalpayiṣyati ||<64>
  133. 2.133na cāpi smṛtyavicchedāt sarvajñaḥ parikalpyate |                    vigānāt, chinnamūlatvāt, kaiś cid eva parigrahāt ||
  134. 2.134sarvajño 'sāv iti hy eva tatkāle tu bubhutsubhiḥ |                    tajjñānajñeyavijñānarahitair gamyate katham ||
  135. 2.135kalpanīyāś ca sarvajñā bhaveyur bahavas tava |                    ya eva syād asarvajñaḥ sa sarvajñaṃ na budhyate ||
  136. 2.136sarvajño 'navabuddhaś ca yenaiva syān na taṃ prati |                    tadvākyānāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ mūlājñāne 'nyavākyavat ||
  137. 2.137rāgādirahite cāsmin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite |                    deśanānyapraṇītaiva syād ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt ||<65>
  138. 2.138sānnidhyamātratas tasya puṃsaścintāmaṇer iva |                    niḥsaranti yathākāmaṃ kuḍyādibhyo 'pi deśanāḥ ||
  139. 2.139evamādyucyamānaṃ tu śraddadhānasya śobhate |                    kuḍyādiniḥsṛtatvāc ca nāśvāso deśanāsu naḥ ||
  140. 2.140kin nu buddhapraṇītāḥ syuḥ kimu kaiś cid durātmabhiḥ |                    adṛśyair vipralambhārthaṃ piśācādibhir īritāḥ ||
  141. 2.141evaṃ yaiḥ kevalaṃ jñānam indriyādyanapekṣiṇaḥ |                    sūkṣmātītādiviṣayaṃ jīvasya parikalpitam ||
  142. 2.142narte tadāgamāt sidhyen na ca tenāgamo vinā |                    dṛṣṭānto 'pi na tasyānyo nṛṣu kaś cit pravartate ||<66>
  143. 2.143nityāgamāvabodho 'pi pratyākhyeyo 'nayā diśā |                    na hi tatrāpi visrambho dṛṣṭo 'nena kṛto 'tha vā ||
  144. 2.144sarvadā cāpi puruṣāḥ prāyeṇānṛtavādinaḥ |                    yathādyatve na visrambhas tathātītārthakīrtane ||
  145. 2.145svapnādijñānavac cāpi pratyayo 'syāgamārthayoḥ |                    bhaved iti saśaṅkānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ gamyate katham ||
  146. 2.146puruṣātiśayaś ceṣṭaḥ saiva cāgamanityatā |                    kalpitaṃ smaraṇaṃ cāsya janmāntaranibandhanam ||
  147. 2.147grāhyatve cāgamasyaivaṃ dveṣo 'rthagrahaṇe vṛthā |                    yo hy anuccāritaṃ śabdaṃ gahṇātyarthe 'sya kā kathā |<67>
  148. 2.148pumāṃs tāvat svatantraḥ syād arthagrahaṇavādinām |                    āgamapratibhāne tu pāratantryaṃ dvayor api ||
  149. 2.149anekapuruṣasthatvād ekatraiva ca janmani |                    grahaṇasmaraṇād vede na svātantryaṃ vihanyate ||
  150. 2.150anyathākaraṇe cāsya bahubhyaḥ syān nivāraṇam |                    ekasya pratibhānaṃ tu kṛtakān na viśiṣyate ||
  151. 2.151ataś ca sampradāye ca naikaḥ puruṣa iṣyate |                    bahavaḥ paratantrāḥ syuḥ sarve hy adyatvavannarāḥ ||
  152. 2.152evaṃ ca kalpayantyanye yāvadāgamasiddhaye |                    tāvan na kalpayaty etat samatvaṃ jaimineḥ paraiḥ ||<68>
  153. 2.153na hi dṛṣṭādhikaṃ kiñ cit prāmāṇye tena kalpyate |                    aprāmāṇyanimitteṣu parasyādṛṣṭakalpanā ||
  154. 2.154dṛṣṭaprāmāṇyabādhaś ca nāstikasya prasajyate |                    utpanne sati vijñāne balād bādhaprakalpanā ||
  155. 2.155sādhite puruṣābhāve nirdoṣajñānajanmanaḥ |                    pratyakṣān nāstikair vācyo viśeṣaś codanādhiyaḥ ||
  156. 2.156upadeśo 'nyathā na syād atīndriyanidandhanaḥ |                    tasya kartrā na ced dṛṣṭaḥ so 'rtha ity arthakalpanā ||
  157. 2.157yad vānumānam evedam upadeśitvam ucyate |                    dṛṣṭārthapūrvatāvyāptam, vyatireko 'sya nanv iti ||<69>
  158. 2.158anyathāpy upapannatvaṃ vyāmohād iti kathyate |                    liṅgasya vyabhicāro vā bālavākyanidarśanāt |
  159. 2.159vedāj jñātvopadiṣṭaṃ ced ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam |                    vedād apītyanenoktam, manvādeś caitad iṣyate ||
  160. 2.160anyathā saṃvidāno 'pi vivakṣaty anyathā yataḥ |                    tasmād ekāntato nāsti puṃvākyāt taddhiyāṃ gatiḥ ||<70>
  161. 2.161bhrāntasyānyavivakṣāyām anyad vākyaṃ ca dṛśyate |                    yathāvivakṣam apy etat tasmān naiva pravartate ||
  162. 2.162vaktṛdhīr āptavākyeṣu gamyate, anyatra viplutiḥ |                    tenotsargāpavādābhyāṃ vacasaḥ śaktir ucyate ||
  163. 2.163padārtharacanāyatto vākyārthapratyayodbhavaḥ |                    vivakṣāpūrvavijñānavaśāc ca racanākṛtiḥ ||
  164. 2.164vivakṣāntarayuktā hi kurvāṇā racanāntaram |                    āvāpodvāpabhedena dṛśyante 'rtheṣu mānavāḥ |
  165. 2.165tenārthapratyayotpāde śroturjāte 'pi vākyataḥ |                    jñāto nūnam aneneti vakturjñāne matir bhavet ||
  166. 2.166āptoktikāraṇaṃ kañ cid anuyuṅkte naraṃ yadā |                    tadā ca nirdiśatyāptaṃ sa jānātyetad ityasau ||<71>
  167. 2.167tajjñānāntaritatvāc ca śabdās tāvad udāsate |                    prāmāṇyasthāpanaṃ tu syād vaktṛdhīhetusambhavāt ||
  168. 2.168arthe pūrvapratīte 'pi niścayo hi tadāśrayaḥ |                    tenārthajñānagamyāpi prāmāṇye saiva pūrvabhāk |
  169. 2.169ato 'tra puṃnimittatvād upapannā mṛṣārthatā |                    na tu syāt tatsvabhāvatvaṃ vede vakturabhāvataḥ |
  170. 2.170tadbuddhyantarayor nāstīty artho 'rthaiś ca pratīyate |<72>                    ato na jñānapūrvatvam apekṣyaṃ nāyathārthatā ||
  171. 2.171apramāṇatvasiddhau vā dṛṣṭānto ya udāhṛtaḥ |                    buddhādivacanaṃ tasya sādhyenāsaṅgatocyate ||
  172. 2.172teṣām api hi yat kāryaṃ pūrvatra pratipāditam |                    tatra samyaktvam arthe tu vyāpāro naiva vidyate ||
  173. 2.173svavyāpārātirikte 'rthe vedasyāpi mṛṣārthatā |                    pūrvapakṣārthavattvena prasaktā siddhasādhyatā ||
  174. 2.174ajñātvaivamabhiprāyaṃ kṛtakākṛtakatvayoḥ |                    satyamithyātvahetūktimātrajñānāt paro 'bravīt ||
  175. 2.175nanu sāmānyatodṛṣṭam, <73> nānyatvād ityadūṣaṇam |                    anyatvād eva dṛṣṭānto na hi pakṣe sapakṣatā ||
  176. 2.176tasmād ayam abhiprāyo bhāṣyakārasya varṇyate |                    abhyupetyārthaviṣayaṃ vākyavyāpāram ucyate |
  177. 2.177yadi syād vyavadhāne 'pi vākyārthāpekṣayānṛtam |                    dṛṣṭānto nṛvaco 'trāpi hetuḥ sādhāraṇo bhavet ||
  178. 2.178satyeṣv api hi dṛṣṭaiva paurṣeyeṣu vākyatā |                    atīndriye 'pi kiñ cid dhi satyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛcchayā ||<74>
  179. 2.179nānyatvād iti cānena paroktād anyatocyate |                    anyo hy eṣa tadābhāsaḥ, vipakṣaṃ vānyam abravīt |
  180. 2.180yad vānyasmād visaṃvādān mithyātvaṃ tatra na tv iha |                    viṣayasyāpi cānyatvāt sādhanāsaṅgataiva sā ||
  181. 2.181na hy anyasyeti naikasmin mṛṣārthe 'nyamṛṣārthatā |                    vivakṣāyā mṛṣārthatve na ca vākye mṛṣārthatā ||
  182. 2.182śyāmatve puṃstvavac caitat sādhāraṇye nidarśanam |<75>                    parokter vāpi duṣṭatvād vikalpasamam ucyate ||
  183. 2.183yad vā pramāṇam evedaṃ samyaktve 'nyatvam ucyate |                    dhiruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ |
  184. 2.184codanājanitā buddhiḥ pramāṇaṃ doṣavarjitaiḥ |                    kāraṇair janyamānatvāl liṅgāptoktyakṣabuddhivat |
  185. 2.185tathānāptāpraṇītoktijanyatvād bādhavarjanāt |                    deśakālādibhedādau cāptoktipratyayo yathā ||
  186. 2.186akartṛkatvasiddhyā ca hetutvaṃ sādhayiṣyate |<76>                    evamādyavabudhyāyaṃ nānyatvād ity avocata |
  187. 2.187pratyakṣas tv iti dārḍhyaṃ vā prāthamyaṃ vāpi lakṣayet |                    svarūpataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ mithyātvaṃ pararūpataḥ ||
  188. 2.188jñānābhāvaś ca mithyātvaṃ dvayasyāsambhavād yadi |                    pratyakṣaṃ tatpareṣāṃ ca siddham asyānumānataḥ ||
  189. 2.189yathā ca tava mithyātvaṃ sādhanaṃ sādhayed idam |                    tathā ca bādhakādhīnaṃ mithyātvam api sādhayet ||
  190. 2.190dharma ity upasaṃhārye yacchreyaskarabhāṣaṇam |                    taddharmapadavācyārthanirūpaṇavivakṣayā ||<77>
  191. 2.191śreyo hi puruṣaprītiḥ sā dravyaguṇakarmabhiḥ |                    codanālakṣaṇaiḥ sādhyā tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatā ||
  192. 2.192anyat sādhyam adṛṣṭvaiva yāgādīnanuniṣṭhataḥ |                    dhārmikatvasamākhyānaṃ tadyogād iti gamyate ||
  193. 2.193paśvādīni ca dharmasya phalānīti vyavasthitam |                    citrāgodohanādīnāṃ tāny uktāni phalāni ca ||
  194. 2.194tasmāt teṣv eva dharmatvam, dhrmāṇīti ca darśanāt |                    liṅgasaṃkhyāvinirmukto dharmaśabdo nidarśanam |<78>
  195. 2.195antaḥkaraṇavṛttau vā vāsanāyāṃ ca cetasaḥ |                    pudgaleṣu ca puṇyeṣu nṛguṇe 'pūrvajanmani ||
  196. 2.196prayogo dharmaśabdasya na dṛṣṭaḥ, na ca sādhanam |                    puruṣārthasya te jñātuṃ śakyante codanādibhiḥ ||
  197. 2.197na ca vastvantaraṃ śakyam apūrvaṃ svargayāgayoḥ |                    jñātuṃ sādhanabhūtaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā nāpy ato 'nyathā |
  198. 2.198śrutasādhanasādhyatvatyāgenāśrutakalpanā |                    prasajyetāsya tādrūpye vyatireke tv arūpatā ||<79>
  199. 2.199tasmāt phale pravṛttasya yāgādeḥ śaktimātrakam |                    utpattau vāpi paśvāder apūrvaṃ na tataḥ pṛthak ||
  200. 2.200śaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ bhāvaśabdair viśeṣataḥ |                    nopākhyāyanta ityevaṃ nāpūrvaṃ dharmaśabdatā |
  201. 2.201purastāc codanāśabdo vidhāv eva vyavasthitaḥ |                    na ca tallakṣaṇā hiṃsā pratyudāharaṇaṃ katham ||<80>
  202. 2.202codanālakṣaṇo yaś ca śyenādir hi gamyate |                    niṣedhābhāvatas tasya kathaṃ brūyād anarthatā ||
  203. 2.203yady api syād vidhispṛṣṭe niṣedho naiva tādṛśaḥ |                    vijñāyate hy anarthatvaṃ ṣoḍaśigrahaṇādivat ||
  204. 2.204codanālakṣaṇaṃ coktvā niṣiddhatvād virudhyate |                    śyenādāv upadiṣṭe ca hiṃsā hīti na yujyate ||
  205. 2.205hiṃsā hi phalam eteṣāṃ bhinnā tebhyaḥ svarūpataḥ |                    sā hi prāṇaviyogātmā śyenas tatrāsivatpṛthak ||
  206. 2.206upadeśābhidhānaṃ ca nāvidheye 'vakalpate |<81>                    śyenāder avidhāne ca kasyānyasya vidheyatā ||
  207. 2.207sarvatrāvasthito nyāyo bhāvanāṃśadvaye vidhiḥ |                    sa bādhyeta, iha ye cāmī jyotiṣṭomādayo matāḥ ||
  208. 2.208dharmatvena na te 'pi syur hiṃsāsādhanakā hi te |                    na cāvidhīyamānasya phalatatsādhanāṅgatā ||
  209. 2.209sādhanatvena vihitaṃ na cāvihitam ucyate |                    sādhyatvena vidhānaṃ tu naiveṣṭaṃ lokavedayoḥ ||
  210. 2.210tenaivamarthaśabdasya prayojanam ihocyate |<82>                    pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yā śabdaśravaṇena dhīḥ |
  211. 2.211sā codaneti sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdaye sthitam |                    pravartakagṛhītis tu syād udāharaṇārthatā ||
  212. 2.212tātparye hy arthaśabdasya neyaṃ vyākhyopapadyate |                    arthagrahaṇalabhyaṃ vā tatpravartakabhāṣaṇam |
  213. 2.213dharme pramāṇabhūtāyās tad vā lakṣaṇam uktavān |                    evaṃ sati vidhibhyaḥ syād vidheyārthāvadhāraṇam ||
  214. 2.214niṣedhebhyo niṣedhyānām anarthatvena nirṇayaḥ |                    tenārthagrahaṇenoktā vidheyasyeha dharmatā ||
  215. 2.215niṣedhyānām anarthatvam arthasiddhaṃ na sūtritam |                    tasmād ubhayam ityatra vidheyapratiṣedhyayoḥ ||
  216. 2.216yāgādibrahmahatyādivargayoḥ syān nidarśanam |<83>                    śyenādīnāṃ vidheyatvādiṣṭasyāpi ca sādhanāt ||
  217. 2.217upacārād anarthatvaṃ phaladvāreṇa varṇyate |                    pratiṣiddhā hi setyatra sphuṭam etat kariṣyate ||
  218. 2.218hiṃsā hīti ca yac cāpi brūte nābhicared iti |                    śyenādīnāṃ svarūpe tu nottaragranthasaṅgatiḥ ||
  219. 2.219vihitatvān niṣedhasya pravṛttis teṣu durlabhā |                    yadā tu codanāśabdo vidhāveva vyavasthitaḥ |
  220. 2.220tadobhayādiko granthaḥ sadhyasādhanasaṃśritaḥ |                    sādhyasādhanasambandhe vidhinā pratipādite ||
  221. 2.221lakṣyamāṇatvam ubhayoḥ, dvividhaṃ ca phalaṃ kratoḥ |                    svargādi prāpyate tatra pratiṣedhānatikramāt ||
  222. 2.222atikrameṇa hiṃsādi, <84> śāstrāntaranirīkṣayā |                    phalāṃśe bhāvanāyāś ca pratyayo na vidhāyakaḥ ||
  223. 2.223vakṣyate, jaiminiś cāha tasya lipsārthalakṣaṇā |                    tena sāmānyataḥ prāpto vidhinā na nivāritaḥ ||
  224. 2.224phalāṃśopanipātinyā hiṃsāyāḥ pratiṣedhakaḥ |                    anarthaprāptihetutvaṃ bodhyate tatra yady api ||
  225. 2.225śyenasvarūpaṃ nānarthas tatphalasya tv anarthatā |                    parastūbhayam ityādeḥ phalasyāpi vidheyatām ||
  226. 2.226bhāvanāntargatatvād vā matvānarthatvam ākṣipat |<85>                    naivetyetāvatā cāsya vidheyatvanirākriyā ||
  227. 2.227kiṃ vidheyam idānīṃ syād āha śyenādayas tv iti |                    praśnāpākaraṇe cātra tavyo vidhivivakṣayā ||
  228. 2.228prayukto na tu sādhye 'rthe, dvaye 'py anupayogataḥ |                    anarthasyāpi sādhyatvam avidheyasya hīṣyate ||
  229. 2.229sādhyatvarahite ceṣṭā vidheye nityam arthatā |                    śatuś ca lakṣaṇārthatvaṃ teṣāṃ cāpy upadeśanam ||
  230. 2.230bruvan sphuṭīkarotīṣṭam upadeśo hi nānyathā |<86>                    vidhitvamādiśabdāt syād itikartavyatāsv api |
  231. 2.231tasmāt phalāṃśe yā hiṃsā vaidikī sā niṣidhyate |                    aṃśadvaye tu yā nāma tanniṣedhābhidhāyinām ||
  232. 2.232aviśeṣeṇa yacchāstraṃ śirovad iti cottaram |                    niṣedhenānavaṣṭabdhe viṣaye na hy anarthatā |
  233. 2.233pratyakṣāder aśakyatvāt kalpyate niṣpramāṇikā |                    na hi hiṃsādyanuṣṭhāne tadānīṃ doṣadarśanam ||
  234. 2.234bāhye 'pi vicikitsā tu śāstrādevopajāyate |                    hiṃsyamānasya duḥkhitvaṃ dṛśyate yan na tāvatā ||
  235. 2.235karturduḥkhānumānaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ tadviparyayaḥ |                    viṣaye 'syāḥ phalaṃ yādṛk pretya krtus tathāvidham ||
  236. 2.236hiṃsā kriyāviśeṣatvāt sūte śāstroktadānavat |<87>                    ya evamāha, tasyāpi gurustrīgamanādibhiḥ ||
  237. 2.237surāpānādibhiś cāpi vipakṣair vyabhicāritā |                    viruddhatā ca, yādṛgdhi dānais tādṛk phalaṃ bhavet ||
  238. 2.238vidhigamyaphalāvāptiḥ, aduḥkhātmakatā tathā |                    na ca yā sampradānasya prītis tādṛk phalaṃ śrutam ||
  239. 2.239dātus tena hi dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyahīnaḥ pratīyate |                    sampradānaṃ ca dāne te viṣayaḥ karma hiṃsane ||
  240. 2.240vaiṣamyam, sampradāne tu pakṣe tv etadviruddhatā |                    prīyate sampradānaṃ hi devateti mataṃ tava ||
  241. 2.241dṛṣṭānte karma dānaṃ cet, <88> tasya kīdṛk phalaṃ bhavet |                    japahomādidṛṣṭāntāt parapīḍādivarjanāt ||
  242. 2.242coditatvasya hetutvād viruddhāvyabhicāritā |                    vihitapratiṣiddhatve muktvānyan na ca kāraṇam ||
  243. 2.243dharmādharmāvabodhasya tenāyuktānumānagīḥ |                    anugrahāc ca dharmatvaṃ pīḍātaś cāpy adharmatām ||
  244. 2.244vadato japasīdhvādipānādau nobhayaṃ bhavet |                    krośatā hṛdayenāpi gurudārābhigāminām ||
  245. 2.245bhūyān dharmaḥ prasajyeta bhūyasī hy upakāritā |                    anumānapradhānasya pratiṣedhānapekṣiṇaḥ ||
  246. 2.246hṛdayakrośanaṃ kasmād dṛṣṭāṃ pīḍām apaśyataḥ |                    poḍātaś cāpy adharmatvaṃ tathā pīḍām adharmataḥ ||
  247. 2.247anyonyāśrayam āpnoti vinā śāstreṇa sādhayan |                    evamādāv aśāstrajñomleccho nodvijate kva cit ||
  248. 2.248tasya nādharmayogaḥ syāt pūrvoktā yadi kalpanā |<89>                    tasmād anugrahaṃ pīḍāṃ tadabhāvam apāsya ca |
  249. 2.249dharmādharmārthibhir nityaṃ mṛgyau vidhiniṣedhakau |                    kva cid asyā niṣiddhatvāc chaktiḥ śāstreṇa bodhitā ||
  250. 2.250pratyavāyanimittatve vidhinā nāpagacchati |                    śāstreṇa na hi śaktīnām āvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
  251. 2.251vidyamānā hi kathyante śaktayo dravyakarmaṇām |                    tad eva cedaṃ karmeti śāstram evānudhāvatā ||
  252. 2.252hiṃsādīnām adharmatvaṃ kathyate nānumānataḥ |                    evaṃ ye nipuṇaṃ prāhus tair apy etat parīkṣyatām ||
  253. 2.253surāpānādibhiḥ śūdraḥ kiṃ yāti narakaṃ kṛtaiḥ |                    vaiśyastomena vā kiṃ syād viprarājanyayoḥ phalam ||
  254. 2.254pañcamyām iṣṭikaraṇānmadhyāhne cāgnihotrataḥ |                    tasmād yady ādṛśaṃ karma yatphalotpattiśaktikam ||
  255. 2.255śāstreṇa gamyate tasya tādṛśasyaiva tat phalam |                    hiṃsā cāṃśadvayādanyā yā tasyāḥ pratiṣedhajam ||
  256. 2.256pratyavāyārthatājñānam, vidhinānyatra vāryate |<90>                    jñānam eva ca śaktīnāṃ nāvāpodvāpanakriyāḥ ||
  257. 2.257jñāyante śāstratas tāstu kriyābhedavyavasthitāḥ |                    vyavasthāḥ śaktibhedānāṃ dṛṣṭārtheṣv api karmasu ||
  258. 2.258abhinnatve 'pi dṛśyante bhujeḥ svasthātur eṣv api |                    rūpābhede 'pi hiṃsāder bhedo 'ṅgānaṅgakāritaḥ ||
  259. 2.259tathāpy ekaphalatvaṃ cet kriyātvāt sarvasaṅkaraḥ |                    yajitvādyaviśeṣāc ca citrādiphalatulyatā ||
  260. 2.260bhedāt tatra vyavasthā ced ihāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyati |                    vidhīnāṃ vāpi sarveṣāṃ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
  261. 2.261puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ tena nānartho 'taḥ pratīyate |                    na caiṣu śrūyate 'narthaḥ, niṣedhān na ca kalpyate ||
  262. 2.262na ca prakaraṇasthatvāt puruṣārthaḥ phalaṃ bhavet |                    karmopakāraḥ kalpyas tu dṛṣṭo 'dṛṣṭo 'tha vā punaḥ ||<91>
  263. 2.263kalpanāvasaras tatra nānarthasyānapekṣaṇāt |                    kratvarthaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ paśor nārādupakriyā ||
  264. 2.264dṛṣṭaiva tv avadānānāṃ niṣpattiḥ kratvapekṣitā |                    abhicāre 'py upāyasthā hiṃsā nādharma ucyate |
  265. 2.265tasmād anaṅgabhūtāyāṃ hiṃsāyām etad ucyate |                    uddeśāc ca phalatvena śyenādau na vidhīyate ||
  266. 2.266bhāvanāvidhir apy eva phalāṃśād vinivartate |                    ataḥ svato na dharmatvaṃ śyenāder nāpy adharmatā ||
  267. 2.267phalānarthānubandhitvāt taddvāreṇopacaryate |                    nirākāṅkṣasya caikena śyenasya na phaladvayam ||<92>
  268. 2.268tasmāt kriyāntarād eva hiṃsāto 'nartha ucyate |                    phalato 'pi ca yatkarma nānarthenānubadhyate ||
  269. 2.269kevalaprītihetutvāt taddharmatvena hīṣyate |                    nanu ceṣṭābhyupāyatvāt śyenāder dharmatā bhavet ||
  270. 2.270phalaṃ tāvad adharmo 'sya śyenādeḥ sampradhāryate |                    yadi yeneṣṭasiddhiḥ syād anuṣṭhānānubandhinī ||
  271. 2.271tasya dharmatvam ucyeta tataḥ śyenādivarjanam |                    yadā tu codanāgamyaḥ kāryākāryānapekṣayā ||
  272. 2.272dharmaḥ prītinimittaṃ syāt tadā śyene 'pi dharmatā |                    yadi tv aprītihetur yaḥ sākṣād vyavahito 'pi vā ||
  273. 2.273so 'dharmaś codanārthaḥ syāt tadā śyene 'py adharmatā |                    yas tu hiṃsātvasādharmyād bāhyavaccodanāsv api ||
  274. 2.274vaded anarthahetutvaṃ tasyāpy āgamabādhanam |                    tam anādṛtya yo brūyād yāgāder apy asau vadet ||
  275. 2.275svargādisādhanāśaktiṃ kriyātvād bhojanādivat |<93>                    gītāmantrārthavādair yā kalpyate 'narthahetutā ||
  276. 2.276pratyakṣaśrutibādhyatvāt sānyārthatvena nīyate |                    śiṣyān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt sūtravaidikavākyayoḥ ||
  277. 2.277aśakteś cobhayoḥ sāmyān na sūtreṣv ity anuttaram |                    prāguktaparisaṃkhyāyāḥ phalam etat prakāśyate ||
  278. 2.278sūtreṣu hy anayā yuktyā gatir eṣāpi yujyate |                    tasmād āvartate sūtram, tantraṃ vā śaktibhedataḥ ||<94>
  279. 2.279ekadeśānumānād vā dve sūtre parikalpite |                    itaretarasāmīpyād etāv eva parasparam ||
  280. 2.280kalpyete vākyaśeṣāya nānyāvayavakalpanā |                    viśiṣṭārthānuvāditvād atha vety api bhāṣite ||
  281. 2.281vākyabhedaḥ sa eveti saṃjñātantratvam uttaram |                    arthaṃ vā pratyupādānāt saṃjñālakṣaṇaśabdayoḥ |
  282. 2.282tantraṃ lakṣaṇaśabdo vā vācyo dharmārthaśabdayoḥ |                    dharme sāmānyataḥ siddhe pramāṇaṃ kathyate yadā ||
  283. 2.283vṛttam eva tadārthatvaṃ kimarthaṃ punarucyate |<95>                    codanālakṣaṇatvasya dharmaṃ prati vidheyatā ||
  284. 2.284labhyate 'rthānuvādena saṃśayo hy anyathā bhavet |                    tathā ca ye 'py anarthasya sādhanatvena kalpitāḥ ||
  285. 2.285niṣedhais te 'pi dharmāḥ syuś codanālakṣaṇatvataḥ |                    tasmād arthāparityāgād ekārthagrahaṇaṃ yathā ||
  286. 2.286labhyate vacanavyaktyā sā syād arthānuvādataḥ |                    viśeṣaṇād vinā caitadarthasāmarthyakāritam ||<96>
  287. 2.287 kathyate bhāṣyakāreṇa phalaṃ hiṃsādivarjanam ||

Chapter 3 nimittasūtra NMS

  1. 3.1pratijñāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa yady api |                    vakṣyamāṇā svapakṣasya yuktiḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitā ||
  2. 3.2pratijñāmātram ityetajjaiminer matam ucyate |                    vṛttikāro 'dhikaṃ vāpi bhūtādi dvāram abravīt ||

Chapter 4 pratyakṣasūtra PAS

  1. 4.1varṇyate sūtrabhedena yena pratyakṣalakṣaṇam |                    tena sūtrasya sambandho vācyaḥ pūrvapratijñayā ||
  2. 4.2lakṣaṇasyābhidhānaṃ tu kenāṃśenopayujyate |                    kimarthaṃ cānumānāder lakṣaṇaṃ nātra kathyate ||
  3. 4.3na tāvad apramāṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ nāpy akṣabuddhiṣu |                    śakyate 'ntargatir vaktuṃ na ca lakṣaṇatulyatā ||
  4. 4.4na cāpi siddhir eṣāṃ syād arthāt pratyakṣalakṣaṇāt |                    na hi tatpūrvakaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇam iti niścitam ||
  5. 4.5pratyakṣalakṣaṇoktiś ca nānumānādilakṣaṇāt |                    vinā na sidhyatītyevamarthākṣepo na yujyate ||<98>
  6. 4.6tadetatpūrvakatve dhīr na ca tallakṣaṇād bhavet |                    tadukter vānumānādi kiṃ na syāt tadapūrvakam ||
  7. 4.7na ca lakṣaṇabhedasya svarūpe yat tayor api |                    pratyakṣalakṣaṇād eṣāṃ kathañ cid avadhāraṇā ||
  8. 4.8prasiddhatvād avācyatvaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi prasajyate |                    tenānyaparisaṃkhyārthaṃ sūtraṃ mūḍhena vocyate ||
  9. 4.9na tv ekaṃ lakṣayed eṣu buddhipūrvaṃ kathañ cana |                    sambhavaty ekavākyatve vākyabhedaś ca neṣyate ||
  10. 4.10na cāpy etena sūtreṇa pratyakṣaṃ lakṣyate sphuṭam |                    tadābhāse 'pi tulyatvāt, svapnajñānaikavarjanāt ||
  11. 4.11taddhīndriyārthasambandhavyāpāreṇa vinā bhavet |                    kena cit samprayoge tu bhrāntyādi syān niyogataḥ ||<99>
  12. 4.12grāhyeṇānyena vety etat kṛtaṃ naiva viśeṣaṇam |                    samprayogasya yena syād viśeṣo vakṣyamāṇavat ||
  13. 4.13asāmarthya ca matvāsya vṛttikāreṇa lakṣaṇe |                    tatsamprayoga ityevaṃ pāṭhāntaramṛdāhṛtam ||
  14. 4.14tenānyenāpi saṃyoge cakṣurāder yadutthitam |                    viṣayāntaravijñānaṃ tatpratyakṣaṃ prasajyate ||
  15. 4.15satsamprayoganirdeśo vyarthaś ced, etad eva hi |                    pratipādyaṃ parasyāpi lakṣaṇāsiddhir eva ca ||
  16. 4.16svapnādīnāṃ nivṛttir vā phalaṃ tasya bhaviṣyati |                    tasmād vidhyanuvāditvaṃ nānukte lakṣaṇe bhavet ||
  17. 4.17tena naiṣā vacovyaktir yatsatīndriyasaṅgame |<100>                    vijñānaṃ jāyate tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ pratīyatām ||
  18. 4.18pratyakṣaṃ yajjane siddhaṃ tasyaivandharmakatvataḥ |                    vidyamānopalambhatvaṃ tena dharme nimittatā ||
  19. 4.19evaṃlakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpavivakṣayā |                    evaṃliṅgakam ityetad bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇyate ||
  20. 4.20yato 'sti tatra dharmo 'yaṃ vidyamānopalambhanam |                    tasmāt tena prasiddhena gamyatām animittatā ||
  21. 4.21pratyakṣatvamado hetuḥ śeṣaṃ hetuprasiddhaye |<101>                    asmād ādau prasiddhatvād yogyartham abhidhīyate ||
  22. 4.22prakṛtena ca sambandhaḥ śeṣāprāmāṇyadarśanāt |                    tadaprāmāṇyasiddhiś ca sambandhāder anīkṣaṇāt ||
  23. 4.23śakyam anyāpramāṇatvam iti sūtrair na paṭhyate |                    na ca paryanuyogo 'tra lakṣaṇānupayogataḥ ||
  24. 4.24na ca nyūnātirekādiprasaṅgo lakṣaṇaṃ prati |<102>                    sarvathā lokasiddhatvād dharmo 'yaṃ tāvad iṣyate ||
  25. 4.25tataś ca mṛgatṛṣṇādi na pratyakṣaṃ prasajyate |                    animittaprasaṅgas tu tasyāpi na nivāryate ||
  26. 4.26atītānāgate 'py arthe sūkṣme vyavahite 'pi ca |                    pratyakṣaṃ yoginām iṣṭaṃ kaiś cin muktātmanām api ||
  27. 4.27vidyamānopalambhatvam asiddhaṃ tatra tān prati |                    bhaviṣyattvasya vā hetor tadgrāhyair vyabhicāritā ||
  28. 4.28mā bhūtāmiti tenāha lokasiddhaṃ sad ity ayam |                    na lokavyatiriktaṃ hi pratyakṣaṃ yoginām api ||
  29. 4.29pratyakṣatvena tasyāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |                    satsamprayogajatvaṃ vāpy asmatpratyakṣavad bhavet ||<103>
  30. 4.30teṣām avartamāne 'rthe vā nāmotpadyate matiḥ |                    pratyakṣaṃ sā tatas tv eva nābhilāṣasmṛtādivat ||
  31. 4.31loke cāpy aprasiddhatvāt pratyakṣatvapramāṇataḥ |                    pratibhāvad dvayāsattvaṃ sad ity etena kathyate ||
  32. 4.32laukikī pratibhā yadvat pratyakṣādyanapekṣiṇī |                    na niścayāya paryāptā tathā syād yoginām api ||
  33. 4.33avidyamānasaṃyogāt syāc cet pratyakṣadhīḥ kva cit |                    bhaviṣyaty api dharme syāc chaktety āha sad ity ayam ||<104>
  34. 4.34pratyakṣaḥ prāganuṣṭhānān na dharmo 'nuṣṭhito 'pi vā |                    phalasādhanarūpeṇa tadānīṃ yena nāsty asau ||
  35. 4.35asmatpratyakṣavac cāpi vidyamānopalambhanam |                    pratyakṣaṃ dhyāyināṃ dharme pratyakṣatvāc ca neṣyate ||
  36. 4.36avidyamānasaṃyogāt pratyakṣatvanirākṛtiḥ |                    yogināṃ kena labhyeta neṣṭaṃ sadgrahaṇaṃ yadi ||<105>
  37. 4.37saptamyāpi tu labhyeta sadarthaḥ, kalpanā punaḥ |                    pareṣāṃ vāraṇīyeti yatno jaimininā kṛtaḥ ||
  38. 4.38samyagarthe ca saṃśabdo duṣprayoganivāraṇaḥ |                    prayoga indriyāṇāṃ ca vyāpāro 'rtheṣu kathyate ||
  39. 4.39duṣṭatvāc chuktikāyogo vāryate, rajatekṣaṇāt |                    evaṃ saty anuvādatvaṃ lakṣaṇasyāpi sambhavet ||
  40. 4.40tataś cāprāpyakāritvād yad bauddhaiḥ śrotracakṣuṣoḥ |<106>                    lakṣaṇāvyāptisiddhyarthaṃ saṃyogo neti kīrtyate ||
  41. 4.41prāpyagrahaṇapakṣe hi sāntarāgrahaṇaṃ kila |                    adhiṣṭānādhikaś cārtho na gṛhyeta tvagādivat ||
  42. 4.42vyāpāramātravācitvād aviruddhaṃ tad atra naḥ |                    yadi vārthārjavasthānaṃ samprayogo 'tra varṇyate ||
  43. 4.43yogyatālakṣaṇo vācyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāryalakṣitaḥ |                    sāṃkhyādīn vā vinirjitya prāptipakṣo 'tra dūṣyatām ||
  44. 4.44tayoś ca prāpyakāritvam indriyatvāt tvagādivat |                    ke cit tayoḥ śarīrāc ca bahirvṛttiṃ pracakṣate ||
  45. 4.45cikitsādiprayogaś ca yo 'dhiṣṭhāne prayujyate |                    so 'pi tasyaiva saṃskāra ādheyasyopakārakaḥ ||
  46. 4.46taddeśaś cāpi saṃskāraḥ sarvavyāptyartha ucyate |<107>                    cakṣurādyupakāraś ca pādādāv api dṛśyate ||
  47. 4.47tasmān naikāntataḥ śakyaṃ saṃskārāt tatra vartanam |                    bahirvṛttis tayoś ceṣṭā pṛthvagrā santatāpi ca ||
  48. 4.48adhiṣṭhānādhikaṃ tena gṛhyate yatra yādṛśam |                    pṛthutvaṃ vṛttibhāge syād, dūre 'pi grahaṇaṃ tathā ||
  49. 4.49dīpaprabhā yathā tasmin vinaśyati vinaśyati |                    tathā bahirgatāpy eṣā mūlacchedād vinaśyati ||
  50. 4.50adhiṣṭhānapidhāne tu saty apy ucchinnayatnayā |                    tayārtho 'nupanītatvād ātmanā nānubhūyate ||
  51. 4.51vicchinna iti buddhiḥ syād adhiṣṭhānam apekṣya ca |                    śabde tv ādhikyavicchedau bhrāntyaivoktāv asambhavāt ||<108>
  52. 4.52puruṣendriyaśabdau ca vyavadhānena kalpitau |                    puruṣo laukiko vā syād yo vāsmin sādhayiṣyate ||<109>
  53. 4.53vikriyā jñānarūpāsya na nityatve virotsyate |                    buddhijanmeti cāpy āha jāyamānapramāṇatām ||
  54. 4.54vyāpāraḥ kārakāṇāṃ hi dṛṣṭo janmātirekataḥ |                    pramāṇe 'pi tathā mā bhūd iti janma vivakṣyate ||
  55. 4.55na hi tat kṣaṇam apy āste, jāyate vāpramātmakam |                    yenārthagrahaṇe paścād vyāpriyetendriyādivat ||
  56. 4.56tena janmaiva viṣaye buddher vyāpāra iṣyate |                    tad eva ca pramārūpaṃ tadvatī karaṇaṃ ca dhīḥ ||
  57. 4.57janma cāvyatirekeṇa bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam |<110>                    tac ca bhūtabhaviṣyattvāt kṛtaṃ buddher viśeṣaṇam ||
  58. 4.58yadāpy aulūkyasiddhāntāt samavāyasya janmatā |                    buddhis tatrendriyādhīnā tena pratyakṣamaśnute ||
  59. 4.59pramāṇaphalabhāvaś ca yayeṣṭaṃ parikalpyatām |                    sarvathāpy animittatvaṃ vidyamānopalambhanāt ||
  60. 4.60yadvendriyaṃ pramāṇaṃ syāt tasya vārthena saṅgatiḥ |                    manaso vendriyair yoga ātmanā sarva eva vā ||
  61. 4.61tadā jñānaṃ phalam, tatra vyāpārāc ca pramāṇatā |                    vyāpāro na yadā teṣāṃ tadā notpadyate phalam ||
  62. 4.62na ca sarvātmanākṣeṇa sambandho 'rthasya vidyate |<111>                    yena sarvārthabodhaḥ syāt tatpramāṇābhidhāyinām ||
  63. 4.63prāptimātraṃ hi sambandho nendriyasyābhyupeyate |                    mā bhūt kāraṇamātreṇa tvacā rūpāvadhāraṇam ||
  64. 4.64yathā pramāṇaniṣpattau yogyatvād indriyārthayoḥ |                    niyatā saṅgatir hetuḥ phale 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
  65. 4.65yogasya dvyāśrayatve 'pi bhavatyanyatarāśrayaḥ |                    vyapadeśaḥ, atha vāpy akṣaṃ tatrāsādhāraṇaṃ bhavet ||<112>
  66. 4.66saṃyoge tv ātmamanasoḥ syāc ced viṣayabhinnatā |                    pramāṇaphalayoḥ, nāsau, arthe hi vyāpṛtaṃ dvayam ||
  67. 4.67athāpy āśraya iṣṭas te na yogād viṣayāntaram |                    ātmasthatvena vijñānaṃ na bhinnaviṣayaṃ tataḥ ||
  68. 4.68prakṛṣṭasādhanatvāc ca pratyāsatteḥ sa eva naḥ |                    karaṇaṃ tena nānyatra kārake syāt pramāṇatā ||
  69. 4.69pramāṇe sarvasaṃyoge doṣo naiko 'pi vidyate |                    pramāṇaṃ tv indriyaṃ yasya tasyaiko viṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
  70. 4.70pramāṇaphalate buddhyor viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |                    yadā tadāpi pūrvoktā bhinnārthatvanirākriyā ||<113>
  71. 4.71viśeṣaṇe tu boddhavye yadālocanamātrakam |                    prasūte niścayaṃ paścāt tasya prāmāṇyakalpanā ||
  72. 4.72niścayas tu phalaṃ tatra, nāsāv ālocite tadā |                    tadā naiva pramāṇatvaṃ syād arthānavadhāraṇāt ||
  73. 4.73hānādibuddhiphalatā pramāṇaṃ ced viśeṣyadhīḥ |                    upakārādisaṃsmṛtyā vyavāyaś cet, iyaṃ phalam ||
  74. 4.74viṣayaikatvam icchaṃs tu yaḥ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ vadet |                    sādhyasādhanayor bhedo laukikas tena bādhitaḥ ||
  75. 4.75chedane khadiraprāpte palāśe na cchidā yathā |                    tathaiva paraśor loke cchidayā saha naikatā ||<114>
  76. 4.76bhavate bhedahānena rucitā viṣayaikatā |                    tattyāgena parebhyas tu bhedo rucim upāgataḥ ||
  77. 4.77karaṇatvopacāras tu phale cet kalpyate tvayā |                    kathañ cid viṣayaikatvaṃ parair vā kiṃ na kalpyate ||
  78. 4.78paricchedaphalatvena vṛttasyānantarasya naḥ |                    pramāṇatvaṃ bhavej jñāne pramāṇe tu paraṃ phalam ||
  79. 4.79svasaṃvittiphalatvaṃ tu tanniṣedhān na yujyate |                    pramāṇe viṣayākāre bhinnārthatvān na yujyate ||<115>
  80. 4.80svākāraś ca svasaṃvittiṃ muktvā nānyaḥ pratīyate |                    prāmāṇyaṃ yasya kalpyeta svasaṃvittiphalaṃ prati ||
  81. 4.81svākārasya paricchedo na cākārāntarād vinā |                    tasyāpy evaṃ tathā ca syān nākārāntaḥ kadā cana ||
  82. 4.82na cāsañcetitaḥ sattāṃ svākāraḥ pratipadyate |                    grāhye ca viṣayākāre grāhako 'nyo na labhyate ||
  83. 4.83manasas tv indriyatvena pratyakṣā dhīḥ sukhādiṣu |                    manasā samprayukto hi tāny ātmā pratipadyate ||
  84. 4.84sambaddhaṃ vartamānaṃ ca grahyate cakṣurādinā |                    sāmānyaṃ vā viśeṣo vā grāhyaṃ nāto 'tra kalpyate ||<116>
  85. 4.85lakṣaṇaṃ yac ca yair uktaṃ pratyakṣe laukike sati |                    vidyamānopalambhitvāt sarvasyaivānimittatā ||
  86. 4.86nirvikalpakapakṣe tu sutarām animittatā |                    sādhyasādhanasambandho nāvikalpya hi gṛhyate ||
  87. 4.87kathaṃ pratyakṣapūrvatvam anumānādi no bhavet |                    yadā smṛtyasamarthatvān nirvikalpendriyasya dhīḥ ||
  88. 4.88na cāvikalpya liṅgasya liṅgisambandhayos tathā |                    gṛhītiḥ, <117> upamāne 'pi sādṛśyagrahaṇāt smṛteḥ ||
  89. 4.89arthāpattiḥ punaḥ prāyo nānyadṛṣṭe 'rtha iṣyate |                    pravartate ca yaṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'py arthaḥ savikalpakaḥ ||
  90. 4.90yatra cānumitaṃ liṅgaṃ sūryagatyādi liṅgi ca |                    tatra pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate ||
  91. 4.91pratyakṣāvagate cārthe kutas teṣāṃ pramāṇatā |                    tair yadā sa pratīyeta tadā nākṣasya gocaraḥ ||
  92. 4.92atha kasya cid arthasya jñānāt tatpūrvatā bhavet |                    tadārthasya bhaviṣyattvaṃ na syād ajñānakāraṇam ||<118>
  93. 4.93vartamāne hi kasmiṃś cid vijñāte 'rthe 'kṣabuddhibhiḥ |                    liṅgād avidyamāno 'pi dharmo gamyeta tais tadā ||
  94. 4.94pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca varṇān vede 'pi gṛhyate |                    prameyam iti so 'pi syāt tatpūrvatvād akāraṇam ||
  95. 4.95ke cit tatpūrvakatvaṃ tu hetur naiveti manvate |                    tatpūrvakatvād yat tāvat prāmāṇyaṃ tadasambhavaḥ ||
  96. 4.96pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā ca, liṅgādyanyatamaṃ dhruvam |                    pravṛttir anumānāder na ca dharme 'sti tādṛśam ||
  97. 4.97anumānānumānāder na cāpy astīha sambhavaḥ |                    sambandhaliṅgiliṅgānāṃ pūrvasiddher asambhavāt ||
  98. 4.98sattā ca nānumānena kasya cit pratipadyate |                    dharmeṇānyad viśeṣyaṃ cet, <119> pakṣo 'siddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
  99. 4.99tasmād adṛṣṭapūrvatvāt kena cid vastunā saha |                    dharmasya nānumeyatvam asādhāraṇavastuvat ||
  100. 4.100adṛṣṭasadṛśatvāc ca svyaṃ cānupalambhanāt |                    dharmasya nopameyatvam asādhāraṇavad bhavet ||
  101. 4.101nanv arthāpattir evaṃ syāj jagadvaicitryadarśanāt |                    sukhiduḥkhādibhedo hi nādṛṣṭāt kāraṇād ṛte ||
  102. 4.102dṛṣṭasya vyabhicāritvāt tadabhāve 'pi sambhavāt |<120>                    sevāvyayanatulyatve dṛṣṭā ca phalabhinnatā ||
  103. 4.103syād evaṃ yadi śakyeta svābhāvikanivāraṇā |                    karmaśakteś ca vaicitrye hetur anyo bhaved yadi ||
  104. 4.104yathā ca phalavaicitrye karmaṇāṃ śaktatā svataḥ |                    tathā ca citratā loke svabhāvād upapatsyate ||
  105. 4.105adharme dharmarūpe vā hy avibhakte phalaṃ prati |                    kim apy astīti vijñānaṃ narāṇāṃ kvopayujyate ||
  106. 4.106kiṃ nu yāgād ito dukhaṃ hiṃsādeḥ kiṃ sukhodbhavaḥ |                    svargaputrādibhedaś ca kīdṛśāt karmabhedataḥ ||
  107. 4.107iti yāvad avijñānaṃ tāvan naiva pravartate |                    pravṛttyaṅgaṃ ca yajjñānaṃ tasya mūlaṃ pratīkṣyate ||
  108. 4.108tasmāt siddhe 'pi sāmānye viśeṣo nāgamād ṛte |<121>                    viśeṣasya tu jijñāsā sūtrakāreṇa sūtritā ||
  109. 4.109gamyamāne viśeṣe ca tadantarbhāvakāritaḥ |                    sāmānyapratyayo 'pi syāc chāstrād evety akāraṇam ||
  110. 4.110yathārthāpattir evaṃ ca nānumānopameṣyate |                    śāstraṃ cet tadapekṣeta tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||
  111. 4.111pratyakṣāgrahaṇaṃ yat tu liṅgāder avikalpanāt |                    tan na, iṣṭatvād vikalpasyāpy artharūpopakāriṇaḥ ||
  112. 4.112asti hy ālocanā jñānaṃ prathamaṃ nirvikapakam |                    bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam ||<122>
  113. 4.113na viśeṣo na sāmānyaṃ tadānīmanubhūyate |                    tayor ādhārabhūtā tu, vyaktir evāvasīyate ||
  114. 4.114mahāsāmānyam anyais tu dravyaṃ sad iti cocyate |                    sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca pratyakṣasyaivam āśritam ||
  115. 4.115viśeṣās tu pratīyante savikalpakabuddhibhiḥ |                    te ca ke cit pratidravyaṃ ke cid bahuṣu saṃśritāḥ ||
  116. 4.116tān akalpayad utpannaṃ vyāvṛttānugatātmanā |                    gavyaśve copajātaṃ tu pratyakṣaṃ na viśiṣyate ||<123>
  117. 4.117tad ayuktam, pratidravyaṃ bhinnarūpopalambhanāt |                    na hy ākhyātum aśakyatvād bhedo nāstīti gamyate ||
  118. 4.118nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi dvyātmakasyāpi vastunaḥ |                    grahaṇam, <124> lakṣaṇākhyeyaṃ jñātrā śuddhaṃ tu gṛhyate ||
  119. 4.119na cāsādhāraṇatvena paravyāvṛttyakalpanāt |                    viśeṣānugamākḷpteḥ sāmānyam iti nāpi tat ||
  120. 4.120tataḥ paraṃ punarvastudharmair jātyādibhir yayā |                    buddhyāvasīyate sāpi pratyakṣatvena sammatā ||
  121. 4.121karaṇaṃ cendriyaṃ buddher na tatra jñānam āhitam |                    tataḥ smṛtyasamarthatvād vikalpo 'to na vāryate ||
  122. 4.122ātmany eva sthitaṃ jñānam, sa hi boddhātra gamyate |                    smaraṇe cāsya sāmarthyaṃ sandhānādau ca vidyate ||
  123. 4.123tenendriyārthasambandhe vicyamāne smarann api |                    vikalpayan svadharmeṇa vastu pratyakṣavān naraḥ ||<125>
  124. 4.124tac caitadindriyādhīnam iti tair vyapadiśyate |                    tadasambandhajātaṃ tu naiva pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
  125. 4.125punaḥ punarvikalpe 'pi satī jātiḥ pratīyate |                    tatsambandhānusāreṇa sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iṣyate ||
  126. 4.126na hi praviṣṭamātrāṇām uṣṇād garbhagṛhādiṣu |                    arthā na pratibhāntīti gṛhyante nendriyaiḥ punaḥ ||
  127. 4.127yathā tv ābhāsamātreṇa pūrvaṃ jñātvā svarūpataḥ |                    paścāt tatrāvabudhyante tathā jātyādidharmataḥ ||
  128. 4.128yadi tv ālocya saṃmīlya netre kaś cid vikalpayet |                    na syāt pratyakṣatā tasya sambandhānanusārataḥ ||
  129. 4.129asambaddhavikalpe 'pi tulyam ātmādi kāraṇam |                    tenāsādhāraṇatvaṃ syād atrākṣasyaiva kalpane ||<126>
  130. 4.130nirvikalpakabodhe 'pi nākṣaṃ kevalakāraṇam |                    tatpāramparyajāte vā rūḍhiḥ syāt paṅkajādivat ||
  131. 4.131animittaiva vā rūḍhiḥ sutarāṃ savikalpakam |                    pratyakṣaṃ sammataṃ loke na tathā nirvikalpakam ||
  132. 4.132vṛddhaprayogagamyāś ca śabdārthāḥ sarva eva naḥ |                    tena yatra prayukto 'yaṃ na tasmād apanīyate ||
  133. 4.133siddhānugamamātraṃ hi kartuṃ yuktaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |                    na sarvalokasiddhasya lakṣaṇena nivartanam ||
  134. 4.134kalpanāyāḥ svasaṃvittāv indriyādhīnatā katham |                    manas tatrendriyaṃ cet syād gotvādāv api tatsamam ||
  135. 4.135svasaṃvittau tad iṣṭaṃ cet, <127> loko na hy evam icchati |                    tasmād rūḍhatvam eṣṭavyaṃ pāribhāṣikatāpi vā ||
  136. 4.136manasas tv indriyatvena sudhaduḥkhādibuddhiṣu |                    yathā pratyakṣataivaṃ nas tadadhīnā bhaviṣyati ||
  137. 4.137tadadhīnatvasāmye 'pi kalpanāpoḍhaśabdanāt |                    pratyakṣaṃ kiñ cid eveṣṭaṃ yathā tatra tathaiva naḥ ||
  138. 4.138liṅgādyabhāvataś cāpi nānumānādidhīr iyam |                    bādhakapratyayāsattvān nāprāmāṇyaṃ ca yujyate ||
  139. 4.139na ca parvamadṛṣṭatvāt smṛtitvam upapadyate |                    tasmāt pratyakṣam evedam, vyavahāras tathaiva ca ||<128>
  140. 4.140jātyādyarthāntaraṃ yasmād atadrūpe 'pi vastuni |                    bhavaty adhyasya dhīs tasmān mṛgatṛṣṇādibhiḥ samā ||
  141. 4.141naitadaśvādibuddhīnām adhyāropādyasambhavāt |                    sthitaṃ naiva hi jātyādeḥ paratvaṃ vyaktito hi naḥ ||
  142. 4.142yadi hy ekāntato bhinnaṃ viśeṣyāt syād viśeṣaṇam |                    svānurūpāṃ sadā buddhiṃ viśeṣye janayet katham ||
  143. 4.143sphaṭikādau tu lākṣādisvarūpā yā matir bhavet |                    avyutpannasya sā mithyā vyutpannānāṃ hi bhedadhīḥ ||<129>
  144. 4.144na tu jātyādinirmuktaṃ vastu dṛṣṭaṃ kadā cana |                    tadvimokena vā tāni lākṣādisphaṭikādivat ||
  145. 4.145tatrāpi cen na dṛśyeta bhedaḥ kaiś cit kadā cana |                    raktādibuddhisamyaktvaṃ vinivāryeta kena vā ||
  146. 4.146na cāpy ayutasiddhānāṃ sambandhitvena kalpanā |                    nāniṣpannasya sambandhaḥ, niṣpattau yutasiddhatā ||
  147. 4.147tathā ca sati sambandhe hetuḥ kaś cin na vidyate |                    tasmāc cāpi na sambandhaḥ padārthānāṃ pratīyate ||<130>
  148. 4.148samavāyaviyogāc ca viśleṣaḥ syāt parasparam |                    tatkḷptāvavyavasthā syāt tasya tasyānyasaṅgateḥ ||
  149. 4.149atha tasyātmarūpatvān nānyasambandhakalpanā |                    abhedāt samavāyo 'stu svarūpaṃ dharmadharmiṇoḥ ||
  150. 4.150na hi sa vyatiriktaḥ san sambandhaṃ pratipadyate |                    tasmiṃs tābhyām abhinne tu na nānātvaṃ tayor bhavet ||
  151. 4.151nanu dharmātirekeṇa dharmiṇo 'nupalambhanāt |                    tatsaṅghamātra evāyaṃ gavādiḥ syād vanādivat ||<131>
  152. 4.152āvirbhāvatirobhāvadharmakeṣv anuyāyi yat |                    taddharmi yatra vā jñānaṃ prāgdharmagrahaṇād bhavet ||
  153. 4.153ato jātyādirūpeṇa dharmi yad gṛhyate naiḥ |                    pārarūpyaṃ na tasyāstīty aprāmāṇyaṃ na yujyate ||
  154. 4.154yasyāpi vyatirekaḥ syād dharmebhyo dharmiṇaḥ sphuṭaḥ |                    nityaṃ tasyāpi tādrūpyān na mithyātvaṃ prasajyate ||
  155. 4.155yo hy asadrūpasaṃvedyaḥ saṃvedyetān yathā punaḥ |                    sa mithyā na tu tenaiva yo nityam avagamyate ||
  156. 4.156na cānekendriyagrāhyaṃ bhinnatāṃ pratipadyate |<132>                    mā bhūd bhinnaśarīrasthagrāhyatvād bhinnarūpatā ||
  157. 4.157jātyabhedād abhedaś cet, indriyatvena tatsamam |                    tulyabuddher ato bhinnā na sattendriyabhedataḥ ||
  158. 4.158buddhibhedāc ca naikatvaṃ rūpādīnāṃ prasajyate |                    ekānekatvam iṣṭaṃ vā sattārūpādirūpataḥ ||
  159. 4.159kva cic ca saṅkarān nākṣam ekam ity avasīyate |                    dārḍhyadaurbalyabhedena vyavasthāpi yataḥ kva cit ||
  160. 4.160yathā hi manasaḥ sārdhaṃ rūpādau cakṣurādinā |                    pravṛttiḥ sukhaduḥkhādau kevalasyaiva dṛśyate ||<133>
  161. 4.161na kva cit saṅkarābhāvāt sarvatraiva nivartate |                    kva cic ca saṅkaraṃ dṛṣṭvā saṅkaro 'nyatra kalpyate ||
  162. 4.162śrotrāder upaghāte 'pi śabdādismṛtidarśanāt |                    vartamānasya cājñānād vyavasthā sampratīyate ||
  163. 4.163ekaṃ yadi bhaved akṣaṃ sarvair gṛhyeta vā na vā |                    kalpyate śaktibhedaś cet, śaktir evendriyaṃ bhavet ||
  164. 4.164śṛṇuyād badhiraḥ śabdaṃ saṅkare cakṣurādinā |                    manaso vā svatantratve vartamānārthabuddhiṣu ||<134>
  165. 4.165na smared badhiraḥ śabdaṃ śrotraṃ cet smṛtikāraṇam |                    smṛtivad vā bhaved asya vartamānārthadhīr api ||
  166. 4.166smṛtiś ca na bhavet paścād gṛhṇīyāt tan na cen manaḥ |                    śrotragrahaṇavelāyām, na cāsarvā smṛtir bhavet ||
  167. 4.167bodhātmakatayā puṃsaḥ sarvatra grahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    yugapadviṣaye 'py asya karaṇāpekṣitā na cet ||
  168. 4.168tasmāj jñānānusāreṇa vyavasthāsaṅkarau kva cit |                    grāhyagrāhakaśaktibhyaḥ kāryadvāreṇa kalpitau ||<135>
  169. 4.169cakṣūrūpādibhedas tu pañcadhaiva vyavasthitaḥ |                    tena nīlādibhede 'pi nendriyānantyakalpanā ||
  170. 4.170tasmāt pañcabhir apy akṣair bodhaḥ sattāguṇatvayoḥ |                    dravyamūrtau punardvābhyāṃ rūpādāv ekaśaḥ sthitaḥ ||
  171. 4.171nanu jātyādirūpe 'pi śabdābhedopacārataḥ |                    pravartamānā mithya syād buddhī rūpeṣu buddhivat ||
  172. 4.172na śabdābhedarūpeṇa buddhir artheṣu jāyate |                    prāk śabdād yādṛśī buddhiḥ śabdād api hi tādṛśī ||
  173. 4.173nanu gotvādirūpeṇa gavākārādibuddhayaḥ |                    na prāk śabdārthasambandhajñānāt santi kadā cana ||
  174. 4.174jātyādes tatsvarūpaṃ ced aśabdajño 'pi lakṣayet |                    anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ śabdarūpatvaniścayaḥ ||<136>
  175. 4.175yathā rūpādayo bhinnāḥ prāk śabdāt svātmanaiva tu |                    gamyante tadvad evaitat saṃjñitvaṃ kevalaṃ param ||
  176. 4.176na cāvikalpitaḥ śabdād iti vācyo na gṛhyate |                    tenāgṛhītaśabdo 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate ||
  177. 4.177śrutisaṃsparśabodhe 'pi gotvādīn pratipadyate |                    vivekād arthaśabdānāṃ cakṣuḥ śrotradhiyā kṛtāt ||
  178. 4.178anantadharmake dharmiṇy ekadharmāvadhāraṇe |                    śabdo 'bhyupāyamātraṃ syān nātmādhyāropakāraṇam ||
  179. 4.179na copeye 'bhyupāyasya rūpādhyāsaḥ prasajyate |                    na hi dīpendriyādīnāṃ rūpādhyāropa iṣyate ||
  180. 4.180nityaṃ yadi ca gotvādi śabdarūpeṇa gṛhyate |                    rūpāntaraṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ ced bhedādhyāsau kuto nvimau ||<137>
  181. 4.181yady abhedo na mithyātvam, bhedaś cet syāt svarūpataḥ |                    nādhyāropaprasaṅgaḥ syād bhrāntyā tv adhyāsakalpanā ||
  182. 4.182śabdenaiva ca nirdeśo gṛhīte 'rthe 'vakalpate |                    gaur ity eva ca nirdeśo vācyatadbuddhivādinām ||
  183. 4.183nirdeśatulyatāyāṃ ca śrotrā vaktṛsvarūpatā |                    śabdajñānaprameyeṣu vijñānasyāvasīyate ||
  184. 4.184bhrāntihetusamānatve 'py upāyatvānmatiśrutī |                    manyate 'rthe samadhyaste nārthādhyāsaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ||
  185. 4.185gotve sāsnādimadrūpāṅgādirūpābhidhāyake |                    nirākārobhayajñāne saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ ||
  186. 4.186yadi cābhedarūpeṇa śabdenārthaḥ pratīyate |                    ekarūpatvam akṣādau devanādeḥ prasajyate ||<138>
  187. 4.187syād anakṣanivṛtyā cet, na prāk śabdāt pratīyate |                    gavādiṣv api tulyaṃ cet, nekarūpasya darśanāt ||
  188. 4.188traye bibhītakādīnāṃ naikadharmānvayo 'sti hi |                    śabdaḥ sādhāraṇas teṣāṃ jātiśabdād vilakṣaṇaḥ ||
  189. 4.189parasparavibhinnaṃ tu jñāyate 'trākṛtitrayam |                    tadadhyāse na yujyeta tadrūpasyāvibhāgataḥ ||
  190. 4.190bhinnāḥ syur akṣaśabdāś cet, nārthe saṃśayadarśanāt |                    na sāmānyād ṛte sa syād, rūpābhedaś ca gamyate ||
  191. 4.191bhavatyādau ca bhinne 'pi nāmākhyātatvasaṃjñayā |                    rūpaikatvena cādhyāse tulyārthatvaṃ prasajyate ||<139>
  192. 4.192śabdaniṣpattyabhedāc ca tiṅantārthasya sādhyatā |                    katham, kathaṃ ca mūrtārtho vācake mūrtivarjite ||
  193. 4.193gavāśvaśuklaśabdāder vācyarūpānapekṣaṇe |                    vācakatvavyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ jātiguṇādiṣu ||
  194. 4.194vṛkṣaplakṣādiśabdānāṃ tulye bhede ghaṭādibhiḥ |                    viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ katham arthānapekṣayā ||
  195. 4.195sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na syad vācakabuddhivat |                    ekatra copasaṃhāro na buddhyor nirvikalpake ||
  196. 4.196vastumātre sa ced evaṃ sarveṣām ekavācyatā |                    bhaved gavādiśabdānāṃ sarvair vastu hi gamyate ||<140>
  197. 4.197na cāsādhāraṇe bhede nīlotpalam itīṣyate |                    na hi śabdapravṛttiḥ syād anyatrānyatra ceṣyate ||
  198. 4.198na ca nīlotpalaṃ nāma vastvekaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate |                    śabdārthayor yato bhedo gamyate 'vayavānugaḥ ||
  199. 4.199śabdadvayasya cādhyāsaḥ paryāyeṣv api dṛśyate |                    ekādhikaraṇās tena syus te nīlotpalādivat ||
  200. 4.200na cānavagate pūrvaṃ padam arthe prayujyate |                    tatra sambandhavelāyāṃ kīdṛśo 'rthaḥ pratīyate ||
  201. 4.201tadānīṃ nārtharūpe hi śabdarūpasya sambhavaḥ |                    na cāsādhāraṇāṃśena sambandhānugamaḥ kva cit ||
  202. 4.202tatra pūrvānapekṣatve yadyātmādhyāsaśaktatā |                    śabdasya prathame 'pi syāc chravaṇe 'dhyastarūpatā ||
  203. 4.203mama vācyānabhijñatvān na bhavet smaraṇaṃ tataḥ |                    bhavatas tv artharūpasya vācakeṣv api darśanāt ||<141>
  204. 4.204yathā tv ajñātaśabdānāṃ vācye taddhīr na jāyate |                    tathaivājñātavācyānām upalabdhe 'pi vācake ||
  205. 4.205tasmān nātīva vācyānāṃ vācakādhīnatā bhavet |                    smārakatvāc ca teṣv eva pāratantryaṃ pratīyate ||
  206. 4.206tena sambandhavelāyām arthātmā yo 'vasīyate |                    śabdād api sa eveti nārtharūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
  207. 4.207pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā yāṃ śabdaḥ kurute matim |                    tādātmyaṃ tasya śabdasya na kathañ cit pratīyate ||
  208. 4.208karahastādiśabdebhyaḥ śabdarūpasya bhedataḥ |                    bhinno 'rthaḥ sampratīyeta tadadhyāropakalpane ||
