  209. 4.209ātmādhyāsas tu sādṛśyād uparāgāc ca dṛśyate |                    na tāvad arthasādṛśyaṃ śabdasyeha pratīyate ||
  210. 4.210na cānurāgaḥ śabdena bhinnadeśasya yujyate |                    dūrasthapratibimbaṃ ca nārūpasya pratīyate ||
  211. 4.211śabdasarvagatatvena yadyarthaprāptir ucyate |                    sarvārthānāṃ bhavec chabdaiḥ sarvair evānurañjanam ||
  212. 4.212na ca bhinnendriyagrāhyaṃ kiñ cid asty anurāgakṛt |<142>                    na hi lākṣānurakte 'pi sphaṭike dhīs tvagādibhiḥ ||
  213. 4.213anumānāgamau mithyā syātāmadhyāsakalpane |                    nirūpaṇasya mithyātvāt sarvābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
  214. 4.214tathās tv iti yadi brūyāt, mithyā svavacane sati |                    katham evaṃ vaded artho nānṛtād dhi pratīyate ||
  215. 4.215śūnyavādottarāccāpi yathārthaṃ buddhiśabdayoḥ |                    pravṛttir na tu tat tantram artharūpaṃ kadā cana ||
  216. 4.216tasmāt prāg api ye śabdād bhirnnaikatvādibuddhibhiḥ |                    gṛhyante sarvadā teṣāṃ paramārthastitā bhavet ||
  217. 4.217śabdābhyupāyake 'py arthe tadabhāve ca yady api |                    arthabuddhir na jāyeta nārthe rūpaṃ praṇaśyati ||
  218. 4.218cakṣurāder abhāve hi rūpādyātmā na gṛhyate |                    svarūpanāśo rūpādes tāvanmātreṇa neṣyate ||<143>
  219. 4.219sambandhasya ca nityatvān nārethasya syād arūpatā |                    yugapanna hi sarveṣām anyākārārthavedanam ||
  220. 4.220tadākāre 'pi tadvac ced, dvaye sati parīkṣyatām |                    kiṃ nv arthasyātathābhāvo grahītuḥ kiṃ nv aśaktatā ||
  221. 4.221sadasadbhāvayor arthe virodhitvād asambhavaḥ |                    grahītṛbhedāc chaktatvam aśaktatvaṃ ca yujyate ||
  222. 4.222yathāndhānandhayoḥ pārśve rūpasyety abhidhāsyate |                    tenārthe dhvanyupāyasya tadhīrnānyasya jāyate ||
  223. 4.223devadattādiśabde tu sambandhādyatvadarśanāt |                    arthasyānityatāyāṃ ca tādrūpyasyāpy anityatā ||<144>
  224. 4.224tatrāpy autpattikī śaktis tadrūpapratyayaṃ prati |                    grāhyagrāhakayor iṣṭā niyogasya tv anityatā ||
  225. 4.225tatra sarvair atādrūpyaṃ prāṅniyogāt pratīyate |                    teneṣṭam eva mithyātvaṃ kaiś cid adhyāsakalpane ||
  226. 4.226yadā tu yādṛśaḥ piṇḍaḥ pūrvaṃ śabdāt pratīyate |                    tādṛśasmaraṇe hetuḥ śabdas tatra yathārthatā ||
  227. 4.227niyogāt parato vāpi śabdena vyajyatām iyam |                    tadgrāhyaśaktir arthasya, pārarūpyaṃ na tāvatā ||<145>
  228. 4.228sarvākāraparicchedyaśakte 'rthe vācake 'pi vā |                    sarvākārārthavijñānasamarthe niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ||
  229. 4.229tatra śabdārthasambandhaṃ pramātuḥ smarato 'pi yā |                    buddhiḥ pūrvagṛhītārthasandhānād upajāyate ||
  230. 4.230cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣṭe 'rthe nāpratyakṣam asau bhavet |                    viviktā eva te 'py arthāḥ smṛtipratyakṣagocarāḥ ||
  231. 4.231smaryete śabdasambandhau mā bhūt pratyakṣatā tayoḥ |                    tadapratyakṣabhāvena na tv arthasyāpi vāryate ||
  232. 4.232gṛhītam api gotvādi smṛtispṛṣṭaṃ ca yady api |                    tathāpi vyatirekeṇa pūrvabodhāt pratīyate ||
  233. 4.233vyaktikālādibhedena tatrāsty avasaro miteḥ |<146>                    yaḥ pūrvāvagato 'ṃśo 'tra sa na nāma pramīyate ||
  234. 4.234idānīn tanam astitvaṃ na hi pūrvadhiyā gatam |                    na hi smaraṇato yatprāk tat pratyakṣam itīdṛśam ||
  235. 4.235vacanaṃ rājakīyaṃ vā vaidikaṃ vāpi vidyate |                    na cāpi smaraṇāt paścād indriyasya pravartanam ||
  236. 4.236vāryate kena cin nātastat tadānīṃ praduṣyati |                    tenendriyārthasambandhāt prāgūrdhvaṃ vāpi yatsmṛteḥ ||
  237. 4.237vijñānaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ pratyakṣam iti gamyatām |                    vimanaskā yadā ke cit sambaddham api cendriyaiḥ ||
  238. 4.238na budhyante tathā cānye sādṛśyādivimohitāḥ |                    tatra yo 'rthaṃ vivekena kauśalāt sadṛśeṣv api ||
  239. 4.239sūkṣmaṃ vāpi prapadyeta tasya bhrāntirnaṃ tāvatā |                    yathā ṣaḍjādibhedena gāne laukikavaidike ||
  240. 4.240vivekenāvagacchanti yeṣāṃ tatsaṃskṛtā matiḥ |                    gānamātraṃ vijānanti tatrānadhikṛtās tu ye ||
  241. 4.241tadajñānān na mithyātvaṃ vaktuṃ śakyaṃ vivekinām |<147>                    te hi ṣaḍjādiśabdebhyo vināpy eṣaṃ viviktatām ||
  242. 4.242yathāvadadhigacchanti, tadvad gotvādivas tv api |                    saṅkīrṇam arthamātraṃ tu budhyante 'bhyāsarvajitāḥ ||
  243. 4.243vivekaṃ pratipadyante ye śabdasmṛtisaṃskṛtāḥ |                    yathā rūpādimatyarthe yasyaivāsti yadindriyam ||
  244. 4.244sa tanmātraṃ gṛhītvānyan na gṛhṇātyanumānataḥ |                    tathā vivekahetūnāṃ yadā yaṃ pratipadyate ||
  245. 4.245tadupeye tadā jñānaṃ vartate tadanugrahāt |                    tena yāvat pramātāṇāṃ vivekopāyadarśanam ||
  246. 4.246na syāt tāvad bhavet teṣāṃ vijñānaṃ nirvikalpakam |                    tasmād yatra prakalpyeta vastu vastvantarātmanā ||
  247. 4.247pramāṇābhāsatā tatra na svadharmavikalpane |                    pratyakṣatvam ataḥ siddhaṃ sāmānyasya tathaiva ca ||
  248. 4.248sambandhasyeti tat pūrvam anumānādi jāyate |                    sarvaṃ cāpy anumānādi pratyakṣe nirvikalpake ||
  249. 4.249na pravartata ity etadanumāne 'bhidhāsyate |<148>                    nanv evaṃ sati yāpy agner dūrād apy auṣṇyakalpanā ||
  250. 4.250sāpi pratyakṣam eva syād yathā gotvādibuddhayaḥ |                    pratyāsannataraṃ gotvaṃ pratyakṣatvena sammatam ||
  251. 4.251vijñānaṃ nānyad astīti pratyakṣam idam eva naḥ |                    tatrāpy akṣair asambandhaṃ manvānasyopajāyate ||
  252. 4.252yadā buddhiḥ, tadā naiva pratyakṣatvena kalpyate |                    sparśanena tu sambandhe pratyakṣatvena jāyate ||
  253. 4.253tasmād yadindriyaṃ yasya grāhakatvena kalpitam |                    tenaiva sati sambandhe pratyakṣaṃ nānyathā bhavet ||
  254. 4.254evaṃ samāne 'pi vikalpamārge yatrākṣasambandhaphalānusāraḥ |                    pratyakṣatā tasya tathā ca loke vināpyado lakṣaṇataḥ prasiddham ||

Chapter 5,1 vṛttikāragrantha VKG

  1. 5,1.1pratyakṣādau niṣiddhe 'pi nanu lokaprasiddhitaḥ |                    dharmādharmau pramāsyete brāhmaṇādivivekavat ||
  2. 5,1.2dhārmikādhārmikatvābhyāṃ pīḍānugrahakāriṇau |                    prasiddhau hi, tathā cāha pārāśaryo 'tra vastuni ||
  3. 5,1.3idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ pāpam ity etasmin padadvaye |                    ācaṇḍālaṃ manuṣyāṇām alpaṃ śāstraprayojanam ||
  4. 5,1.4nirmūlāsambhavād atra pramāṇaiḥ saiva mṛgyate |                    kutaḥ punaḥ pravṛtteti, pratyakṣādi tu vāritam ||<150>
  5. 5,1.5na caitāni parityajya pṛthag loke pramāṇatā |                    saṃsāramocakādeś ca hiṃsā puṇyatvasammatā ||
  6. 5,1.6na paścāt puṇyam icchanti ke cid evaṃ vigānataḥ |                    mlecchāryāṇāṃ prasiddhatvaṃ na dharmasyopapadyate ||
  7. 5,1.7na cāryāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'sti yāvacchāstram anāśritam |                    tanmūlārthaprasiddhis tu tatprāmāṇye sthite bhavet ||
  8. 5,1.8tasmād abhāvaktrasthau dharmādarmau na śaknuyāt |                    codanā cet samuddhartuṃ grastau tenaiva paśyatām ||
  9. 5,1.9upadeśo hi bhavati jñānaṃ tasyeti yojyate |                    jñāyate yena tajjñānam ekādhikaraṇatvataḥ ||
  10. 5,1.10autpattikagirā doṣaḥ kāraṇasya nivāryate |                    abādho 'nyatirekeṇa, svatas tena pramāṇatā ||<151>
  11. 5,1.11sarvasyānupalabdhe 'rthe prāmāṇyaṃ smṛtir anyathā |                    codanā copadeśaś ca vidhiś caikārthavācinaḥ ||
  12. 5,1.12vākyāntare samarthe 'pi kimarthaṃ vidhir āśritaḥ |                    sādhyasādhanasambandhaḥ sarvākhyāteṣu vidyate ||
  13. 5,1.13sarvavākyeṣu cākhyātaṃ tenākāṅkṣānivartanāt |                    pravṛttisiddhir icchātaḥ, pratiṣedhāt tu varjanam ||
  14. 5,1.14vidhāvanāśrite sādhyaḥ puruṣārtho na labhyate |                    śrutasvargādibādhena dhātvarthaḥ sādhyatāṃ vrajet ||
  15. 5,1.15vidhau tu tam atikramya svargādeḥ sādhyateṣyate |                    tatsādhanasya dharmatvam evaṃ sati ca labhyate ||<152>
  16. 5,1.16svapratyayāntarāpekṣā syād anāptanaroktiṣu |                    āptoktiṣu narāpekṣā nobhayaṃ codanāsu naḥ ||

Chapter 5.2

  1. 5,2.17ādiśabdo makārāntaḥ, luki kleśena saṅgatiḥ |                    nañadhyāhriyate sūtre, saṅkarāt paricodanā ||
  2. 5,2.18pramāṇalakṣaṇājñānād vyabhicārāt parīkṣaṇam |                    naitat pratyakṣam ityevamaparīkṣopasaṃhṛtā ||
  3. 5,2.19tatrānyasyāyathārthatvaṃ pratyakṣe tu yathārthatā |<153>                    yadābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ tatsaṃyoge tad iṣyate ||
  4. 5,2.20sampūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hy etat, tatsator vyatyayaḥ kṛtaḥ |                    śobhanārthas tu sacchabdaḥ, yad vākhyāhārakalpanā ||
  5. 5,2.21arthāpattyetareṣāṃ ca pratyakṣābhāsalakṣaṇam |                    bādhakajñānalābho hi pūrvābādhe na sambhavet ||
  6. 5,2.22sa cāstīti, avabodhatve sati nānyonyasaṃśrayam |                    na cānāgatabādhe ca pūrveṇātmā hi labhyate ||<154>
  7. 5,2.23nimittadoṣabodhena paścād yatrāpy abādhanam |                    bhavaty eva hi tatrāpi narāntaraviparyayaḥ ||
  8. 5,2.24sarveṣāṃ sarvadā yatra dhīḥ syāt tatra na bādhanam |                    na hi kāraṇaduṣṭatvabuddhis tatra balīyasī ||<155>
  9. 5,2.25jātyādiṣu yadā jātā buddhiḥ paścād asambhavāt |                    nāśyate yuktibhis tatra vyaktam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
  10. 5,2.26svataḥ prāmāṇyataś cātra nirṇayo 'stitvabodhanāt |                    tadrūpapratyayotpattes tadasadvādinām api ||

Chapter 5,3 nirālambanavāda NAV

  1. 5,3.1pramāṇatvāpramāṇatve puṇyapāpādi tatphalam |                    vidhyarthavādamantrārthanāmadheyādikalpanā ||
  2. 5,3.2sarveṣu lakṣaṇeṣv evaṃ svapramāṇagaṇaiḥ sthitiḥ |                    vacanavyaktibhedena pūrvasiddhāntapakṣatā ||
  3. 5,3.3karmabhyaḥ phalasambandhaḥ pāralaukyaihalaukike |                    sarvam ityādy ayuktaṃ syād arthaśūnyāsu buddhiṣu ||<156>
  4. 5,3.4tasmād dharmārthibhiḥ pūrvaṃ pramāṇair lokasammataiḥ |                    arthasya sadasadbhāve yatnaḥ kāryaḥ kriyāṃ prati ||
  5. 5,3.5yadā saṃvṛtisatyena sarvam etat prakalpyate |                    jñānamātre 'pi kasmād vo vṛthāgraho 'rthakalpane ||
  6. 5,3.6saṃvṛter na tu satyatvaṃ satyabhedaḥ kuto 'nvayam |                    satyā cet saṃvṛtiḥ keyaṃ mṛṣā cet satyatā katham ||
  7. 5,3.7satyatvaṃ na ca sāmānyaṃ mṛṣārthaparamārthayoḥ |<157>                    virodhāt, na hi vṛkṣatvaṃ sāmānyaṃ vṛkṣasiṃhayoḥ ||
  8. 5,3.8tulyārthatve 'pi tenaiṣāṃ mithyāsaṃvṛtiśabdayoḥ |                    vañcanārtha upanyāso lālāvaktrāsavādivat ||
  9. 5,3.9nāstikyaparihārārthaṃ saṃvṛtiḥ, kalpaneti ca |                    kalpanāpi tv abhinnasya naiva nirvastuke bhavet ||
  10. 5,3.10tasmād yan nāsti nāsty eva, yat tv asti paramārthataḥ |                    tat satyam anyanmithyeti, na satyadvayakalpanā ||
  11. 5,3.11svapnādibhogavac cāpi yopabhogatvakalpanā |                    tannivṛttyartham eveha paramārthe kaś cit pravartate ||
  12. 5,3.12na hi svapnasukhādyarthaṃ dharme kaś cit pravartate |                    yādṛcchikatvāt svapnasya tūṣṇīmāsyeta paṇḍitaiḥ ||
  13. 5,3.13paramārthaphalāvāptim icchadbhis tena yatnataḥ |                    pratipattir vidhātavyā yuktibhir bāhyavastuṣu ||<158>
  14. 5,3.14tatrārthaśūnyaṃ vijñānaṃ yogācārāḥ samāśritāḥ |                    tasyāpy abhāvam icchanti ye mādhyamikavādinaḥ ||
  15. 5,3.15tatra bāhyārthaśūnyatvaṃ tulyaṃ tāvad dvayor api |                    nivṛttyāsya tato jñāne tadvat saṃvṛtikalpanā ||
  16. 5,3.16tasmāt sādhāraṇatvena tanmūlatvena cāpy ayam |                    bāhyārthasadasadbhāve yatno bhāṣyakṛtā kṛtāḥ ||
  17. 5,3.17bāhyārthāpahnave 'dvaitam ekārthasya parīkṣaṇāt |                    pramāṇam āśritaś caikas tatrāstāṃ yaḥ prameyataḥ ||
  18. 5,3.18pramāṇasthas tu mūlatvād ihedānīṃ parīkṣyate |                    prastutaḥ sa dvidhā cātra prathamaṃ tv anumānataḥ ||
  19. 5,3.19pratyakṣabādhane cokte paścāt tacchaktyavekṣaṇāt |                    tatrānumānamāhedaṃ nanv iti, asya ca saṅgatiḥ ||
  20. 5,3.20tatsamprayogajaṃ nāma pratyakṣam iti bhāṣitam |                    tatrendriyārthasambandhabhedo na paramārthataḥ ||
  21. 5,3.21kalpitaḥ samprayogas tu svapnādāv api vidyate |                    tadatadyogajanyasya vibhāgas tena durlabhaḥ ||<159>
  22. 5,3.22mithyātvaṃ yad dvidhaivoktaṃ nāyathety atra cocyate |                    sarvasyaiva ca mithyātve kiṃ viśiṣyābhidhīyate ||
  23. 5,3.23stambhādipratyayo mithyā pratyayatvāt tathā hi yaḥ |                    pratyayaḥ sa mṛṣā dṛṣṭaḥ svapnādipratyayo yathā ||
  24. 5,3.24siddhasādhanabhāvo 'ṃśe dṛṣṭāntābhāva eva ca |                    mā bhūtām evaśabdaś ca vyartho 'śeṣaprasādhane ||
  25. 5,3.25sarva eveti tenātra jāgradbuddhiparigrahaḥ |                    svāṃśābhyupagamāc cāpi bāhyagrāhyanivāraṇam ||
  26. 5,3.26pratyayasyeti sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanam |                    hetuś copanyenātra jāgrato 'pīti darśataḥ ||<160>
  27. 5,3.27vipakṣābhāvataś cātra vyatireko na kathyate |                    sāmānyasya ca hetutvāt kasmāt pakṣaikadeśatā ||
  28. 5,3.28jāgrajjñāne viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ supariniścayaḥ |                    bāhyālambanasambandho na prasiddhaḥ paraṃ prati ||
  29. 5,3.29tasmād yad bhāṣyakāreṇa dattam uttam atra tu |                    vikalpasamatā vā syād vaidharmyasamatāpi vā ||
  30. 5,3.30dṛṣṭatvāt pūrvapakṣasya jātyukti kaiś cid āśritā |                    pratijñādoṣam evāhuḥ ke cit pratyakṣabādhanam ||<161>
  31. 5,3.31śakṣyāmo yadi vispaṣṭaṃ svāṃśagrāhyanivāraṇam |                    tadā te śuddha eva syāt pakṣo grāhyanivāraṇaḥ ||
  32. 5,3.32pratyakṣādeś ca viṣayo bāhya evāvatiṣṭhate |                    tanniṣedhakṛtas tasya tair bhavet pakṣabādhanam ||
  33. 5,3.33suniścayena caiteṣāṃ bādhakapratyayād ṛte |                    pramāṇābhāsatā nāstīty etasmāt katyate balam ||
  34. 5,3.34duṣṭajñānagṛhītāpratiṣedho hi yujyate |                    gṛhītamātrabādhe tu svapakṣo 'pi na sidhyati ||
  35. 5,3.35agrāhyatvāc ca bhedena viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |                    aprasiddhobhayatvaṃ vā vācyam anyatarasya vā ||
  36. 5,3.36vaktṛśrotroś ca yajjñānaṃ viśeṣaṇviśeṣyayoḥ |                    tannirālambanatvena svavāgbādho dvyor api ||
  37. 5,3.37sambhavo na ca bhedasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ |                    tasmān nirūpaṇaṃ nāsti pratijñārthasya śobhanam ||<162>
  38. 5,3.38nirālambanatā nāma na kiñ cid vastu gamyate |                    tena yadvyatirekādau praśno naivopapadyate ||
  39. 5,3.39yady avastu kathaṃ tv asmāṃs tvaṃ bodhayitum icchasi |                    budhyase vā svabuddhyā tvam, kalpitā tv atha sādhyate ||
  40. 5,3.40asataḥ kalpanā kīdṛk, kḷptau vastu prasajyate |                    katham iṣṭam abhāve ced, vastu so 'pīti vakṣyate ||
  41. 5,3.41tathā pratyaya ity eṣa karma bhāvādi vā bhavet |                    bhāvādiṣu virodhaḥ syāt karma cet siddhasādhanam ||
  42. 5,3.42pratyāyyasya hi rūpāder nirālambanateṣyate |                    avijñānātmakatvena kiñ cin nālambate hy asau ||
  43. 5,3.43kartṛtve karaṇatve vā pakṣatvaṃ śabdayor api |                    tannirālambanatvena pakṣābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||<163>
  44. 5,3.44pratyāyyena ca bhinnena vinā kartrādyasambhavaḥ |                    pratyaye tannimitte vā bādhaḥ svavacanena te ||
  45. 5,3.45athāpi rūḍhirūpeṇa pratyayaḥ syāt tathāpi tu |                    grāhakaṃ vastu siddhaṃ naḥ pratyayo 'nyasya vastunaḥ ||
  46. 5,3.46tam abhyupetya pakṣaś ced abhyupetaṃ virudhyate |                    viśeṣyasyāprasiddhaś ca tava, asmākam atādṛśe ||
  47. 5,3.47ātmadharmasvatantratvakalpane 'pi tathā bhavet |                    na ca pratyayamātratvaṃ kiñ cid asty anirūpaṇāt ||
  48. 5,3.48śabdārthamātrarūpeṇa yathānyeṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |                    tathā ca bhavato na syād vācyabhedamanicchataḥ ||
  49. 5,3.49nirālambanatā cāpi sarvathā yadi sādhyate |                    viśeṣaṇāprasiddhiś ca dṛṣṭāntaś ca na vidyate ||<164>
  50. 5,3.50kena cic cet prakāreṇa nirālambanatocyate |                    rasajñānasya rūpādiśūnyatvāt siddhasādhanam ||
  51. 5,3.51atha buddhir yadākārā tadālambanavāraṇam |                    svākārasyābhyupetatvāt tadabhāvo virudhyate ||
  52. 5,3.52bāhyānālambanatve 'pi bāhya ity agraho yadi |                    stambhādau naiva tadbuddhir ityevaṃ siddhasādhanam ||
  53. 5,3.53atha stambhādirūpeṇa nirālambanatocyate |                    saṃvedanasya dṛṣṭatvāt tadvirodhaḥ prasajyate ||
  54. 5,3.54dvicandrādiṣu tulyaś cet, nendriyāprāptito hi naḥ |                    tatrānālambanoktiḥ syān nārthasaṃvittyabhāvataḥ ||
  55. 5,3.55sarvatrārthendriyāṇāṃ naḥ saṃyogasadasattayā |                    saṃvittau vidyamānāyāṃ sadasadgrāhikā sthitiḥ ||<165>
  56. 5,3.56bhavatas tv indriyādīnām abhāvād grahaṇād ṛte |                    nālambanasya hetuḥ syān niṣedho 'to na yujyate ||
  57. 5,3.57bahirbhāvāprasiddhatvāt tenānālambanā matiḥ |                    kathañ cit sādhyate naiṣa pakṣo hi jñāyate tadā ||
  58. 5,3.58yathānyabodhanāśakter nāprasiddhe viśeṣaṇe |                    pakṣasiddhis tathaiva syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣaṇe ||
  59. 5,3.59nāprasiddhe padārthe hi vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate |                    tatpūrvakatvāt pakṣaś ca vākyārthaḥ sthāpayiṣyate ||
  60. 5,3.60paryudāse niṣedhe vā vyatiriktasya vastunaḥ |                    prameyatvādyabhedena jagataḥ siddhasādhanam ||<166>
  61. 5,3.61yadi cātyantabhedena nirālambanatocyate |                    kathañ cic ced virudhyeta prākpakṣaḥ kalpitena ||
  62. 5,3.62vastvādyākārataś cāpi dhīr nirālambaneṣyate |                    grāhakāc ced abhinnatvaṃ śaktibhedo virudhyate ||
  63. 5,3.63nirālambanabuddheś ca yady utpattiḥ prasādhyate |                    dṛṣṭatvāt seṣyate 'smābhir bāhyagrāhyavivarjitā ||
  64. 5,3.64samyaktvaṃ punar etasyās tvaṃ necchasi kathañ cana |                    ātmāṃśe 'vasitā hy eṣā mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat ||
  65. 5,3.65caitrādipratyayānāṃ ca nirālambanatā yadi |                    dharmabhūtā na gṛhyeta sādhanotthitayā dhiyā ||
  66. 5,3.66tato viṣayanānātvāt pratiyogyanirākṛtā |                    rūpāt sālambanaprāptiḥ satī kena nivāryate ||<167>
  67. 5,3.67yadi pratyayaśabdo 'pi pratyayatvena gṛhyate |                    saṃvittyālambanatvaṃ ca vāryate, siddhasādhanam ||
  68. 5,3.68buddhyutpādanaśaktiś ced vāryā, sādhayaṃ na sidhyati |                    sādhanasya prayogo 'tra bodhakatvād vinā na te ||
  69. 5,3.69na cābhidhāstyasambandhād ṛte bhedāc ca nāsty asau |                    na cāsau tadgataṃ bhedaṃ bodhayantya dhiyā vinā ||
  70. 5,3.70prāśnikair agṛhīte ca vākyasyāvayave pṛthak |                    pakṣe hetau ca dṛṣṭānte vādini prativādini ||
  71. 5,3.71sādhanasyāprayogaḥ syād abhyupetyocyate yadi |                    pūrvābhyupagamenaiva pratijñā bādhyate tataḥ ||
  72. 5,3.72dharmādharmādibhede ca nāsiddhe paramārthataḥ |                    śiṣyātmanoś ca dharmāder upadeśo 'vakalpate ||
  73. 5,3.73tadanuṣṭhānato buddher iṣṭo bhedaḥ, <168> sphuṭaṃ ca taiḥ |                    sūtrāntare 'bhyupetatvād bhaved āgamabādhanam ||
  74. 5,3.74sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca pakṣabādho 'tra te dhruvam |                    kṛtsnasādhanabuddhiś ca yadi mithyeṣyate tataḥ ||
  75. 5,3.75sarvābhāvo yatheṣṭaṃ vā nyūnatā vābhidhīyate |                    teṣāṃ sālambanatve vā tair anaikāntiko bhavet ||
  76. 5,3.76tadanyasya pratijñā cet, tadanyapratyayo mṛṣā |                    tanmithyātvaprasaṅge ca sarvaṃ pūrva na sidhyati ||
  77. 5,3.77stambhādisādhanajñānabhedo na hi tathā bhavet |                    yāvad yāvat pratijñeyaṃ tadaṅgasya pratīyate ||
  78. 5,3.78tāvat tāvat pareṣāṃ syān mithyātvād anyabādhanam |<169>                    viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ bādho vāpy anumānataḥ ||
  79. 5,3.79itthaṃ sarveṣu pakṣeṣu vaktavyaṃ pratisādhanam |                    bāhyārthālambanā buddhir iti samyak ca dhīr iyam ||
  80. 5,3.80bādhakāpetabuddhitvād yathā svapnādibādhadhīḥ |                    sāpi mithyeti ced brūyāt, svapnādīnām abādhanāt ||
  81. 5,3.81tasmāt sādharmyadṛṣṭānto bhavataḥ sādhane na hi |                    vijñānāstitvabhinnatvakṣaṇikatvādidhīs tathā ||
  82. 5,3.82samyak ced abhyupeyeta tadānaikāntiko bhavet |                    tanmithyābhyupapattau ca pakṣabādhaḥ prasajyate ||
  83. 5,3.83tathā ca baddham uktādivyavasthā na prakalpate |                    tataś ca mokṣayatnasya vaiphalyaṃ vaḥ prasajyate ||<170>
  84. 5,3.84vikalpotpadyamānā ca jñānāstitvādidhīr yadi |                    mṛṣeṣṭā, na ca dṛṣṭātra pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
  85. 5,3.85pramāṇābhāvatas tena jñānāstitvādi durlabham |                    sarvaṃ cāpy asmadādīnāṃ mithyā jñānaṃ vikalpanāt ||
  86. 5,3.86sānnidhyaviprakṛṣṭatve sattvāsattve ca durlabhe |                    mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi sāṃkhyādiparivarjanāt ||
  87. 5,3.87bauddhadarśana ekasmin pakṣapāto na yujyate |                    mṛṣātvaṃ yadi buddheḥ syād bādhaḥ kiṃ nopalabhyate ||
  88. 5,3.88bādhād vināpi tac cet syād vyavasthā na prakalpate |                    pratiyogini dṛṣṭe ca jāgrajjñāne mṛṣā bhavet ||
  89. 5,3.89svapnādibuddhir asmākaṃ tava bhedo 'pi kiṅkṛtaḥ |                    na cānyat pratiyogyasti jāgrajjñānasya śobhanam ||
  90. 5,3.90yaddarśanena mithyātvaṃ stambhādipratyayo vrajet |                    svapnādipratiyogitvaṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
  91. 5,3.91tadīyadharmavaidharmyād bādhakapratyayo yathā |<171>                    yogināṃ jāyate buddhir bādhikā pratiyoginī ||
  92. 5,3.92jāgratstambhādibuddhīnāṃ tataḥ svapnāditulyatā |                    prāptānāṃ tām avasthāṃ ca sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api ||
  93. 5,3.93bādho 'yaṃ bhavitā tena siddhā sapratiyogitā |                    iha janmani keṣāñ cin na tāvad upalabhyate ||
  94. 5,3.94yogyavasthāgatānāṃ tu na vidmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati |                    yogināṃ cāsmādīyānāṃ tvaduktapratiyoginī ||
  95. 5,3.95tvaduktiviparītā vā bādhabuddhir bhaviṣyati |                    īdṛktve yogibuddhīnāṃ dṛṣṭānto na tavāsti ca ||
  96. 5,3.96dṛṣṭāntas tv asmādīnāṃ yo gṛhītaḥ sa vidyate |                    atha stambhādibuddhīnāṃ vadet sapratiyogitām ||
  97. 5,3.97bādhyatvaṃ cāpi buddhitvān mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat |<172>                    iṣṭaṃ sapratiyogitvaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhibhiḥ ||
  98. 5,3.98tadātmanā ca bādhyatvaṃ grāhyāntaratayāpi ca |                    bādhakaiś cāpy anekāntaḥ, tadanyatve ca pūrvavat ||
  99. 5,3.99mithyādhīpratiyogitvaṃ svapnādāv iva te bhavet |                    rāgādikṣayayogitvanimittādhigatis tathā ||
  100. 5,3.100yāvān viśeṣa iṣṭaś cet sarvābhāvād viruddhatā |                    mahājanasya vā bādhādivānīmbādhabuddhivat ||
  101. 5,3.101vācyo 'numānabādho vā yadi vā pratisādhanam |                    pūrvasādhanadoṣāś ca sandheyāḥ, tasya cādhunā ||
  102. 5,3.102sādhyābhedād avācyatvād hetor nobhayasiddhatā |                    pratyayatvaṃ ca, <173> sāmānyaṃ bhinnābhinnaṃ na vidyate ||
  103. 5,3.103bhavato 'tyantabhinnaṃ ca matpakṣe 'pi kathañ cana |                    sārūpyānyanivṛttī ca netyetat sādhayiṣyate ||
  104. 5,3.104tasmād dhetur na sāmānyam asti siddhaṃ dvayor api |                    viśeṣayoś ca hetutvaṃ pakṣatattulyasaṃsthayoḥ ||
  105. 5,3.105na syād anvayahīnatvād ataddharmatayāpi ca |                    na cārthahīnā tadbuddhir hetutvena bhaviṣyati ||
  106. 5,3.106āśrayāsiddhitā coktā viśeṣyasyāprasiddhitaḥ |                    tathā hetor viruddhatvaṃ dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
  107. 5,3.107viśeṣaṇāprasiddhatvavikalpenaiva bodhite |                    svapnādipratyaye bāhyaṃ sarvathā na hi neṣyate ||
  108. 5,3.108sarvatrālambanaṃ bāhyaṃ deśakālānyathātmakam |<174>                    janmany ekatra bhinne vā tathā kālāntare 'pi vā ||
  109. 5,3.109taddeśo vānyadeśo vā svapnajñānasya gocaraḥ |                    alātacakre 'lātaṃ syāc chīghrabhramaṇasaṃskṛtam ||
  110. 5,3.110gandharvanagare 'bhrāṇi pūrvadṛṣṭaṃ gṛhādi ca |                    pūrvānubhūtatoyaṃ ca raśmitaptoṣaraṃ tathā ||
  111. 5,3.111mṛgatoyasya vijñāne kāraṇatvena kalpyate |                    dravyāntare viṣāṇaṃ ca śaśasyātmā ca kāraṇam ||
  112. 5,3.112śaśaśṛṅgadhiyaḥ, mauṇḍyaṃ niṣedhe śiraso 'sya ca |                    vastvantarair asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ padārthaḥ śūnyatādhiyaḥ ||<175>
  113. 5,3.113kāraṇatvaṃ padārthānām asadvākyārthakalpane |                    atyantānanubhūto 'pi baddhyā yo 'rthaḥ prakalpyate ||
  114. 5,3.114tasyotpattau kathañ cit syuḥ pṛthivyādīni kāraṇam |                    eṣa pratyakṣadharmaś ca vartamānārthataiva yā ||
  115. 5,3.115sannikṛṣṭārthavṛttiś ca na tu jñānāntareṣv iyam |                    katham utpādayej jñānaṃ tatrāsaṃścet, kuto nviyam ||
  116. 5,3.116arthasyāvidyamānasya vijñānotpattyaśaktatā |                    bāhyālambanatāyāṃ nau vivādo 'rthasya saṃnidhiḥ ||
  117. 5,3.117yadi nāsti, kim evaṃ syād asmatpakṣanivartanam |                    tasmād yadanyathāsantam anyathā pratipadyate ||
  118. 5,3.118tannirālambanaṃ jñānam, <176> abhāvālambanaṃ ca tat |                    bhāvāntaram abhāvo 'nyo na kaś cid anirūpaṇāt ||
  119. 5,3.119bhavatā dvayamatyetad durnirūpaṃ sahetukam |                    pratijñādoṣavac cāpi yojyā hetor viruddhatā ||
  120. 5,3.120samastavyastadharmādisvarūpādiviparyayāt |<177>                    dṛṣṭāntadoṣāḥ sarve ca yojyāḥ, na hy ekavastuni ||
  121. 5,3.121tava sādhyāṃśahetvaṃśavyāptadharmādisambhavaḥ |                    ke cid vaidharmyadṛṣṭānto nāstīty apy anuyuñjate ||
  122. 5,3.122tadabhāvād avṛtteś ca nāsty atrāvasaras tava |                    vidhirūpapratijñāyām etad vaktuṃ hi śakyate ||
  123. 5,3.123tatrāvastuvipakṣe 'pi prayogasya hi sambhavaḥ |                    yasminn anityatā nāsti kāryatāpi na vidyate ||
  124. 5,3.124tasmin, yathā khapuṣpādāv iti śakyaṃ hi bhāṣitum |                    atra tv avastusādhyatvaṃ vastunaś ca vipakṣatā ||
  125. 5,3.125tena syād vyatireko 'sya vācyaḥ, <178> yaś cāpi darśayet |                    pratiṣedhadvayāt tena vidhir eva pradarśitaḥ ||
  126. 5,3.126na ca śakyo vidhir vaktuṃ vastuny asati kena cit |                    evaṃ sthite ca sarvajñaniṣedhādāv iyaṃ gatiḥ ||
  127. 5,3.127pratyakṣāder asāmarthyaṃ tadīyasyāsmadādivat |                    vaidharmyāsambhave 'py etadanye tv āhur adūṣaṇam ||
  128. 5,3.128vinaiva tatprayogeṇa hetur aikāntiko yataḥ |                    sarvathā sadupāyānāṃ vādamārgaḥ pravartate ||
  129. 5,3.129adhikāro 'nupāyatvān na vāde śūnyavādinaḥ |                    nanu sarvaṃ bhavatsiddhaṃ mayedaṃ sādhanaṃ kṛtam ||
  130. 5,3.130kimarthaṃ tadasiddhyā tvaṃ vikalpyātrātthadūṣaṇam |                    vipralipsur ivāhaivaṃ kimarthaṃ nyāyavid bhavān ||<179>
  131. 5,3.131nāśrauṣīḥ sādhanatvaṃ kiṃ prasiddhasya dvayor api |                    yo 'pi tāvat parāsiddhaḥ svayaṃ siddho 'bhidhīyate ||
  132. 5,3.132bhavet tatra pratīkāraḥ svato 'siddhe tu kā kriyā |                    taṃ sādhayan virundhyād dhi pūrvābhyupagataṃ naraḥ ||
  133. 5,3.133asādhite tu sādhyo 'rtho na tena pratipadyate |                    parāsiddho na paryāptaḥ pareṣāṃ pratipattaye ||
  134. 5,3.134tenāsādhanatā yuktā, svato 'siddhe tu kiṅkṛtā |                    dvayoḥ siddhasya hetutvaṃ nādṛṣṭāyopadiśyate ||
  135. 5,3.135pratyeṣyanti svasiddhena sādhanena svayaṃ yataḥ |                    vadet katham asiddhaṃ cet, ityanenāpi kiṃ tava ||
  136. 5,3.136gṛhītam agṛhītaṃ vā sādhyaṃ vā sādhanāpi vā |                    mayocyate cet tv asiddhaṃ kiṃ tvaṃ na pratipadyase ||
  137. 5,3.137yatra syāt puruṣādhīnā buddhis tatredam ucyate |                    kuto 'sya pūrvavijñānam ityatretanna yujyate ||<180>
  138. 5,3.138yadi caivaṃ bhaved atra pratijñāmātra eva hi |                    maddoṣājñānamātreṇa pratipattir bhavet tava ||
  139. 5,3.139yatas tu sādhanāpekṣā tenāsyaiva pramāṇatā |                    tatsmṛtyutpattimātre tu vākyavyāpāra iṣyate ||
  140. 5,3.140tasmād yathaiva sādhyāṃśavyāptahetunidarśanāt |                    sādhyaṃ gṛhṇan na vaktāram apekṣeta tathā bhavān ||
  141. 5,3.141yac cāpi bhavato jñānaṃ pratyakādiḥ kim atra te |                    matprasiddhāsti yuktir vā sādhyaṃ vātra yathecchasi ||
  142. 5,3.142tasmān na viduṣām etaduttaṃ yujyate yataḥ |                    tava hetur asiddho 'yaṃ mama tena na sādhanam ||
  143. 5,3.143satyaṃ yadi mamaivātra pratipattiḥ phalaṃ bhavet |                    tadā tvadaprasiddhe 'pi hetau māṃ prati hetutā ||
  144. 5,3.144yadā tu jñānamātratvapratipattau bhavān mayā |                    pṛṣṭaḥ ko hetur atreti tadaivaṃ nopapadyate ||
  145. 5,3.145svayaṃ na hy agṛhītena matprasiddhena vā bhavān |                    hetunā sādhyam etat tu pratipannaḥ kathañ cana ||<181>
  146. 5,3.146na ca vyāpriyate 'nyatra vacanaṃ prāśnikān prati |                    svaniścayāya yo hetus tasyaiva pratipādanāt ||
  147. 5,3.147matprasiddhatvam etasya kutaś cāvagataṃ tvayā |                    kathaṃ cetthaṃ vivakṣā te svayam artham ajānataḥ ||
  148. 5,3.148mayi jijñāsamāne 'pi buddhipūrvābhidhāyinaḥ |                    iti jñātvā ca vo vṛddhair bhāṣitobhayasiddhatā ||
  149. 5,3.149tena yadvanmamaitena tvamadhitsasi hetunā |                    sādhyajñānam, tathaivāham ajñānaṃ tava dūṣaṇaiḥ ||
  150. 5,3.150yathaiva ca bhavānīdṛk sādhyam uktvāsya sādhanam |                    sādhyānurūpam ajñātvā vihataḥ pratipādanāt ||
  151. 5,3.151tathaiva pratipādyo 'pi tādṛksādhyabubhutsayā |                    manvānaḥ sādhanaṃ duṣṭaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ na budhyate ||
  152. 5,3.152saṃvittyā sādhanaṃ matvā tatsadbhāve dṛḍhe sthite |                    sādhyasyāsambhavād eva tvaduktaṃ nāvabudhyate ||
  153. 5,3.153tenāśeyaṃ na kartavyā mohād api mayerite |                    sādhane sādhanaṃ jñātvā para evāvabhotsyate ||<182>
  154. 5,3.154vispaṣṭaś cākṣapādokto virodho hetusādhyayoḥ |                    yamadṛṣṭvā parair uktam adūṣaṇam idaṃ kila ||
  155. 5,3.155nanu lokaprasiddhena pūrvam etena hetunā |                    sādhyasiddhir mamāpy āsīt paramārtho 'sya nāstitā ||
  156. 5,3.156yo 'dhunā paramārthena nāstītyevaṃ prakāśate |                    kathaṃ pūrvam asāv āsīd asaṃścet sādhanaṃ katham ||
  157. 5,3.157sādhanaṃ ced avaśyaṃ ca paramārthāstitā bhavet |                    siddhir nāparamārthena paramārthasya yujyate ||
  158. 5,3.158na dṛṣṭā śaśaśṛṅgādeḥ samyagjñānādihetutā |<183>                    bāṣpādināpy adhūmena mithyā vahnyādibodhanam ||
  159. 5,3.159tasmād asatyahetor yā paramārthe matis tava |                    sāpy asatyā na satyaṃ hi satyābhāsena gamyate ||
  160. 5,3.160ye 'pi rekhādayo dṛṣṭā varṇānāṃ pratipādakāḥ |                    na te svenāpi rūpeṇa paramārthatvavarjitāḥ ||
  161. 5,3.161varṇātmanā na satyāś cet, sarvabhāveṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ |                    padārthāntararūpeṇa na satyaṃ kiñ cid iṣyate ||
  162. 5,3.162svarūpe vidyamāne tu yad apy evaṃ prakāśate |                    svarūpābhāvakḷptau tu na satyaṃ nāpy asatyatā ||
  163. 5,3.163hetvādīnāṃ tu bhavataḥ svarūpeṇāpy asatyatā |                    tena bāṣpādivat teṣām upāyatvam, na lekhyavat ||<184>
  164. 5,3.164upāyānāṃ svarūpaṃ hi saṃvṛttyātmakam eva naḥ |                    tathā ca satyateṣṭaiva svarūpāsatyatā katham ||
  165. 5,3.165saṃvṛtyā yat svarūpaṃ hi tadvāṅmātranibandhanam |                    hetutvaṃ paramārthasya pratipattuṃ na śaknuyāt ||
  166. 5,3.166paramāthāc ca lokasya na bhede hetur asti te |                    laukikopāyagamyasya kena syāt paramārthatā ||
  167. 5,3.167nanv asty api bāhye 'rthe buddhyārūḍhe na sidhyati |                    vāsanāśabdabhedotthavikalpapravibhāgataḥ ||
  168. 5,3.168nyāyavidbhir idaṃ coktaṃ dharmādau buddhim āśrite |                    vyavahāro 'numānādeḥ kalpyate na bahiḥsthite ||<185>
  169. 5,3.169astīdaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām idaṃ tatra parīkṣyatām |                    bhedo 'sataḥ kathaṃ hi syād buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
  170. 5,3.170nirvastuke kathañ cin nu prasavo buddhiśabdayoḥ |                    śabdabhedo 'pi bhavatas tadabhāvān na sidhyati ||
  171. 5,3.171yadi vā vidyamāno 'pi bhedo buddhiprakalpitaḥ |                    sādhyasādhanadharmāder vyavahārāya kalpyate ||
  172. 5,3.172tato bhavatprayukte 'smin sādhane yāvad ucyate |                    sarvatrotpadyate buddhir iti dūṣaṇatā bhavet ||
  173. 5,3.173yaś ca mantras tv ayokto 'yaṃ dharmyādau buddhim āśrite |                    na bāhyāpekṣayā sa syād asiddhyādau mayerite ||
  174. 5,3.174buddhiprakḷptisidhiś ca bhavatāṃ vyavahāriṇam |                    maduktaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ siddhaṃ tvaduktaṃ tu na sādhanam ||
  175. 5,3.175bāhyārthavyavahāritvāj jñānotpāde sthite 'pi naḥ |                    kathañ cin na hi kalpyeta vyavahāro 'rthavarjitaḥ ||
  176. 5,3.176nanu yadvanmayā hetur neṣyate dūṣaṇaṃ tathā |                    tena me dūṣaṇābhāvād aduṣṭaṃ sādhanaṃ bhavet ||<186>
  177. 5,3.177nedānīṃ dūṣaṇaiḥ kāryam, sādhanābhāvato yadi |                    tvayaivāsmadabhipretā svapakṣāsiddhir āśritā ||
  178. 5,3.178na cāsti vāsanābhedo nimittāsambhavāt tava |                    jñānabhedo nimittaṃ cet, tasya bhedaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ ||
  179. 5,3.179vāsanābhedataś cet syāt, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |                    svacchasya jñānarūpasya na hi bhedaḥ svato 'sti te ||
  180. 5,3.180pramāṇaṃ vāsanāstitve bhede vāpi na vidyate |                    kuryād grāhakabhedaṃ sā grāhyabhedas tu kiṅkutaḥ ||
  181. 5,3.181saṃvittyā jāyamānā hi smṛtimātraṃ karoty asau |                    kṣaṇikeṣu ca cit teṣu vināśe ca niranvaye ||
  182. 5,3.182vāsyavāsakayoś caivam asāhityān na vāsanā |                    pūrvakṣaṇair anutpanno vāsyate nottaraḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||
  183. 5,3.183uttareṇa vinaṣṭatvān na ca pūrvasya vāsanā |<187>                    sāhitye 'pi tayor naiva sambandho 'stīty avāsanā ||
  184. 5,3.184kṣaṇikatvād dvyasyāpi vyāpāro na parasparam |                    vinaśyac ca kathaṃ vastu vāsyate 'nyena naśyatā ||
  185. 5,3.185avasthitā hi vāsyante bhāvābhāvair avasthitaiḥ |                    avasthito hi pūrvasmād bhidyate nottaro yadi ||
  186. 5,3.186pūrvavad vāsanā tatra na syād evāviśeṣataḥ |                    bhaṅgure pūrvasādṛśyād bhinnatvāc cāsti vāsanā ||<188>
  187. 5,3.187naitad asty anurūpaṃ tu kṣaṇikatve dhiyāṃ tava |                    pūrvajñānaṃ tv anutpannaṃ kāryaṃ nārabhate kvacit ||
  188. 5,3.188na vinaṣṭaṃ, na tasyāsti niṣpannasya kṣaṇaṃ sthitiḥ |                    tenotpannavinaṣṭatvān nāsty ārambhakṣaṇo 'pi hi ||
  189. 5,3.189niranvayavinaṣṭatvād ānurūpyaṃ kutaḥ punaḥ |                    na tadīyosti kaś cic ca dharma uttarabuddhiṣu ||
  190. 5,3.190samānadharmatāṃ muktvā nānurūpyaṃ ca vidyate |                    yadi syād ānurūpyāc ca vāsanā godhiyo yadā ||
  191. 5,3.191hastibuddhir bhavet tatra vailakṣaṇyān na vāsanā |                    tataḥ paraṃ ca gojñānaṃ nirmūlatvān na sambhavet ||
  192. 5,3.192sarvaṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ na syād eva vilakṣaṇāt |<189>                    bāhyārthānugrahābhāvāt pārārthyenāvaśīkṛtāḥ ||
  193. 5,3.193niranvayavināśinyaḥ kuryuḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ kramāt |                    vināśe kāraṇasyeṣṭaḥ kāryārambhaś ca nānyathā ||
  194. 5,3.194tataiva jñānanāśena vinaṣṭāḥ sarvavāsanāḥ |                    tena sarvābhya etābhyaḥ sarvākāraṃ yadutthitam ||
  195. 5,3.195jñānam ekakṣaṇenaiva vināśaṃ gantum arhati |                    yady āśrayavināśe 'pi śaktyanāśo 'bhyupeyate ||
  196. 5,3.196kṣaṇikatvaṃ ca hīyeta na cārambho 'nyathā bhavet |                    vāsanānāṃ pravāho 'pi yadi jñānapravāhavat ||<190>
  197. 5,3.197vāsanātas tato jñānaṃ na syāt tasmāc ca vāsanā |                    kuryātāṃ tulyam evaite nānyonyaṃ tu kadā cana ||
  198. 5,3.198nānyo vilakṣaṇo hetur yenānyādṛk phalaṃ bhavet |                    tasmāt saṃvṛtisatyaiṣā kalpitā nāsti tattvataḥ ||
  199. 5,3.199na cedṛśena bhavena kāryam utpadyate kva cit |                    yasya tv avasthito jñātā jñānābhyāsena yujyate ||
  200. 5,3.200sa tasya vāsanādhāro vāsanāpi sa eva vā |                    kusume bījapūrāder yallākṣādyupasicyate |<191>                    tadrūpasyaiva saṃkrāntiḥ phale tasya, ity avāsanā ||
  201. 5,3.201yuktyānupetām asatīṃ prakalpya yadvāsanām arthanirākriyeyam ||                    āsthānivṛttyarthamavādi bauddhair grāhaṃ gatās tatra kathañ cid anye ||

Chapter 5,4 śunyavāda SNV

  1. 5,4.1evam ukte 'numānasya jñānam āśritya dūṣaṇe |                    jñānapravṛttyaśaktyā tu paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ||
  2. 5,4.2yat tāvanmanyamānena pratyakṣaṃ bhavatocyate |                    dūṣaṇaṃ tadvirodhādi tadidānīṃ parīkṣyatām ||
  3. 5,4.3pravartituṃ hi kiṃ śaktaṃ stambhādyarthe bahiḥ sthite |                    atha vātmāṃśa evaitat grāhye kṣīṇaṃ na vastuni ||
  4. 5,4.4tad yady etena bāhyo 'rtho gṛhyate dūṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |                    tvaduktaṃ sarvam ātmāṃśe grāhye tannopapadyate ||<192>
  5. 5,4.5tatra tāvad idaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtām api |                    grāhyataṃ nīlapītādidīrghādyākāravastunaḥ ||
  6. 5,4.6na cāpy ākārabhedena jñānajñeyāvadhāraṇā |                    na cānyataradharmatvaṃ vispaṣṭaṃ tatra gṛhyate ||
  7. 5,4.7gṛhyamāṇasya cāstitvaṃ nāgrāhyasyāpramāṇakam |                    tasmād ākāravad vastu grāhyatvād vidyate dhruvam ||
  8. 5,4.8ataḥ parīkṣamāṇānāṃ jñānam ākāravad yadi |                    tanmātre ca pramā kṣīṇā tato nāsty arthakalpanā ||
  9. 5,4.9yadi vākāravattā syād bāhyasyaiveha vastunaḥ |                    tad asti gṛhyamāṇatvāt tatsiddhaivāsti dhīr api ||
  10. 5,4.10kiṃ tāvad atra yuktaṃ syāj jñānam ākāravat, <193> kutaḥ |                    ekam ākāravad vastu grāhyam ity adhyagīṣmahi ||
  11. 5,4.11tad yady ākāravānartho bāhyaḥ kalpyate tasya ca |                    grāhyatvam anyathā na syād iti grāhakakalpanā ||
  12. 5,4.12tenākāravataḥ kḷptād grāhyād ākāravarjitam |                    vastvantaraṃ prakalpyaṃ syād grāhakaṃ niṣpramāṇakam ||
  13. 5,4.13tasyākalpanam icchaṃś ced arthe grāhakatāṃ vadeḥ |                    saṃjñāmātre visaṃvadaḥ sidddhā tv ekārthakalpanā ||
  14. 5,4.14grāhyagrāhakayor aikyaṃ sarvathā pratipādyate |                    bāhyābhyantararūpaś ca parikalpyo mṛṣeṣyate ||<194>
  15. 5,4.15matpakṣe yady api svaccho jñānātmā paramārthataḥ |                    tathāpy anādau saṃsāre pūrvajñānaprasūtibhiḥ ||
  16. 5,4.16citrābhiś citrahetutvād vāsanābhir upaplavāt |                    svānurūpyeṇa nīlādi grāhyagrāhakarūṣitam ||
  17. 5,4.17pravibhaktam ivotpannaṃ nānyam artham apekṣate |                    anyonyahetutā caiva jñānaśaktyor anādikā ||
  18. 5,4.18anekakalpanāyāś ca jyāyasī hy ekakalpanā |                    śaktimātrasya bhedaś ca vastubhedād viśiṣyate ||<195>
  19. 5,4.19tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāj jñānasyākārakalpanā |                    jyāyasī, bhavatas tv arthaṃ kalpayitvā bhaved iyam ||
  20. 5,4.20tadasiddhāvaśaktatvāt, tenaivaṃ viprakṛṣṭatā |                    pratyāsannaṃ ca, <196> sambaddhaṃ grāhyaṃ mama bhaviṣyati ||
  21. 5,4.21itaś cākāravajjñānam, yasmāt tadvat prakāśakam |                    svayamprakāśahīnasya bāhyasyopāsanaṃ matam ||<197>
  22. 5,4.22na cāgrhīte jñānākhye prakāśyo 'rtho 'vadhāryate |                    tadadhīnaprakāśatvād dīpābhāse yathā ghaṭaḥ ||
  23. 5,4.23utpanneṣv api cārtheṣu prakāśābhāvataḥ kva cit |                    pratibandhakayogād vā saṃvittir nopajāyate ||
  24. 5,4.24jñānasyotpadyamānasya pratibandho na kaś cana |                    na cāprakāśarūpatvaṃ yenāsyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
  25. 5,4.25prāk cārthagrahaṇādiṣṭā tasyotpattis tadaiva ca |                    saṃvedanaṃ bhaved asya, na cet kālāntare 'pi na ||
  26. 5,4.26kiṃ hi tasya bhaved ūrdhvaṃ prāk ca nāsīn na yena tat |                    pūrvaṃ gṛhītaṃ paścāt ca gṛhītam iti bhāṣyate ||
  27. 5,4.27jñānāntarasya cotpattiṃ prakāśo na pratīkṣate |                    tasya tasyāpi cānyena saṃvittāvasthitir bhavet ||<198>
  28. 5,4.28jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvam arthābhāve 'pi |                    parāmarśo 'rthorūpasya sa kathaṃ vopapadyate ||
  29. 5,4.29tadrūpamārthamālikhya yadi dhīrnopajāyate |                    bhūtakāle ca yadyarthas tatpūrvaṃ nopalakṣitaḥ ||
  30. 5,4.30vaktāraś cāpi dṛśyante varttamānārthabuddhiṣu |                    nīlo 'rtho 'yaṃ yato me 'tra tadrūpā jāyate matiḥ ||
  31. 5,4.31tasmāt pūrvagṛhītāsu buddhiṣv arthopalmbhanam |                    na copalabdhir astīhi nirākārāsu buddhiṣu ||
  32. 5,4.32vivekabuddhyabhāvāc ca, sākārasya ca darśanāt |                    ākāravattayā bodho jñānasyaiva prasajyate ||
  33. 5,4.33na hy evaṃ kalpanā śakyā nirākārād ito matiḥ |                    gṛhyate 'rthas tataḥ paścāt sākāraḥ sampratīyate ||<199>
  34. 5,4.34ākāravattvabhedo hi jñātvā śakyeta bhāṣitum |                    prāgbuddhigrahaṇād arthe saṃvittir neti sādhitam ||
  35. 5,4.35na cārthākāra evāyaṃ jñānārūḍhaḥ pratīyate |                    na hi so 'ntaḥpraveśāya paryāpto nārthahānaye ||
  36. 5,4.36itthambhāve pramāṇaṃ ca tasya vaktuṃ na śakyate |                    tadīyapratibimbatvam etasmād eva neṣyate ||
  37. 5,4.37niścandre bimbarūpaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ yena divā jalam |                    sa rātrau khe ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā jānāti pratibimbatām ||
  38. 5,4.38vijñāne na kadā cit tu prāṅ nirākāradarśanam |                    bāhye vākāravattādhīr yenaivaṃ kalpanā bhavet ||
  39. 5,4.39śabdagandharasānāṃ ca kīdṛśī pratibimbatā |                    jñāne ca gṛhyamāṇasya kathaṃ syād arthadharmatā ||
  40. 5,4.40bāhyābhyantaradeśatvān na cārthajñānayor mithaḥ |                    samparko 'sti yato mohādavivekamatir bhavet ||<200>
  41. 5,4.41asammūḍhasya cādṛṣṭe na sammohaprakalpanā |                    kalpyamāne 'tha vāpy evaṃ tad dvayor avatiṣṭhate ||
  42. 5,4.42saṃsargadhama ākāras tasmād eva na yujyate |                    deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, mūrāmūrtatayā tathā ||
  43. 5,4.43tailokyena prasaṅgāc ca saṃsargo naikakālatā |                    na cāpy ārjavataḥ sthānaṃ jñāne nārthasya vidyate ||
  44. 5,4.44sarvathā kalpanāyāṃ ca cakṣuṣāpi rasādayaḥ |                    gṛhyeran sarvabhāvānāmaṇvākārāś ca tadgatāḥ ||
  45. 5,4.45na cāpi viṣayatvena sthāne saṃsargakalpanā |                    viṣayatvaṃ hi kīdṛk syāt prāgākāropalambhanāt ||<201>
  46. 5,4.46na hy asañcetito bhāvo viṣayatvena kalpyate |                    viṣayatvāt tadākāra ākārād viṣayaś ca saḥ ||
  47. 5,4.47dvayor ākāranirmuktaṃ sattvaṃ saṃsṛṣṭatā tathā |                    svarūpataḥ paricchidya vaktum ityādi yujyate ||
  48. 5,4.48na cāpy asyeha sadbhāvaḥ prāg gṛhīto na copari |                    na hy ākāravinirmuktaṃ grāhyam astīti bhāṣitam ||
  49. 5,4.49tasmād arthena saṃsargo niṣpramāṇaka eva te |                    jñānavaicitryasiddhyarthaṃ na cāstyarthasya kalpanā ||
  50. 5,4.50tadadhīnaṃ hi vaicitryaṃ kva dṛṣṭaṃ yena kalpyate |                    nirākāreṇa cotpattir vaicitryākārayoḥ katham ||<202>
  51. 5,4.51nirākārāc ca viṣayād buddhyākāro 'tivismayaḥ |                    smṛtisvapnādibodhe ca syād anākāratā tava ||
  52. 5,4.52na hi tatrārthasaṃsargaḥ kevalā vāsanaiva tu |                    hetutvenopapanneti saiva jāgraddhiyām api ||
  53. 5,4.53anvayavyatirekābhyām evaṃ jñānasya gamyate |                    na hi bāhyasya jñānāpeto nidarśyate ||
  54. 5,4.54bāhyāpeto mayā yadvat, <203> tasmāt saṃsargavāgiyam |                    nirākāre 'pi vijñāne vāsanāsv eva yujyate ||
  55. 5,4.55dvayor apy eka ākāra ityetasyāpramāṇatā |                    deśabhedād asaṃsargaḥ, dvayoś cānavadhāraṇāt ||
  56. 5,4.56evam evārthabuddhyoḥ syāt sādṛśyān nāvibhaktatā |                    bhede jñāte hi sādṛśyaṃ nājñāte syāt khapuṣpavat ||
  57. 5,4.57tathā dvicandramāyādāv anyathārthe vyavasthite |                    yā syād ākārasaṃvittir nāsāv arthanibandhanā ||
  58. 5,4.58nakṣatraṃ tārakā tiṣyo dārā ityevamādiṣu |                    naikatrārthe viruddhatvāl liṅgānekatvasambhavaḥ ||<204>
  59. 5,4.59parivrāṭkāmukaśunāṃ kuṇapādimatis tathā |                    dīrghahrasvatvabuddhiś ca hy ekasminn apy apekṣayā ||
  60. 5,4.60ghaṭatvāt pārthavadravyaprameyādimatis tathā |                    yugapadgrāhakāṇāṃ ca na syād aikātmyavattayā ||
  61. 5,4.61nārthe hy ekatra yugapad viruddhākārasambhavaḥ |                    pratyayānāṃ tu bhinnatvād bhavec chaktyanusārataḥ ||
  62. 5,4.62nirapekṣaṃ svarūpeṇa tasmāj jñānaṃ yadākṛti |                    tathārtho na yathārthaṃ tu jñānam utpadyate kva cit ||
  63. 5,4.63itthaṃ vijñānatantratve ko nv arthaṃ kalpayiṣyati |                    dhīranāropitākārā svātmany evopayokṣyate ||<205>
  64. 5,4.64naitad asti, tvayaikaṃ hi grāhyaṃ grāhakam iṣyate |                    na caikasyaivam ātmatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ kaścid asti te ||
  65. 5,4.65agnyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ prasiddhā ye prakāśakāḥ |                    na te prakāśyarūpā hi prakāśasya, anapekṣaṇāt ||
  66. 5,4.66grāhyatvaṃ tu yadā teṣāṃ tadākṣaṃ grāhakaṃ matam |                    akṣagrahaṇakāle tu grāhikā dhīr bhaviṣyati ||
  67. 5,4.67tasyāṃ tu gṛhyamāṇāyām anyā dhīr grāhikeṣyate |<206>                    nanv ātmā grāhako grāhyo bhavatābhyupagamyate ||
  68. 5,4.68kathañcid dharmarūpeṇa bhinnatvāt pratyayasya tat |                    grāhakatvaṃ bhavet tatra grāhyaṃ dravyādi cātmanaḥ ||
  69. 5,4.69yas tu nātyantabhedo 'tra kva vāsāv iṣyate mayā |                    pratyāsattinimittā tu pratyagātmapravarttitā ||
  70. 5,4.70asmatprayogasambhinnā jñānasyaiva tu kartari |                    bhavantī tatra saṃvittir yujyetāpy ātmakartṛkā ||
  71. 5,4.71na cātra karaṇajñānagrāhakākāravedanam |                    grāhyatvaṃ yena buddheḥ syād abhinnatve 'pi pūrvavat ||<207>
  72. 5,4.72anyarūpāpi saṃvittir yady anyaviṣayeṣyate |                    jñānākārāpi saṃvittiḥ kasmān nārthasya kalpyate ||
  73. 5,4.73abhinnatvaṃ yadā ceṣṭaṃ grāhyagrāhakavastunoḥ |                    tadānyatarasaṃvittau dvyākāraṃ grahaṇaṃ bhavet ||
  74. 5,4.74yadā tu grāhyam ākāraṃ nīlādi pratipadyate |                    na tadā grāhakākārā saṃvittir dṛśyate kva cit ||
  75. 5,4.75tasmād abhinnatā cet syāt tasyāpy anubhavo bhavet |                    grāhyo vā nānubhūyeta grāhakānanubhūtivat ||
  76. 5,4.76grāhakagrahaṇe 'py evaṃ grāhyasaṃvedanaṃ bhavet |                    śuddham eva nirākāraṃ grāhakaṃ saṃvidasti hi ||
  77. 5,4.77grāhyād abhinnatāyā ca sā saṃvittir na yujyate |                    grāhako vā na gṛhyeta tadgrāhyānanubhūtivat ||
  78. 5,4.78yathāvad grāhyasaṃvittau grāhakagrahaṇe 'pi vā |                    grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittir nāsty eva syād dvayor api ||<208>
  79. 5,4.79sa bahirdeśasambaddhaḥ ity anena nirūpyate |                    grāhyākārasya saṃvittir grāhakānubhavād ṛte ||
  80. 5,4.80paraṃ prati hi sādhyatvad arthasyākārasiddhaye |                    bahirdeśena sambandho na hetutvāya kalpate ||
  81. 5,4.81tasmād bahir itīhedaṃ niṣkṛṣṭaṃ grāhakāṃśataḥ |                    saṃvedyaṃ nīlapītādi pratyakṣāder udāhṛtam ||
  82. 5,4.82na pūrvaṃ jñāyate buddhir ityatraitad vadiṣyate |                    grāhakasyaiva saṃvittir lakṣyate grahaṇe kva cit ||
  83. 5,4.83na smarāmi mayā ko 'pi gṛhīto 'rthas tadeti hi |                    smaranti grāhakotpādagrāhyarūpavivarjitam ||
  84. 5,4.84tasmād abhinnatāyāṃ ca grāhye 'pi smaraṇaṃ bhavet |                    grāhakasmṛtinirbhāsāt tatrāpy eṣaiva gṛhyate ||
  85. 5,4.85tadatyantāvinābhāvān naikākāraṃ hi jāyate |<209>                    anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ siddhaivaṃ bhinnatā tayoḥ ||
  86. 5,4.86grāhyāṃśo grāhakāṃśena gṛhyate, grāhakaḥ punaḥ |                    gṛhyeteti na vaktavyam, grāhakāntaravarjanāt ||
  87. 5,4.87grāhyāṃśenāpy aśaktatvān na tasya grahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    grāhakatvena caitasya hīyetaiva dvirūpatā ||
  88. 5,4.88grāhake gṛhyamāṇe ca grāhyamātraprasañjanam |                    na syād ākāra ekaś ced itarasyāpi nāstitā ||
  89. 5,4.89udbhavābhibhavābhyāṃ ca grāhyāgrāhyatvadarśanam |                    yathā dīpaprabhādīnāṃ rūpamātropalambhanam ||
  90. 5,4.90divā cāgneḥ samīpasthaiḥ sparśa evopalabhyate |                    gandhavad dravyavṛttau ca gandhasyaivopalambhanam ||
  91. 5,4.91na guṇāntarasaṃvittir yathātrābhibhavāt, tathā |                    nākārāntarasaṃvittir grāhyagrāhakabuddhiṣu ||<210>
  92. 5,4.92grāhyād ananyabhūto 'pi kaś cin naivopalabhyate |                    nityānityādayo dharmāḥ śabdādigrahaṇe yathā ||
  93. 5,4.93abhedaṃ vābhyupetyāyaṃ prasaṅgo yadi gīyate |                    ekasmin gṛhyamāṇe 'śe na gṛhyetāparaḥ katham ||
  94. 5,4.94tasmād yat syād yadā yogyaṃ tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ tadā |                    dvayaṃ ca tvadupanyastaṃ śaktyabhāvān na gṛhyate ||
  95. 5,4.95kuto 'yam ekavastutve yogyāyogyatvasambhavaḥ |                    udbhavābhibhavātmatvaṃ kathaṃ caikasya kalpitam ||
  96. 5,4.96ekāṃśābhibhave ca syād itarābhibhavo 'pi te |                    tathā tasyābhibhūtatvād grāhyatvaṃ na ca yujyate ||
  97. 5,4.97ayogyatā vikalpyaivam, dṛṣṭāntā ye 'tra kīrtitāḥ |                    rūpādibhedāt tatra syād udbhavābhibhavādyapi ||
  98. 5,4.98yadāpy ekāntato bhedo rūpāder na parasparam |                    tadāpi dravyarūpasya pariṇāmas tathā tathā ||<211>
  99. 5,4.99abhinnatve 'pi na grāhyam iti yac cābravīd bhavān |                    kṛtakatvādidharmāṇāṃ dhībhede 'nanyatā katham ||
  100. 5,4.100na hy anyatpratyayād asti bhinnād grāhyasya bhedakam |                    na ceyattaiva bhedasya deśato mūrtito 'pi vā ||
  101. 5,4.101kāraṇānāṃ hi sambandhaḥ kāryaiḥ kṛtakocyate |                    vibhāgo 'vayavānāṃ ca bhavet kva cid anityatā ||
  102. 5,4.102buddhyāder ātmarūpādisthānaṃ nāśitvam ucyate |                    nityatvaṃ sarvadā sattā, vastutvaṃ saiva kīrtyate ||
  103. 5,4.103pramāṇajñānasambandhaḥ prameyajñeyatocyate |<212>                    sarvatra cātra bhinnatvam asti kena cid ātmanā ||
  104. 5,4.104tasmād yathaiva rūpāder deśabhedādibhir vinā |                    buddhibhedena bhedo 'sti tathaivātra pratīyatām ||
  105. 5,4.105atyantabhinnatāsmābhir naiva kasya cid iṣyate |                    sarvaṃ hi vasturūpeṇa bhidyate na parasparam ||
  106. 5,4.106sarvaṃ ca kṛtakatvādi kriyāhetvādyapekṣayā |                    gṛhyate tadasaṃvittāvabhede 'pi na gṛhyate ||
  107. 5,4.107jñāne naivaṃvidho bhedo nāpekṣānyatra vidyate |                    paraspareṇa cāpekṣā syāc cet, sannihitaś ca saḥ ||
  108. 5,4.108nanu grāhakam ityevaṃ grāhyam ity api vā matiḥ |                    nīlādigrahaṇe nāstīty apekṣā katham ucyate ||<213>
  109. 5,4.109mā bhūd evaṃ tathāpy atra dvyākāre grahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    evaṃ cāgṛhyamāṇe vā jñāne dvyākāratā katham ||
  110. 5,4.110uttarottaravijñānaviśeṣād yā prakalpyate |                    grāhakākārasaṃvittiḥ smaraṇāc cānumānikī ||
  111. 5,4.111ekākāraṃ kila jñānaṃ prathamaṃ yadi kalpyate |                    tatas tadviṣayāpy anyā tadrūpaiva matir bhavet ||
  112. 5,4.112ghaṭavijñānatajjñānaviśeṣo 'to na sidhyati |                    grāhakākārasaṃvittau tv ākārapracayo bhavet ||
  113. 5,4.113jāyate pūrvavijñānaṃ dvyākāraṃ yatra tat punaḥ |                    tasyātmīyaś ca pūrvau ca viṣayasthāvupaplutau ||<214>
  114. 5,4.114preṣv ākāravṛddhyaivaṃ pūrvebhyo bhinnatā, tathā |                    grāhyavat smaraṇāt paścāt saṃvittau grāhakaḥ purā ||
  115. 5,4.115na tāvad evamākārān paśyāmaḥ pracayānvitān |                    viṣayavyapadeśāc ca narte jñānanirūpaṇam ||
  116. 5,4.116tasmāj jñānātmanaikatve grāhyabhedanibandhaḥ |                    saṃvittibhedaḥ siddho 'tra kimākārāntareṇa naḥ ||
  117. 5,4.117nirākāratasāmye 'pi yathākāravatāṃ dhruvam |                    bhedaḥ svābhāvikas tadvajjñānānāṃ kiṃ na sidhyati ||<215>
  118. 5,4.118smṛter uttarakālaṃ cetyetanmithyaiva gīyate |                    tadaiva hy asya saṃvittir arthāpattyopajāyate ||
  119. 5,4.119gṛhītam eva yac coktaṃ tadabhedāt, na tad, yataḥ |                    nāsmabhir vākyavṛttes tvaṃ nimittam anuyujyase ||
  120. 5,4.120grāhyagrāhakataivāsya kena cin nopalabhyate |                    pratyakṣajñānapakṣe ca naiṣā syād ānumānikī ||
  121. 5,4.121ekākāre ca vijñāne yady anyo 'py atra kalpyate |                    sahasrākārataikasya kasmān na parikalpyate ||
  122. 5,4.122grāhyagrāhakayor bhedo nanv asty eva parasparam |                    siddho naḥ pakṣa evaṃ syāt, <216> na, jñānatvād abhedataḥ ||
  123. 5,4.123bhinnābhinnatvam ekasya kuto 'tra parikalpitam |                    tvayā sāṃkhyamatenaivam uktvā buddhasya śāsanam ||
  124. 5,4.124ekaṃ ced grāhakaṃ grāhyaṃ kuto bhinnatvavāgiyam |                    bhinnaṃ cet katham ucyeta tasyaikatvaṃ punas tvayā ||
  125. 5,4.125ekajñānād ananyatvād grāhyagrāhakayor mithaḥ |                    ekatvena bhavej jñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grākam eva vā ||
  126. 5,4.126tatra cānyatarāpāye dvitīyāpāyataḥ punaḥ |                    jñānasyāṃśadvayāsattvān naiḥsvābhāvyād abhāvatā ||
  127. 5,4.127bhinnābhyāṃ vāpy abhinnatvād bhedo jñānātmano bhavet |                    tatsvātmanaḥ, tataś caivaṃ siddhaṃ vastudvayaṃ hi naḥ ||
  128. 5,4.128tayoś ca yadi saṃjñeyaṃ jñānam ity astv arthāpi vā |                    jñānaṃ jñāyata ityartho dhīrbhāve karaṇe 'pi vā ||
  129. 5,4.129sarvathā vastubhedo naḥ siddhaḥ śabdo yathāruci |                    pravartatāṃ na nas tatra kācid vipratipannatā ||<217>
  130. 5,4.130atha saty api bhinnatve grāhyaṃ jñānāntaraṃ bhavet |                    jñānatve tasya kā yuktiḥ, pūrvoktā yadi seṣyate ||
  131. 5,4.131jñānaṃ jñānam itīdaṃ tu na dvayor anuvartate |                    vyatiriktaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ tvayā nābhyupagamyate ||
  132. 5,4.132vyatireke tayor jñānān na jñānātmakatā bhavet |                    tadrūparahitatve ca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate ||
  133. 5,4.133tābhyāṃ ca tasya sambandhe pratyekaṃ vyatiṣajya ca |                    bhedasāvayavatvādi doṣo vaiśeṣikādivat ||
  134. 5,4.134yathā hi teṣāṃ jātyādau doṣā hy uktāḥ parair amī |                    tathaivaiṣāṃ prasajyante bhinnābhinnārthasaṅgatau ||
  135. 5,4.135tābhyām avyatireke vā bhedaḥ pūrvokta eva te |<218>                    sādṛśyāpohasāmānyakalpanā vārayiṣyate ||
  136. 5,4.136vastvantarasya cābhāvāt tvayāpoho 'pi duṣkaraḥ |                    nājñānaṃ nāma kiñ cit syād apohyaṃ jñānavādinaḥ ||
  137. 5,4.137apoho na hy abhāvasya kathañ cid upapadyate |                    vastvantaram abhāvaḥ syād, apohyatvāc ca vastutā ||
  138. 5,4.138tenājñānanivṛttau hi jñāne 'nyārtha prasajyate |                    kalpitaṃ syād apohyaṃ cet, nātyantāsatyakalpanā ||
  139. 5,4.139buddhir ajñānanirbhāsā tavājñānaṃ prakalitam |                    tataś ca jñānam evaikam apohyatvena sammatam ||<219>
  140. 5,4.140na cātmāpoha evāsti kva cit sāmānyakalpane |                    vṛkṣasya na hy apohyatvaṃ vṛkṣeṇaiva kadā cana ||
  141. 5,4.141apohye caiva vijñāne jñānatvaṃ na bhavet tava |                    vṛkṣatvaṃ na hy apohyeṣu kalaśādiṣu yujyate ||
  142. 5,4.142tataś cājñānam evārtha ity abhinnārthatā bhavet |                    ajñānapratyayaś cāyaṃ kimālambana iṣyate ||
  143. 5,4.143na tāvaj jñānanirmuktam ajñānaṃ grāhyam asti te |                    na ca vastu niṣiddhaṃ tadabhāvaḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate ||
  144. 5,4.144bhāvo na gṛhyate yena tasyābhāveṣu kā kathā |                    svāṃśaparyavasānaṃ ca tulyam atrāpi kāraṇam ||
  145. 5,4.145tena jñānāntaraṃ vā syād grāhyam ātmāṃśa eva vā |                    svarūpaviparītaṃ ca kathaṃ grāhyaṃ pratīyate ||<220>
  146. 5,4.146yathoṣṇe 'nuṣṇadhīr nāsti, jñāne 'py ajñānadhīs tathā |                    tena na jñānamātratve syād apohyaṃ kathañ cana ||
  147. 5,4.147grāhyagrāhakayoś cāto na jñānātmasamānatā |                    tasmād anyataratredaṃ jñānatvaṃ sampratīyate ||
  148. 5,4.148tatrāpy ubhayasiddhatvād grāhakasyeti gamyate |                    vastubhede prasiddhe ca vyapadeśo yathāruci ||
  149. 5,4.149jñānam astūbhayaṃ vārtho grāhako vārtha ucyatām |                    buddhyor ayugapadbhāvān na dvayor mayamānatā ||
  150. 5,4.150kṣaṇikā hītyanenoktam, <221> artho hy ekaḥ prasajyate |                    anyonyanirapekṣatvād yugapac cāpi janmani ||
  151. 5,4.151mānameyatvāstitvam, kriyākārakavarjanāt |                    arthavijñānayor atra yā mitiṃ prati saṅgatiḥ ||
  152. 5,4.152kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'yam, nānyatraivaṃ ca dṛśyate |                    niyamaś ca na labhyeta savyadakṣiṇaśṛṅgavat ||
  153. 5,4.153idaṃ kāryam ayaṃ hetuḥ, dvayaṃ na, <222> anyonyasaṃśrayāt |                    tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ hetuḥ kair naiva varṇyate ||
  154. 5,4.154paurvāparyavinirmuktaṃ kāryakāraṇalakṣaṇam |                    gavāśvasya yathā nāsti paurvāparye 'pi tat tathā ||
  155. 5,4.155yugapajjāyamāne 'pi santatyantaraje kṣaṇe |                    rūpādiṣu ghaṭe yadvat, tasmāt pūrvam avasthite ||
  156. 5,4.156yo yasmāj jāyate paścāt sa tatkāryam itīṣyate |                    hetuhetumatāṃ siddhaṃ yaugapadyanidarśanam ||
  157. 5,4.157yat pradīpaprabhādyuktaṃ sūkṣamaḥ kālo 'sti tatra naḥ |                    durlakṣas tu yathā vedhaḥ padmapattraśate tathā ||
  158. 5,4.158bhāgayor yaugapadyena tathaiva syān nirākriyā |<223>                    na ca śaktyarpaṇadvāraṃ krameṇālambanaṃ bhavet ||
  159. 5,4.159grāhyaṃ tadā hy atītaṃ syāt, tadrūpyaṃ cāpramāṇakam |                    atītvānuviddho hi smṛtyā grāhyo 'nubhūyate ||
  160. 5,4.160tadvad eva bhaved atra, svapne na syāt, viparyayāt |                    tatra hy avartamāno 'pi gṛhyate vartamānavat ||
  161. 5,4.161bādhajñānād idaṃ bhrāntam, na tv atraivaṃ viparyayaḥ |                    tasmāt pratyakṣabuddhīnāṃ nātito viṣayo bhavet ||
  162. 5,4.162atītatvād yathaivāsāṃ vṛtto janmāntareṣu yaḥ |                    tadrūpatvena vā jñānaṃ hetur bhāvivad ucyate ||<224>
  163. 5,4.163atītatve 'pi nārtho 'yaṃ dhr eṣety atra kā pramā |                    atītaṃ yac ca vijñānaṃ grāhyatvena prakalpitam ||
  164. 5,4.164tasmād grāhakarūpaṃ vā grāhyaṃ vobhayathāpi vā |                    grāhyākāratvamātre syād arthaḥ śabdāntareṇa te ||
  165. 5,4.165svakāle cāpy asaṃvitter na syāc chaktyarpaṇaṃ tataḥ |                    yathaivānāgatāj jñānāt santatyantarajād api ||
  166. 5,4.166dṛḍhatvenāpy avijñātāt tathotpannād vinaśyataḥ |                    kevalagrāhakatve tu viṣayatvaṃ na yujyate ||
  167. 5,4.167kimapekṣya ca tasyedaṃ grāhakatvaṃ prakalpyate |                    dvyākāratā nirastaiva, <225> saṃvedyeta tadaiva ca ||
  168. 5,4.168tataś cottaravijñānaṃ na pratīkṣeta bodhakam |                    dvyākārakalpanāyāṃ ca parasyātmāṃśa eva te ||
  169. 5,4.169pramāparyavasānena nātīto viṣayo bhavet |                    pūrvagrāhyasarūpatve grāhakatvaṃ prahīyate ||
  170. 5,4.170grāhakākāramātre syād viṣayo nāsarūpataḥ |                    na ca śaktyarpaṇasyātra vyāpāra upalabhyate ||
  171. 5,4.171śaktyarpaṇasya cābhāvo yuṣmatpakṣe prasādhitaḥ |                    santānāntaravac caiṣāṃ niṣedhyā hetusādhyatā ||
  172. 5,4.172vāsyavāsakabhāvaś ca jñānatvād ekasantatau |                    tasmād yadbhāsakaṃ rūpaṃ tadgrāhyāt tasya bhinnatā ||
  173. 5,4.173tatsaṃvittāv asaṃvitte rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |                    grāhyaṃ tadgrāhakāc caiva tatparāmṛśatā yataḥ ||
  174. 5,4.174na parāmṛśyate 'vaśyaṃ rasādigrāhakaṃ yathā |<226>                    dvayaṃ paraspareṇaivaṃ bhinnaṃ sādhyaṃ rasādivat ||
  175. 5,4.175aikarūpyeṇa cājñānāt santānāntarabuddhivat |                    jñānaṃ svāṃśaṃ na gṛhṇāti jñānotpatteḥ svaśaktivat ||
  176. 5,4.176grāhyatvapratiṣedhaś ca dvayahīnā hi vāsate |                    caitrajñānaṃ tadudbhūtajñānāṃśagrāhyabodhakam ||
  177. 5,4.177jñānatvān na bhaved yadvat tasya dehāntarodbhavam |                    etayaiva diśā vācyā śaktidvayanirākriyā ||
  178. 5,4.178pramāṇāntarasiddhatvād anyatrānekaśaktitā |                    na tv atra kāraṇaṃ tādṛk śaktibhedakṛdasti te ||<227>
  179. 5,4.179tasmād ubhayasiddhatvāl lāghavād yaḥ parigrahaḥ |                    upāyatvāc ca yat tasya pūrvagrahaṇakalpanam ||
  180. 5,4.180cakṣuradīndriyair atra tadanaikāntikaṃ bhavet |                    yad apy apratibaddhatvād utpattau gṛhyatām iti ||
  181. 5,4.181tatrātmanā na śaktyaṃ tannānyotpattis tadasti vā |                    tenaitat kāraṇābhāvāt tadānīṃ nānubhūyate ||
  182. 5,4.182nānyathā hy arthasadbhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ sannupapadyate |                    jñānaṃ cen netyataḥ paścāt pramāṇam upajāyate ||<228>
  183. 5,4.183na cāpy apratibandhena kevalena graho bhavet |                    viśiṣṭakāraṇābhāve 'py artho naivānubhūyate ||
  184. 5,4.184vyāpṛtaṃ cārthasaṃvittau jñānaṃ nātmānamṛcchati |<229>                    tena prakāśakatve 'pi bodhāyānyat pratīkṣyate ||
  185. 5,4.185īdṛśaṃ vā prakāśatvaṃ tasyārthānubhavātmakam |                    na cātmānubhavo 'sty asyetyātmano na prakāśakam ||
  186. 5,4.186sati prakāśakatve ca vyavasthā dṛśyate yathā |                    rūpādau cakṣurādīnāṃ tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
  187. 5,4.187prakāśakatvaṃ bāhye 'rthe śaktyabhāvāt tu nātmani |                    anyena vānubhāve 'sāv anavasthā prasajyate ||
  188. 5,4.188tatra tatra smṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvānubhavakalpanā |                    ekena tv anubhūtatve sarvaṃ tatraiva sambhavet ||
  189. 5,4.189tatrāpi smṛtir ity etan na lokānumataṃ vacaḥ |                    na hi vijñānasantānaṃ kaś cit smarati laukikaḥ ||<230>
  190. 5,4.190ghaṭādāv agṛhīte 'rthe yadi tāvad anantaram |                    arthāpattyāv abudhyante vijñānāni punaḥ punaḥ ||
  191. 5,4.191yāvacchramaṃ tataḥ paścāt tāvatyeva smariṣyati |                    tadā tv akalpite 'py evaṃ smṛtivarndhyāsutādivat ||
  192. 5,4.192smṛtibhrāntaś ca yāpy atra paścāj jñāneṣu jāyate |                    tadaivārthasmṛter eṣāṃ tajñānādipramāṇatā ||
  193. 5,4.193yāvacchramaṃ ca tadbuddhis tatprabandhe mahaty api |                    śramād rucyānyasamparkād vicchedo viṣayeṣv iva ||<231>
  194. 5,4.194tatrāpi smṛtir ity eṣāṃ prathame pratyaye yadi |                    tanmātragrahaṇād evaṃ nānavasthā prasajyate ||
  195. 5,4.195smaraṇaṃ tv atha sarveṣu tatsiddhyai grahaṇaṃ tathā |                    pramāṇavattvād āyātaḥ pravāhaḥ kena vāryate ||
  196. 5,4.196atha tānyādyavijñānaviṣayāṇīti kalpyate |                    nottarottarabuddhīnāṃ viśeṣa upapadyate ||
  197. 5,4.197vijñānaviṣayatvaṃ ca yasya sarvāsu buddhiṣu |                    ghaṭavijñāna tajñānaviśeṣas tena durlabhaḥ ||
  198. 5,4.198smaran yathaiva vijñānaṃ nirākāraṃ smaratyayam |                    tathā smaran gṛhītārthaṃ nirākāratayā smaret ||
  199. 5,4.199jñānapṛṣṭena yo 'py ūrdhvaṃ parāmarśo bhavaty asau |                    tasyārtheṣv abhyupāyatvān na tu grāhyatvakāritaḥ ||<232>
  200. 5,4.200pratyāsannatvasambandhau grāhyatvāsambhavāc cyutau |                    viṣayatvena vāpy etau staḥ kiṃ deśāvibhāgataḥ ||
  201. 5,4.201arthākārasya yo 'py ukto mithyājñāneṣv asambhavaḥ |                    dośakālānyathāmātrasambhavaḥ keṣu cit kṛtaḥ ||
  202. 5,4.202pratyakṣād anyavijñānam atītānāgatair api |                    janyate 'rthe bhavantīṣu vāsanāsvasatīṣu vā ||
  203. 5,4.203yaḥ punar nānubhūto 'rtho na vāpy anubhaviṣyate |                    vāsanābhāvatas tatra tavāpy anubhavaḥ katham ||<233>
  204. 5,4.204vināpi vāsanātaś ced buddhir utpadyate tataḥ |                    vāsanāyā nimittatvam abhyupetaṃ virudhyate ||
  205. 5,4.205vāsanā ced bhavet tatra sā ca saṃvittipūrvikā |                    tathā sati ca pūrvatra gṛhītaḥ kvāpy asau dhruvam ||
  206. 5,4.206evaṃ ca naiva vaktavyam atyantābhavanaṃ kva cit |                    anyathānupapatyā hi siddhā janmāntare 'stitā ||
  207. 5,4.207duṣṭatvena ca vijñānam anyathāpi vyavasthitam |                    pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhṇīyād ākāraṃ tannibandhanam ||
  208. 5,4.208tānyapāsya tu naivārthe kva cid ākārakalpanā |                    na jñānaṃ hy anavaṣṭambham ātmānaṃ labdhum arhati ||<234>
  209. 5,4.209vijñānasyaiva vā kāryaṃ yady eṣo 'nye ca kalpitāḥ |                    viśeṣaḥ ko 'tra yenāyam atyantāsannitīṣyate ||
  210. 5,4.210tasmād bhrāntir api tv eṣāṃ kalpayantyartham eva naḥ |                    kalpayatyanyathā santaṃ na tv ātmānaṃ vyavasyati ||
  211. 5,4.211tataś ca bādhakajñānād vācoyuktir iyaṃ bhavet |                    arthe 'nyathāpi saty eṣa dhiyākāraḥ pratīyate ||
  212. 5,4.212dvicandrādimatiṣv evam, tārakādimatau tathā |                    strītvādyanyatra dṛṣṭaṃ syāt, kathañ cid veha sambhavet ||<235>
  213. 5,4.213śabdamātrapratīyā vā, dṛṣṭair vā kaiś cid iṅganāt |                    saṃstyānaprasavasthānair yathā pātañjale mate ||
  214. 5,4.214tena liṅgatrayasyātra sadbhāvaḥ syāt pramāṇavān |                    apekṣābhedataś cātra virodho 'pi na vidyate ||
  215. 5,4.215kuṇapādimatau caivaṃ sārvarūpye vyavasthite |                    vāsanāḥ sahakāriṇyo vyavasthākāradarśane ||<236>
  216. 5,4.216svapratyayānukāro hi bahvākāreṣu vastuṣu |                    nirdhāraṇe bhaved dhetur nāpūrvākārakalpane ||
  217. 5,4.217tathā dīrghaghaṭatvādau bhinnāpekṣānibandhanā |                    ākārabhedasampattir aviruddhā bhaviṣyati ||
  218. 5,4.218nānekākārasaṃvitter nirākāratvakalpanā |                    yuktā, pratītibhedāt tu bahvākāratvasambhavaḥ ||
  219. 5,4.219saṃvitteś ca viruddhānām ekasminn api sambhavaḥ |                    ekākāraṃ bhaved ekam iti neśvarabhāṣitam ||
  220. 5,4.220tathaiva tadupetavyaṃ yad yathaivopalabhyate |                    na cāpy aikāntikaṃ tasya syād ekatvaṃ ca vastunaḥ ||<237>
  221. 5,4.221tasmād deśādisadbhāvanimittaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pṛthak |                    vastvākārāḥ pratīyerann udbhavābhibhavātmakāḥ ||
  222. 5,4.222yugapadgrāhāṇāṃ ca yo yadākāravācinam |                    śabdaṃ smarati tenāsāv ākāraḥ sampratīyate ||
  223. 5,4.223nityaṃ satsu tathā loke rūpādiṣu ghaṭe pṛthak |                    cakṣurādyanurodhena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
  224. 5,4.224evam eva ghaṭatvādau sarvān prati bhavaty api |                    vācakasmṛtibhedena saṃvittir vyavatiṣṭhate ||
  225. 5,4.225tasmād bahiḥ sthito 'py ātmā narāṇāṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ |                    prāpya vāprāpya vā buddher viṣayatvena kalpyate ||
  226. 5,4.226vadanti laukikā yac ca yādṛg jñānaṃ tathā bahiḥ |                    te punar jñānasaṃvittyā tathārthaṃ prati jānate ||<238>
  227. 5,4.227grāhakatvena vijñānaṃ yathārthaṃ naḥ samarpayet |                    tādṛgarthaḥ sa ityevaṃ teṣāṃ vā tadupāyataḥ ||
  228. 5,4.228laiṅgikāsattvam aprāptair etair bāhyārthavādibhiḥ |                    jñānānubhavam utkramya bāhya eva pratīyate ||
  229. 5,4.229yathā loke ca tadbuddhir vācyam evaṃ parīkṣakaiḥ |                    na yādṛgantarākāras tādṛg bāhyo 'vakalpate ||
  230. 5,4.230utpadyamānā gṛhyeta dhīrarthagrahaṇe yadi |                    pūrvapakṣasya kiṃ siddham, kathaṃ cārthāntaraṃ vadet ||
  231. 5,4.231bāhyārthavādinaṃ brūte bhavān kiṃ naivam icchati |                    pratibandho na tasyāsti gṛhṇātyarthāntaraṃ yadā ||<239>
  232. 5,4.232uttaraṃ grahakābhāvāl liṅgābhāvāc ca nāsti naḥ |                    tadā grahaṇam ity etat, anyatarkeṣu cocyate ||
  233. 5,4.233teṣu tarkeṣu vijñānam arthakāle 'vagamyate |                    tathā satyarthanāśaḥ syād ity etadupadiśyate ||
  234. 5,4.234nanv ity etadasambaddhaṃ pareṣṭasyaiva codanāt |<240>                    paurvāpryavibhāgo 'pi prāguktena virudhyate ||
  235. 5,4.235kṣaṇikatvena yuktaṃ syāj jñātatvam atha cet tadā |                    bhūtakālāśrayād brūyād, pṛthoktasya punarvacaḥ ||
  236. 5,4.236atrāpi na svasiddhāntamūce vyājāt parasya tu |                    bhrāntatvād anyathā pakṣaṃ gṛhītveti sma pṛcchati ||
  237. 5,4.237sahotpattyupalabdhā hi jñānasyaikāntataḥ sthitiḥ |                    prāgūrdhvaṃ vārthasaṃvitter yugapad veti cintyate ||
  238. 5,4.238evaṃ cārthasya saṃvitteḥ paścāj jñānāvabodhanam |                    bravītu nūnam etasya paścād utpadyate 'pi tat ||
  239. 5,4.239na caitac chaktyate tasmād utpatter apakarṣaṇam |                    karomi tāvat tatkālā saṃvittir api setsyati ||<241>
  240. 5,4.240prāk ca tadgrahaṇe siddhe bāhyābhyantarayor dhruvam |                    vivekādarśanam, tasmād idam, pūrvaṃ ca coditam ||
  241. 5,4.241yugapad gṛhyamāṇe 'pi nākāro 'rthasya lakṣyate |                    tasmād arthasya saṃvittiḥ pūrvaṃ yatnena sādhyate ||
  242. 5,4.242yas tv etasyottaro granthaḥ prāg evāsau nirūpitaḥ |                    na tv etat sādhanaṃ sākṣāt pūrvaṃ buddher abodhane ||
  243. 5,4.243na parāmṛśyate 'rthātmā jñāto 'py ajñātavad yataḥ |                    tasān na grahaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ buddheḥ kiṃ kena saṅgatam ||<242>
  244. 5,4.244ataḥ pūrvopalabdhyā yo buddhyākāro 'tra vāñchitaḥ |                    tannirākaraṇenaiva phalatvād granthavarṇanā ||
  245. 5,4.245kāmaṃ buddher iti tv etadarthādhīnatvam ucyate |                    na cārtharūpād bhedena dhiyām asti nirūpaṇam ||
  246. 5,4.246pararūpanirūpyaṃ ca na meyaṃ mṛgatoyavat |                    asadgrāhyānusāreṇa jñānasaṃvedyatā tava ||
  247. 5,4.247svacchatvāt tu svarūpasya kalpitā grāhyatā dhiyām |                    vāsanopaplavāt tena na meyaṃ pāramārthikam ||<243>
  248. 5,4.248nimittaniyatatvaṃ tu samānam ubhayor api |                    nijaśaktyanusāritvāj jñānabāhyārthavādinoḥ ||
  249. 5,4.249tantvarthair api kasmād vaḥ kriyate kevalaḥ paṭaḥ |                    nārabhyate ghaṭaḥ kiṃ tair mṛtpiṇḍārthena vā paṭaḥ ||
  250. 5,4.250tantumṛtpiṇḍavijñāne hy anuyojye mate yadi |                    arthaparyanuyogo 'pi tadvad eva prasajyate ||
  251. 5,4.251arthārambhavyavasthā cet sāmarthyaniyamāśrayā |                    jñānārambhavyavasthāyāṃ sāmarthyaṃ kena vāryate ||
  252. 5,4.252tasmād yatrobhayor doṣaḥ parihāro 'pi vā samaḥ |                    naikaḥ paryanuyoktavyas tādṛgarthavicāraṇe ||
  253. 5,4.253deśakālanimittāni vyañjakānyarthavādinaḥ |                    śaktīnāṃ kāraṇasthānāṃ svakāryaniyamaṃ prati ||
  254. 5,4.254śaktayo 'pi ca bhāvānāṃ kāryārthāpattikalpitāḥ |                    prasiddhāḥ pāramārthikyaḥ pratikāryaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
  255. 5,4.255bhavatas tu na vijñānād bhinnābhinnā nirūpyate |                    śaktiḥ saṃvṛtisadbhāvam utsṛjya paramārthataḥ ||<244>
  256. 5,4.256vāsanaiva ca yuṣmābhiḥ śaktiśabdena gīyate |                    nimittaniyatatvaṃ ca vāsanāyā yad ucyate ||
  257. 5,4.257tasyāś cāsambhavenaitad apārārthyāc ca durlabham |                    deśakālanimittādi na ca te 'sti niyāmakam ||
  258. 5,4.258matvaitad api cety āha bhāṣyakāraḥ paraṃ prati |                    tasmād aparihāro 'yaṃ tantubhyas te yathā paṭaḥ ||
  259. 5,4.259tathā me tantubuddhibhyaḥ paṭabuddhir itīdṛśaḥ |                    evamādyapramāṇābhyāṃ na tāvad bāhyaśūnyatā ||
  260. 5,4.260āgamasya tu naiveha vyāpāraḥ, ato 'nyathāpi vā |<245>                    nopamā sadṛśābhāvāt, nārthāpattir viparyayāt ||
  261. 5,4.261tasmād abhāvagamyatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sthitaṃ hi naḥ |                    evaṃ pramāṇato 'siddhā yaiḥ prameyāśrayocyate ||
  262. 5,4.262 bāhyasyāṇusamūhāder grāhyasyāsambhavekṣaṇāt ||
  263. 5,4.263tairāntarāsambhavato yathoktād jñeyatvam anyasya balād upeyam |                    grāhyā na ceṣṭāḥ paramāṇavo 'taḥ satyaḥ samūhaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ ||
  264. 5,4.264iti bahirviṣayapratipādanād tadabhāvakṛtā matisaṃvṛtiḥ |                    ubhayatattvavidāṃ paramārthataḥ, kṣamam idaṃ dhuri dharmavicāraṇe ||

Chapter 5,5 anumānapariccheda AMP

  1. 5,5.1pratyakṣāvyabhicāritvād evaṃlakṣaṇakaṃ ca yat |                    prasiddham anumānādi na parīkṣyaṃ tad apy ataḥ ||
  2. 5,5.2pramātā jñātasambandhaḥ, ekadeśyatha vocyate |                    karmadhārayapakṣo vā sambandhinyekadeśatā ||
  3. 5,5.3dvayaṃ vā jñātasambandham upalabdhaṃ parasparam |                    tasyaikadeśaśabdābhyām ucyete samudāyinau ||<247><248>
  4. 5,5.4sambandho vyāptir iṣṭātra liṅgādharmasya liṅginā |                    vyāpyasya gamakatvaṃ ca vyāpakaṃ gamyam iṣyate ||
  5. 5,5.5yo yasya deśakālābhyāṃ samo nyūno 'pi vā bhavet |                    sa vyāpyo vyāpakas tasya samo vābhyadhiko 'pi vā ||
  6. 5,5.6tena vyāpye gṛhīte 'rthe vyāpakas tasya gṛhyate |                    na hy anyathā bhavaty eṣā vyāpyavyāpakatā tayoḥ ||
  7. 5,5.7vyāpakatvagṛhītas tu vyāpyo yady api vastutaḥ |                    ādhikye 'py aviruddhatvād vyāpyaṃ na pratipādayet ||
  8. 5,5.8vispaṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭam etac ca goviṣāṇitvayor mitau |                    vyāpyatvād gamikā gāvo vyāpikā na viṣāṇitā ||
  9. 5,5.9tena yatrāpy ubhau dhrmau vyāpyavyāpakasammatau |                    tatrāpi vyāpyataiva syād aṅgaṃ na vyāpitā miteḥ ||<249>
  10. 5,5.10tena dharmyantareṣv eṣā yasya yenaiva yādṛśī |                    deśe yāvati kāle vā vyāpyatā prāṅ nirūpitā ||
  11. 5,5.11tasya tāvati tādṛk sa dṛṣṭo dharmyantare punaḥ |                    vyāpyāṃśo vyāpakāṃśasya tathaiva pratipādakaḥ ||
  12. 5,5.12bhūyodarśanagamyā ca vyāptiḥ, sāmānyadharmayoḥ |                    jñāyate bhedahānena, kva cic cāpi viśeṣayoḥ ||
  13. 5,5.13kṛttikodayamālakṣya rohiṇyāsattikḷptivat |<250>                    vyāpteś ca dṛśyamānāyāḥ kaś cid dharmaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
  14. 5,5.14asmin saty amunā bhāvyam iti śaktyā nirūpyate |                    anye paraprayuktānāṃ vyāptīnām upajīvakāḥ ||
  15. 5,5.15tair dṛṣṭair api naiveṣṭā vyāpakāṃśāvadhāraṇā |                    ye tu tān api visrabdhaṃ sādhyasiddhyau prayuñjate ||
  16. 5,5.16sulabhaiḥ pratihetvādidoṣair bhrāmyanti te ciram |                    teṣv āgamaviruddhatvaṃ svayaṃ ceṣṭavighātitā ||
  17. 5,5.17alaukikavivādāś ca varṇyas te haitukais tataḥ |                    niṣiddhitvena hiṃsānām adharmatvaṃ prayujyate ||
  18. 5,5.18tadabhāve na tatsiddhir hiṃsātvād aprayojakāt |                    hetudvayaprayukte ca mithyātve sarvabuddhiṣu ||<251>
  19. 5,5.19jñānatvotpattimattvādisādhako naprayojakaḥ |                    traivarṇikaprayuktā ca yāgādeḥ svargahetutā ||
  20. 5,5.20na manuṣyatvamātreṇa śūdrasthena prayujyate |                    kṛtasāvayavatvādiprayuktā ca vināśitā ||
  21. 5,5.21prayatnānantarajñānasadṛśair na prayujyate |                    jātimattvendriyatvādi vastusanmātrabandhanam ||
  22. 5,5.22śadānityatvasiddhyarthaṃ ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ |                    tasmād ya eva yasyārtho dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanaśaktitaḥ ||
  23. 5,5.23sa eva gamakas tasya na prasaṅgānvito 'pi yaḥ |                    upāttaś caikadeśābhyāṃ dharmy apy atraikadeśatā ||
  24. 5,5.24apārārthye hi dhūmādeḥ svarūpair naikadeśatā |                    sa eva cobhayātamāyaṃ gamyo gamaka eva vā ||<252>
  25. 5,5.25asiddhenaikadeśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ |                    ataḥ pṛthagabhinno vāprayoktāṇāṃ vivakṣaya ||
  26. 5,5.26anityaḥ kṛtako yasmād dhūmavān agnimān iti |                    dharmyabhinnam upādānam, bhedo 'trāgnir itīdṛśe ||
  27. 5,5.27ekadeśaviśiṣṭaś ca dharmyevātrānumīyate |                    na hi tannirapekṣatve sambhavaty anumeyatā ||
  28. 5,5.28na dharmamātraṃ siddhatvāt, tathā dharmī, tathobhayam |                    vyastaṃ vāpi samastaṃ vā svātantryeṇānumīyate ||
  29. 5,5.29ekadeśasya liṅgatvaṃ sādhyenānugamo 'sya ca |                    dvayaṃ ca na syād iṣṭaṃ sat pakṣeṣv eṣu yathākramam ||
  30. 5,5.30anityatvādayo dharmāḥ kṛtakatvādayo na hi |                    dhvaninānugamo naiṣāṃ nobhayasyobhayena vā ||<253>
  31. 5,5.31sambandho 'py anupādānān nāmnā ṣaṣṭhyāpi vā mitau |                    na cāpy anugamas tena liṅgasyeha nidarśyate ||
  32. 5,5.32na cākāradvayaṃ tasya sādhyasādhanabhāg bhavet |                    tasmad arthagṛhītatvānmatubarthasya gamyatā ||
  33. 5,5.33na svāntantryeṇa mantavyā, yathā daṇḍyādiśabdataḥ |                    viśīṣṭārthapratītau syāt sambandho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
  34. 5,5.34viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvam āpannau dvāv imāv ataḥ |                    gamyau, aṅgāṅgibhāvas tu kaiś cid iṣṭo vikalpataḥ ||<254>
  35. 5,5.35sarvathā dharmiṇo dharmo dharmeṇa tv avagamyate |                    viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve na viśeṣo 'vadhāryate ||
  36. 5,5.36tatrotaraṃ vadanty anye yadi dharmī viśeṣaṇam |                    hetudharmeṇa samandhas tasyāprādhānyataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
  37. 5,5.37pradhānatvād dhi dharmeṇa sambandho vākyato bhavet |                    tatrāsambhavataḥ paścāt kalpyo 'sau dharminā saha ||
  38. 5,5.38dhvaner ity atha vā vācyam, anvayasya tu darśane |                    bhedopāttasya dharmasya guṇābhāvo na duṣyati ||
  39. 5,5.39agner deśaviśiṣṭatve na caitat pakṣalakṣaṇam |                    viśiṣṭatāsya deśena bhaved evamprakārikā ||
  40. 5,5.40yo 'gniḥ so 'sti kva cid deśe yo dṛṣṭo yatra tatra vā |                    agniḥ pūrvānubhūto vā deśamātreṇa saṅgataḥ ||
  41. 5,5.41yo 'gniḥ so 'nena yukto vā, yo dṛṣṭo 'nena so 'tha vā |                    yo 'yaṃ sa deśamātreṇa yuktaḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy ayam ||
  42. 5,5.42etaddeśaviśiṣṭo vā yo 'yam agnir iti, <255> iha tu |                    pūrvayoḥ siddhasādhyatvaṃ pareṣu syād viruddhatā ||
  43. 5,5.43vyāptir etena deśena sarvāgnīnāṃ na yujyate |                    nāpi pūrvasya, nāpy eṣa vahniḥ sarvair viśiṣyate ||
  44. 5,5.44deśaiḥ, pūrveṇa vāpy asya na deśena viśeṣyatā |                    etaddeśaviśiṣṭo 'yam ity etat kathyate katham ||
  45. 5,5.45yadā deśānapekṣo 'gnir nāyam ity avadhāryate |                    agneḥ pūrvataraṃ cātra deśa evāvadhāryate ||
  46. 5,5.46tajjñānakālabuddhaś ca na deśaḥ syād viśeṣaṇam |                    deśasya parvatādes tu svarūpe pāvakād ṛte ||
  47. 5,5.47gṛhīte 'gniviśiṣṭasya punarjñānaṃ na duṣyati |<256>                    tasmād dharmaviśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā ||
  48. 5,5.48sā deśasyāgniyuktasya, dhūmasyānyaiś ca kalpitā |                    nanu śabdavad eva syāl liṅgamyaṃ viśiṣaṇam ||
  49. 5,5.49naivam, na hy atra liṅgasya śaktyanekatvakalpanā |                    na ca tasyānumeyatvam, viśeṣyaś cāvadhāritaḥ ||
  50. 5,5.50viśiṣṭatvena cājñānāt tanmātrasyānumeyatā |                    nanu dhūmaviśeṣyatve hetoḥ pakṣaikadeśatā ||
  51. 5,5.51naitad asti, viśeṣe hi sādhye sāmānyahetutā |<257>                    dhūmatajjānasambandhasmṛtiprāmāṇyakalpane ||
  52. 5,5.52phalena viṣayaikatvaṃ tadvyāpārāt puroditam |                    prameyadhīpramāṇatvaṃ bhāṣyakāras tu manyate ||
  53. 5,5.53pratyakṣāniyamoktaś ca sarvatraivānuṣajyate |                    anumānagṛhītasya tenaiva pratipādanam ||
  54. 5,5.54parebhyo vāñchatā vācyaḥ pūrvapakṣo yathoditaḥ |<258>                    tatra dharmiṇam uddiśya sādhyadharmo vidhīyate ||
  55. 5,5.55niyamas tadvipakṣāc ca kalpyate nāvirodhinaḥ |                    asannikṛṣṭavācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam ||
  56. 5,5.56tādrūpyeṇa paricchittis tadviparyayato 'pi ca |                    pramitasya pramāṇe hi nāpekṣā jāyate punaḥ ||
  57. 5,5.57tādrūpyeṇa paricchinne pramāṇaṃ niṣphalaṃ param |<259>                    vaiparītyaparicchinne nāvakāśaḥ parasya tu ||
  58. 5,5.58mūle tasya hy anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayo hṛtaḥ |                    pratyakṣādeś ca ṣaṭkasya yenaivārtho 'vadhāritaḥ ||
  59. 5,5.59tenaivottarabādhaḥ syād, vikalpāder asambhavāt |<260>                    agrāhyatā tu śabdādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virudhyate ||
  60. 5,5.60teṣām aśrāvaṇatvādi viruddham anumānataḥ |                    na hi śrāvaṇatā nāma pratyakṣeṇāvagamyate ||
  61. 5,5.61sānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ gamyate badhirādiṣu |                    tridhā śabdavirodhaḥ syāt pratijñādivibhāgataḥ ||<261>
  62. 5,5.62pratijñāpūrvasañjalpasarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ |                    yāvajjīvam ahaṃ maunīty uktimātreṇa bādhyate ||
  63. 5,5.63sarvavākyamṛṣātve tu dharmoktyaivātmabādhanam |                    dharmyuktyāhaṃ yato jātaḥ sā vandhyā jananī mama ||
  64. 5,5.64bauddhasya śabdanityatvaṃ pūrvopetena bādhyate |                    candraśabdābhidheyatvaṃ śaśino yo niṣedhati ||
  65. 5,5.65sa sarvalokasiddhena candrajñānena bādhyate |                    jñātagogavayākāraṃ prati yaḥ sādhayed idam ||
  66. 5,5.66na gor gavayasādṛśyaṃ tasya bādhopamānataḥ |                    gehāvagatanāstitvo jīvaṃś caitro yadā bahiḥ ||
  67. 5,5.67nāstīti sādhyate bādhas tatrārthāpattito bhavet |<262>                    agnāvadāhake sādhye śabde cānabhidhāyake ||
  68. 5,5.68śrotrādināstitāyāṃ ca śabdānityatvasādhane |                    śrutārthāpattibādho 'tra yadāptoktinivārite ||
  69. 5,5.69divābhujau niṣidhyeta hetunā rātribhojanam |                    śaśaśṛṅgādisadbhāvavirodho 'nupalabdhitaḥ ||
  70. 5,5.70evaṃ ca dharmasambandhabādhas tāvad udāhṛtaḥ |                    dharmadharmyubhayeṣāṃ ca svarūpasvaviśeṣayoḥ ||
  71. 5,5.71śrutyarthākṣiptayor vākye vācyaḥ sarvapramāṇakaḥ |<263>                    tṛṇādivikriyāhetor agnimaddhimasādhane ||
  72. 5,5.72pratyakṣāvagatāc chaityāt tadviśeṣotthabādhanam |                    adharmo vihito duḥkhaṃ karotyalpam itīha tu ||
  73. 5,5.73vihitatvād adharmasya svarūpasyaiva bādhanam |                    tathā duḥkhanimittatvaṃ viśeṣas tasya bādhyate ||
  74. 5,5.74ayathārthā dhiyaḥ sarvāḥ ity ukte dvayabādhanam |                    svarūpasvaviśeṣābhyām, taddhīmithyātvasādhanāt ||
  75. 5,5.75kṣaṇikātyantamithyātve viśeṣau ca dvayor iha |<264>                    darśanād ekadeśasyety anenaitad vyudasyate ||
  76. 5,5.76yatraikasyobhayor vāpi saṃśayādhīviparyayāḥ |                    śaityān na dāhako bahniś cākṣuṣatvād anityatā ||
  77. 5,5.77śabdasyetyevamādau tu dvayoḥ siddho viparyayaḥ |                    kṛtakatvaguṇatvādau parokte yājñikaṃ prati ||
