  78. 5,5.78svokte caivamprakāre syād asiddho 'nyatarasya tu |                    bāṣpādibhāvasandigdho dvayor anyatarasya vā ||
  79. 5,5.79dhūmas tridhāpy asiddhaḥ syāt, evaṃ tāvat svarūpataḥ |                    eta eva prakārāḥ syur āśrayāsiddhikalpane ||<265>
  80. 5,5.80jñāte 'pi hi svarūpeṇa nātaddharme 'sti hetutā |                    sarvatra dṛṣṭakāryatvād ātmā sarvagatas tv iti ||
  81. 5,5.81bauddhaṃ pratyāśrayāsiddhaḥ, laukikādes tu saṃśayaḥ |                    bāṅmātrāsiddhimātreṇa vyavahārāprakalpanāt ||
  82. 5,5.82dvābhyāṃ yo 'sattvato jñātas tadvaco dūṣaṇaṃ matam |                    itarat sādhanaṃ tu syād vādinā yadi sādhyate ||
  83. 5,5.83nirākaraṇasiddhau vā dūṣaṇaṃ prativādinaḥ |                    sandehaviparītatvahetū cātra nirākṛtau ||
  84. 5,5.84jñātasambandhavacanāt, <266> trayaḥ saṃśayahetavaḥ |                    san sādhye tadabhāve vā dvābhyāṃ vyāvṛtta eva ca ||
  85. 5,5.85dvau viruddhārthasambaddhau yāv ekatraikadeśini |                    prameyānityatāmūrtidharmāḥ sādhāraṇā dvayoḥ ||
  86. 5,5.86nityāyatnotthayatnotthānityeṣu dviranityataḥ |                    nityā bhūrgandhavattvena syād asādhāraṇas tvayam ||
  87. 5,5.87niścayaikāṅgavaikalyād eṣa saṃśayakāraṇam |<267>                    sādhāraṇo yathā dṛṣṭo buddhidvayanimittakaḥ ||
  88. 5,5.88viruddhaikānavāpteś ca saṃśaye kāraṇaṃ matam |                    atrāsādhāraṇo nāsti tadabhāvamukhena tu ||
  89. 5,5.89dvayāsattvavirodhāc ca mataḥ saṃśayakāraṇam |                    sandigdhahetutā caiṣāṃ viṣayāpekṣayocyate ||
  90. 5,5.90nirṇayasyāpi hetutvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ sādhyāntare yataḥ |                    vyavacchedānvayau labdhvā, niṣkriyādāv amūrtivat ||
  91. 5,5.91kṣityekadeśasiddhatve gandhavattvasya hetutā |<268>                    yatrāpratyakṣatā vāyor arūpatvena sādhyate ||
  92. 5,5.92sparśāt pratyakṣatā vāsau viruddhāvyabhicāritā |                    ke cij jātyantaraṃ caināṃ varṇayantyapare punaḥ ||
  93. 5,5.93sādhāraṇatvam aṃśena samastaṃ vāpy ananvayam |                    pratijñā yatra bādhyeta pūrvoktair yasya sādhanaiḥ ||
  94. 5,5.94tat parājayataḥ kāryo nirṇayo bādhavarjanāt |                    kva cit saṃśayahetū yau pratyekatvena lakṣitau ||
  95. 5,5.95saṅghāte nirṇayas tābhyāmūrdhvatākākavattvavat |                    pratyekaṃ saṃhatau vāpi gamakāvavirodhinau ||
  96. 5,5.96tasmād bhinnau viruddhārthau hetū cātra nidarśitau |                    ṣoḍhā viruddhatām āhuś caturddhā vaikadhāpi vā ||<269>
  97. 5,5.97śrutyarthoktasya bādhāyāṃ pratijñārthasya hetunā |                    nityatve kṛtakatvasya dharmabādhād viruddhatā ||
  98. 5,5.98bādho dharmaviśeṣasya yadā tv evaṃ prayujyate |                    arthavacchabdarūpaṃ syāt prāksambandhāvadhāraṇāt ||
  99. 5,5.99vibhaktimattvāt paścādvat svarūpeṇeti cāśrite |                    asvarūpārthayogas tu paścāc chabdasya dṛśyate ||
  100. 5,5.100tena prāg api sambandhād asvarūpārthatā bhavet |                    ihapratyayahetutvād dravyāder vyatiricyate ||
  101. 5,5.101samavāyo yathehāyaṃ ghaṭa ityādisaṅgatiḥ |                    atrāpy asamavāyatvaṃ saṃyogasyeva sidhyati ||
  102. 5,5.102tena dharmisvarūpasya vaiparītyād viruddhatā |<270>                    yac ca sattāvad ekatvaṃ samavāyasya kalpitam ||
  103. 5,5.103tatra saṃyogavadbhedāt syād viśeṣaviruddhatā |                    nityam ātmāstitā kaiś cid yadā sautrāntikaṃ prati ||
  104. 5,5.104sādhyate 'vayavābhāvād vyomavad dvayabādhanam |                    tadobhayaviśeṣasya bādho 'yaṃ sādhyate yadā ||
  105. 5,5.105pārārthyaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ saṅghātāc chayanādivat |                    śayane saṅghapārārthyaṃ bhautikavyāptahetuke ||
  106. 5,5.106ātmānaṃ prati pārārthyam asiddham iti bādhanam |                    asaṃhataparārthatve dṛṣṭe saṃhatatāpi ca ||
  107. 5,5.107anahaṅkārikatvaṃ ca cakṣurādeḥ prasajyate |                    gamakasyaikadeśasya vyāptir gamyeti bhāṣitum ||
  108. 5,5.108sādhyasādharmyavaidharmyadṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipādyate |<271>                    tatra hetvartham uddiśya sādhyopādānam iṣyate ||
  109. 5,5.109uddeśyo vyāpyate dharmo vyāpakaś cetaro mataḥ |                    yadvṛttayoḥ prāthamyam ity ādyuddeśalakṣaṇam ||
  110. 5,5.110tadvṛttam eva kāraś ca syād upādeyalakṣaṇam |                    vadatyarthaṃ svaśaktyā ca śabdo vaktranapekṣayā ||
  111. 5,5.111sādhyahetutvam arthānāṃ vyāptiśaktyanurodhataḥ |                    tatrājñānād yadā vakta sahacāravivakṣayā ||
  112. 5,5.112viparyayeṇa vā hetau na vyāptatvaṃ vivakṣati |                    vivakṣann api vā śabdaṃ tadyogyaṃ na vaded yadi ||<272>
  113. 5,5.113ghaṭe kṛtakanāśitve nāśivyāptaṃ kṛtena vā |                    na tadeṣṭasya hetutvam, syād aniṣṭasya caiva tat ||
  114. 5,5.114tasmād vyāpyatvarūpeṇa vācyo hetutvasammataḥ |                    yadā samyak prayukte 'pi vākye 'rtho na tathā bhavet ||
  115. 5,5.115sādhyahetūbhayavyāptiśūnyatvāt paramārthataḥ |                    nityo dhvaniramūrttatvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ||
  116. 5,5.116ghaṭavad vyomavaccāpi, tadasadvādinaṃ prati |                    dharmyasiddhāv api hy evaṃ dṛṣṭāntābhāsatā bhavet ||
  117. 5,5.117tat sadbhāve 'pi ca vyomni dvayayukte 'pi kīrtite |                    karmādyālocanād vyāptir hetor nāstīti varjanam ||
  118. 5,5.118vyāptyā sādharmya ukte ca na vaidharmyam apekṣyate |                    sahabhāvitvadṛṣṭyā tu yadā vyāptiṃ na lakṣayet ||<273>
  119. 5,5.119paraḥ sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt tac ca nāpekṣate yadā |                    vaktā vā sahabhāvitvaṃ śuddhaṃ tena vaded yadā ||
  120. 5,5.120viparītānvayaṃ vāpi tat samādhitsayā tadā |                    pūrvajñānopamardena vaidharmyeṇeṣṭasādhanam ||
  121. 5,5.121sāhityamātraṃ pūrvoktaṃ hetos tatropayujyate |                    vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo hi bhāvayor yādṛg iṣyate ||
  122. 5,5.122tayor abhāvayos tasmād viparītaḥ pratīyate |                    dhūmabhāve 'gnibhāvena vyāpte 'nagnis tataś cyutaḥ ||
  123. 5,5.123adhūma eva vidyetetyevaṃ vyāpyatvamaśnute |                    tathānagnāvadhūmena vyāpte dhūmas tatacyutaḥ ||
  124. 5,5.124anyatrānavakāśatvād vyāpyate dhruvam agninā |<274>                    vyāpakau tu yadocyete bhāvābhāvau tadā tataḥ ||
  125. 5,5.125naiva vyāpyād vipakṣasya pracyutiḥ kathitā bhavet |                    tasmād dhūmena sādhyatvam agneḥ prārthayate yadā ||
  126. 5,5.126tadānagnir adhūmena vyāpto vācyaḥ, na cānyathā |                    anagnyadhūmasāhitye vyāpter vāpi viparyaye ||
  127. 5,5.127na prastutopakāraḥ syād anyad vāpi prasādhyate |                    yatrāpy arthasya śūnyatvaṃ dvābhyām ekena vā bhavet ||
  128. 5,5.128yad anityaṃ tu tan mūrtam aṇuvad buddhivat khavat |<275>                    sādhyena vyāptisiddhyaiva vyatireko 'tra kathyate ||
  129. 5,5.129yasyāyaṃ nāsty asau hetus tena sādhyena nāpyate |                    tena dṛṣṭe 'pi sāhitye na sarvo gamya iṣyate ||
  130. 5,5.130sahadṛṣṭir na sambandho vyāptir naiva ca tāvatā |                    mūrtānityatvayukte 'pi tasmād aṅgīkṛte ghaṭe ||
  131. 5,5.131karmādau vyāptyabhāvena na dṛṣṭāntatvam iṣyate |                    aśeṣāpekṣitatvāc ca saukaryāc cāpy adarśanāt ||
  132. 5,5.132sādhane yadyapīṣṭo 'tra vyatireko 'numāṃ prati |                    tāvatā na hy anaṅgatvaṃ yuktiḥ śābde hi vakṣyate ||<276>
  133. 5,5.133bodhaprasaṅgo bhedānāṃ na cāvyāpter bhaviṣyati |                    astisāmānyavastveṣu vyāpitā tatra gamyatām ||
  134. 5,5.134ke cit sādharmyadṛṣṭānte vyāptyāpi kathite punaḥ |                    vaidharmyoktim apīcchanti, vyāvṛttiniyamecchayā ||
  135. 5,5.135hetau sādharmyadṛṣṭāntāt sādhyenaivāvadhārite |                    vyāvṛttiḥ sarvataḥ prāptā sādhyābhāve niyamyate ||<277>
  136. 5,5.136tat tu mandaphalaṃ yasmāt pakṣe 'py evaṃ nirūpitam |                    vyāpakābhāvamātraṃ hi vyāpyān nityaṃ nivartate ||
  137. 5,5.137tasmād yathaiva śuklatve paṭasyokte virodhinām |                    nivṛttir na tu dairdhyādes tathātrāpi bhaviṣyati ||
  138. 5,5.138dvaividhyaṃ nopapannaṃ tu yathaiva hy agnidhūmayoḥ |                    pratyakṣadṛṣṭaḥ sambandho gatiprāptyos tathaiva hi ||
  139. 5,5.139āditye 'nupalabdhiś cen na deśe 'py adhunātane |                    kva cit tatropalabdhiś ced devadatte 'pi dṛśyatām ||<278>
  140. 5,5.140yadi dharmyantarāpekṣā tatra sāmānyadṛṣṭatā |                    syād agnidhūmayoḥ saiva, tasmād evaṃ pracakṣate ||
  141. 5,5.141pratyakṣadṛṣṭasambandhaṃ yayor eva viśeṣayoḥ |                    gomayendhanatajjanyaviśeṣādimatiḥ kṛtā ||
  142. 5,5.142taddeśasthena tenaiva gatvā kālāntare 'pi tam |                    yadāgnir budhyate, <279> tasya pūrvabodhāt punaḥ punaḥ ||
  143. 5,5.143sandihyamānasadbhāvavastubodhāt pramāṇatā |                    viśeṣadṛṣṭam etac ca likhitaṃ vindhyavāsinā ||
  144. 5,5.144ākṛtyor eva caiṣeṣṭā vyavacchedena kena cit |                    hetusādhyavyavastheti viśeṣo nopadarśitaḥ ||
  145. 5,5.145agnidhūmāntaratve ca vācye sāmānyato mitau |                    sāmānyadṛṣṭam ekāntād atretyāditya ucyate ||
  146. 5,5.146pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ ca sāmānyasya prasādhitam |                    vastutvaṃ ca, atra hetur vā dvayasyāpy abhidhīyate ||
  147. 5,5.147dhūmād agnyanumānasya vastvālambanatā bhavet |                    abhāvānyapramāṇatvāt svārthe śrotrādibuddhivat ||
  148. 5,5.148sāmānyasya ca vastutvaṃ pratyakṣagrāhyatāpi ca |                    abhāvānyaprameyatvād asādhāraṇavastuvat ||<280>
  149. 5,5.149sāmānyaṃ nānumānena vinā yasya pratīyate |                    na ca liṅgavinirmuktam anumānaṃ pravartate ||
  150. 5,5.150asāmānyasya liṅgatvaṃ na ca kena cid iṣyate |                    na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ kiñ cid asti prakāśakam ||
  151. 5,5.151tasya vāpy anumānena syād anyena gatiḥ punaḥ |                    tadutpattiś ca liṅgāt syāt sāmānyajñānasaṃhitāt ||
  152. 5,5.152tasya cāpy anumānatvāt bhavel liṅgena codbhavaḥ |                    anumānāntarād eva jñānenaivaṃ ca kalpane ||
  153. 5,5.153liṅgaliṅgyanumānānām ānantyād ekaliṅgini |                    gatir yugasahasreṣu bahuṣv api na vidyate ||
  154. 5,5.154atha sāmānyabhūte 'pi liṅge 'nyasmād gatir bhavet |                    pramāṇād apramāṇād vā, tathā liṅgigatir bhavet ||
  155. 5,5.155evam apy anumānasya nityocchedaḥ prasajyate |<281>                    pramāṇāntaram eva syāt sāmānyasyāvabodhakam ||
  156. 5,5.156apramāṇāvabuddhād vā liṅgāl liṅgini yā matiḥ |                    sāpi mithyā bhaven nityaṃ bāṣpajātāgnibuddhivat ||
  157. 5,5.157nanv apramāṇabhūtāpi sambandhasmṛtir iṣyate |                    yathā liṅgigatau hetus tathā liṅgagatir bhavet ||
  158. 5,5.158tatra yat pūrvavijñānaṃ tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate |                    tadupasthānamātreṇa smṛteḥ syāc caritārthatā ||<282>
  159. 5,5.159na tu liṅgagatau kiñ cit pramāṇam upapadyate |                    tadabhāvāsmṛtiś cātra na kathañ cit pravartate ||
  160. 5,5.160smārtam etadabhedena vijñānam iti yo vadet |                    tasya vandhyāsute 'py asti nūnaṃ smaraṇaśaktatā ||
  161. 5,5.161na cāsādhāraṇo 'rthātmā sāmānyajñānakāraṇam |                    yasmān nāsyāvinābhāvas tena dṛṣṭaḥ kathañ cana ||
  162. 5,5.162syād vā sambandhadṛṣṭyāsau sāmānyaṃ kṛtakatvavat |                    na hy asādhāraṇaṃ vastu pūrvatreha ca vidyate ||
  163. 5,5.163na cāpy avyapadeśasya vikalparahitasya ca |                    vinā pūrvānusandhānāl liṅgatvam upapadyate ||<283>
  164. 5,5.164kalpyante ca viśeṣā ye te 'py aliṅgam ananvayāt |                    etasmād eva hetoḥ syāt tajñānasyāpy aliṅgatā ||
  165. 5,5.165sāmānyarūpatāyāṃ vā tathaivānavadhāraṇam |                    kva cid vā dṛṣṭasambandhe sarvaḥ pratyāyako bhavet ||
  166. 5,5.166sambandhānubhavo 'vaśyam eṣitavyaś ca liṅganaḥ |                    anumānapravṛttes tu prāg jñānaṃ tatra nāsti te ||
  167. 5,5.167na cāpi vāsanāmātrāl liṅgajñānasya sambhavaḥ |                    liṅgijñānaṃ ca tadvat syāt trirūpāl liṅgato na tat ||<284>
  168. 5,5.168tatrābhāvasya liṅgatvaṃ na cāsāv ānumānikaḥ |                    pramāṇāntaragamyatvāt tatra doṣo na jāyate ||
  169. 5,5.169pratyakṣāvagatāl liṅgād yasya liṅgigatir bhavet |                    tasya nāto 'dhikaṃ kiñ cit prārthanīyaṃ prasajyate ||
  170. 5,5.170yatrāpy anumitāl liṅgāl liṅgini grahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    tatrāpi maulikaṃ liṅgaṃ pratyakṣād eva gamyate ||
  171. 5,5.171liṅgatvaṃ kṛtakatvādau kriyāyāḥ kārakasya vā |                    pratyakṣatvaṃ ca tasyeṣṭam iti dūraṃ na gamyate ||
  172. 5,5.172evaṃ śabdopamānādau sāmānyāśrayatā yataḥ |                    taddaussthityena daussthityaṃ sarvatrātaḥ prasajyate ||
  173. 5,5.173tasmāt pratyakṣapūrvatvaṃ pramāṇāntara iṣyate |                    pratyakṣatvaṃ ca sāmānye nānyathā hi gatir bhavet ||
  174. 5,5.174pratyakṣālambanatvaṃ ca viśeṣasya kathaṃ bhavet |                    yadā vastvantarāpekṣaḥ sāmānyāṃśaḥ sa kīrtyate ||<285>
  175. 5,5.175rūpādayo hi sāmānyaṃ sarve nīlādyapekṣayā |                    svaviśeṣānapekṣyātha nīlādīnāṃ samānatā ||
  176. 5,5.176te cāpi tāvat sāmānyaṃ yāvat syuḥ paramāṇavaḥ |                    dvyaṇukasyāpi yadrūpaṃ tad dhi sādhāraṇaṃ dvayoḥ ||
  177. 5,5.177na cāntyena viśeṣeṇa vyavahāro 'sti kasya cit |                    na ca pratyakṣatā tasya saṅghāte kevalasya vā ||
  178. 5,5.178bhedenāgṛhyamāṇasya nābhedo grāhyatāṃ vrajet |                    na ca bhinneṣv abhinnatvabuddher grāhyatvasambhavaḥ ||<286>
  179. 5,5.179samudāyo na vāpy asti bhavatāṃ na ca sarvadā |                    sarveṣām asatārthena pratyayotpattisambhavaḥ ||
  180. 5,5.180na caikajātiyogena vināsti samudāyatā |                    samudāye 'pi cāṇutvaṃ naiteṣām apagacchati ||
  181. 5,5.181sāmānyam ity adṛśye 'pi tena sāmānya eva naḥ |                    vyāsaṅginī bhavaty eṣā dhīrvināpy ekakalpanāt ||
  182. 5,5.182vyāsajya vartamānasya sāmānyasya yathendriyaiḥ |                    grahaṇaṃ tadvad eva syāt prativyaktiniveśinaḥ ||
  183. 5,5.183mīmāṃsakaiś ca nāvaśyam iṣyante paramāṇavaḥ |                    yadbalenopalabdhasya mithyātvaṃ kalpayed bhavān ||
  184. 5,5.184samūharūpaṃ pratyakṣam adṛśyaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ |                    yo 'pahnute śaśasyāpi so 'bhāvaṃ śṛṅgato vadet ||
  185. 5,5.185samūhaparamārthatve sthite tatsiddhihetukā |                    yadi nāmāvagamyeta paramāṇvastitā punaḥ ||<287>
  186. 5,5.186tasmād yad gṛhyate vastu yena rūpeṇa sarvadā |                    tat tathaivābhyupetavyaṃ sāmānyam atha vetarat ||
  187. 5,5.187sattādisāmānyam apekṣya sarvaṃ gotvādi sādhāraṇatām upaiti |                    tasmād asādhāraṇam akṣagamyaṃ vadan na sāmānyam apahnuvīta ||
  188. 5,5.188sāmānyarupeṇa na gṛhyate cet, kiṃ vāstyasādhāraṇabuddhir atra |                    yadvastu lokaḥ pratipadyate 'smin dvidhāpi tacchaktyata eva vaktum ||

Chapter 5,6 śabdapariccheda SBP

  1. 5,6.1pratyakṣādiṣu vaktavyaṃ śabdamātrasya lakṣaṇam |                    adatitvariteneha kiṃ śāstrād abhidhīyate ||<288>
  2. 5,6.2sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tyaktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam |                    na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ito 'py asya na vācyatā ||
  3. 5,6.3yac coktaṃ śabdavijñānād arthe jñānam itīdṛśamū |                    aviśiṣṭaṃ viśiṣṭasya na tacchāstrasya lakṣaṇam ||
  4. 5,6.4pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā |                    puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstram abhidhīyate ||
  5. 5,6.5svarūpakathanaṃ yat tu kasya cit tatra dṛśyate |                    tadaṅgatvena tasyāpi śāstratvam avagamyate ||
  6. 5,6.6bhāvanāyāṃ samastāyāṃ vākyād evopajāyate |                    pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā tacchāstraṃ na padād yataḥ ||
  7. 5,6.7aparīkṣāmiṣeṇāpi lakṣaṇāni vadannayam |                    na svatantropayogitvanirapekṣāṇi jalpati ||
  8. 5,6.8tatra yallokavākyasthaṃ kathayecchabdalakṣaṇam |                    vedaṃ vyākhyātukāmasya tannātīvopayujyate ||<289>
  9. 5,6.9pratyakṣādyupayogaṃ tu varṇamātrāditaḥ puraḥ |                    śāstrārthajñānavelāyāṃ matvā tallakṣaṇaṃ kṛtam ||
  10. 5,6.10yat tu gāmānayetyādivākyasthaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam |                    tasya nehopayogo 'sti tasmāc chāstragataṃ kṛtam ||
  11. 5,6.11veśeṣaś ca na sāmānyam antareṇāsti kaś cana |                    tasmāt tam apy udāhṛtya sāmānyaṃ lakṣayet sukham ||
  12. 5,6.12sāmānyarūpam apy etadadhikārād viśiṣyate |<290>                    codanā copadeśaś ca śāstram evety udāhṛtam ||
  13. 5,6.13yathā ca codanāśabdo vaidikyām eva vartate |                    śabdajñānārthavijñānaśabdau śāstre tathā sthitau ||
  14. 5,6.14pratyakṣādyaparīkṣyatve tadantarbhāvahetukam |                    śāstrasyāpy aparīkṣyatvamanayaiva dhiyoditam ||
  15. 5,6.15tatrānumānam evedaṃ bauddhair vaiśeṣikaiḥ śritam |                    bhedaḥ sāṃkhyādibhis tv iṣṭo na tūktaṃ bhedakāraṇam ||
  16. 5,6.16pūrvasaṃskārayuktāntyavarṇavākyādikalpanā |                    vivakṣādi ca dhūmādau nāstīty etena bhinnatā ||
  17. 5,6.17yair uktā tatra vaidharmyavikalpasamajātitā |<291>                    dhūmānityaviṣāṇyādiviśeṣān na hi bhinnatā ||
  18. 5,6.18tailakṣaṇyaparityāgo yāvan na pratipādyate |                    tāvad viśeṣamātreṇa vadato jātitā bhavet ||
  19. 5,6.19yatheṣṭaviniyogena pratītir yāpi śabdataḥ |                    na dhūmāder itīhāpi vyabhicāro 'ṅgavṛttibhiḥ ||
  20. 5,6.20hastasaṃjñādayo ye 'pi yadarthapratipādane |                    bhaveyuḥ kṛtasaṅketāste na liṅgam iti sthitiḥ ||<292>
  21. 5,6.21puruṣākṣiptatayāṃ ca tathaiva vyabhicāritā |                    padavaidikavākyānāṃ na satyavyāpitā bhavet ||
  22. 5,6.22sambandhātubhavaś cāyaṃ so 'nyatrāpi vilakṣaṇaḥ |                    etasmin puruṣāpekṣā deśāpekṣāgnidhūmayoḥ ||
  23. 5,6.23kālādyapekṣayā cānyaḥ, uktā cānyair abhinnatā |                    āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyād anumānataḥ ||
  24. 5,6.24na cāpūrvādiśabdānāṃ bhedāt sarvatra bhinnatā |                    na cehāśvādiśabdebhyo bhedas teṣāṃ pratīyate ||
  25. 5,6.25na cāpy ajñātasambandhaṃ padaṃ kiñ cit prakāśakam |                    sambandhān anubhūtyāto na syād ananumānatā ||<293>
  26. 5,6.26tulyākāratayāpy atra śabdajñānārthataddhiyām |                    agnidhūmeṣv adṛṣṭatvān na bhedas tannivāraṇāt ||
  27. 5,6.27pratibimbeṣv anaikānto bimbaṃ yādṛgghi darpaṇe |                    tādṛṅ mukhādi budhyante, na cātrānanumānatā ||
  28. 5,6.28pratyakṣatā tadāpy atra tadānyair vyabhicāritā |                    yatra pādādi bambena gatānām anumīyate ||
  29. 5,6.29ekavākyāt sakṛc coktān nāpy anekasya tatkṣaṇam |                    syād viruddhāviruddhasya bodhād etasya bhinnātā ||
  30. 5,6.30liṅgasyāpi hi tādrūpyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hetuviruddhayoḥ |<294>                    virodhān nānumānaṃ cet, syād anāgamatāpi te ||
  31. 5,6.31yatra caikārthatā vākye tatra syād anumānatā |                    sakṛduccarite cāsmin vivakṣaikaiva dṛśyate ||
  32. 5,6.32yas tv anirdhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |                    sa liṅge 'py asphuṭe dṛṣṭas tasmān naitena bhidyate ||
  33. 5,6.33dṛṣṭāntānabhidhānaṃ ca dhūmādau vyabhicāritam |                    prasiddhatvād dhi tatrāpi na dṛṣṭānto 'bhidhīyate ||
  34. 5,6.34anabhyas te tv apekṣante śabde sambandhinaḥ smṛtim |                    atra pratyukta ity evaṃ budhyante hi cirāt kva cit ||
  35. 5,6.35paroktā hetavaś cātra nābhedasya nivāritāḥ |                    śabdānumānayor aikyaṃ dhūmād agnyanumānavat ||
  36. 5,6.36anvayavyatirekābhyām ekapratyakṣadarśanāt |                    sambandhapūrvakatvāc ca pratipattir ito yataḥ ||
  37. 5,6.37pratyakṣānyapramāṇatvāt tadadṛṣṭārthabodhanāt |                    sāmānyaviṣayatvāc ca traikālyaviṣayāśrayāt ||<295>
  38. 5,6.38kaiś cin mīmāṃsakair ukto bhedo 'tra viṣayāntarāt |                    pūrvābhyāṃ hy aparicchinne śāstram arthe pravartate ||
  39. 5,6.39tatrāpi nāgamatvaṃ syāt puruṣokte, tathās tu cet |                    pratyayaḥ kin nimitto 'rthe, vaktṛbuddheḥ, kuto nv asau ||
  40. 5,6.40na śabdārthasya sāliṅgaṃ na śabdo 'syāḥ kathañ cana |                    viśeṣo gamyate tābhyāṃ na caitasyānumeyatā ||
  41. 5,6.41tena vaktur abhiprāye pratyakṣādyanirūpite |                    puruṣoktir api śroturāgamatvaṃ prapadyate ||
  42. 5,6.42na cāpy ananumeyatvam āgamārthasya śakyate |<296>                    liṅgaṃ hi śabda evāsya dhūmo 'gner iva kalpyate ||
  43. 5,6.43na cāpy ananumeyavāt pramāṇāntaragamyatā |                    rūpasyāśrāvaṇatvena na hy apratyakṣateṣyate ||
  44. 5,6.44evaṃ sati svayūthyā na ke cin nātiprapañcinaḥ |                    anumānaviśeṣo 'yam īdṛg dharmasya bodhakaḥ ||
  45. 5,6.45bhaviṣyatyartharūpaṃ tu liṅgaṃ dharme nirākṛtam |                    saṃjñānumānatecchā tu na duṣyedāgame 'pi naḥ ||
  46. 5,6.46lakṣaṇena tv abhinnatvaṃ yadi śabdānumānayoḥ |                    vedajñānāpramāṇatvaṃ syād atallakṣaṇatvataḥ ||
  47. 5,6.47āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyān nṛvacassu hi |                    lakṣaṇenānumānatvāt prāmāṇyaṃ siddhimṛcchati ||
  48. 5,6.48vede tv āptanarābhāvāt sambandhānubhavād ṛte |                    lakṣaṇaṃ nānumānasyety aprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||<297>
  49. 5,6.49nanv ekadeśasatyatve tasya syād anumānatā |                    vedatvād agnihotrādau vāyukṣepiṣṭhavākyavat ||
  50. 5,6.50nādityayūpe 'naikāntāt, tadvad vā gauṇatā bhavet |                    nātaḥ pratyanumānānām evaṃ pūrvoktayā viśā ||
  51. 5,6.51tasmāl lakṣaṇabhedena yadi śabdapramāṇatā |                    samā loke ca vede ca siddhā vedapramāṇatā ||
  52. 5,6.52tena cāptopadeśatvaṃ na syād āgamalakṣaṇam |                    nāptasya sambhavo vede, loke nāsmāt pramāṇatā ||
  53. 5,6.53purastād varṇitaṃ hy etat, tsmāc chabdena yā matiḥ |<298>                    tasyāḥ svataḥ pramāṇatvaṃ na cet syād doṣadarśanam ||
  54. 5,6.54anumānena caitasya prāmāṇyaṃ kevalaṃ samam |                    pade tāvat kṛto yatnaḥ parair ity atra varṇyate ||
  55. 5,6.55viṣayo 'nyādṛśas tāvad dṛśyate liṅgaśabdayoḥ |                    sāmānyaviṣayatvaṃ ca padasya sthāpayiṣyati ||
  56. 5,6.56dharmādharmaviśiṣṭaś ca liṅgīty etac ca sādhitam |                    na tāvad anumānaṃ hi yāvat tadviṣayaṃ na tat ||
  57. 5,6.57sāmānyād atiriktaṃ tu śābde vākyasya gocaraḥ |                    sāmarthyād anumeyatvād aśrute 'pi padāntare ||
  58. 5,6.58saṃkhyādimān padārthaś cet, na tāvat so 'vyayādiṣu |                    yatrāpi te pratīyante tatra vyakter viśeṣaṇam ||
  59. 5,6.59padāntarābhidheyasya tādarthyāc ca kriyātmanaḥ |<299>                    vākyārthe 'pi padaṃ yatra gomadādi prayujyate ||
  60. 5,6.60saty apy atra viśeṣṭatve siddhatvān naiva pakṣatā |                    tāvān eva hi tatrārtho yaḥ pūrvam avadhāritaḥ ||
  61. 5,6.61bhedabuddheś ca vaiṣamyaṃ prakṛtipratyayārthayoḥ |                    viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyārthasvātantryagrahaṇaṃ na ca ||
  62. 5,6.62viśeṣyapūrvikā tatra buddhiś cātra viparyayaḥ |                    atha śabdo 'rthavattvena pakṣaḥ kasmān na kalpyate ||
  63. 5,6.63pratijñārthaikadeśo hi hetus tatra prasajyate |                    pakṣe dhūmaviśeṣe ca sāmānyaṃ hetur iṣyate ||
  64. 5,6.64śabdatvaṃ gamakaṃ nātra gośabdatvaṃ niṣetsyate |<300>                    vyaktir eva viśiṣyāto hetuś caikā prasajyate ||
  65. 5,6.65bhaved vyañjakabhedāc cet, na tv evaṃ pratyayo 'sti naḥ |                    kathaṃ cāsya viśiṣṭatvaṃ na tāvad deśakālataḥ ||
  66. 5,6.66tatpratītiviśiṣṭaś cet, paraṃ kim anumīyate |                    na pratyāyanaśaktiś ca viśeṣasyānumīyate ||
  67. 5,6.67viśeṣāṇāṃ na śaktir hi saikadeśe 'gnijātivat |                    sāmānyasyaiva śaktatvaṃ pakṣo hetus tad eva ca ||<301>
  68. 5,6.68tasmād arthaviśiṣṭasya na śabdasyānumeyatā |                    kathaṃ ca pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyeha nirūpyate ||
  69. 5,6.69na kriyākartṛsambandhād ṛte sambandhanaṃ kva cit |                    rājā bharttā manuṣyasya tena rājñaḥ sa ucyate ||
  70. 5,6.70vṛkṣas tiṣṭhati śākhāsu tā vā tatreti tasya tāḥ |                    deśe 'gnimati dhūmasya kartṛtvaṃ bhavanaṃ prati ||
  71. 5,6.71kāryakāraṇabhāvādau kriyā sarvatra vidyate |                    na cānavagatākāraḥ sambandho 'stīti gamyate ||
  72. 5,6.72na cāsty asati sambandhe ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣo 'pi vā |                    tasmān na pakṣadharmo 'yam iti śakyā nirūpaṇā ||
  73. 5,6.73nivṛtte 'nyatra sambandhe ye 'pi tadviṣayātmanā |                    vadeyuḥ pakṣadharmatvaṃ śabdasyānupalabdhivat ||
  74. 5,6.74tair apy etannirūpyaṃ tu śabdas tadviṣayaḥ katham |                    na taddeśādisadbhāvo nābhimukhyādi tasya vā ||
  75. 5,6.75tasmād utpādayaty eṣa yato 'rthaviṣayā matim |                    tena tadviṣayaḥ śabda iti dharmatvakalpanā ||<302>
  76. 5,6.76tatra vācakatāyāṃ ca siddhāyāṃ pakṣadharmatā |                    na pratītyaṅgatāṃ gacchen na caivam anumānatā ||
  77. 5,6.77gamakatāc ca dharmatvaṃ dharmatvād gamako yadi |                    syād anyonyāśrayatvaṃ hi tasmān naiṣāpi kalpanā ||
  78. 5,6.78na cāgṛhītasambandhāḥ svarūpavyatirekataḥ |                    śabdaṃ jānanti yenātra pakṣadharmamatir bhavet ||
  79. 5,6.79na ca svarūpamātreṇa dhūmādeḥ pakṣadharmatā |                    na cāpi pūrvasambandham apekṣyaiṣā prasajyate ||
  80. 5,6.80dhūmavān ayam ity evam apūrvasyāpi jāyate |                    pakṣadharmamatiḥ, tena bhidyetottaralakṣaṇāt ||
  81. 5,6.81na tv atra pūrvasambandhād adhikā pakṣadharmatā |<303>                    na cārthapratyayāt pūrvam ity anaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
  82. 5,6.82na ca dharmī gṛhīto 'tra yena taddharmatā bhavet |                    parvatādir yathā deśaḥ prāgdharmatvāvadhāraṇāt ||
  83. 5,6.83yaś cātra kathyate dharmī prameyo 'sya sa eva naḥ |                    na cānavadhṛte tasmiṃs taddharmatvāvadhāraṇam ||
  84. 5,6.84prāk sa cet pakṣadharmatvād gṛhītaḥ kiṃ tataḥ param |                    paṣadharmādibhir jñātair yena syād anumānitā ||
  85. 5,6.85anvayo na ca śabdasya prameyeṇa nirūpyate |                    vyāpāreṇa hi sarveṣām anvitatvaṃ pratīyate ||
  86. 5,6.86yatra dhūmo 'sti tatrāgner astitvenānvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |                    na tv evaṃ yatra śabdo 'sti tatrārtho 'stīti niścayaḥ ||
  87. 5,6.87na tāvat tatra deśe 'sau tatkāle vāvagamyate |                    bhaven nityavibhutvāc cet, sarvārtheṣu ca tat samam ||
  88. 5,6.88tena sarvatra dṛṣṭatvād vyatirekasya cāgateḥ |                    sarvaśabdair aśeṣārthapratipattiḥ prasajyate ||<304>
  89. 5,6.89athaivaṃ deśakālābhyām asatyatvaprakalpane |                    vācakapratyayaṃ kaś cid brūyād arthadhiyānvitam ||
  90. 5,6.90naivam apy asti dṛṣṭo hi vināpy arthadhiyā kva cit |                    vācakapratyayo 'smābhir avyutpannanarān prati ||
  91. 5,6.91dvitīyādiprayoge ca bhaved anvayakalpanā |                    śatakṛtvaḥ prayukte 'pi na ca dṛṣṭārthadhīḥ kva cit ||
  92. 5,6.92nanu ye jñātasambandhās teṣāṃ dṛṣṭo 'nvayaḥ sphuṭaḥ |                    yady evam anvayāt pūrvaṃ sambandhaḥ ko 'pi kalpitaḥ ||
  93. 5,6.93nāṅgam arthadhiyām eṣā bhaved anvayakalpanā |                    anvayādhīnajanmatvam anumānasya ca sthitam ||
  94. 5,6.94jñāte pratītisāmarthye tadvaśād eva jāyate |                    paścād anvaya ity eṣa kāraṇaṃ katham ucyate ||
  95. 5,6.95tasmāt tannirapekṣaiva śabdaśaktiḥ pratīyate |<305>                    na ca dhūmānvayāt pūrvaṃ śaktatvam avagamyate ||
  96. 5,6.96vyatireko 'py avijñātād arthāc chabdadhiyau yadi |                    so 'pi paścāt sthitatvena nārthapratyayasādhanam ||
  97. 5,6.97sambandhaṃ yaṃ tu vakṣyāmastasya nirṇayakāraṇam |                    syād anvayo 'tirekaś ca na tv arthādhigamasya tau ||
  98. 5,6.98tasmād ananumānatvaṃ cābde pratyakṣavad bhavet |                    trairūpyarahitatvena tādṛgviṣayavarjanāt ||
  99. 5,6.99sati cāsya pramāṇatve bhedābhedanirūpanā |                    yuktā na tu padajñānāt padārtho 'tra pramīyate ||<306>
  100. 5,6.100padaṃ prayujyamānaṃ hi caturddhārthe prayujyate |                    pratyakṣe ca parokṣe ca jñāte 'jñāte 'pi vā purā ||
  101. 5,6.101tatra yat pūrvavijñāte pratyakṣe ca prayujyate |                    pramite ca prayuktatvād anuvādo 'dhikād vinā ||
  102. 5,6.102adṛṣṭapūrve tv ajñānaṃ sambandhapratyayo 'pi vā |                    sambandho na ca tasyārthaḥ, yo 'rthaḥ sa tv anyagocaraḥ ||
  103. 5,6.103parokṣe 'nanubhūte ca nābhidheye matir bhavet |                    parokṣaś cānubhūtaś ca yas tatra smṛtir iṣyate ||
  104. 5,6.104pramite ca pravṛttatvāt smṛter nāsti pramāṇatā |                    paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyam upajāyate ||
  105. 5,6.105tādātvikaparicchedaphalatvena pramāṇatā |                    pratyabhijñānavat kasmāt smṛter api na kalpyate ||
  106. 5,6.106yāvān pūrvaparicchinnas tāvān evāvadhāryate |                    smṛtyā tadanusāreṇa tadāsattve 'sya naiva dhīḥ ||
  107. 5,6.107padam abhyadhikābhāvāt smārakān na viśiṣyate |                    padādhikyaṃ bhavet kiñ cit tatpadasya na gocaraḥ ||<307>
  108. 5,6.108prāṇam anumānaṃ vā yady api syāt padānmitiḥ |                    vākyārthasyāgamārthatvād doṣo nāgamavādinām ||
  109. 5,6.109vākyārthe tu padārthebhyaḥ sambandhānubhavād ṛte |                    buddhir utpadyate tena bhinnā 'sāvakṣabuddhivat ||
  110. 5,6.110vākyādhikaraṇe cāsya hetoḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati |                    sarveṣāṃ ca paroktānāṃ vākyabuddhāvasiddhatā ||
  111. 5,6.111vākyeṣv adṛṣṭeṣv api sārthakeṣu padārthavinmātratayā pratītim |                    dṛṣṭvānumānavyatirekabhītāḥ kliṣṭāḥ padābhedavicāraṇāyām ||

Chapter 5,7 upamānapariccheda UMP

  1. 5,7.1kīdṛggavaya ityevaṃ pṛṣṭo nāgarikair yadi |                    bravītyāraṇyako vākyaṃ yathā gaur gavayas tathā ||<308>
  2. 5,7.2etasminn upamānatvaṃ prasiddhaṃ śabare punaḥ |                    tasyāgamābahirbhāvād anyathaivopavarṇitam ||
  3. 5,7.3puruṣapratyayenaiva tatrārthaḥ sampratīyate |                    tadīyavacanatvena tasmād āgama eva saḥ ||
  4. 5,7.4sadṛśād upajāyeta yā matiḥ sadṛśāntare |                    dhyānādismṛtitulyatvāt sā pramāṇaṃ kathaṃ bhavet ||
  5. 5,7.5deśakālādibhedena yathānyatra viśiṣyate |                    prameyaṃ naivam asty atra nagarasthānusārataḥ ||
  6. 5,7.6śrutātideśavākyānām āraṇye gavaye matiḥ |                    yā sopamānaṃ keṣāñ cid gosādṛśyānurañjitā ||
  7. 5,7.7pratyakṣo gavayas tāvat sādṛśyasmṛtir atra tu |                    nanu sādṛśyayukte 'rthe na smṛtir nendriyād gatiḥ ||<309>
  8. 5,7.8pūrvavākyārthavijñānān nādhikyaṃ gavaye yadi |                    smaraṇād aviśiṣṭatvāt saṅgater na pramāṇatā ||
  9. 5,7.9atha tv adhikatā kā cit pratyakṣādivaśād bhavet |                    yāvaddhīndriyasambandhas tat pratyakṣam iti sthitam ||
  10. 5,7.10syaryamāṇasya cāṃśasya vivedenāpramāṇatā |                    śrutātideśavākyatvaṃ na cātīvopayujyate ||
  11. 5,7.11ye 'pi hy aśrutatadvākyās teṣām api bhavaty ayam |                    pratyakṣadṛṣṭagotvānāṃ vane gavayadarśinām ||
  12. 5,7.12atha saṃjñānusandhānaṃ teṣāṃ nāstīti varṇyate |                    na nāma vastu tat tāvat sarvathā taiḥ pratīyate ||
  13. 5,7.13na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ prameyo 'tra tadeṣyate |<310>                    sādṛśyāvadhṛte vākye vākyād avagato hy asau ||
  14. 5,7.14na cāsya pratyabhijñānaṃ punarutpadyate vane |                    śaktyor atīndriyatvena smṛtir eva hi seṣyate ||
  15. 5,7.15śabdānuviddhabodhe 'pi pratyakṣam upapāditam |                    tasmāt sādṛśyayuktārthaḥ prameyo 'pūrva ucyatām ||
  16. 5,7.16vyavasāyātmakatvaṃ tu pratyakṣasya yadeṣyate |                    jātyādivat tadā tena sādṛśyaṃ kiṃ na mīyate ||
  17. 5,7.17pratyakṣābhāsam etat tu nirvikalpakavādinām |<311>                    prameyavastvabhāvāc ca nābhipretā pramāṇatā ||
  18. 5,7.18sādṛśyasyāpi vastutvaṃ na śakyam apabādhitum |                    bhūyo 'vayavasāmānyayogo jātyantarasya tat ||<312>
  19. 5,7.19sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra padmadalākṣivat |                    tat svāvayavasāmānyabhūmnā teṣā bhaviṣyati ||
  20. 5,7.20evaṃ jātiguṇadravyakriyāśaktisvadharmataḥ |                    ekaikadvitrisāmastyabhedād etasya citratā ||
  21. 5,7.21na dharmā eva sādṛśyaṃ bhūyastā vā tadāśrayā |                    bhūyastvavaddhi jātyādi sadṛśatvena dṛśyate ||
  22. 5,7.22yamayoḥ katham etac ced, dṛṣṭatvāt kim ihocyate |                    kva cid dhi bhūyasām etat kva cid alpīyasām api ||
  23. 5,7.23naitāvatā viśeṣeṇa vastutvaṃ tasya hīyate |<313>                    sāmānyāny api caitāni nāśīnyāśrayanāśataḥ ||
  24. 5,7.24anantāśrayayogāc ca na nāśo 'nyatra vidyate |                    tena sarvaṃ na sāmānyaṃ nityatvena prakalpyate ||
  25. 5,7.25sāmānyānāṃ na vā nāśaḥ kva cid abhyupagamyate |                    sarvasya hy āśrayaḥ kaś cid asti deśāntarādiṣu ||
  26. 5,7.26teṣāṃ bhūyas tayā cedaṃ sādṛśyam atiricyate |                    tāni vyastāni santy evaṃ pratyakṣe 'pi kva cit kva cit ||
  27. 5,7.27sadṛśāvayavatvaṃ tu yatra nāma pratīyate |                    tad apy avayavānāṃ syāt samānavayavāntaraiḥ ||
  28. 5,7.28evaṃ tāvad yato nāsti parābhedaprakalpanā |                    tataḥ paraṃ tu sāmānyaṃ bhavet sādṛśyavarjitam ||
  29. 5,7.29pradhānānāṃ tu sāmānyaṃ yatraikaṃ sampratīyate |                    sa eveti bhavet tatra tadbhede sadṛśatvadhīḥ ||<314>
  30. 5,7.30citrādau yatra sādṛśyaṃ sāmānyaṃ tatra kiṃ bhavet |                    tatrāpi pṛthivīvarṇaviśeṣādisamānatā ||
  31. 5,7.31rūpagandharasānāṃ ca kasya cit tulyatā kva cit |                    nāvaśyaṃ sarvasāmānyāt sādṛśyam upajāyate ||
  32. 5,7.32pṛthivyādiṣu caiteṣāṃ satām eva svabhāvataḥ |                    pariṇāmādibhir vyaktir yathādṛṣṭyavadhāryate ||
  33. 5,7.33na hi śaktyātmanā kiñ cid asajjama prapadyate |<315>                    dharmāṇāṃ na ca nānātvam, asti cāvāntararasthitiḥ ||
  34. 5,7.34vastutve sati cāsyaivaṃ sambandhasya ca cakṣuṣā |                    dvayor ekatra vā dṛṣṭeḥ pratyakṣatvaṃ na vāryate ||
  35. 5,7.35sāmānyavac ca sādṛśyam ekaikatra samāpte |                    pratiyoginyadṛṣṭe 'pi tasmāt tadupapadyate ||
  36. 5,7.36tatra yady api gāṃ smṛtvā tadbhānam upajāyate |                    sannidhergavayasthatvād bhaved indriyagocaraḥ ||
  37. 5,7.37tasmād yat smaryate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam |                    prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyaṃ vā tadanvatam ||<316>
  38. 5,7.38pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhe 'pi sādṛśye gavi ca smṛteḥ |                    viśiṣṭasyānyato 'siddher upamānanapramāṇatā ||
  39. 5,7.39pratyakṣe 'pi yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake |                    viśiṣṭaviṣayatvena nānumānāpramāṇatā ||
  40. 5,7.40yatra tv asadṛśād eva kalpayitvopajāyate |                    sādṛśyapratyayas tatra tadābhāsatvakalpanā ||
  41. 5,7.41bādhakapratyayāc caiṣā sādṛśyābhāsatā matā |                    yathā palālakūṭasya sādṛśyaṃ kuñjarādinā ||<317>
  42. 5,7.42samīpastho 'pi jānāti sādṛśyaṃ neti tatra hi |                    na bādhyate samīpādau yat tu sādṛśyam eva tat ||
  43. 5,7.43na caitasyānumānatvaṃ pakṣadharmādyasambhavāt |                    prāk prameyasya sādṛśyaṃ na dharmatvena gṛhyate ||
  44. 5,7.44gavaye gṛhyamāṇaṃ ca na gavām anumāpakam |                    pratijñārthaikadeśatvād gogatasya na liṅgatā ||
  45. 5,7.45gavayaś cāpy asambandhān na gor liṅgatvamṛcchati |                    sādṛśyaṃ na ca sarveṇa pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadanvayi ||
  46. 5,7.46ekasminn api dṛṣṭe 'rthe dvitīyaṃ paśyato vane |                    sādṛśyena sahaivāsmiṃs tadaivotpadyate matiḥ ||<318>
  47. 5,7.47śṛṅgitvāder athocyeta sambandhāl liṅgatā gavi |                    na, teṣāṃ gavayajñānavyāpāraṃ pratyupakṣayāt ||
  48. 5,7.48yadi tebhyaḥ pratītiḥ syān niḥsādṛśyaiva sā bhavet |                    na gauḥ śṛṅgādisadṛśī sadṛśī gavayena tu ||
  49. 5,7.49sadṛśapratyayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śṛṅgādipratyayāt param |                    gavayapratyayād eva gojñānam upajāyate ||
  50. 5,7.50sadṛśāvayavatve tu teṣām evopamā bhavet |                    na ca śṛṅgādayo yatra tatra gaur anumīyate ||
  51. 5,7.51itthaṃ cānumimānasya bhrāntajñānaṃ prasajyate |                    nagarasthe tu gojñānaṃ smaraṇān nātivartate ||<319>
  52. 5,7.52bhinnānumānād upameyam uktam, sauryādivākyair asahāyi dṛṣṭam |                    sādṛśyato 'gnyādiyutaṃ kathaṃ nu, pratyāyayed ity upayujyate naḥ ||
  53. 5,7.53pratinidhir api caivaṃ vrīhisādṛśyayogād bhavati tadapacāre yatra nīvārajātau |                    tad api phalam abhīṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇasyopamāyāḥ pratikṛtir api gauṇair bodhyate yatra cānyaiḥ ||
  54. 5,7.54matir api ca tathaiva drāgivotpadyate 'sminn |                    itaraviṣayabodhe 'saty apītthaṃ ca bādhaḥ ||

Chapter 5,8 arthāpattipariccheda AAP

  1. 5,8.1pramāṇaṣaṭkavijñāto yatrārtho nānyathā bhavet |                    adṛṣṭaṃ kalpayed anyaṃ sārthāpattir udāhṛtā ||
  2. 5,8.2dṛṣṭaḥ pañcabhir apy asmād bhedenoktā śrutodbhavā |                    pramāṇagrāhiṇītvena yasmāt pūrvavilakṣaṇā ||
  3. 5,8.3tatra pratyakṣato jñānād dāhād dahanaśaktatā |                    vahner anumitāt sūrye yānāt tacchaktiyogyatā ||
  4. 5,8.4śrutārthāpattir atraiva parastād abhidhāsyate |                    gavayopamitā yā gaus tajjñānagrāhyatā matā ||
  5. 5,8.5abhidhānaprasiddhyartham arthāpattyāvabodhitāt |                    śabde bodhakasāmarthyāt tannityatvaprakalpanam ||<321>
  6. 5,8.6abhidhā nānyathā sidhyed iti vācakaśaktatām |                    arthāpattyāvagamyaivaṃ tadananyagateḥ punaḥ ||
  7. 5,8.7arthāpattyantareṇaiva śabdanityatvaniścayaḥ |                    darśanasya parārthatvād ity asminn abhidhāsyate ||
  8. 5,8.8pramāṇābhāvanirṇītacaitrābhāvaviśeṣitāt |                    gehāc caitrabahirbhāvasiddhir yā tv iha darśitā ||
  9. 5,8.9tām abhāvotthitām anyām arthāpattim udāharet |                    pakṣadoṣeṣu cānyāsāmudāharaṇavistaraḥ ||
  10. 5,8.10abhāvāvagatāc caitrād bahirbhāvasya sūcanam |                    pakṣadharmādyanaṅgatvād bhinnaivāpy anumānataḥ ||
  11. 5,8.11bahirdeśaviśiṣṭe 'rthe deśe vā tadviśeṣite |                    prameye yo gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmas tv asau katham ||
  12. 5,8.12tadabhāvaviśiṣṭaṃ tu gṛhaṃ dharmo na kasyacit |                    gṛhābhāvaviśiṣṭas tu tadāsau na pratīyate ||
  13. 5,8.13gamyate tu gṛhaṃ tatra na ca caitraḥ pratīyate |<322>                    na cātrādarśanaṃ hetur yathābhāve 'bhidhāsyate ||
  14. 5,8.14tena veśmanyadṛṣṭatvād iti hetur na kalpyate |                    adarśanād abhāve ca prameyasyāvadhārite ||
  15. 5,8.15bahirbhāvamatir nāsau tenādarśanahetukā |                    caitrābhāvasya hetutvaṃ gehe 'bhāvaś ca saṃsthitaḥ ||
  16. 5,8.16pūrvaṃ na cāgṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ syāt prameyatā |                    na cātra bāhyadeśo vā caitro vā gṛhyate purā ||
  17. 5,8.17nadīpūreṇa yā vṛṣṭir upariṣṭāt pratīyate |                    deśe katham adṛṣṭe tu pakṣadharmatvasambhavaḥ ||
  18. 5,8.18vṛṣṭimatparadeśatvaṃ nadīpuravato 'tra tu |                    deśasya pratipadyante yadvārthāpattir eva sā ||<323>
  19. 5,8.19jīvataś ca gṛhābhāvaḥ pakṣadharmo 'tra kalpyate |                    tatsaṃvittir bahirbhāvaṃ na cābuddhvopajāyate ||
  20. 5,8.20agnimattānapekṣā tu dhūmavattā pratīyate |                    na tadgrahaṇavelāyām agnyadhīnaṃ hi kiñcana ||
  21. 5,8.21gehābhāvas tu yaḥ śuddho vidyamānatvavarjitaḥ |                    sa mṛteṣv api dṛṣṭatvād bahirvṛtter na sādhakaḥ ||
  22. 5,8.22vidyamānatvasaṃsṛṣṭagṛhābhāvadhiyānayā |                    gehād utkālitaś caitro vidyate bahir eva hi ||
  23. 5,8.23gehābhāvatvamātraṃ tu yat svatantraṃ pratīyate |                    na tāvatā bahirbhāvaś caitrasyaivāvadhāryate ||<324>
  24. 5,8.24siddhe sadbhāvavijñāne gehābhāvadhiyātra tu |                    gehād utkālitā sattā bahir evāvatiṣṭhate ||
  25. 5,8.25tenāsya nirapekṣasya vyabhicāro mṛtādinā |                    yasya tv avyabhicāritvaṃ na tato 'nyat pratīyate ||
  26. 5,8.26tasmāt pratyakṣato gehe caitrābhāve hy abhāvataḥ |                    jñāte yat sattvavijñānaṃ tad evedaṃ bahiḥ sthitam ||
  27. 5,8.27pakṣadharmātmalābhāya bahirbhāvaḥ praveśitaḥ |                    tadviśiṣṭo 'numeyaḥ syāt pakṣadharmānvayādibhiḥ ||
  28. 5,8.28pakṣadharmādivijñānaṃ bahiḥ sambodhato yadi |                    taiś ca tadbodhato 'vaśyam anyonyāśrayatā bhavet ||
  29. 5,8.29anyathānupapattau tu prameyānupraveśitā |                    tādrūpyeṇaiva vijñānān na doṣaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ||<325>
  30. 5,8.30avinābhāvitā cātra tadaiva parikalpyate |                    na prāg avadhṛtety evaṃ saty apy eṣā na kāraṇam ||
  31. 5,8.31gṛhābhāvabahirbhāvau na ca dṛṣṭau niyogataḥ |                    sāhitye 'pi pramāṇaṃ ca tayor anyan na vidyate ||
  32. 5,8.32anyathānupapattyaiva hy ekenānyat pratīyate |                    tathā na kalpyate tac cet sāhityaṃ na pratīyate ||
  33. 5,8.33tena sambandhavelāyāṃ sambandhyanyataro dhruvam |                    arthāpattyāvagantavyaḥ paścād asty anumānatā ||
  34. 5,8.34gṛhadvāri sthito yas tu bahirbhāvaṃ prakalpayet |                    yadaikasminn ayaṃ deśe na tadānyatra vidyate ||
  35. 5,8.35tadāpy avidyamānatvaṃ na sarvatra pratīyate |                    na caikadeśe nāstitvād vyāptir hetor bhaviṣyati ||<326>
  36. 5,8.36nanv atrāvidyamānatvaṃ gamyate 'nupalabdhitaḥ |                    sā cāprayatnasādhyatvād ekasthasyaiva sidhyati ||
  37. 5,8.37naitayānupalabdhyātra vastvabhāvaḥ pratīyate |                    taddeśāgamanāt sā hi dūrastheṣv asti satsv api ||
  38. 5,8.38gatvā gatvā tu tān deśān yady artho nopalabhyate |                    tato 'nyakāraṇābhāvād asann ity avagamyate ||
  39. 5,8.39nanu cāgnyādyabhāve 'pi dhūmādivyatirekiṇām |                    taddeśāgamanāt spaṣṭo vyatireko na sidhyati ||
  40. 5,8.40yasya vastvantarābhāvaḥ prameyas tasya duṣyati |                    mama tv adṛṣṭamātreṇa gamakaḥ sahacāriṇaḥ ||
  41. 5,8.41nanv evam itaratrāpi sambandho 'nupalabdhitaḥ |                    caitrābhāvasya bhāvena dṛṣṭatvād upapadyate ||<327>
  42. 5,8.42sāhitye mitadeśatvāt prasiddhe cāgnidhūmayoḥ |                    vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer gamakatvaṃ prakalpyate ||
  43. 5,8.43iha sāhityam evedam ekasya sahabhāvinaḥ |                    anantadeśavarttitvān na tāvad upapadyate ||
  44. 5,8.44nanu deśāntaraṃ śūnyaṃ caitreṇaivaṃ pratīyate |                    taddeśavyatiriktatvāt samīpasthitadeśavat ||
  45. 5,8.45viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ tadvad eva hi gamyate |                    samīpadeśabhinnatvāt caitrādhiṣṭhitadeśavat ||
  46. 5,8.46puruṣasya tu kārtsnyena yad ekatropalambhanam |                    tasyānyathā na siddhiḥ syād ity anyeṣv asya nāstitā ||<328>
  47. 5,8.47tenārthāpattipūrvatvam atra yatra ca kāraṇe |                    kāryādarśanataḥ śakter astitvaṃ sampratīyate ||
  48. 5,8.48kāryasya nanu liṅgatvaṃ na sambandhānapekṣaṇāt |                    dṛṣṭvā sambandhitāṃ caiṣā śaktir gamyeta nānyathā ||
  49. 5,8.49taddarśane tadānīṃ ca pratyakṣāder asambhavāt |                    arthāpatteḥ pramāṇatvaṃ trailakṣaṇyād vinā bhavet ||<329>
  50. 5,8.50anumānād abhinnatvān noktau jayaparājayau |                    vadhyaghātakabhāvena yau sarpanakulādiṣu ||
  51. 5,8.51pīno divā na bhuṅkte cety evamādivacaḥ śrutau |                    rātribhojanavijñānaṃ śrutārthāpattir ucyate ||
  52. 5,8.52tām arthagocarāṃ kecid apare śabdagocarām |                    kalpayanty āgamāc cainām abhinnāṃ pratijānate ||
  53. 5,8.53prāyaśaś cānayā vede vyavahāro vyavasthitaḥ |                    so 'vaidikaḥ prasajyeta yady eṣā bhidyate tataḥ ||
  54. 5,8.54vacanasya śrutasyaiva so 'py arthaḥ kaiścid āśritaḥ |                    tadarthopaplutasyānyair iṣṭo vākyāntarasya tu ||
  55. 5,8.55na tāvac chrūyamāṇasya vacaso 'rtho 'yam iṣyate |                    na hy anekārthatā yuktā vākye vācakatā tathā ||
  56. 5,8.56padārthānvayarūpeṇa vākyārtho hi pratīyate |                    na rātryādipadārthaś ca divāvākyena gamyate ||<330>
  57. 5,8.57na divādipadārthānāṃ saṃsargo rātribhojanam |                    na bhedo yena tadvākyaṃ tasya syāt pratipādakam ||
  58. 5,8.58anyārthavyāpṛtatvāc ca na dvitīyārthakalpanā |                    tasmād vākyāntareṇāyaṃ buddhisthena pratīyate ||
  59. 5,8.59tasya cāgamikatve 'pi yat tad vākyaṃ pratīyate |                    pramāṇaṃ tasya vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣādiṣu yad bhavet ||
  60. 5,8.60na hy anuccārite vākye pratyakṣaṃ tāvad iṣyate |                    nānumānaṃ na cedaṃ hi dṛṣṭaṃ tena saha kvacit ||
  61. 5,8.61yadi tv anupalabdhe 'pi sambandhe liṅgateṣyate |                    taduccāraṇamātreṇa sarvavākyamatir bhavet ||
  62. 5,8.62na cārthāpattigamyāni sarvaiḥ sarvavacāṃsi hi |                    sambaddhāny upalabdhāni yena teṣv anumā bhavet ||
  63. 5,8.63na ca sattānumānena viśeṣo vānumīyate |<331>                    iha vākyaviśeṣasya sattaiva tv avagamyate ||
  64. 5,8.64pūrvasiddhaḥ svatantro 'rthaḥ svatantreṇa viśeṣitaḥ |                    dharmādharmaviśiṣṭo 'tra nānumeyaḥ pratīyate ||
  65. 5,8.65atha śrutasya vākyasya mīyate tadviśiṣṭatā |                    tataḥ pakṣo 'bhyupetaḥ syād aprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
  66. 5,8.66kiñ ca liṅgāntarābhāvād etasya yadi liṅgatā |                    pratijñārthaikadeśatvaṃ padavat te prasajyate ||
  67. 5,8.67tadvad eva nirākāryā vacaso dharmadharmitā |                    nāgṛhīte hi taddharmo gṛhīte nānumeyatā ||
  68. 5,8.68kriyākārakasambandhād ṛte nāsti tu dharmatā |                    avācakatayā caitan na dharmo viṣayātmanā ||
  69. 5,8.69pratīter vācakatvaṃ cet prasaktānekaśaktitā |                    anumāviṣayotthaṃ tu dharmatvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet ||
  70. 5,8.70padārthair api tadvākyaṃ nāsambandhāt pratīyate |<332>                    sāmānyānyanyathāsiddher viśeṣaṃ gamayanti hi ||
  71. 5,8.71na tu vākyāntareṇaiṣāṃ vinā kiñcin na sidhyati |                    na cāpy anyaḥ prakāro 'sti tena vākyena saṅgatau ||
  72. 5,8.72athaitad vāci kalpyeta vākyam anyat tathaiva ca |                    prasaṅgāt tatra dūre 'pi nāsambandhāt pramucyate ||
  73. 5,8.73tataś ca prathamād eva varaṃ jñātum asaṅgatāt |                    anvayavyatirekau ca pratiṣedhyau pade yathā ||
  74. 5,8.74śrutavākyena sādṛśyaṃ nāśrutasyāsti kiñcana |                    tasmād anupamānatvam arthasyāpy anayā diśā ||
  75. 5,8.75upamānatvaliṅgatve vākyaṃ prati nivārite |                    arthe 'pi caivam eva syāt, <333> tasmāt pūrveṣv asambhavaḥ ||
  76. 5,8.76ataḥ śrutasya vākyasya yad arthapratipādanam |                    tadātmalābha eva syād vinā nety etad iṣyate ||
  77. 5,8.77etadarthād vinā nāyam ity arthaḥ kiṃ na kalpyate |                    vākyārthavac ca kiṃ nāyam āgamārthaḥ pratīyate ||
  78. 5,8.78savikalpakavijñānaiḥ śabdaḥ pūrvaṃ pratīyate |                    labdhaprayojane vākye paraṃ nāgamikaṃ ca naḥ ||<334>
  79. 5,8.79nanu cāsati sambandhe sati vānavadhārite |                    gamyajñānam idaṃ vākyaṃ prasajyetāpramāṇakam ||
  80. 5,8.80sambandhasya pramāṇatvaṃ sthitaṃ kiñceśvarājñayā |                    pratyakṣasya pramāṇatvaṃ kathaṃ vā saṅgater vinā ||
  81. 5,8.81astīndriyārthasambandhas tatra cen nānapekṣaṇāt |                    na hi pratyakṣavelāyāṃ sarveṇāsau nirūpyate ||
  82. 5,8.82yenāpi tu nirūpyeta paścād anubhavād asau |                    na syād eva pramāṇāṅgam asatā tulya eva saḥ ||
  83. 5,8.83aprāpyakāriṇī yeṣāṃ cakṣuḥśrotre ca te yathā |                    tajjñānasya pramāṇatvam icchanty evaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
  84. 5,8.84tasmād asattve sattve vā sambandhasya yad eva naḥ |                    jāyetābhaṅguraṃ jñānaṃ tasyaiva syāt pramāṇatā ||<335>
  85. 5,8.85na cāpy asyāḥ pramāṇatve kaścid vipratipadyate |                    bhedābhede visaṃvādaḥ kṛtas tatra ca nirṇayaḥ ||
  86. 5,8.86kṛte yatra ca sambandhād buddhir eva na jāyate |                    tatra ki kriyatāṃ so 'pi prāmāṇye naiva kāraṇam ||
  87. 5,8.87smṛtyā śrutir yā parikalpyate 'smin liṅgādibhir yā viniyojikā ca |                    phalādibhir yat paripūraṇaṃ ca sambandhadṛk tatra na kācid asti ||
  88. 5,8.88tat sarvam ityādy asamañjasaṃ syān na cediyaṃ syād anumānato 'nyā |                    evaṃsvabhāvāpy anumānaśabdaṃ labheta ced asti yathepsitaṃ naḥ ||

Chapter 5,9 abhāvapariccheda ABH

  1. 5,9.1pramāṇapañcakaṃ yatra vasturūpe na jāyate |<336>                    vastusattāvabodhārthaṃ tatrābhāvapramāṇatā ||
  2. 5,9.2vastvasaṅkarasiddhiś ca tatprāmāṇyasamāśrayā |                    kṣīre dadhyādi yan nāsti prāgabhāvaḥ sa ucyate ||
  3. 5,9.3nāstitā payaso dadhni pradhvaṃsābhāva iṣyate |                    gavi yo 'śvādyabhāvas tu so 'nyonyābhāva ucyate ||
  4. 5,9.4śiraso 'vayavā nimnā vṛddhikāṭhinyavarjitāḥ |                    śaśaśṛṅgādirūpeṇa so 'tyantābhāva ucyate ||
  5. 5,9.5kṣīre dadhi bhaved evaṃ dadhni kṣīraṃ ghaṭe paṭaḥ |                    śaśe śṛṅgaṃ pṛthivyādau caitanyaṃ mūrtir ātmani ||
  6. 5,9.6apsu gandho rasaś cāgnau vāyau rūpeṇa tau saha |                    vyomni saṃsparśitā te ca na ced asya pramāṇatā ||
  7. 5,9.7na ca syād vyavahāro 'yaṃ kāraṇādivibhāgataḥ |                    prāgabhāvādibhedena nābhāvo bhidyate yadi ||
  8. 5,9.8na cāvastuna ete syur bhedās tenāsya vastutā |<337>                    kāryādīnām abhāvaḥ ko yo 'bhāvaḥ kāraṇāditaḥ ||
  9. 5,9.9yadvānuvṛttivyāvṛttibuddhigrāhyo yatas tv ayam |                    tasmād gavādivad vastu, prameyatvāc ca gamyate ||
  10. 5,9.10na caupacārikatvaṃ vā bhrāntir vāpi yadṛcchayā |                    bhavaty ato na sāmānyaviśeṣātmakatā mṛṣā ||
  11. 5,9.11pratyakṣāder anutpattiḥ pramāṇābhāva ucyate |                    sātmanaḥ pariṇāmo vā vijñānaṃ vākyavastuni ||
  12. 5,9.12svarūpapararūpābhyāṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmake |                    vastuni jñāyate kaiś cid rūpaṃ kiñ cit kadā cana ||<338>
  13. 5,9.13yasya yatra yadodbhūtir jighṛkṣā vopajāyate |                    cetyate 'nubhavas tasy tena ca vyapadiśyate ||
  14. 5,9.14tasyopakārakatvena varttate 'śastadetaraḥ |                    ubhayor api saṃvittāv ubhayānugamo 'sti hi ||
  15. 5,9.15ayam eveti yo hy eṣa bhāve bhavati nirṇayaḥ |                    naiṣa vastvantarābhāvasaṃvittyanugamād ṛte ||<339>
  16. 5,9.16nāstīty api ca saṃvittir na vastvanugamād ṛte |                    jñānaṃ na jāyate kiñ cid upaṣṭambhanavarjitam ||
  17. 5,9.17pratyakṣādyavatāras tu bhāvāṃśo gṛhyate yadā |                    vyāpāras tadanutpatter abhāvāṃśe jighṛkṣite ||
  18. 5,9.18na tāvad indriyair eṣā nāstīty utpadyate matiḥ |<340>                    bhāvāṃśenaiva saṃyogo yogyatvādindriyasya hi ||
  19. 5,9.19nanu bhāvād abhinnatvāt samprayogo 'sti tena ca |                    na hy atyantam abhedo 'sti rūpādivad ihāpi naḥ ||
  20. 5,9.20dharmayor bheda iṣṭo hi dharmyabhede 'pi naḥ sthite |                    udbhavābhibhavātmatvād grahaṇaṃ cāvatiṣṭhate ||
  21. 5,9.21idam eva nimittaṃ ca vivekasya pratīyate |                    bhāvābhāvadhiyor akṣaiḥ sambandho 'kṣānapekṣaṇam ||
  22. 5,9.22rūpāder api bhedaṃ ca ke cid grāhakabhedataḥ |                    varṇayanti yathaikasya puṃsaḥ putrādirūpatām ||
  23. 5,9.23buddhimātrakṛto bhedo rūpādau nityam eva hi |<341>                    na ca deśādyabhinnānāṃ samudāyāvakalanā ||
  24. 5,9.24sadguṇadravyarūpeṇa rūpāder ekateṣyate |                    svarūpāpekṣayā caiṣāṃ parasparavibhinnatā ||
  25. 5,9.25yadi tadvadapekṣātra na syād bhedo 'tra naiva hi |                    sadasadrūpatā buddher bhaved anyataratra naḥ ||
  26. 5,9.26tatsambandhe sad ityevaṃ tadrūpatvaṃ pratīyate |                    nāsty atredam itīdaṃ tu tadasaṃyogahetukam ||<342>
  27. 5,9.27gṛhītvā vastusadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam |                    mānasaṃ nāstitājñānaṃ jāyate 'kṣānapekṣaṇāt ||<343>
  28. 5,9.28svarūpamātraṃ dṛṣṭvāpi paścāt kiñ cit smarann api |                    tatrānyanāstitāṃ pṛṣṭas tadaiva pratipadyate ||
  29. 5,9.29na cāpy atrānumānatvaṃ liṅgābhāvāt pratīyate |                    bhāvāṃśo nanu liṅgaṃ syāt, tadānīṃ nājighṛkṣaṇāt ||
  30. 5,9.30abhāvāvagater janma bhāvāṃśe hy ajighṛkṣite |<344>                    tasmin pratīyamāne tu nābhāve jāyate matiḥ ||
  31. 5,9.31na caiṣa prakṣadharmatvaṃ padavat pratipadyate |                    saha sarvair abhāvaiś ca bhāvo naikāntato gataḥ ||
  32. 5,9.32kva cid bhāve 'pi sadbhāvo jñāto yasya kadā cana |                    tasyābhāvo 'pi tatraiva kadā cid avagamyate ||
  33. 5,9.33yatrāpy adṛṣṭapūrvatvaṃ yadabhāvasya tatra ca |                    tadabhāvamatir dṛṣṭā sambandhe 'kṣānapekṣayā ||
  34. 5,9.34kasya cid yadi bhāvasya syād abhāvena kena cit |                    sambandhadarśanam, tatra sarvamānaṃ prasajyate ||
  35. 5,9.35gṛhīte 'pi ca bhāvāṃśe naivābhāve 'nyavastunaḥ |                    sarvatra matir ityevaṃ vyabhicārād aliṅgatā ||<345>
  36. 5,9.36sambandhe gṛhyamāṇe ca sambandhigrahaṇaṃ dhruvam |                    tatrābhāvamatiḥ kena pramāṇopajāyate ||
  37. 5,9.37tadānīṃ na hi liṅgena sambandhigrahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    tatrāvaśyam abhāvasya pramāṇāntarato gatiḥ ||
  38. 5,9.38pratyakṣāder anutpattir na tu liṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati |                    na viśeṣaṇasambandhas tasyāḥ sāmānyato bhavet ||
  39. 5,9.39na cāpy abhāvasāmānye pramāṇam upajāyate |                    vyabhicārād viśeṣās tu pratīyeran kathaṃ tayā ||<346>
  40. 5,9.40na cānavagataṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhyate ced asāv api |                    abhāvatvād abhāvena gṛhyetānyena hetunā ||
  41. 5,9.41sa cānyena grahītavyo nāgṛhīte hi liṅgatā |                    tadgṛhītir hi liṅgena syād anyenety anantatā ||
  42. 5,9.42liṅgābhāve tathaiva syād anavastheyam ity ataḥ |                    kvāpy asya syāt pramāṇatvaṃ liṅgatvena vinā dhruvam ||
  43. 5,9.43nāstīti dhīḥ phalaṃ caiṣā pratyakṣāder ajanmanaḥ |                    tasyaiva ca pramāṇatvam ānantaryāt pratīyate ||
  44. 5,9.44trilakṣaṇena yā buddhir janyate sānumeṣyate |                    na cānutpattirūpasya kāraṇāpekṣitā kva cit ||
  45. 5,9.45mānaṃ katham abhāvaś cet, prameyaṃ cāsya kīdṛśam |                    meyo yadvadabhavo hi mānam apy evam iṣyatām ||<347>
  46. 5,9.46bhāvātmake tathā meye nābhāvasya pramāṇatā |                    tathābhāvaprameye 'pi na bhāvasya pramāṇatā ||
  47. 5,9.47bhāvātmakasya mānatvaṃ na ca rājājñayā sthitam |                    paricchedaphalatvād dhi prāmāṇyaṃ syād dvayor api ||
  48. 5,9.48yadi cāsya pramāṇatvam abhāvatvena neṣyate |                    vastunaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ hi dṛṣṭam ity abhimānitā ||
  49. 5,9.49na liṅgatvaprameyatve bhavetāṃ tadvad eva hi |                    tathā sati ca pūrvokto vyavahāro na sidhyati ||
  50. 5,9.50pramāṇānām anutpatter nābhāvasyāpi dharmatā |                    yatrābhāvo 'sti tenāsyāḥ sambandho naiva vidyate ||
  51. 5,9.51yo na sannihitas tatra tasya dharmo bhaved iyam |                    na ca tasya prameyatvaṃ dharmadharmitvavarjanāt ||<348>
  52. 5,9.52abhāvena tu sambandho bhavet tadviṣayatvataḥ |                    tajjānād viṣayatvaṃ ca jñāne meyaṃ na vidyate ||
  53. 5,9.53saṃyogasamavāyādisambandho naiva vidyate |                    nāgṛhīte hi dharmatvaṃ gṛhīte siddhasādhanam ||
  54. 5,9.54abhāvaśabdavācyatvāt pratyakṣādeś ca bhidyate |                    pramāṇānām abhāvo hi prameyāṇām abhāvavat ||
  55. 5,9.55abhāvo vā pramāṇena svānurūpeṇa mīyate |                    prameyatvād yathā bhāvas tasmād bhāvātmakāt pṛthak ||
  56. 5,9.56karmāṇi sarvāṇi phalaiḥ samastaiḥ sarvair yathāvac ca yadaṅgakāṇḍaiḥ |                    na saṅgatānīha parasparaṃ ca nāṅgaṃ tadetat prabhavaṃ kratūnām ||
  57. 5,9.57yuktyāgamābhyām iti tarkito 'yaṃ pramāṇaṣaṭkaṃ pravibhajya bhāṣye |                    tato 'dhikaṃ yad dvayam iṣṭam anyair bhedo na tasyety api siddham etat ||<349>
  58. 5,9.58iha bhavati śatādau sambhavādyāsahasrānmatir aviyutabhāvāt sānumānād abhinnā |                    jagati bahu na tathyaṃ nityam aitihyam uktaṃ bhavati tu yadi satyaṃ nāgamād bhidyate tat ||

Chapter 5,10 citrākṣepavāda CAV

  1. 5,10.1paralokaphalāḥ pūrvam ākṣiptāś codanāḥ paraiḥ |                    idānīm aihikākṣepaḥ, <350> sūtrakāreṇa codyate ||
  2. 5,10.2citrāpaśuphalatvādiviṣayāś codaṇā mṛṣā |                    pratyakṣādyadhikāre 'pi tair arthāsaṅgatir yataḥ ||
  3. 5,10.3yadīdṛk tanmṛṣā dṛṣṭaṃ vipralipsor yathā vacaḥ |                    nadītīre phalānīti tatrādṛśyāni tāni cet ||
  4. 5,10.4na vā paśuphalā citrā svakāle tadadānaḥ |                    snānabhujyādivat te 'pi tatsādhyā na bhavanti vā ||
  5. 5,10.5tadutpattāvasadbhāvāt svarge tṛptisukhādivat |                    vaidharmyeṇobhayatrāpi bhavetāṃ sukham ardane ||
  6. 5,10.6ānantaryam ayuktaṃ cet, <351> na sāmarthyāvabodhanāt |                    śabdaikadeśabhūtena tena tat pratipāditam ||
  7. 5,10.7kālāntarānupādānāt karmasvābhāvyato 'pi ca |                    codyamānasya citrāder ānantaryaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
  8. 5,10.8atra tāvadasaṃvādo virodhaś cottarasya tu |                    svargayānaviruddho hi bhasmībhāvo 'tra dṛśyate ||
  9. 5,10.9yajñāyudhivaco mithyā pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ |                    sādharmyeṇa śilāvākyaṃ vaidharmyeṇāptabhāṣitam ||
  10. 5,10.10śarīrād yadi cānyaḥ syān nāsau yajñāyudhī bhavet |                    na cāsya yajamānatvaṃ sadbhāvo 'pi ca durlabhaḥ ||<352>
  11. 5,10.11yadi syād vidhiśabdo 'tra naivādarśanato bhavet |                    viśeṣo 'syeti bhedena nopāttaṃ syād idaṃ tataḥ ||
  12. 5,10.12vidhiśabde bhaviṣyattvaṃ phalasya parikalpya hi |                    virodhaparihāraḥ syād vartamāne 'pi nāsty asau ||
  13. 5,10.13phalaṃ ca na bhaved evaṃ bhasmībhāvād vidhāv api |                    tatsāmarthyena yā cānyā kalpanā tāṃ niṣedhati ||
  14. 5,10.14prāyaś caivamprakāratvam arthavādeṣu dṛśyate |                    mantreṣu ceti te sarve pakṣīkāryāḥ prayatnaḥ ||
  15. 5,10.15evaṃ saty agnihotrādivākyeṣv api mṛṣārthatā |                    vedavākyaikadeśatvāc citrādivacaneṣv api ||

Chapter 5,11 sambandhākṣepavāda SAV

  1. 5,11.1svapakṣasādhanaṃ tāvat na mṛṣā vaidikaṃ vacaḥ |                    svārthe vaktranapekṣatvāt padārthapadabuddhivat ||
  2. 5,11.2tatkṛtaḥ pratyayaḥ samyaṅ nityavākyodbhavatvataḥ |                    vākyabuddhivad eva atra pūrvoktāś cāpi hetavaḥ ||
  3. 5,11.3nityān śabdārthasambandhānāśrityoktena hetunā |                    svataḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyartham aprāmāṇye nir kṛte ||
  4. 5,11.4asambandhodbhavatvena paro mithyātvam abravīt |                    sambandho 'sti ca nityaś cety uktam autpattikādinā ||
  5. 5,11.5mithyā tv asya nirāsārthaṃ tatparair neṣyate dvayam |                    naiva cāsty atra sambandhaḥ kṛtako veti vakṣyate ||<354>
  6. 5,11.6asambhavena śeṣāṇāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ pariśiṣyate |                    asminn eva ca sambandhe pratītir laukiko dhruvā ||
  7. 5,11.7tanniṣedhamataḥ prāha na śabdo 'rthena saṅgataḥ |                    taddeśānantarādṛṣṭer vindhyo himavatā yathā ||
  8. 5,11.8evam artho dvayaṃ vāpi sādhanīyam asaṅgatam |                    kṣuretyādi ca siddhyarthahetor uktam athāparaḥ ||
  9. 5,11.9śaktirūpaṃ gṛhītvāha saṃśleṣo yadi vāryate |                    sambandhasiddhasādhyatvam atha sambandhamātrakam ||
  10. 5,11.10pitāputrādisambandhair anekāntaḥ prasajyate |                    ekabhūmyādisambandhād dṛṣṭānte sādhyahīnatā ||
  11. 5,11.11vācyavācakasambandhaniṣedhe lokabādhanam |                    virodhaś ca svavākyena na hi sambandhavarjitaiḥ ||
  12. 5,11.12pratijñārthaṃ padaiḥ śākyaḥ pratīpādayituṃ paraḥ |                    abhidhānakriyāyāṃ hi karmatvaṃ vācyasaṃśritam ||
  13. 5,11.13śabdānāṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā kartṛtvaṃ vā nirūpitam |<355>                    pratipattāv upādānāt sāhitye ca vivakṣite ||
  14. 5,11.14niyamyate yadekasyāṃ sambandhaḥ so 'rthaśabdayoḥ |                    tatra yady apy asambandhaḥ kārakāṇāṃ parasparam ||
  15. 5,11.15tathāpi yatkriyā tasyām upakāryopakāritā |                    sa kriyāsaṅgateḥ paścāt sambandhaḥ kīrtyate tayoḥ ||<356>
  16. 5,11.16na cātrāpy avinābhāva upayogīti sādhitam |                    saṃjñeti gamakatvaṃ cen na tadaṅgam iyaṃ bhavet ||
  17. 5,11.17gamayantīṃ śrutiṃ dṛṣṭvā kalpyate vyavahārataḥ |                    na caiṣā gamayatyarthaṃ sambandhe 'navadhārite ||
  18. 5,11.18tasmād gamakatā paścād dhūmāder iva jāyate |                    sānaṅgaṃ tadvad eva syād neyaṃ dhūmādibhiḥ samā ||
  19. 5,11.19nirūpite 'vinābhāve tatra tatkāritā hy asau |                    gamakatvena pūrvaṃ ca tatra notpadyate matiḥ ||
  20. 5,11.20iha vācakatāyāḥ prāṅ nāvinābhāvitāmatiḥ |                    yad eva ceha sambandhaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ pratipadyate ||
  21. 5,11.21tadaiva gamako 'syāyam iti nānyasvarūpataḥ |                    kathayanti kva cit tāvad boddhavyo 'smād ayaṃ tv iti ||
  22. 5,11.22kva cid vācaka ity evaṃ vācyo 'yam iti cocyate |                    kva cid uccaritācchabdād dṛṣṭvārthaviṣayāṃ kriyām ||<357>
  23. 5,11.23keṣāñ cit tatra boddhṛtvam anumānāt pratīyate |                    etenāsmād yataḥ śabdād artho 'yam avadhāritaḥ ||
  24. 5,11.24tena nūnam imau siddhau vācyavācakaśaktikau |                    itthaṃ vācakatā siddhā saṅkīrṇāpi tataḥ param ||
  25. 5,11.25anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ niṣkṛṣṭe 'rthe niyamyate |                    bahujātiguṇadravyakarmabhedāvalamvinaḥ ||
  26. 5,11.26pratyayāt sahasā jātā śrautalākṣaṇikātmakāt |                    na lokaḥ kāranābhāvān nirdhārayitum icchati ||
  27. 5,11.27balābalādisiddhyarthaṃ vākyajñāstu viviñcate |                    kakṣāntaritasāmānyaviśeṣeṣu hi durbalaḥ ||
  28. 5,11.28sāmānyavacanaḥ śabdo jāyate lakṣaṇābālāt |                    tenāvaśyaṃ vivektavyaṃ jāyate lakṣaṇābalāt ||
  29. 5,11.29kiyad vā nityasambandhād abhidheyena lakṣyate |<358>                    tatra prayogabāhulyāt tadviśeṣeṣv asatsv api ||
  30. 5,11.30prayogāt parasāmānye sati vācyaprayogataḥ |                    sāsnādyekārthasambandhigotvamātrasya vācakaḥ ||
  31. 5,11.31gośabda iti vijñānam anvayavyatirekajam |                    tasmād gamakataivādau abhidhāyakatā punaḥ ||
  32. 5,11.32tannimitteti sambandhaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitvalakṣaṇaḥ |                    sambandhaniyamo 'yaṃ tu yā 'vinābhāvitocyate ||<359>
  33. 5,11.33sambandhagrahaṇāt pūrva yasmān na gamayaty ataḥ |                    gavāder nābhidhāśaktir devadattapade yathā ||
  34. 5,11.34yathaiva gamakaḥ śabdo vyavahārāt pratīyate |                    tathaiva śaktivijñānaṃ tasyopāyo 'vagamyate ||
  35. 5,11.35svarūpagrahaṇaṃ cāsya yathā vyāpriyate phale |                    tathā sambandhivijñānaṃ nāśaktis tatkṛtā bhavet ||
  36. 5,11.36yatsādhakatamatvena kasya cit kiñ cid ucyate |                    tasyānugrāhakāpekṣā na svaśaktivighātinī ||
  37. 5,11.37na hi tat kāraṇaṃ loke vede vā kiñ cid īdṛśam |                    itikartavyatāsādhye yasya nānugrahe 'rthitā ||
  38. 5,11.38pratyātmaniyatatvāc ca yathaiva karaṇaṃ bhavet |                    bāhyāntaravibhāgena kva cit syād vā vivakṣayā ||
  39. 5,11.39udvigno hy andhakāreṇa kaś cid evaṃ bravīty api |                    kiṃ cakṣuṣā mamaitena dṛṣṭaṃ dīpena yanmayā ||<360>
  40. 5,11.40nityavṛttau tu nāndhānāṃ dṛṣṭir dīpaśatair api |                    rūpādidarśane yasmāt tasmāc cakṣuḥ prakāśakam ||
  41. 5,11.41śarīrātmamanoyogād asādhāraṇātābalāt |                    vijñānāsattibhāvāc ca cakṣuḥ kāraṇam iṣyate ||
  42. 5,11.42tathaivehāpi sambandhajñānam aṅgaṃ prasiddhitaḥ |                    gauravāt karaṇatvena mataṃ cet kena vāryate ||
  43. 5,11.43yathā cakṣur itīdaṃ tu vyabhicāritvam ucyate |                    devadatte 'pi cāvyaktāṃ śaktim icchanti yuktitaḥ ||
  44. 5,11.44prakāśe 'vasthite bāhye nāndho rūpaṃ pratīyate |                    phalānantaryataś cāpi cakṣuḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||
  45. 5,11.45puruṣādhīnavijñānas tebhyaḥ prāganirūpitaḥ |                    yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ sa ceṣṭaś ced dhruvaṃ kṛtaḥ ||<361>
  46. 5,11.46bhinnadeśādyadhiṣṭhānād yathā rajjughaṭādiṣu |                    samaṃ nāsty anayoḥ kiñ cit tenāsaṅgatatā svataḥ ||

Chapter 5,12 sphoṭavāda SPH

  1. 5,12.1ādhārātmani viñāte sukham ādheyabodhanam |                    tasyaiva tāvat prastāvād atha gaur ity ato 'bravīt ||
  2. 5,12.2pratyakṣe 'pi visaṃvādo yeṣāṃ kaḥ svayam uttaram |                    tebhyo dadyād iti jñātvā vṛddhānāṃ matam abravīt ||<362>
  3. 5,12.3tatrārthapratyayadvāraṃ kṛtaṃ śabdanirūpaṇam |                    yair āsatāṃ tu te tāvat pratyakṣeṇa parīkṣyate ||
  4. 5,12.4pratyakṣaṃ nāsamarthaṃ nastena cārthe 'vadhārite |                    na hetur balavān anyaḥ parīkṣyeta yatas tataḥ ||
  5. 5,12.5tasmāc chrotraparicchinno yady arthaṃ gamayen na vā |                    sarvathā tasya śabdatvaṃ lokasiddhaṃ na hīyate ||
  6. 5,12.6yadi tv arthagatau śaktir na syād asya tataḥ punaḥ |                    vastvantaraṃ prakalpyeta vinā śabdaprasiddhitaḥ ||
  7. 5,12.7agnyādīn gamayanto 'pi śabdā dhūmādayo na hi |                    na vā 'pratyāyakatvāt syād ekavarṇeṣv aśabdatā ||
  8. 5,12.8na ca prāgarthavijñānāś chotragrāhye na śabdadhīḥ |                    na cārthajñānataḥ paścād aśrautre 'pi ca śabdatā ||
  9. 5,12.9parasparānapekṣāś ca śrotrabuddhyā svarūpataḥ |                    varṇā evāvagamyante na pūrvāparavastunī ||<363>
  10. 5,12.10alpīyasāpi yatnena śabdam uccaritaṃ matiḥ |                    yadi vā gṛhṇāti varṇaṃ vā sakalaṃ sphuṭam ||
  11. 5,12.11pṛthaṅ na copalabhyante varṇasyāvayavāḥ kva cit |                    na ca varṇeṣv anusyūtā dṛśyante tantuvat paṭe ||
  12. 5,12.12teṣām anupalabdheś ca na jñātā liṅgasaṅgatiḥ |                    nāgamas tatparaś cāsti nādṛṣṭe copamā kva cit ||
  13. 5,12.13na cāpy anupapattiḥ syād varṇasyāvayavair vinā |                    yathānyāvayavānāṃ hi vināpy avayavāntaraiḥ ||
  14. 5,12.14pratyakṣeṇāvabuddhaś ca varṇo 'vayavavarjitaḥ |                    kiṃ na syād, vyomavac cātra liṅgaṃ tadrahitā matiḥ ||
  15. 5,12.15tadvac cāsyaikabuddhitvād deśabhede 'py abhinnatā |                    nanu bhedamatir na syāt, <364> tavāpy ekatvadhīḥ kutaḥ ||
  16. 5,12.16sāmānyeṣu mamaikā dhīs tadvyaktiṣu ca bhedadhīḥ |                    na hīṣṭaṃ bhedamātraṃ hi na syād ekatvadhīr yataḥ ||
  17. 5,12.17vyaktes tāvan na sāmānyaṃ bhinnarūpaṃ pratīyate |                    varṇeṣv anyatra śabdatvān nānyac ced varṇa eva saḥ ||
  18. 5,12.18sa eveti matir nāpi sādṛśyam, na ca tat kva cit |                    vināvayavasāmānyād varṇeṣv avayavā na ca ||
  19. 5,12.19pratyakṣaviṣayatvāc ca nānyāpoho 'pi yujyate |                    vācakaś cātra liṅgaṃ vā na tadānīṃ pratīyate ||
  20. 5,12.20gakārādiṣu sāmānyaṃ śabdatvaṃ kalpyate yathā |                    gotvaṃ ca śābaleyādau tathaitat kiṃ na kalpyate ||
  21. 5,12.21śābaleyagakāradīn niṣpannān vyaktirūpataḥ |                    sāmānyadhīr na gṛhṇātīty ato jātir apīṣyate ||
  22. 5,12.22na tu drutādibhede 'pi niṣpannā sampratīyate |                    gavyaktyantaravyāvṛttā gavyaktir aparā sphuṭā ||
  23. 5,12.23tenaikatvena varṇasya buddhir ekopajāyate |<365>                    viśeṣabuddhisadbhāvo bhaved vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
  24. 5,12.24yathaiva tava gatvādi gamyamānaṃ drutādibhiḥ |                    viśeṣair api nānekam evaṃ varṇo 'pi no bhavet ||
  25. 5,12.25tvayāpi vyañjakavyaktibhedād bhedo 'bhyupeyate |                    mamāpi vyañjakair nādair bhedabuddhir bhaviṣyati ||
  26. 5,12.26tena yat prārthyate jāte tad varṇād eva labhyate |                    vyaktilabhyaṃ ca nādebhya iti gatvādidhīr yathā ||
  27. 5,12.27kalpayitvāpi tatpaścād vibhutvaikatvanityatāḥ |                    pratyekavṛttitā cāsya bhaveyur mahataḥ śramāt ||
  28. 5,12.28dvayasiddhas tu varṇātmā nityatvādi yathaiva ca |                    kalpitasyeṣyate tadvat siddhasyaivābhyupeyatām ||<366>
  29. 5,12.29pratyekasamavāye ca kleśo naiva bhaviṣyati |                    vyañjaneṣu ca dhībhedo naiva tādṛk pratīyate ||
  30. 5,12.30dṛśyate 'janurāgeṇa bhedo yo nāma, tatra naḥ |                    vivedo 'sty eva na hy eṣa kevalānāṃ pratīyate ||
  31. 5,12.31akṣv apy evaṃ paropādhir drutādipratyayo yathā |                    varṇā ''śritatvād varṇatvavyañjanapratyayo yathā ||
  32. 5,12.32gakāro 'tyantaniṣkṛṣṭagatvādhāro na gamyate |                    gānyabuddhyanirūpyatvāt paraiḥ kalpitagatvavat ||
  33. 5,12.33avastutvena sādhyatvān niṣedhād dhetusādhyayoḥ |                    sapakṣe 'nyatarāsiddhir na doṣāyātra jāyate ||
  34. 5,12.34varṇatvāc cāpi sādhyo 'yaṃ yakārādivad eva ca |                    vyatirekasya cādṛṣṭer nātra dṛṣṭaṃ nirvartakam ||<367>
  35. 5,12.35gotvādivāraṇe tv eva dṛṣṭabādhaḥ sphuṭo bhavet |                    nānyathā hi matis tatra syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
  36. 5,12.36na cāpy atraikavastutve bhedo vyañjakabhedataḥ |                    na piṇḍavyatirekeṇa vyañjako 'tra dhvanir yathā ||
  37. 5,12.37piṇḍavyaṅgyaiva gotvādir jātir nityaṃ pratīyate |                    tena bhinneṣu piṇḍeṣu jātir ekā pratīyate ||
  38. 5,12.38nanu yasya dvayaṃ śrotraṃ tasya buddhidvayaṃ bhavet |                    bhavato 'tīndriyatvāt tu kathaṃ nādair viśeṣadhīḥ ||
  39. 5,12.39nādena saṃskṛtāc chrotrād yadā śabdaḥ pratīyate |                    tadupaśleṣas tat asya bodhaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
  40. 5,12.40naiva vā grahaṇaṃ teṣāṃ śabde buddhis tu tadvaśāt |<368>                    saṃskārānukṛteḥ so 'pi mahatvādyavabudhyate ||
  41. 5,12.41madhuraṃ tiktarūpeṇa śvetaṃ pītatayā tathā |                    gṛhṇanti pittadoṣeṇa viṣayaṃ bhrāntacetasaḥ ||
  42. 5,12.42tathā vegena dhāvanto nāvyārūḍhāś ca gacchataḥ |                    parvatādīn vijānanti bhrameṇa bhramataś ca tān ||
  43. 5,12.43maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragabuddhibhiḥ |                    vyaktyalpatvamahattvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ ca tadāśrtayam ||
  44. 5,12.44gṛhṇanti yadvadetāni nimittagrahaṇād vinā |                    vyañjakasthamabudhvaiva vyaṅgye bhrāntir bhaviṣyati ||
  45. 5,12.45varṇāntaratvam evāhuḥ ke cid dīrghapluptādiṣu |                    na hi drutādivat tatra prayoho nāntarīyakaḥ ||
  46. 5,12.46tathā ca sati sāmānyaṃ triṣvatvaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate |                    sāmānyakalpanā tv anyair na yuktety abhidhīyate ||<369>
  47. 5,12.47atvam ity ucyamānaṃ hi na dīrghaplutayor bhavet |                    ātvaṃ na hrasvaplutayos traimātryaṃ na ca pūrvayoḥ ||
  48. 5,12.48sarvasādhāraṇatvena tad vijñātuṃ na śakyate |                    pratyekaṃ śābaleyādirūpe gotvaṃ yathā sphuṭam ||
  49. 5,12.49avarṇakulaśabdo 'pi sthānasāmyād vanādivat |                    samudāyārthavācīti na jātivacano bhavet ||
  50. 5,12.50svato hrasvādibhedas tu nityavāde virudhyate |                    sarvadā yasya sadbhāvaḥ sa kathaṃ mātrikaḥ svayam ||
  51. 5,12.51tasmād uccāraṇaṃ tasya mātrākālaṃ pratīyate |                    dvimātraṃ vā trimātraṃ ā na varṇo mātrikaḥ svayam ||
  52. 5,12.52dīrghāder nanv anaṅgatvaṃ vācakādharmato bhavet |                    itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇā na pratipādakāḥ ||
  53. 5,12.53yādṛśāt pūrvadṛṣṭo 'sāv artho gamyate tādṛśāt |                    bhrāntyā kathaṃ pratītiś cet, <370> nāsāv artham iti prati ||
  54. 5,12.54yathāśvādijavaḥ puṃsāṃ kāryāṅgatvaṃ prakalpayet |                    paradharmo 'pi varṇānāṃ dhvanidharmās tathaiva naḥ ||
  55. 5,12.55nanu dīrghādyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet |                    ānupūrvīvad evāsya parihāro bhaviṣyati ||
  56. 5,12.56tathodāttādibhedānāṃ saṃskāravaśagā matiḥ |                    teṣāṃ dīrghādivad bhedo na kadā cit pratīyate ||
  57. 5,12.57tatraikavarṇarūpatve bhedo 'pi syād drutādivat |<371>                    nātra varṇāntaravyaktir iva dhvanyantarodbhavaḥ ||
  58. 5,12.58ta eva mṛdutīvratvaśīghratvādisamanvitāḥ |                    abhede cāpi varṇasya dhvanīnāṃ dviprakāratā ||
  59. 5,12.59ke cit svarūpabodhārthāḥ ke cid bodhānuvartinaḥ |                    yugapatkramarūpeṇa saṃskārotpādahetavaḥ ||
  60. 5,12.60tatra dīrghādibodhaḥ syāt pūrveṣāṃ pracayo yadā |                    varṇātmaiva hi kālena tāvatā taiḥ pratīyate ||
  61. 5,12.61yugapatpracitais taiś ca syād udāttādikalpanā |                    pracaye tv itareṣāṃ syād vatibhedo drutādikaḥ ||<372>
  62. 5,12.62varṇātmanyavabuddhe 'pi tadrūpām eva te matim |                    śanair utpādayanti, iti nānyo varṇaḥ pratīyate ||
  63. 5,12.63vyaktyākṛtikṛto bhedo yady apy ekāntato bhavet |                    varṇeṣu jaimineḥ pakṣas tathāpi na virudhyate ||
  64. 5,12.64nityatvayatnaḥ sarvo 'pi gatvādiṣu bhaviṣyati |                    gakārādivacaś caitat teṣv eva na virotsyate ||
  65. 5,12.65vicchinnayatnavyaṅgyaiś ca nityaiḥ sarvagatair api |                    vyatiriktapadārambho varṇair nātropapadyate ||
  66. 5,12.66anārabdhe ca gośabde gośabdatvaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |                    varṇasāmānyavac cāpi na tatkalpanam arhati ||<373>
  67. 5,12.67varṇātmanām abhedāc ca siddhā sāmānyadhīr api |                    samudāyo 'pi tebhyo 'syo vāraṇīyo 'nayā diśā ||
  68. 5,12.68abhedasamudāyas tu teṣāṃ dharmo na duṣyati |                    teṣām asti hi sāmarthyam arthapratyāyanaṃ prati ||
  69. 5,12.69yāvanto yādṛśo ye ca yadarthapratipādane |                    varṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathivāvabodhakāḥ ||
  70. 5,12.70teṣāṃ tu guṇabhūtānām arthapratyāyanaṃ prati |                    sāhityam ekakartrādikramaś cāpi vivakṣitaḥ ||
  71. 5,12.71kartraikatve nimitte ca krame sati niyāmakam |                    prayuñjānasya yat pūrvaṃ vṛddhebhyaḥ kramadarśanam ||<374>
  72. 5,12.72yaugapadyaṃ tv aśakyatvān naiva teṣām ihāśritam |                    kartṛbhedaś ca tatra syāt, na caivaṃ dṛśyate 'bhidhā ||
  73. 5,12.73yugapad dṛśyasāmarthyā naiva śaktāḥ krame yathā |                    bhāvās tathā krame śaktā yaugapadye na śaknuyuḥ ||
  74. 5,12.74dṛṣṭaś ca pūrṇamāsādeḥ kramaḥ saṃhatyakāriṇaḥ |                    abhyāsānāṃ ca loke 'pi svādhyāyagrahaṇādiṣu ||
  75. 5,12.75sādhanāditrayāṇāṃ ca vyāpārasyaikakālatā |                    sarvatrāstīti neha syād upālambhaḥ kramaṃ prati ||
  76. 5,12.76niṣpannā eva dṛśyante vyāpārāḥ sarva eva hi |                    sūkṣmā vyāpārabhedās tu dṛśyate na kadā cana ||<375>
  77. 5,12.77ekasādhanasāṃsthāś ca vyāpārāvayavā yadā |                    svarūpato nirīkṣyante yaugapadyam asat tadā ||
  78. 5,12.78kiṃ punar bahavo bhinnā bhinnasādhanasaṃśritāḥ |                    bhaveyur yaugapadyena vyāpārāḥ kramavartinaḥ ||
  79. 5,12.79yadā tv ādyaparispandād prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ |                    kriyā pūrvaparībhūtā lakṣyate varttate tadā ||
  80. 5,12.80tenātrāpi vivakṣātaḥ prabhṛtyā 'rthāvabodhanāt |                    sākalyenekṣyamāṇe syād vyāpāre varttamānatā ||
  81. 5,12.81pratyekaṃ ye punas tatra vyāpārās tannirūpaṇam |                    phalāniṣpattito na syān nāstitvaṃ na ca tāvatā ||
  82. 5,12.82phalānumeyatāyāṃ ca vyāpārasya phalaṃ prati |                    kārakāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ vyāpāre vartamānatā ||<376>
  83. 5,12.83avaśyam bhāvinī nityaṃ pratyāsattiś ca kasya cit |                    na tāvatā vyapetatvāt itareṣām anaṅgatā ||
  84. 5,12.84dvyantaraikāntaratvena gakārau kārayor dhruvam |                    arthaṃ pratyāyane śaktis tatra sthau gamakau yataḥ ||
  85. 5,12.85yathā visarjanīyasya vyavadhāne na śaktatā |                    tathaivetarayoḥ śaktir ānantarye na vidyate ||
  86. 5,12.86na ca yatraikaśo 'śaktis tatra sarveṣv aśaktatā |                    tathā hy aṅgāni dṛśyante śālyādivahanādiṣu ||
  87. 5,12.87śaktis tatrāsti kā cid dhi vahane sā samṛddhyate |                    saṅghātena tu varṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ kā cidīkṣyate ||
  88. 5,12.88na hy arthāvayavaḥ kaś cit pratyekaṃ taiḥ pratīyate |                    samastasyātha vā kaś cid bodhaleśo 'tra jāyate ||
  89. 5,12.89rathasyāpi tu yat kāryaṃ śālyādivahanaṃ na tat |<377>                    pratyekaṃ dṛśyate kiñ cin manāg api yathehitam ||
  90. 5,12.90atha yatkiñcid ucyeta vahane tad ihāpi naḥ |                    svātmapratyayahetutvaṃ varṇeṣv arthe 'pi vā kva cit ||
  91. 5,12.91yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥ |                    so 'pi paryanuyogena vaivaitena vimucyate ||
  92. 5,12.92tatrāpi prativarṇaṃ hi padasphoṭo na gamyate |                    na cāvayavaśo vyaktis tadabhāvān na cātra śrīḥ ||
  93. 5,12.93pratyekaṃ cāpy aśaktānāṃ samudāye 'py aśaktayā |                    tatra yaḥ parihāras te sa no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||<378>
  94. 5,12.94sadbhāvavyatirekau ca tathāvayavavarjanam |                    tavādhikaṃ bhavet tasmād yatno 'sāv arthabuddhiṣu ||
  95. 5,12.95nānyathānupapattiś ca bhaved arthamatiṃ prati |                    tad evāsyā nimittaṃ syāj jāyate yadanantaram ||
  96. 5,12.96sā ca varṇadvayajñāne 'tīte 'ntyajñānataḥ parā |                    bhavatītīdṛg evāsyā nimittam avakalpate ||
  97. 5,12.97vinā saṃskārakalpena tadanantaravṛttitaḥ |                    kṛtānugrahasāmarthyo varṇo 'ntyaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
  98. 5,12.98eṣa eva tu saṃskāra iti ke cit pracakṣate |                    adṛṣṭakalpanātītaṃ tāvan mātraṃ hi dṛśyate ||
  99. 5,12.99atha vā vāsanaivāstu saṃskāraḥ, sarva eva hi |                    dṛḍhajñānagṛhīte 'rthe saṃskāro 'stīti manvate ||<379>
  100. 5,12.100tasyārthabuddhihetutve visaṃvādo 'sya nirṇaye |                    tadbhāvabhāvitāhetur anyatreva pratīyate ||
  101. 5,12.101saṃskāre niṣpramāṇe tu pūrvavṛttattvakalpanam |                    niṣpramāṇakam eveti nānugrahaphalaṃ bhavet ||
  102. 5,12.102yady api smṛtihetutvaṃ saṃskārasya vyavasthitam |                    kāryāntareṣu sāmarthyaṃ na tasya pratiṣidhyate ||
  103. 5,12.103tena saṃskārasadbhāvo nānenaivaṃ prakalpyate |                    tasyārthabuddhihetutvam adṛṣṭaṃ kevalaṃ kṛtam ||
  104. 5,12.104śabdapakṣe 'pi tac caitad adṛṣṭatvān na mucyate |                    kāryabodhanaśaktatvaṃ tulyaṃ saṃskāraśabdayoḥ ||
  105. 5,12.105kṣīṇārthāpattir evaṃ ca na sphoṭaṃ parikalpayet |                    saṃskārakalpanā pūrvam avaśyam bhāvinī hi te ||
  106. 5,12.106dhvanibhyo 'py aparas tāvan neṣyetārthamatiṃ prati |                    te vā yady upalabhyeran varṇāḥ pratyakṣato na ca ||<380>
  107. 5,12.107varṇānāṃ yaugapadyena yadi cāvaśyam arthitā |                    nityatvāt sarvadā tat syān na tu kāraṇatā tathā ||
  108. 5,12.108itthaṃ kramagṛhītānāṃ yugapad yātha vā parā |                    sthitiḥ sā kāraṇaṃ tu syān nityam arthadhiyaṃ prati ||
  109. 5,12.109yad vā pratyakṣataḥ pūrvaṃ kramajñāneṣu yat param |                    samastavarṇavijñānaṃ tadarthajñānakāraṇam ||
  110. 5,12.110tatra jñāne ca varṇānāṃ yaugapadyaṃ pratīyate |                    nāvaśyaṃ yaugapadyena pratyakṣasthena tad bhavet ||
  111. 5,12.111citrarūpāṃ cā tāṃ buddhiṃ sadasadvarṇagocarām |                    ke cid āhur yathā varṇo gṛhyate 'ntaḥ pade pade ||
  112. 5,12.112antyavarṇe 'pi vijñāte pūrvasaṃskārakāritam |                    smaraṇaṃ yaugapadyena sarveṣv anye pracakṣate ||
  113. 5,12.113sarveṣu caivam artheṣu mānasaṃ sarvavādinām |                    iṣṭaṃ samuccayajñānaṃ kramajñāneṣu satsv api ||<381>
  114. 5,12.114na cet tadābhyupeyeta kramadṛṣṭeṣu naiva hi |                    śatādirūpaṃ jāyeta tatsamuccayadarśanam ||
  115. 5,12.115tena śrotramanobhyāṃ syāt kramād varṇeṣu yady api |                    pūrvajñānaṃ parastāt tu yugapat smaraṇaṃ bhavet ||
  116. 5,12.116tadārūḍhās tato varṇā na dūre 'rthāvabodhanāt |                    śabdārthamatis tena laukikair abhidhīyate ||
  117. 5,12.117citrabuddhyānayā bhrāntyā varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |                    paścād gaur iti vijñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ kaiś cid iṣyate ||
  118. 5,12.118vailakṣaṇyaṃ tu tasyeṣṭam ekaikajñānataḥ sphuṭam |                    varṇarūpāvabodhāt tu na tadarthāntaraṃ bhavet ||
  119. 5,12.119yadi cārthāntaratvaṃ syād ekaikasmād trayasya tat |                    varṇatrayaparityāge buddhir nānyatra jāyate ||
  120. 5,12.120gaur ity ekamatitvaṃ tu naivāsmābhir nivāryate |                    tadgrāhyaikārthatābhyāṃ ca śabde syād ekatāmatiḥ ||<382>
  121. 5,12.121śaidhyād alpāntaratvāc ca gośabde sābhaved api |                    devadattādiśabdeṣu sphuṭo bhedaḥ pratīyate ||
  122. 5,12.122na gauṇaḥ śabda ity evaṃ granthasambandhanaṃ bhavet |                    asy akṣareṣu hetutvaṃ tatparaṃ vacanaṃ hi tat ||
  123. 5,12.123śabdād iti ca hetutvaṃ pañcamyātrābhidhīyate |                    bhavatpakṣe 'pi caikāntāj jñānena vyavadhir bhavet ||
  124. 5,12.124gauṇo 'nyathā prasiddho vā prayujyetānyathā yadi |                    na cānyādṛṅnimittatvaṃ kasya cit sampratīyate ||
  125. 5,12.125svavyāpāravyavāyo hi sarvasminn eva kārake |                    dṛṣṭo vyāpāra īdṛk tu śabdasyety avyavetatā ||
  126. 5,12.126gakārāder yadā cānyo na loke śabda ucyate |                    tadā tasmāt pratīte 'rthe śabdād iti kathaṃ bhavet ||<383>
  127. 5,12.127śabdajñānādisaṃskāravyaktasphoṭakṛte 'tha vā |                    pratyaye śabdajanyatvam iti gauṇaṃ prasajyate ||
  128. 5,12.128saṃskārajananārthaṃ ca na śabdoccāraṇaṃ matam |                    arthapratītim uddiśya prayuktasya kramādayam ||
  129. 5,12.129tasmāt tādarthyataḥ śabdaḥ phalena vyapadiśyate |                    samuccayāvabodhe tu vyavadhānaṃ na kena cit ||
  130. 5,12.130yadi cāpūrvasaṃskāra itikartavyateṣyate |                    varṇo 'ntyo gamakas tasya śabdatvān mudhyatā bhavet ||
  131. 5,12.131varṇā vā dhvanayo vāpi sphoṭaṃ na padavākyayoḥ |                    vyañjanti vyañjakatvena yathā dīpaprabhādayaḥ ||
  132. 5,12.132sattvād ghaṭādivac ceti sādhanāni yathāruci |                    laukikavyatirekeṇa kalpite 'rthe bhavanti hi ||
