  133. 5,12.133nārthasya vācakaḥ sphoṭo varṇebhyo vyatirekataḥ |                    ghaṭāvivat, na dṛṣṭena virodho dharmasiddhitaḥ ||<384>
  134. 5,12.134pratiṣedhet tu yo varṇān tajjñānānantarodbhavān |                    dṛṣṭabādho bhavet tasya śaśicandraniṣedhavat ||
  135. 5,12.135varṇotthā vārthadhīreṣā tajjñānānantarodbhavā |                    yedṛśī sā tadutthā hi dhūmāder iva bahnidhīḥ ||
  136. 5,12.136dīpavad vā gakārādir gavādeḥ pratipādakaḥ |                    dhruvaṃ pratīyamānatvāt, tatpūrvaṃ pratipādanāt ||
  137. 5,12.137varṇātiriktaḥ pratiṣidhyamānaḥ padeṣu mandaṃ phalam ādadhāti |                    kāryāṇi vākyāvayavāśrayāṇi satyāni katuṃ kṛta eṣa yatnaḥ ||

Chapter 5,13 ākṛtivāda AKV

  1. 5,13.1ākṛtivyatirikte 'rthe sambandho nityatāsya ca |                    na sidhyetām iti jñātvā tad vācyatvam ihocyate ||
  2. 5,13.2tatsadbhāvaprasiddhyartham atra tāvat prayatyate |                    vācyatve vakṣyate yuktir vyaktyā saha balābale ||
  3. 5,13.3jātim evākṛtiṃ prāhur vyaktir ākriyate yayā |                    sāmānyaṃ tac ca piṇḍānām ekabuddhinibandhanam ||
  4. 5,13.4tannimittaṃ ca yatkiñcit sāmānyaṃ śabdagocaram |                    sarva evecchatīty evam avirodho 'tra vādinām ||<386>
  5. 5,13.5sarvavastuṣu buddhiś ca vyāvṛttyanugamātmikā |                    jāyate dvyātmatvena vinā sā ca na siddhyati ||
  6. 5,13.6viśeṣamātra iṣṭe ca na sāmānyamatir bhavet |                    sāmānyamātrabodhe tu nirnimittā viśeṣadhīḥ ||
  7. 5,13.7na cāpy anyatarā bhrāntir upacāreṇa ceṣyate |                    dṛḍhatvāt sarvadā buddher bhrāntis tadbhrāntivādinām ||
  8. 5,13.8mukhyayoś cāpy adṛṣṭatvān nopacāreṇa kalpanā |                    bāhyārthaviṣayatvaṃ ca buddhīnāṃ pratipāditam ||
  9. 5,13.9anyonyāpekṣitā nityaṃ syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |                    viśeṣāṇāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ te ca tasya bhavanti hi ||<387>
  10. 5,13.10nirviśeṣaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhavec chaśaviṣāṇavat |                    sāmānyarahitatvāc ca viśeṣās tadvad eva hi ||
  11. 5,13.11tadanātmakarūpeṇa hetū vācyāvimau punaḥ |                    tena tātyantabhedo 'pi syāt sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ ||
  12. 5,13.12sāmānyabuddhiśaktitvaṃ viśeṣeṣv eva yo vadet |                    vinā vastvantarāt, tena vācyā śaktis tu kīdṛśī ||
  13. 5,13.13grāhyā kiṃ vāpy asambodhā bhinnaikā vā tathaiva ca |                    gṛhyate yadi saikā ca jātir evānyaśabdikā ||
  14. 5,13.14bhaven nirviṣayā buddhir yadi śaktir na gṛhyate |                    na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa viśayaḥ kaś cid iṣyate ||<388>
  15. 5,13.15parasparavibhinnatvād viśeṣā naikabuddhibhiḥ |                    gṛhyante viṣayāsattvāc chaktiś caiṣāṃ na vidyate ||
  16. 5,13.16bhinnatve vāpi śaktīnām ekabuddhir na labhyate |                    viśeṣaśaktyabhede ca tāvanmātramatir bhavet ||
  17. 5,13.17bhinnā viśeṣaśaktibhyaḥ sarvatrānugatāpi ca |                    pratyekaṃ samavetā ca tasmāj jātir apīṣyatām ||
  18. 5,13.18tenātmadharmo bhedānām ekadhīviṣayo 'sti naḥ |                    sāmānyam ākṛtir jātiḥ śaktir vā so 'bhidhīyatām ||
  19. 5,13.19nanu bhinne 'pi sattādau sāmānyam iti jāyate |                    buddhir vināpi sāmānyād anyasmāt sā kathaṃ bhavet ||
  20. 5,13.20vanopanyāsatulyo 'yam upanyāsaḥ kṛtas tvayā |                    bhrāntitvena hi naitasyā bhrāntir gotvādidhīr api ||<389>
  21. 5,13.21śabdāt pūrvaṃ hi sarveṣu gavādāv iva naikadhīḥ |                    vastutvaṃ cātra sāmānyaṃ dharmaṃ ke cit pracakṣate ||
  22. 5,13.22evaṃ tu kalpyamāne syāt sāmānyānām anantatā |                    punas tena sahānyeṣu sāmānyamatir asti hi ||
  23. 5,13.23viśeṣeṣv api vastutvāt sāmānyam iti dhīr bhavet |                    sattādiṣv iva, ttenaitat sāmānyaṃ nopapadyate ||
  24. 5,13.24tasmād ekasya bhinneṣu yā vṛttis tannibandhanaḥ |                    sāmānyaśabdaḥ sattādāv ekadhīkaraṇena vā ||
  25. 5,13.25piṇḍeṣv eva ca sāmānyam, nāntarā gṛhyate yataḥ |                    na hy ākāśavadicchanti sāmānyaṃ nāma kiñ cana ||
  26. 5,13.26yad vā sarvagatatve 'pi vyaktiḥ śaktyanurodhataḥ |<390>                    śaktiḥ kāryānumeyā hi vyaktidarśanahetukā ||
  27. 5,13.27tena yatraiva dṛśyeta vyaktiḥ śaktaṃ tad eva tu |                    tenaiva ca na sarvāsu vyaktiṣv etat pratīyate ||
  28. 5,13.28bhinnatve 'pi hi kāsāñ cic chaktiḥ kāś cid aśaktikāḥ |                    na ca paryanuyogo 'sti vastuśakteḥ kadā cana ||
  29. 5,13.29vahnir dahati nākāśaṃ ko 'tra paryanuyujyatām |                    na cānyā mṛgyate yuktir yathā sandṛśyate tathā ||
  30. 5,13.30na hi yuktyantaraṃ nāstīty etaj jñānam anarthakam |                    dharmaś cāvyabhicāryasya na mṛgya upalakṣaṇe ||
  31. 5,13.31nānumānāvagamyaṃ tat, pratyakṣe lakṣaṇena kim |<391>                    svābhāvikaś ca sambandho jātivyaktyor na hetumān ||
  32. 5,13.32tenaitasya prasiddhyarthaṃ nānyat sāmānyam iṣyate |                    śaktisiddhivadetasya svabhāvo 'tra na vāryate ||
  33. 5,13.33yad vā naimittikatve 'pi tāvanmātrapratīkṣaṇāt |                    viśeṣeṣv eva labdheṣu keṣu cin nānyavāñchanam ||
  34. 5,13.34na vyañjantyapare kasmād, yatas teṣu na dṛśyate |                    tebhyo 'pi na nivṛttyarthaṃ mṛgyo hetuḥ svabhāvataḥ ||
  35. 5,13.35sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet tasya vṛtter niyāmakam |                    gotvenāpi vinā kasmād gobuddhir na niyamyate ||<392>
  36. 5,13.36yathā tulye 'pi bhinnatve keṣu cid vṛttyapekṣitā |                    gotvāder animitte 'pi tathā buddhir bhaviṣyati ||
  37. 5,13.37viṣayeṇa hi buddhīnāṃ vinā notpattir iṣyate |                    viśeṣād anyad icchanti sāmānyaṃ tena tad dhruvam ||
  38. 5,13.38tā hi tena vinotpannā mithyāḥ syur viṣayād ṛte |                    na tv anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasyeha duṣyati ||
  39. 5,13.39aniṣyamāṇe sāmānye vṛttiḥ śabdānumānayoḥ |                    naiva syāt, na hi sambandho bhedair ānantyato bhavet ||
  40. 5,13.40anubhūtatayā vāsau puruṣasyopayujyate |                    jātivyaktyos tu sambandhe nānubhūtyā prayojanam ||
  41. 5,13.41siddhe viṣayarūpe ca gotvādāv indriyaiḥ punaḥ |                    arthāpattyupalabdhā syāc chaktir ekā niyāmikā ||
  42. 5,13.42na cātmahetum evāsau siddhaṃ bādhitum arhati |<393>                    śaktiś ca naitayā buddhyā, nendriyaiḥ sā hi gṛhyate ||
  43. 5,13.43sāmānyāntarayogānām aniṣṭhā yā ca varṇyate |                    tayā sāmānyanāśaḥ syāt sa ca dṛṣṭena bādhyate ||
  44. 5,13.44sambandhas tasya hetur vā tadgrahe na ca kāraṇam |                    svarūpato gṛhīte 'rthe paścād etad vikalpyate ||
  45. 5,13.45sāsnādyekārthasambandhi gotvam ity upalakṣaṇam |                    na ca svasamavāyy eva kevalaṃ cihnam iṣyate ||
  46. 5,13.46sāsnādibhyas tu piṇḍasya bhedo nātyantato yadā |                    sāmānyasya ca piṇḍebhyas tadā syād etad uttaram ||<394>
  47. 5,13.47kasmāt sāsnādimatsv eva gotvaṃ yasmāt tadātmakam |                    tādātmyam asya kasmāc cet svabhāvād iti gamyatām ||
  48. 5,13.48upalabdhyanusāreṇa vyavasthāsiddhir īdṛśī |                    svato gotvādibhedas tu na tu vyañjakabhedataḥ ||
  49. 5,13.49sā bhūd drutādivanmithyā, nyañjakasya tu kiṃkṛtaḥ |                    bhedo hastyādipiṇḍebhyaḥ, svataś cet, iha tatsamam ||<395>
  50. 5,13.50vyaṅgyajātiviśeṣāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam |                    tasmāt svābhāviko bhedo jātivyaktyoḥ pratīyate ||
  51. 5,13.51anekānanyavṛttittvān na sāmānyaviśeṣayoḥ |                    ekavastvātmatā yuktā varaṃ tenaupacārikam ||
  52. 5,13.52bhinnebhyaś cāpy abhinnatvād bhedas tat svātmavad bhavet |                    ekasmād vāpy abhinnatvād vyaktyekatvaṃ pratīyate ||
  53. 5,13.53ekānekatvam ekasya tathānyānanyatā katham |                    tat sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaś cety evamādi ca duṣkaram ||
  54. 5,13.54virodhas tāvad ekāntād vaktum atra na yujyate |                    sāmānyānanyavijñāte viśeṣe naikavṛttitā ||
  55. 5,13.55sāmānyānanyavṛttitvaṃ viśeṣātmaikabhāvataḥ |<396>                    evañ ca parihartavyā bhinnābhinnatvakalpanā ||
  56. 5,13.56kena cid dhy ātmanaikatvaṃ nānātvaṃ cāsya kena cit |                    sāmānyasya tu yo bhedaṃ brūte tasya viśeṣataḥ ||
  57. 5,13.57darśayitvābhyupetavyam, viśeṣaikyaṃ ca jātitaḥ |                    yathā kalmāṣavarṇasya yatheṣṭaṃ varṇanigrahaḥ ||
  58. 5,13.58citratvād vastuno 'py evaṃ bhedābhedāvadhāraṇam |                    sāmānyāṃśe tu niṣkṛṣya bhedo yena prasādhyate ||
  59. 5,13.59tasya hetor asiddhatvaṃ siddhaś cet siddhasādhanam |<397>                    bhedebhyo 'nanyarūpeṇa sāmānyaṃ gṛhyate yadā ||
  60. 5,13.60tadāviśeṣamātreṇa vastu pratyavabhāsate |                    tadudbhūtyā ca sāmānyaṃ tadbhāvānuguṇaṃ sthitam ||
  61. 5,13.61sad apy agrāhyarūpatvād asadvat pratibhāti naḥ |                    viśeṣān api sāmānyād yadā bhedena buddhyate ||
  62. 5,13.62tadā sāmānyamātratvam evam eva pratīyate |                    yadā tu śabalaṃ vastu yugapat pratipadyate ||
  63. 5,13.63tadānyān anyabhedādi sarvam eva pralīyate |                    na ca tat tādṛśaṃ kaś cic chabdaḥ śaknoti bhāṣitum ||
  64. 5,13.64sāmānyāṃśān apoddhṛtya padaṃ sarvaṃ pravarttate |                    samastavastvapekṣāṃ ca padārthānām apoddhṛtim ||
  65. 5,13.65ke cid āhur asadrūpam, aṃśatvaṃ tu na vāryate |                    sārūpyam eva sāmānyaṃ piṇḍānāṃ yena kalpyate ||
  66. 5,13.66tena sārūpyaśabdena kiṃ punaḥ pratipadyate |<398>                    samānarūpabhāvaś cej jātiḥ sāsmābhir iṣyate ||
  67. 5,13.67sādṛśyam atha sārūpyaṃ kasya keneti kathyatām |                    na tāvacchālaleyena bāhuleyādayaḥ samāḥ ||
  68. 5,13.68viśeṣarūpataḥ, ye 'pi tatsaṃsthānādibhiḥ samāḥ |                    śābaleya iveti syāt tatra buddhir na gaur iva ||
  69. 5,13.69śābaleyo 'yam iti vā bhrāntyā gaur iti nāsti dhīḥ |                    śābaleyasvarūpaṃ ca na gaur ity avatiṣṭhate ||
  70. 5,13.70tadanyeṣu hi gobuddhir na syāt susadṛśeṣv api |                    dṛśyate sā na cānyatra gorūpaṃ tatra vidyate ||
  71. 5,13.71na cānyo gauḥ prasiddho 'sti tatsādṛśyena dhīr bhāvet |                    na cāpi sa iti jñānaṃ sadṛśeṣv asti sarvadā ||<399>
  72. 5,13.72sarvapuṃsām ato bhrāntir naiṣā bādhakavarjanāt |                    sarvajñānāni mithyā ca prasajyante 'tra kalpane ||
  73. 5,13.73viśeṣagrahaṇābhāvād eva gauḥ kaś ca kathyatām |                    babhūva yady asau pūrvam asmadādes tadagrahāt ||
  74. 5,13.74sādṛśyāvadhṛtir nāstīty ato godhīr na labhyate |                    na cāvayavasāmānyair vinā sādṛśyakalpanā ||
  75. 5,13.75sāmānyapratyayotpādo na viśeṣeṣu jāyate |                    vyaktitaś cātireko 'sya syān na veti vicārite ||
  76. 5,13.76sāmānyam eva sādṛśyaṃ bhaved vā vyaktimātrakam |                    tena nātyantabhinno 'rthaḥ sārūpyam iti varṇitam |                    granthe vindhyanivāsena bhrānteḥ sādṛśyam ucyate ||

Chapter 5,14 apohavāda APV

  1. 5,14.1agonivṛttiḥ sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ yaiḥ parikalpitam |                    gotvaṃ vastv eva tair uktam ago 'pohagirā sphuṭam ||
  2. 5,14.2bhāvāntaram abhāvo hi purastāt pratipāditaḥ |                    tatrāśvādinivṛttyātmā bhāvaḥ ka iti kathyatām ||
  3. 5,14.3neṣṭo 'sādhāraṇas tāvad viṣayo nirvikalpanāt |                    tathā ca śābaleyādeḥ, asāmānyaprasaṅgataḥ ||
  4. 5,14.4śābaleyādirūpaṃ hi na sāmānyaṃ parasparam |                    na vaikamitareṣāṃ vastatrānantārthatā bhavet ||<401>
  5. 5,14.5na ca sākṣād viśeṣasya te 'pohyā iti yuktimat |                    na śābaleyavijñānam agovyāvṛttibandhanam ||
  6. 5,14.6nivṛttyā bāhuleyādes tadvijñānaṃ pravartate |                    kuryād agonivṛttiṃ cen nāpohetātmavad dhi tān ||
  7. 5,14.7tenāṃśenānapohaś ca svarūpeṇāpy apohanam |                    kalpyate ced virodhaḥ syāt samamākṣepavāraṇe ||
  8. 5,14.8tasmāt prātyātmikai rūpair ago 'poho na yujyate |                    samudāye 'pi naiteṣām agovyāvṛttisambhavaḥ ||
  9. 5,14.9sarvopalabdhau tadbuddhir vyāsajyaivaṃ pravartate |                    na pratyekaṃ bhaved eṣā, na samasteṣv aśaktitaḥ ||<402>
  10. 5,14.10tasmāt sarveṣu yad rūpaṃ pratyekaṃ pariniṣṭhitam |                    gobuddhis tannimittā syād gotvād anyac ca nāsti tat ||
  11. 5,14.11nanu ca prāgabhāvādau sāmānyaṃ vastu neṣyate |                    sattaiva hy atra sāmānyam anutpattyādirūṣitā ||
  12. 5,14.12tām utpattyādyanusyūtāṃ satteti pratijānate |                    anyāpohānuviddhā tu saivābhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
  13. 5,14.13anityatvaṃ vināśākhyakriyāsāmānyam ucyate |                    abrāhmaṇatvaṃ kin tu syād bhinneṣu kṣattriyādiṣu ||
  14. 5,14.14puruṣatvaṃ catuḥsaṃstham, <403> viśeṣeṣu ca nāstidhīḥ |                    sāmānyapratyayaś caiṣu pratyekam upajāyate ||
  15. 5,14.15tenātra brāhmaṇābhāvaḥ sāmānyaṃ syād avastu tat |                    gotvādāv api tenaiva sāmānyapratyayo bhavet ||
  16. 5,14.16kaiś cit tv atraikaśabdatvam akṣādāv iva kalpitam |                    jātitrayasya, naivaṃ tu sambhavatyaghaṭādiṣu ||
  17. 5,14.17nātra hy anantake bhede sādhāraṇyaṃ nirūpyate |                    tasmāt kriyāguṇāḥ ke cid dhetavo 'nanyavartinaḥ ||
  18. 5,14.18puruṣatvaṃ nañā caitad brāhmaṇebhyo nivartitam |                    cāturvarṇyaprasaktaṃ sad gamyate 'rthādibhir yathā ||
  19. 5,14.19yady apy avāntarā nāsti triṣu jātir vyavasthitā |                    nañsāmārthyān naratvaṃ tu tryādhāraṃ sampratīyate ||<404>
  20. 5,14.20śabdasāmarthyabhedena varṇeṣu matibhinnatā |                    puṃstve tricaturādhāre paryudāsasvarūpataḥ ||
  21. 5,14.21dūrāntike kṣaṇe śaktir gṛdhravāyasacakṣuṣoḥ |                    yathā rūpe tathā puṃstve pumabrāhmaṇaśabdayoḥ ||
  22. 5,14.22brāhmaṇavyatiriktārthavṛtti puṃstvam itīdṛśam |                    vākyaṃ yatra pravarteta tatrābrāhmaṇadhīpade ||
  23. 5,14.23pārthivatvādisāmānyam evam evāghaṭādiṣu |                    ghaṭatvādivinirmuktaṃ viṣayaḥ sampratīyate ||
  24. 5,14.24asādhāraṇabhāvāc ca nañā śabdo viśeṣitaḥ |                    tāvanmātreṇa rahite sāmānye vyavatiṣṭhate ||<405>
  25. 5,14.25viśeṣe pratiṣiddhe hi sāmānyaṃ yadanantaram |                    sāmānyākāṅkṣiṇaṃ śabdaṃ niruṇad dhi tadātmani ||
  26. 5,14.26prathamātikrame tasya kāraṇaṃ naiva vidyate |                    brāhmaṇatvād ato 'petaṃ naratvam avaśiṣyate ||
  27. 5,14.27vyudasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ ca nañi jāte viśeṣaṇe |                    naratvodasanaṃ yat tu kalpetāśrutam eva tat ||
  28. 5,14.28tasmād yasyaiva te bhedā niṣiddhyeraṃs tadarthataḥ |                    bhedāntarasthaṃ sāmānyam, loke 'py evaṃ pratīyate ||
  29. 5,14.29prasaṅginyāṃ ca tadbuddhau niṣedho 'rthād apīṣyate |                    tanmātrarahite cārthe sādṛśyāt tanmatir bhavet ||<406>
  30. 5,14.30sādṛśyam eva vā vācyam iṣṭam abrāhmaṇādiṣu |                    tac cāvayavasāmānyād, vināpy etena lakṣyate ||
  31. 5,14.31kva cid vināpi sādṛśyāt sāhacaryādihetukā |                    nañyuktaśabdavṛttiḥ syād yathā vakṣyaty anīkṣaṇe ||
  32. 5,14.32īkṣaṇavyatiriktā hi kriyā tatrāpy apekṣitā |                    pratyāsatter na saṅkalpam atikramya pratīyate ||
  33. 5,14.33nāmadhātvarthayogī ca naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ |                    vadato 'brāhmaṇādharmāv anyamātravirodhinau ||<407>
  34. 5,14.34yatrāpy ākhyātasambandhāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate |                    tatraudāsīnyavastv eva pratipattā 'valambate ||
  35. 5,14.35tasmād vastuny apohāḥ syuḥ, api cāvastukalpane |                    prāgntyebhyo viśeṣebhyo na kiñ cid vastu labhyate ||
  36. 5,14.36na cāntyair vyavahāro 'sti, śakyaṃ naiṣāṃ nirūpaṇam |                    apohaśabdavācyātha śūnyatānyaprakārikā ||
  37. 5,14.37tasyāṃ cāśvādibuddhīnātmāṃśagrahaṇaṃ bhavet |                    tatrānyāpohavācyatvaṃ mudhaivābhyupagamyate ||
  38. 5,14.38sāmānyaṃ vasturūpaṃ hi buddhyākāro bhaviṣyati |                    śabdārtho 'rthānapekṣo hi vṛthāpohaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||
  39. 5,14.39vasturūpā ca sā buddhiḥ śabdārtheṣūpajāyate |                    tena vastv eva kalpeta vācyaṃ buddhyanapohakam ||<408>
  40. 5,14.40asaty api ca bāhye 'rthe vākyārthapratibhā tathā |                    padārthe 'pi tathaiva syāt kim apohaḥ prakalpyate ||
  41. 5,14.41buddhyantarād vyavacchedo na ca buddheḥ pratīyate |                    svarūpotpādamātrāc ca nānyam aṃśaṃ bibharti sā ||
  42. 5,14.42bhinnasāmānyavacanā viśeṣavacanāś ca ye |                    sarve bhaveyuḥ paryāyā yady apohasya vācyatā ||
  43. 5,14.43nanu bhedād apohānāṃ prasaṅgo 'yaṃ na yujyate |                    sāmānyāpohakḷptyā ced vastumātre samaṃ tava ||
  44. 5,14.44bhidyante mama vastutvāt sāmānyāni parasparam |                    asaṅkīrṇasvabhāvāni na caikatvaṃ vitanvate ||
  45. 5,14.45saṃsṛṣṭaikatvanānātvavikalparahitātmanām |                    avastutvād apohānāṃ tva syād bhinnatā katham ||
  46. 5,14.46yadi vā bhidyamānatvād vastvasādhāraṇāṃśavat |<409>                    avastutve tv anānātvāt paryāyatvān na mucyate ||
  47. 5,14.47nanu cāpohyabhedena bhedo 'pohasya setsyati |                    na viśeṣaḥ svatas tasya parataś caupacārikaḥ ||
  48. 5,14.48tenaivādhārabhedenāpy asya bhedo na yujyate |                    na hi sambandhibhedena bhedo vastuny apīṣyate ||
  49. 5,14.49kim utāvastvasaṃsṛṣṭam anyataś cānivartitam |                    anavāptaviśeṣāṃśaṃ yat kim apy anirūpitam ||
  50. 5,14.50tasmād yathaiva bhede 'pi piṇḍānāṃ naiva bhidyate |                    tathaivāpohyabhede 'pi nāneko 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
  51. 5,14.51bhede vā pratipiṇḍaṃ syād ago 'pohaḥ, tathā sati |                    sāmānyaṃ śābaleyāder iti neṣṭaṃ prasidhyati ||
  52. 5,14.52saṃsargiṇo 'pi cādhārā yaṃ na bhindanti rūpataḥ |                    apohyaiḥ sa bahirbhūtair bhidyetety atikalpanā ||
  53. 5,14.53agavyaśvātirekaḥ syād anaśvaś ca gavādhikaḥ |                    śeṣaṃ hastyādyapohyaṃ tu dvayor api na bhidyate ||
  54. 5,14.54tatraikabhedād bhedo 'stu bahvabhedād abhinnatā |                    bhūyasāṃ syāt sadharmatvam ity abhedaḥ prasajyate ||<410>
  55. 5,14.55gauś ca hastyādyapohena nāśvarūpād viśeṣyate |                    karoti tadapohaṃ ced aikarūpyaṃ virudhyate ||
  56. 5,14.56sarvaśabdeṣu caikaikam apohyamatiricyate |                    tatrāsādhāraṇatvena tanmātrāpohyatā bhavet ||
  57. 5,14.57tato 'śvāpoharūpatvāt siṃhādiḥ sarva eva te |                    tannimittam ago 'pohaṃ bibhrad ucyeta gaur iti ||
  58. 5,14.58sarvāpoho yadīṣyeta, <411> sa vaktavyaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ |                    yadi pratyekarūpeṇa nāpohyānantatā bhavet ||
  59. 5,14.59bhinnatvāc cāpy apohyānāṃ bhinno 'pohaḥ prasajyate |                    tatraikasmin bhavet piṇḍe 'nantajātisamanvayaḥ ||
  60. 5,14.60tato gaur iti sāmānyaṃ vācyam ekaṃ na sidhyati |                    jātyantaramatiś caiṣu bhavej jātyantareṣv iva ||
  61. 5,14.61samudāyātmanā nāpi bhaved eṣām apohyatā |                    samudāyo hi naikena vinā dharmeṇa jāyate ||
  62. 5,14.62nāpy ekadeśatā teṣām asti nāpy ekakālatā |                    vyatiriktaś ca saṅghātas teṣāṃ kaś cin na vidyate ||
  63. 5,14.63yadi tv avyatiriktaḥ syād ānanyaṃ tadavasthitam |                    yadi sāmānyarūpeṇa te 'pohyante, na vastutā ||
  64. 5,14.64kathaṃ vā vastv apohyeta, <412> nābhāvo bhāvamṛcchati |                    apohyamāne cābhāve bhāva evāvaśiṣyate ||
  65. 5,14.65apohyabhedakḷptiś ca nābhāvābhedato bhavet |                    tadbhedo 'pohabhedāc cet, prāptam anyonyasaṃśrayam ||
  66. 5,14.66gosāmānyasya bhinnatvād agaur ity eṣa bhidyate |                    agaur ity asya bhedena gosāmānyaṃ ca bhidyate ||
  67. 5,14.67agāvo 'śvādayaś ca syus te 'py abhāvātmakāḥ punaḥ |                    karkādyapekṣayā te 'pi tathety evaṃ na gamyate ||
  68. 5,14.68kim apohyam, kva cāpohaḥ, gopiṇḍeṣv evam eva ca |<413>                    tatra syād dvayam apy etadantyeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||
  69. 5,14.69na cāntyeṣu dvayor asti vyavahāro bhidāṃ prati |                    gavāśvaparamāṇūnāṃ viśeṣaś ca na vidyate ||
  70. 5,14.70svarūpajātisaṃsthānaparimāṇādilakṣaṇaḥ |                    kim apohyaṃ kva cāpohas tatrāpi na viśiṣyate ||
  71. 5,14.71na cāprasiddhasārūpyānapohaviṣayātmanā |                    śaktaḥ kaś cid api jñātuṃ gavādīnaviśeṣataḥ ||
  72. 5,14.72apohyān api cāśvādīnekadharmānvayād ṛte |                    na nirūpayituṃ śaktis tatrāpoho na siddhyati ||
  73. 5,14.73na cānvayavinirmukte pravṛttir liṅgaśabdayoḥ |                    tābhyāṃ ca na vināpoho na cāsādhāraṇe 'nvayaḥ ||
  74. 5,14.74apohaś cāpy aniṣpannaḥ sāhacaryaṃ kva dṛśyatām |                    tasminn adṛśyamāne ca na tayoḥ syāt pramāṇatā ||<414>
  75. 5,14.75na cādarśanamātreṇa tābhyāṃ pratyāyanaṃ bhavet |                    sarvatraiva hy adṛṣṭatvāt pratyāyyaṃ nāvaśiṣyate ||
  76. 5,14.76athāsaty api sārūpye syād apohasya kalpanā |                    gavāśvayor ayaṃ kasmād ago 'poho na kalpyate ||
  77. 5,14.77śābaleyāc ca bhinnatvaṃ bāhuleyāśvayoḥ samam |                    sāmānyaṃ nānyadiṣṭaṃ cet kvāgo 'pohaḥ pravartatām ||<415>
  78. 5,14.78indriyair nāpy ago 'pohaḥ prathamaṃ vyavasīyate |                    nānyatra śabdavṛttiś ca kiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa prayujyatām ||
  79. 5,14.79pūrvoktena prabandhena nānumāpy atra vidyate |                    sambandhānubhāvo 'py asya tena naivopapadyate ||
  80. 5,14.80nivṛttivācinaḥ śabdā na prasiddhāś ca yān prati |                    teṣām agor asiddhatvān na sāmānyanirākriyā ||
  81. 5,14.81agośabdābhidheyatvaṃ gamyatāṃ ca kathaṃ punaḥ |                    na dṛṣṭo yatra gośabdaḥ sambandhānubhavakṣaṇe ||
  82. 5,14.82ekasmāt tarhi gopiṇḍād yadanyat sarvam eva tat |                    bhaved apohyam ity evaṃ na sāmānyasya vācyatā ||
  83. 5,14.83siddhaś cāgaur apohyeta goniṣedhātmakaś ca saḥ |                    tatra gaur eva vaktavyo nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate ||
  84. 5,14.84sa ced agonivṛttyātmā bhaved anyonyasaṃśrayaḥ |<416>                    siddhaś ced gaur apohyārthaṃ vṛthāpohaprakalpanā ||
  85. 5,14.85gavyasiddhe tv agaur nāsti tadabhāve ca gauḥ kutaḥ |                    nādhārādheyavṛttyādisambandhaś cāpy abhāvayoḥ ||
  86. 5,14.86na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'pohavat tayā |                    kathaṃ vā parikalpyeta sambandho vastvavastunoḥ ||
  87. 5,14.87svarūpasattvamātreṇa na ca kiñ cid viśeṣaṇam |                    svabuddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyaṃ tad viśeṣaṇam ||
  88. 5,14.88na cāpy aśvādiśabdebho jāyate 'pohabodhanam |                    viśiṣṭabuddhir iṣṭeha na cājñātaviśeṣaṇā ||<417>
  89. 5,14.89na cānyarūpam anyādṛk kuryāj jñānaṃ viśeṣaṇam |                    kathaṃ cānyādṛśe jñāte tad ucyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
  90. 5,14.90athānyathā viśeṣye 'pi syād viśeṣaṇakalpanā |                    tathā sati hi yatkiñcit prasajyeta viśeṣaṇam ||
  91. 5,14.91abhāvarūpagamye ca na viśeṣye 'sti vastutā |                    viśeṣitam apohena vastu vācyaṃ na te 'sty ataḥ ||
  92. 5,14.92yady apy apohanirmukte na vṛttiḥ śabdaliṅgayoḥ |                    yuktā tathāpi buddhis tu jñātur vastvavalambate ||
  93. 5,14.93na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu buddhau viparivarttate |                    na cāpi nirvikalpatvāt tasya yuktā viśeṣyatā ||<418>
  94. 5,14.94śabdenāgamyamānaṃ ca viśeṣyam iti sāhasam |                    tena sāmānyam eṣṭavyaṃ viṣayo buddhiśabdayoḥ ||
  95. 5,14.95yadā cāśabdavācyatvān na vyaktīnām apohyatā |                    tadāpohyeta sāmānyaṃ tasyāpohāc ca vastutā ||
  96. 5,14.96nāpohyatvam abhāvānām abhāvābhāvavarjanāt |                    vyakto 'pohāntare 'pohas tasmāt sāmānyavastunaḥ ||
  97. 5,14.97abhāvasya ca yo 'bhāvaḥ sa cet tasmād vilakṣaṇaḥ |                    bhāva eva bhaven no ced gaur agaus te prasajyate ||
  98. 5,14.98yady apy aneṣu śabdeṣu vastunaḥ syād apohyatā |                    sacchabdasya tv abhāvākhyān nāpohyaṃ bhinnam iṣyate ||
  99. 5,14.99tatrāsato 'pi bhāvatvam itikleśo mahān bhavet |<419>                    tadasiddhau na sattāsti na cāsattā prasidhyati ||
  100. 5,14.100na cāpi vāsanābhedād bhedaḥ sadrūpatāpi vā |                    apohānāṃ prakalpyeta, na hy avastuni vāsanā ||
  101. 5,14.101smṛtiṃ muktvā na cāsty asyāḥ śaktiyogaḥ kriyāntare |                    tasmān nānyādṛśe sārthe karoty anyādṛśīṃ matim ||
  102. 5,14.102bhavadbhiḥ śabdabhedo 'pi tannimitto na labhyate |                    na hy asādhāraṇaḥ śabdo vācakaḥ prāgadṛṣṭitaḥ ||
  103. 5,14.103bhinnatvāc cāpi naivaikā vāsanā taiḥ prakalpyate |                    na cāsti śabdavastv ekaṃ vāsanāṃ yat kariṣyati ||<420>
  104. 5,14.104tatra śabdāntarāpohe sāmānye parikalpite |                    tathaivāvasturūpatvāc chabdabhedo na kalpyate ||
  105. 5,14.105vācakānāṃ yathā caivaṃ vācyavācakayor mithaḥ |                    na cāpy apohyabhedena bhedo 'stīty upapāditam ||
  106. 5,14.106nāgṛhītaś ca gamakaḥ śabdāpohaḥ kathañ cana |                    pratyakṣaṃ na ca tacchaktaṃ na ca sto liṅgavācakau ||
  107. 5,14.107yataḥ syād grahaṇaṃ tasya, liṅgādīnāṃ ca kalpane |                    na vyavastheti vācyaivaṃ vinā pratyakṣamūlataḥ ||
  108. 5,14.108na gamyagamakatvaṃ syād avastutvād apohayoḥ |                    bhavatpakṣe, yathā loke khapuṣpaśaśaśṛṅgayoḥ ||
  109. 5,14.109vṛṣṭimeghāsator dṛṣṭvā yady anaikāntikaḥ vadet |                    vastv evātrāpi matpakṣe bhavatpakṣe 'py adaḥ kutaḥ ||
  110. 5,14.110vidhirūpaś ca śabdārtho yena nābhyupagamyate |                    na bhaved vyatireko 'pi tasya tatpūrvako hy asau ||<421>
  111. 5,14.111niṣedhadvayayogitvād asato yāpy abhāvatā |                    savastuke bhavet sāpi na tucche buddhyasambhavāt ||
  112. 5,14.112nanu yuktyānayaivāyaṃ vastunāpi na bhidyate |                    apohas tena doṣo 'tra pūrvokto na bhaviṣyati ||
  113. 5,14.113siddham evaṃ madiṣṭaṃ syāt, naivānyā gatir asti hi |                    abhāve vastubuddhir vā yad vā vastunyabhāvadhīḥ ||
  114. 5,14.114tatrābhāvātmakatve syān nirnimittaiva vastudhīḥ |                    vastuny abhāvabodhas tu sidhyaty anyam apekṣya tu ||<422>
  115. 5,14.115apohamātravācyatvaṃ yadi cābhyupagamyate |                    nīlotpalādiśabdeṣu śabalārthābhidhāyiṣu ||
  116. 5,14.116viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyayoḥ |                    na siddhiḥ, na hy anīlatvavyudāse 'nutpalacyutiḥ ||
  117. 5,14.117nāpi tatretaras tasmān na viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe |                    śabdayor nāpi te syātām abhidheyānapekṣayoḥ ||
  118. 5,14.118sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca na bhinnatvād apohayoḥ |                    arthataś caitad iṣyeta kīdṛśyādheyatā tayoḥ ||
  119. 5,14.119na cāsādhāraṇaṃ vastu gamyate 'nyac ca nāsti te |<423>                    agamyamānam aikārthyaṃ śabdayoḥ kvopayujyate ||
  120. 5,14.120athānyāpohavad vastu vācyam ity abhidhīyate |                    tatrāpi paratantratvād vyāptiḥ śabdena durbalā ||
  121. 5,14.121khaṇḍe bhinnavyapohyatvād yathaiva madhurādibhiḥ |                    śuklādivyāptyabhāvena nākṣepo na viśeṣaṇam ||
  122. 5,14.122tathaivāsadvyudāsāṃśāvacchinnārthāvadhāraṇe |                    nāghaṭādinivṛttyaṃśavyāptiḥ śabdāt pratīyate ||<424>
  123. 5,14.123vyāptiś ced artharūpeṇa sattayaivaṃ hi sā bhavet |                    na ghaṭatvādimān arthaḥ kaś cin na vyāpyate tayā ||
  124. 5,14.124na ca vastutayā vyāptis tayā śabdasya vāryate |                    pratītiṃ prati tulyas tu vyāpāro vastvavastunoḥ ||
  125. 5,14.125nirbhāgo 'pi hi vastvātmā śabdair bhāgena gamyate |                    na hi sacchabdavijñānād ghaṭādyarthaḥ pratīyate ||
  126. 5,14.126tenānākṣepadoṣo 'sti, bhāktadoṣaś ca vidyate |                    viśeṣaṇatvān mukhyatvam apohasya hi jātivat ||<425>
  127. 5,14.127tasmāt tadvati gauṇatvān nābhidheyatvasambhavaḥ |                    avastutvān na mukhyaś cet, na syād evaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
  128. 5,14.128bhedāś cāpohavantaḥ syus teṣāṃ cāvācyatoditā |                    ānantyavyabhicārābhyām, anyo nāsti tv apohavān ||
  129. 5,14.129nāpohavattvam anyad dhi bhedāpohāntare 'sti te |                    tac cāpi kalpyamānaṃ syād abhāvo bhāva eva vā ||
  130. 5,14.130vastu cej jātir eva syād avastutve 'pi pūrvavat |                    sambandho vaiṣa kalpyeta tasya ceṣṭā na vācyatā ||<426>
  131. 5,14.131na caiko 'pohavān artho vartate 'rthāntare kva cit |                    tasmād api na sāmānyaṃ vācyaṃ na ca viśeṣaṇam ||
  132. 5,14.132nātmanyavidyamānatvād viśeṣo 'pohasūcakaḥ |                    tasmān na tair viśeṣyatvaṃ prakṛṣṭatvena nīlavat ||
  133. 5,14.133arthākṣepo 'pi nāsty eva sandehāl liṅgaliṅgivat |                    na sāmānyātmanāpohas tair vinā na ca siddhyati ||<427>
  134. 5,14.134evam eva tv anākṣepaḥ syād apohena vastunaḥ |                    yataḥ śaśaviṣāṇe 'pi tadapohasya sambhavaḥ ||
  135. 5,14.135liṅgasaṃkhyādisambandho na vāpohasya vidyate |                    vyakter avyapadeśyatvāt taddvāreṇāpi nāsty asau ||
  136. 5,14.136na hy asādhāraṇatvena sāpohenāpi gamyate |                    na cāpy agamyamānasya vastunaḥ syād viśeṣyatā ||
  137. 5,14.137liṅgasaṃkhyādyapohānāṃ nopakāraḥ svarūpataḥ |                    vastunaś copakāryatvaṃ kathaṃ śabdaiḥ pratīyate ||<428>
  138. 5,14.138na vinānupalabdhyā ca syād abhāvamatiḥ kva cit |                    na cābhāvaprameyatvaṃ gotvāder iha gamyate ||
  139. 5,14.139ākhyāteṣu ca nānyasya nivṛttiḥ sampratīyate |                    na paryudāsarūpaṃ hi niṣedhyaṃ tatra vidyate ||
  140. 5,14.140na neti hy ucyamāne 'pi niṣedhasya niṣedhanam |                    pacatīty aniṣiddhaṃ tu svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate ||
  141. 5,14.141sādhyatvapratyayaś cātra tathābhūtādirūpaṇam |                    niṣpannatvād apohasya nirnimittaṃ prasajyate ||
  142. 5,14.142vidhyādāv artharāśau ca nānyāpohanidarśanam |                    nañaś cāpi nañā yuktād apohaḥ kīdṛśo bhavet ||
  143. 5,14.143cādīnām api nañyogo naivāstīty anapohanam |                    vākyārtho 'nyanivṛttiś ca vyapadeṣṭuṃ na śakyate ||
  144. 5,14.144ananyāpohaśabdādau vācyaṃ na ca nirūpyate |                    prameyajñeyaśabdāder apohyaṃ kuta eva tu ||
  145. 5,14.145apohyakalpanāyāṃ tu varaṃ vastv eva kalpitam |<429>                    jñānākāraniṣedhāc ca nāntarārthābhidheyatā ||
  146. 5,14.146na cāpy apohyatā, tasmān nāpohas teṣu sidhyati |                    evam ityādiśabdānāṃ na vāpohyaṃ nirūpyate ||
  147. 5,14.147virodhitvena bhedānām apoho yadi kalpyate |                    virodho 'pohatas tatra virodhāc cāpy apohanam ||
  148. 5,14.148na sāmānyāpahāritvaṃ vidhirūpeṇa tatra te |                    palaśādīn apohyāto vṛkṣaṃ harati śiṃśapā ||<430>
  149. 5,14.149sāmānyādyanapohaś ca nāvirodhena kalpyate |                    na hi śabdasvarūpāṇāṃ syād viruddhāviruddhatā ||
  150. 5,14.150na ca vastusvarūpeṇa tasya śabdair asaṅgateḥ |                    prāk śabdavyāpṛter nāpi sāpohānāṃ pratīyate ||
  151. 5,14.151anyenānavabuddhe 'rthe sadā śabdaḥ pravartate |                    sāmānyātmakatā tasya kena rūpeṇa gamyate ||
  152. 5,14.152śabdānurūpataś cet syād anyāpohanirūpaṇam |                    bhinnatvād vṛkṣatarvāder apohaḥ kena vāryate ||
  153. 5,14.153śabdaspṛṣṭer vināpoho na ca liṅgena gamyate |                    na viruddhāviruddhatvaṃ tasya liṅgāc ca sidhyati ||<431>
  154. 5,14.154adṛṣṭatvād vyudāsas tu purastād eva vāritaḥ |                    sāmānyaśabdo bhedena neṣyate vācakātmanā ||
  155. 5,14.155vyudāsas tatra durvāraḥ, kathañ cid dṛṣṭatā punaḥ |                    brāhmaṇe kṣattriyasyāpi paryudāsaḥ prasajyate ||
  156. 5,14.156ākāṅkṣaṇādathātyāgas tulyo dravyakriyādiṣu |                    vṛkṣeṇāto 'napohaḥ syāt tiṣṭhatyāder asaṃśayam ||
  157. 5,14.157puruṣasya tathā rājño vyudāse na viśeṣyatā |                    avyudāsatvapakṣe ca syān nīlotpalatulyatā ||<432>
  158. 5,14.158vṛkṣatvapārthivadravyasajjñeyeṣu yaducyate |                    prātilomyānulomyena vidhau sarvārthabodhanam ||
  159. 5,14.159tadayuktam, na sarvo hi śabdaḥ sarvatra dṛśyate |                    deśāvibhāgato vṛttir netrasyāpi rasādiṣu ||
  160. 5,14.160grāhakatvena vṛttis tu pratijāti vyavasthitā |                    cakṣurādivad evātra saṅkaro na bhaviṣyati ||
  161. 5,14.161nivṛttaceṣṭe śabde ca vyāptyavyāptikṛtaṃ punaḥ |                    sattvāder bodhakatvaṃ syād ekanyūnātirekataḥ ||
  162. 5,14.162tavaiva doṣaḥ syād eṣa viśeṣe yasya varttate |                    sāmānyaśabdaḥ, <433> vācyānāṃ bhedo nāpy asti vastutaḥ ||
  163. 5,14.163api caikatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ |                    nirupākhyeṣv apoheṣu kurvato 'sūtrakaḥ paṭaḥ ||
  164. 5,14.164tasmād yeṣv eva śabdeṣu nañyogas teṣu kevalam |                    bhaved anyanivṛttyaṃśaḥ svātmaivānyatra gamyate ||
  165. 5,14.165jñeyārthānyānapohatvaṃ pramāṅgatvāt tvagādivat |                    yenoktaṃ tasya nañyuktaiḥ śabdaiḥ syād vyabhicāritā ||
  166. 5,14.166pakṣīkuryād yadā sarvāṃs tadāthāvītahetubhiḥ |                    anaikānto virodhaś ca sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
  167. 5,14.167nāpohata itīdaṃ ca kārakatvena ced bhavet |                    kevalāpohabuddher vā tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatā ||
  168. 5,14.168athānyāpohavatyarthe vṛttir nāstīti sādhyate |                    tataḥ prāk pakṣabādhaḥ syād gotve 'thāśvādyabhāvataḥ ||<434>
  169. 5,14.169sādhyahīnaś ca dṛṣṭāntaś cakṣurādy api tasya hi |                    varttate 'pohavatyeva taṃ yady api na budhyate ||
  170. 5,14.170athānyāpohanirbhāsā na buddhiḥ siddhasādhanam |                    apoharūpam apy etad vastv ity eva hi gamyate ||
  171. 5,14.171athāpohanimittāsya vṛttir arthe niṣidhyate |                    vyatirekāṅgateṣṭatvāt punaḥ prāk pakṣabādhanam ||
  172. 5,14.172anumāne tathā caitad ity anaikāntiko bhavet |                    sandehabādhajātena pratyakṣeṇāpi cetasā ||
  173. 5,14.173viruddhatā ca hetoḥ syāt, śabdaḥ śrotrādivad yataḥ |                    ātmāntaḥ karaṇākāśaiḥ svavācitvaṃ jahāti vāḥ ||
  174. 5,14.174vidhirūpapravṛttir vā śabdo 'pohena varttate |                    anumānāṅgabhūtatvād yathaiva pratiṣedhakaḥ ||<435>
  175. 5,14.175jātiṃ vā na bravīty eṣa vyaktiṃ vā tadviśeṣitām |                    pramāyām aṅgabhūtatvāt tvakśrotrādi yathaiva ca ||
  176. 5,14.176evaṃ sādhanamārgeṇa vācyāvācyanirūpaṇā |                    nāvātiṣṭhata ity atra kathyate lokavartmanā ||

Chapter 5,15 vanavāda VAV

  1. 5,15.1sāsnādibhir viśiṣṭatvam ākṛter ucyate katham |                    yadāvayavisambandhi gotvaṃ nāvayave sthitam ||
  2. 5,15.2ekāvayavisambandhas teṣāṃ gotvena vidyate |                    tenāsādhāraṇatvāt te syur gotvasyopalakṣaṇam ||
  3. 5,15.3piṇḍe sattādijātīnāṃ bahvīnāṃ samavetatā |                    tābhyo viśiṣyate gotvaṃ sāsnādibhir asaṃśayam ||
  4. 5,15.4na caite vyañjakās tasya guṇavad vā viśeṣaṇam |<436>                    tathā hi nāgṛhīteṣu teṣu syād gotvabodhanam ||
  5. 5,15.5teṣāṃ ca vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ syāt punargrahaṇakalpanā |                    tathā satyanavasthā syāt na syād gotvāvadhāraṇam ||
  6. 5,15.6sarveṣu ca gṛhīteṣu sāsnādiṣu bhavenmatiḥ |                    gotve, na caiṣu sarveṣu yugapad buddhisambhavaḥ ||
  7. 5,15.7tasmāt sadbhāvamātreṇa mahattvādau yathaiva dhīḥ |                    kriyate 'vayavaiḥ piṇḍe tathā jātiguṇādiṣu ||
  8. 5,15.8yady evam agṛhīteṣu teṣu kiṃ sā na jāyate |                    taddeśavyatirekeṇa grāhyaṃ yena na vidyate ||
  9. 5,15.9gṛhyamāṇe tu gotvādau nāntarīyakahetukaḥ |                    sāsnādeḥ kasya cid bodhas taddeśatvena jāyate ||
  10. 5,15.10tadanatyantabhedād vā tadviśiṣṭeti kīrtyate |<437>                    bādhaḥ parānumānasya na pratyakṣeti bodhyate ||
  11. 5,15.11pareṣāṃ sādhanaṃ hy atra nākṛtiḥ piṇḍataḥ pṛthak |                    taddhīhānāv avijñānāt paṅktiyūthavanādivat ||
  12. 5,15.12sarvatra lokasiddhatvān na vācyaṃ sādhanaṃ svayam |                    niṣedhatāṃ pareṣāṃ tu virodhaṃ lokato vadet ||
  13. 5,15.13visaṃvādo na dṛśyeta yadi pratyakṣatākṛteḥ |                    pramāṇe 'pi visaṃvādāt tārkikeṣu kuto nv iyam ||
  14. 5,15.14rūpādāv api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvena sammate |                    vivādaḥ, naiva lokas tu jātau vipratipadyate ||
  15. 5,15.15vyavahārā hi dṛśyante sāmānyārthanibandhanāḥ |                    dadhitakrādidānādau kauṇḍinyabrāhmaṇādiṣu ||<438>
  16. 5,15.16ākṛtir jātir evātra saṃsthānaṃ na prakalpyate |                    na hi vāyvagniśabdādau kiñ cit saṃsthānam iṣyate ||
  17. 5,15.17anyadanyac ca saṃsthānaṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ pratīyate |                    saṃyogātmakatāyāṃ tu vibhāgeṣu vinaśyati ||
  18. 5,15.18atha saṃsthānasāmānyam, aśvādāv api tatsamam |                    na gotvena vinā hy etad vyavacchinnaṃ pratīyate ||
  19. 5,15.19sarvapratikṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsthāne saty apīdṛśe |                    na gotvādimatir dṛṣṭā, tasmāj jātiḥ pṛthak tataḥ ||
  20. 5,15.20rucakādiṣu sāmānyaṃ rucakatvād yudāhṛtam |                    bhinneṣu caiṣu sāmānyaṃ suvarṇatvaṃ pratīyate ||<439>
  21. 5,15.21vardhamānakabhaṅge ca rucakaḥ kriyate yadā |                    tadā pūrvārthinaḥ śokaḥ prītiś cāpy uttarārthinaḥ ||
  22. 5,15.22hemārthinas tu mādhyasthaṃ tasmād vastu trayātmakam |                    notpādasthitibhaṅgānām abhāve syān matitrayam ||
  23. 5,15.23na nāśena vinā śoko notpādena vinā sukham |                    sthityā vinā na mādhyasthyam, tena sāmānyanityatā ||
  24. 5,15.24mudgamāṣatilādau ca yatra bhedo na lakṣyate |                    tatraikabuddhinirgrāhyā jātir indriyagocaraḥ ||
  25. 5,15.25ārād dṛṣṭe ca puruṣe sandeho brāhmaṇādiṣu |                    na syād yadi na gṛhyeta sāmānyaṃ cakṣurādinā ||
  26. 5,15.26tasyopalakṣaṇaṃ cāpi kva cit kena cid iṣyate |                    rūpādīnāṃ viśeṣeṇa deśakālādy apekṣayā ||<440>
  27. 5,15.27suvarṇaṃ bhidyate rūpāt tāmratvāder asaṃśayam |                    tailād ghṛtaṃ vilīnaṃ ca gandhena ca rasena ca ||
  28. 5,15.28bhasmapracchādito vahniḥ sparśanenopalabhyate |                    aśvatvādau ca dūrasthe niścayo jāyate svanaiḥ ||
  29. 5,15.29saṃsthānena ghaṭatvādi brāhmaṇatvādi yonitaḥ |                    kva cid ācārataś cāpi samyag rājānupālitāt ||
  30. 5,15.30pratyekasamavetatvaṃ dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate |                    tathā saty api nānātvaṃ naikabuddher bhaviṣyati ||
  31. 5,15.31na hi sambandhibhedena svarūpaikatvabādhanam |                    vibhutvāvayavābhāvau pratipādyau ca śabdavat ||
  32. 5,15.32yathā ca vyatirekaiva dṛśyamānā punaḥ punaḥ |                    kālabhede 'py abhinnaiva jātir bhinnāśrayā satī ||
  33. 5,15.33kārtsyāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ praṣṭuṃ jātau na yujyate |<441>                    na hi bhedavinirmukte kārtsnyabhāgavikalpanam ||
  34. 5,15.34tasmād vyaktiṣu jātīnāṃ vṛttir astīti gamyate |                    viśeṣāvasarābhāvāt tanmātraivāvatiṣṭhate ||
  35. 5,15.35yā cāvayavaśo vṛttiḥ sraksūtrādiṣu dṛśyate |                    bhūtakaṇṭhaguṇādeś ca pratipiṇḍaṃ samāptitaḥ ||
  36. 5,15.36tatrāvayavayogitvam avibhutvaṃca kāraṇam |                    ākṛtes tadabhāvena na prasaktamado dvayam ||
  37. 5,15.37na ca dvaividhyam eveti vṛtter asti niyāmakam |                    trividhāpi hi dṛṣṭatvāt sambhaved dvividhā yathā ||
  38. 5,15.38itaratra na dṛṣṭaṃ cet sragādiṣv api tatsamam |                    naiva hy anyonyatulyatvaṃ tayor nāpy anayā saha ||
  39. 5,15.39na hy anyasminn adṛṣṭatvād vahner auṣṇyaṃ praṇaśyati |<442>                    na cānumānagamyeyaṃ vāñched yena nidarśanam ||
  40. 5,15.40svarūpataś ca dṛṣṭāyā vṛtter na pararūpataḥ |                    nirākriyopapadyeta tadviśeṣam apaśyatām ||
  41. 5,15.41aṅgāṅgāsambhavāc cāpi yā pradhānanirākriyā |                    sā 'yuktaiva, anumānena pratyakṣajñānabādhanāt ||
  42. 5,15.42tasmād asambhavo yasya tanmātrasyaiva bādhanam |                    yuktaṃ na tāvatānyo 'pi sambhavan bādham arhati ||
  43. 5,15.43tena vaiśeṣikoktāpi jātiḥ sarvagatā satī |                    vyajyate yatra piṇḍena varṇavat tatra gṛhyate ||
  44. 5,15.44tasmāt piṇḍeṣu gobuddhir ekagotvanibandhanā |                    gavābhāsaikarūpyābhām ekagopiṇḍabuddhivat ||<443>
  45. 5,15.45na śābaleyād gobuddhis tato 'nyālambanāpi vā |                    tadabhāve 'pi sadbhāvād ghaṭe pārthivabuddhivat ||
  46. 5,15.46pratyekasamavetārthaviṣayā vāpi gomatiḥ |                    pratyekaṃ kṛtsnabuddhitvāt pratyekavyaktibuddhivat ||
  47. 5,15.47pratyekasamavetāpi jātir ekaikabuddhitaḥ |                    nañyukteṣv api vākyeṣu brahmaṇādinivartanam ||
  48. 5,15.48na ca sādṛśyaviṣayā godhīs tādrūpyajanmataḥ |                    prāmāṇye sati yadvad dhi pratyabhijñaikavastuni ||
  49. 5,15.49naikarūpamatir gotve mithyā vaktuṃ ca śakyate |                    nātra kāraṇadoṣo 'sti bādhakapratyayo 'pi vā ||
  50. 5,15.50yadā vyaktyatirekeṇa grāhyatvād anyatākṛteḥ |                    vanavannāsty anaikāntāt tatrāsambaddhatā katham ||
  51. 5,15.51sādhanaṃ cen mayocyeta yujyeta vyabhicāritā |                    dūṣaṇatvadhiyā tv etad asambaddhatvam ucyate ||<444>
  52. 5,15.52nāstitvahetor uktaiṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā |                    parasya sādhanaṃ hy atra yat tat pūrvam udāhṛtam ||
  53. 5,15.53pratyakṣābhāsatā cātra naivāsti vanabuddhivat |                    kasya cin na hi mithyātvāt sarvaṃ mithyety asaṅgatiḥ ||
  54. 5,15.54yathā vanādibuddhīnāṃ mithyātvān na rasādidhīḥ |                    mithyaivaṃ jātibuddhiḥ syād viśeṣo vābhidhīyatām ||
  55. 5,15.55vṛkṣebhyo vyatirekeṇa vane yaikamatir bhavet |                    dūratvadoṣāt tatra syād ākṛtau tu na vidyate ||
  56. 5,15.56sannikṛṣṭasya vṛkṣeṣu buddhyekatvaṃ nivartate |                    kena cit tu prakāreṇa jātibuddhir na naśyati ||
  57. 5,15.57yaikatvadhīr vinā śabdāt saivaṃ tāvan nirākṛtā |                    vanaśabdānuraktā tu madhyasthasyāpi jāyate ||
  58. 5,15.58mithyātvakalpanā tv asyāḥ pratyakṣāder asambhavāt |                    jātiḥ sarvapramāṇais tu tadrūpaivāvagamyate ||<445>
  59. 5,15.59pramāṇāntaradṛṣṭe ca padam arthe prayujyate |                    tasmād dṛṣṭe prayuktasya mithyātvaṃ syād vanādiṣu ||
  60. 5,15.60ke cin nityaṃ vanaikatvaṃ śabdagamyaṃ samāśritāḥ |                    anyaiḥ saṅgatyabhāve 'pi satyaṃ tat syād rasādivat ||
  61. 5,15.61mithyātvaṃ yadasaṅgatyā tadajñāne prasajyate |                    jñāyamānasya doṣas tu na tu kaś cid asaṅgateḥ ||
  62. 5,15.62pramāṇāntaragamye 'rthe padaṃ nityaṃ prayujyate |                    dharmo 'yaṃ na ca sarveṣāṃ padānām abhyupeyate ||
  63. 5,15.63asty eva saṅgatiś cātra vṛkṣā hi bahavo vanam |                    te pramāṇāntarāj jñātāḥ, saṃkhyā caiṣānyavastuni ||<446>
  64. 5,15.64nānekasyaikaśabdyaṃ ced, ekaśeṣavad iṣyatām |                    tatra saṃkhyāvivṛddhiś ced, astu tanmātravarjanam ||
  65. 5,15.65tasmāt sāmānyadṛṣṭena siddhaikatvasya saṅgatiḥ |                    tenānyānavagamyāpi saṃkhyā syāt sūryayānavat ||
  66. 5,15.66ke cid bahutvasāmānyam āhur vṛkṣasthitaṃ vanam |                    tatra caikatvam asty eva, vanatvaṃ vāpi vidyate ||<447>
  67. 5,15.67vināpy ekāśrayatvena yathaivāvayavo tathā |                    asaṃyuktair abhivyaktir dṛṣṭatvān na virotsyate ||
  68. 5,15.68anyatrāpi ca tadbuddheḥ sāmānyaṃ tad abhaviṣyati |                    yathā ca bhramaṇatvādibhaṅgiṣv avayaveṣv api ||
  69. 5,15.69vyaktaṃ nānāśrayatve 'pi gṛhyate vanatā tathā |                    yadvaikakāryahetutvād ekagośabdavad vanam ||
  70. 5,15.70nityaṃ ye vyastavijñātā vṛkṣā neṣṭā hi te vanam |                    yad vā lakṣaṇayaikatvaṃ deśakālakriyādibhiḥ ||
  71. 5,15.71dravyaikatvād vināpīṣṭaṃ paṅktiyūthavanādiṣu |<448>                    vṛkṣāṇāṃ samudāye ca vanadhīr jāyate yathā ||
  72. 5,15.72naivaṃ gosamudāye 'pi gotvadhīr upajāyate |                    yādṛśī vṛkṣadhīs tatra gotvadhīr api tādṛśī ||
  73. 5,15.73vanavan nāpṛthaksiddheḥ samudāyatvakalpanā |                    na ca sāsnādisaṅghātas tadbuddhyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
  74. 5,15.74kṣīṇeṣu piṇḍabuddhyaiṣu tatsāmānye hi gotvadhīḥ |                    tenāvayavyabhāve 'pi sāmānyaṃ vyatiricyate ||
  75. 5,15.75pūrvoktād eva tu nyāyāt sidhyed atrāvayavy api |                    tasyāpy atyantabhinnatvaṃ na syād avayavaiḥ saha ||
  76. 5,15.76vyaktibhyo jātivac caiṣa na niṣkṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate |<449>                    kaiś cid avyatiriktatvaṃ kaiś cic ca vyatiriktatā ||
  77. 5,15.77dūṣitā sādhitā vāpi na ca tatra balābalam |                    kadā cin niścitaṃ kaiś cit tasmān madhyasthatā varam ||
  78. 5,15.78tato 'nyānanyate nasya sto na staś ceti kīrttyate |                    tasmāc citravadevāsya mṛṣā syād ekarūpatā ||
  79. 5,15.79vastvanekatvavādāc ca na sandindhāpramāṇatā |                    jñānaṃ sandihyate yatra tatra na syāt pramāṇatā ||
  80. 5,15.80ihānaikāntikaṃ vastv ityevaṃ jñānaṃ suniścitam |                    niṣkṛṣyāvayavān buddhyā yāvayavyapratītatā ||
  81. 5,15.81buddhisthatvād vināśasya saulūkyasyāpi yujyate |<450>                    vṛttiś cāvayaveṣv asya vyāsajyaiva pratīyate ||
  82. 5,15.82tataḥ kārtsnyādisampraśnaḥ pratyākhyeyo 'tra jātivat |                    sāsnādiguṇahetuś cen nānyasmin gotvadhīr bhavet ||
  83. 5,15.83bhinna eva hi sāsnādiḥ piṇḍāt piṇḍāntareyataḥ |                    na cāvayavasāmānyaṃ pareṣām upapadyate ||
  84. 5,15.84tasmāt sāsnādito 'nyena gotvadhīr upajanyate |                    vanāntareṣa yā buddhir vanam ity upajāyate ||
  85. 5,15.85tasyās tad eva vṛkṣatvaṃ grāhyaṃ bahvāśrayaṃ viduḥ |                    ekatve 'py ākṛter yadvad bahutvaṃ vyaktyapekṣayā ||
  86. 5,15.86bahutve hi tathā vyakter ekatvaṃ jātyapekṣayā |<451>                    ekānekābhidhāne ca śabdā niyataśaktayaḥ ||
  87. 5,15.87ke cid vyaktiṃ tv asaṃkhyākāṃ gamayanty ambarādiṣu |                    eko vrīhiḥ suniṣpannaḥ iti jātiṃ svasaṃkhyayā ||
  88. 5,15.88patnīsannahanādau tu vyaktim ākṛtisaṃkhyayā |                    kapiñjalādijātes tu pratītir vyaktisaṃkhyayā ||
  89. 5,15.89vyaktijātī vadanty anye dravyāvayavasaṃkhyayā |                    asmān iti yathaikasmin pāśānaditir ity api ||
  90. 5,15.90tatra vrīhyādiśabdānāṃ saṃkhyāyogo yathāruci |                    vanadārādiśabdās tu pravartante vyavasthayā ||
  91. 5,15.91jaṅgame sthāvare cārthe yathā yūthavanādayaḥ |                    tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dārādiś cet prayujyate ||
  92. 5,15.92vyakter avayavānāṃ ca saṃkhyām ādāya vartate |<452>                    vanaśabdaḥ punarvyaktīr jātisaṃkhyāviśeṣitāḥ ||
  93. 5,15.93bahvīrāhātha vā jātiṃ bahuvyaktisamāśrayām |                    evaṃ paṅktyādiśabdānāṃ saṃyogādi viśeṣaṇam ||
  94. 5,15.94sarveṣāṃ kiñ cid astīti na nirālambanaikadhīḥ |                    tulyaṃ pratyakṣayā ''kṛtyā vane yat tadasad yadi ||
  95. 5,15.95vṛkṣās tatra tayā tulyā iti śūnyatvavāditā |                    pratyakṣābhāsagamyatvād vṛkṣebhyo 'nyat tu tadvanam ||
  96. 5,15.96nā''kṛtyā saha tasyāsti sparddhā pratyakṣagamyayā |                    athā''kṛtyā vanaṃ tulyaṃ sadbhāvena prasajyate |                    jātipakṣavimokena vanasiddhāntadūṣaṇam ||
  97. 5,15.97iti nigaditam etallokasiddhaiḥ padārthair vyavahṛtir iha śāstre na svatantrābhyupetaiḥ |                    bhavati ca janadṛṣṭyā jātipaṅktyādibhedo yadi tu na ghaṭate 'sau naiva bādho 'sti kaś cit ||

Chapter 5,16 sambandhākṣepaparihāra SAP

  1. 5,16.1bhavetāṃ nāma śabdārthau yāvetāvuditau tvayā |                    yadarthas tu prayāso 'yaṃ sa sambandho nirūpyatām ||
  2. 5,16.2pūrvam evopadiṣṭaḥ san sambandhaḥ kin tu pṛcchyate |                    svarūpākathanāc caitad uttaraṃ nopapadyate ||
  3. 5,16.3kim auṣadhaṃ jvarasyeti pṛṣṭo yadi vaded idam |                    yenāsau naśyatīty evaṃ kiṃ tena kathitaṃ bhavet ||
  4. 5,16.4tatra ke cid vanty eva pūrvatrāparitoṣataḥ |                    praśnaḥ punarupakrāntaḥ sambandhāntaram icchatā ||
  5. 5,16.5yaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhaḥ pratītyuttaro yataḥ |                    sā cānyapūrvikā tasmān nāsya pratyāyanāṅgatā ||<454>
  6. 5,16.6ajānāno 'pi saṃjñātvaṃ sambandhāntaradarśanāt |                    buddhyate 'rthaṃ tataḥ paścāt kaś cit saṃjñeti manyate ||
  7. 5,16.7tam evānyo 'vinābhāvam atra sambandham icchati |                    na hi tasmād vinā śabde jñāte syād arthabodhanam ||
  8. 5,16.8tattvayuktam, na bhāṣye 'sti tādṛksambandhakīrtanam |                    yadi hy etāvatocyeta kiṃ nānuktaḥ pratīyate ||
  9. 5,16.9prayuktaś cāvinābhāvasaṃjñā lokāt tu gamyate |                    saṃjñetyagamyamāne 'pi gamakatvaṃ pratīyate ||<455>
  10. 5,16.10tasmāt sa eva śabdārthacintāvyavahito 'dhunā |                    nityānityavicārārthaṃ sambandhaḥ smāryate punaḥ ||
  11. 5,16.11yacchabde jñāta ity evaṃ śaktir evātra kīrtyate |                    kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ vā yat tasyārthābhidhāṃ prati ||
  12. 5,16.12svato naivāsti śaktatvaṃ vācyāvācakayor mithaḥ |                    pratītiḥ samayāt puṃsāṃ bhaved akṣinikocavat ||
  13. 5,16.13samayaḥ pratimartyaṃ yā pratyuccāraṇam eva vā |                    kriyate jagadādau vā sakṛdekena kena cit ||
  14. 5,16.14pratyekaṃ vāpi sambandho bhidyetaiko 'tha vā bhavet |                    ekatve kṛtako na syād, bhinnaś ced bhedadhīr bhavet ||
  15. 5,16.15bhinnatve pratisambandhaṃ śaktiḥ kalpyābhidhā prati |                    ekasmin jñātaśaktau vā nānyenārthamatir bhavet ||<456>
  16. 5,16.16atha yo yasya puṃsaḥ syāt sa tena pratipadyate |                    yasyānekena sambandhaḥ kṛtas tasya kathaṃ bhavet ||
  17. 5,16.17ekārthānāṃ vikalpaś cet, netarātyantabādhanāt |                    samuccayo 'pi naiteṣāṃ vyavahāre 'vagamyate ||
  18. 5,16.18kiñ cid evaikamādāya vyavahāro hi dṛśyate |                    bahubhiḥ kṛtasambandhe na caiko gamako bhavet ||
  19. 5,16.19śabdārthayor abhede 'pi pumbahutve 'pi kartari |                    nāyaṃ veti matir dṛṣṭā vikalpo 'to na yujyate ||
  20. 5,16.20gośabde sakṛdukte ca bhinneṣu pratipattṛṣu |                    vikalpyamāne sambandhe kaś cid budhyeta netare ||<457>
  21. 5,16.21samuccayo nṛbhedāc cet, na, vaktraikyād asambhavāt |                    vaktṛśrotṛdhiyor bhedād vyavahāraś ca duṣyati ||
  22. 5,16.22vaktur anyo hi sambandho buddhau śrotus tathāparaḥ |                    śrotuḥ kartuṃ ca sambandhaṃ vaktā kaṃ pratipadyatām ||
  23. 5,16.23pūrvadṛṣṭo hi yas tena śrotur naiva karoti tam |                    yaṃ karoti navaṃ so 'pi na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipādakaḥ ||
  24. 5,16.24sarvathā śrotṛsiddhiś ced, asiddhaṃ netaro vadet |                    ghaṭādāv api tulyaṃ cet, na, sāmānyaprasiddhitaḥ ||<458>
  25. 5,16.25yady api jñātasāmarthyā vyaktiḥ kartuṃ na śakyate |                    kriyate yā na tasyāś ca śaktiḥ kārye 'vadhāritā ||
  26. 5,16.26tathāpy ākṛtitaḥ siddhā śaktir utpādanādiṣu |                    tasyā na cādimattāsti, sambandhas tvādimāṃs tava ||
  27. 5,16.27yadi tatrāpi sāmānyaṃ nityam abhyupagamyate |                    tathāpy asmanmataṃ siddham, na tu dvyākārasambhavaḥ ||
  28. 5,16.28śaktir eva hi sambandho bhedaś cāsyā na vidyate |                    sā hi kāryānumeyatvāt tadbhedam anuvartate ||
  29. 5,16.29anyathānupapattyā ca śaktisadbhāvakalpanam |                    na caikayaiva siddhe 'rthe bahvīnāṃ kalpaneṣyate ||
  30. 5,16.30sambandhākhyānakāle ca gośabdādāv udīrite |                    ke cit sambandhabuddhyārthaṃ buddhyante nāpare tathā ||
  31. 5,16.31tatra sambandhanāstitve sarvo 'rthaṃ nāvadhārayet |<459>                    astitve sarvabodhaś cet, na kaiś cid anupagrahāt ||
  32. 5,16.32jñāpakatvād dhi sambandhaḥ svātmajñānam apekṣate |                    tenāsau vidyamāno 'pi nāgṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ ||
  33. 5,16.33vidyamānasya cārthasya dṛṣṭam agrahaṇaṃ kva cit |                    na tv atyantāsato 'stitvaṃ kāṃś cit pratyupapadyate ||
  34. 5,16.34viruddhau sadasadbhāvau na syātām ekavastuni |                    nanu tulyaṃ virodhitvaṃ jñātājñātatvayor api ||
  35. 5,16.35jñānaṃ hi puruṣādhāraṃ tadbhedān na virotsyate |                    puruṣāntarasaṃsthaṃ ca nājñānaṃ tena bādhyate ||
  36. 5,16.36sambandhādhāratāyāṃ ca virodhaḥ sadasattvayoḥ |                    pratyuktatvāc ca bhedasya tadvaśān nāvirodhitā ||
  37. 5,16.37andhānandhasamīpasthaḥ śuklo 'ndhair nāvagamyate |                    gamyate cetarais tasya sadasattvena tāvatā ||<460>
  38. 5,16.38śaktyaśaktyor narāṇāṃ tu bhedāt tatrāvirodhitā |                    na hy anyo darśanasyāsti sambandhād dhetur atra hi ||
  39. 5,16.39evam evendriyais tulyaṃ vyavahāropalambhanam |                    yeṣāṃ syāt te 'vabhotsyante tato 'rthaṃ netare 'ndhavat ||
  40. 5,16.40ādhānavat sakṛś caitat tantreṇopakariṣyati |                    smaraṇaṃ bhetsyate cāsya vahnipraṇayanādivat ||
  41. 5,16.41sarveṣām anabhijñānāṃ pūrvapūrvaprasiddhitaḥ |                    siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate ||
  42. 5,16.42pratyuccāraṇanirvṛttir bhāṣya eva nirākṛtā |<461>                    sargādau ca kriyā nāsti, tādṛkkālo hi neṣyate ||
  43. 5,16.43yadi tv ādau jagat sṛṣṭvā dharmādharmau sasādhanau |                    yathā śabdārthasambandhān vedān kaś cit pravartayet ||
  44. 5,16.44jagaddhitāya vedasya tathā kiñ cin na duṣyati |                    sarvajñavat tu dussādham ity atraitan na saṃśritam ||
  45. 5,16.45yadā sarvam idaṃ nāsīt kvāvasthā tatra gamyatām |                    prajāpateḥ kva vā sthānaṃ kiṃ rūpaṃ ca pratīyatām ||
  46. 5,16.46jñātā ca kas tadā tasya yo janān bodhayiṣyati |                    upalabdher vinā caitat katham adhyavasīyatām ||
  47. 5,16.47pravṛttiḥ katham ādyā ca jagataḥ sampratīyate |<462>                    śarīrāder vinā cāsya katham icchāpi sarjane ||
  48. 5,16.48śarīrādy atha tasya syāt, tasyotpattir na tatkṛtā |                    tadvadanyaprasaṅgo 'pi, nityaṃ yadi tad iṣyate ||
  49. 5,16.49pṛthivyādāv anutpanne kimmayaṃ tatpunarbhavet |                    prāṇināṃ prāyaduḥkhā ca sisṛkṣāsya na yujyate ||
  50. 5,16.50sādhanaṃ cāsya dharmādi tadā kiñ canna vidyate |                    na ca nissādhanaḥ kartā kaś cit sṛjati kiñ cana ||
  51. 5,16.51nādhāreṇa vinā sṛṣṭirūrṇanābher apīṣyate |                    prāṇināṃ bhakṣaṇāc cāpi tasya lālā pravarttate ||<463>
  52. 5,16.52abhāvāc cānukampyānāṃ nānukampāsya jāyate |                    sṛjec ca śubham evaikam anukampāprayojitaḥ ||
  53. 5,16.53athāśubhād vinā sṛṣṭiḥ sthitir vā nopapadyate |                    ātmādhīnābhyupāye hi bhavet kiṃ nāma dṛṣkaram ||
  54. 5,16.54tathā cāpekṣamāṇasya svātantryaṃ pratihanyate |                    jagac cāsṛjatas tasya kiṃ nāmeṣṭaṃ na sidhyati ||
  55. 5,16.55prayojanam anuddiśya na mando 'pi pravartate |                    evam eva pravṛttiś cec caitanyenāsya kiṃ bhavet ||
  56. 5,16.56krīḍārthāyāṃ pravṛttau ca vihanyeta kṛtārthatā |                    bahuvyāpāratāyāṃ ca kleśo bahutaro bhavet ||
  57. 5,16.57saṃhārecchāpi caitasya bhaved apratyayāt punaḥ |                    na cakaiś cid asau jñātuṃ kādā cid api śakyate ||<464>
  58. 5,16.58svarūpeṇopalabdhe 'pi sraṣṭṛtvaṃ nāvagamyate |                    sṛṣṭyādyāḥ praṇino ye ca budhyantāṃ kiṃ nu te tadā ||
  59. 5,16.59kuto vayam ihotpannāḥ iti tāvan na jānate |                    prāgavasthāṃ ca jagataḥ sraṣṭṛtvaṃ ca prajāpateḥ ||
  60. 5,16.60na ca tadvacanenaiṣāṃ pratipattiḥ suniścitā |                    asṛṣṭvāpi hy asau brūyād ātmaiśvaryaprakāśanāt ||
  61. 5,16.61evaṃ vedo 'pi tatpūrvastatsadbhāvādibodhane |                    sāśaṅko na pramāṇaṃ syāt, nityasya vyāpṛtiḥ kutaḥ ||
  62. 5,16.62yadi prāg apy asau tasmād arthādāsīn na tena saḥ |                    sambaddha iti tasyānyas tadartho 'nyaprarocanā ||<465>
  63. 5,16.63stutivākyakṛtaś caiṣa janānāṃ mativibhramaḥ |                    paurvāparyāparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdo 'nyāṃ kurute matim ||
  64. 5,16.64upākhyānādirūpeṇa vṛttir vedavad eva naḥ |                    dharmādau bhāratādīnāṃ bhrāntis tebhyo 'py ato bhavet ||
  65. 5,16.65ākhyānānupayogitvāt teṣu sarveṣu vidyate |                    stutinindāśrayaḥ kaś cid vedas tac codito 'pi vā ||
  66. 5,16.66vedasyādipravṛttau ca nākṛtatvamatir bhavet |                    pralayeṣu sthitiś cāsya sāśaṅkā syāt prajāpatau ||<466>
  67. 5,16.67kartṛsargavināśānām athānāditvakalpanā |                    saivaṃ yuktāyathedānīṃ bhūtānāṃ dṛśyate kramāt ||
  68. 5,16.68pralaye 'pi pramāṇaṃ naḥ sarvocchedātmake na hi |                    na ca prayojanaṃ tena syāt prajāpatikarmaṇā ||
  69. 5,16.69na ca karmavatāṃ yuktā sthitis tadbhogavarjitā |                    karmāntaraniruddhaṃ hi phalaṃ na syāt kriyāntarāt ||
  70. 5,16.70sarveṣāṃ tu phalāpetaṃ na sthānam upapadyate |                    na cāpy anupabhogo 'sau kasya cit karmaṇaḥ phalam ||
  71. 5,16.71aśeṣakarmanāśe vā punaḥ sṛṣṭir na yujyate |<467>                    karmāṇāṃ vāpy abhivyaktau kiṃ nimittaṃ tadā bhavet ||
  72. 5,16.72īśvarecchā yadīṣyeta, saiva syāl lokakāraṇam |                    īśvarecchāvaśitve hi niṣphalā karmakalpanā ||
  73. 5,16.73na cānimittayā yuktam utpattuṃ hīśvarecchayā |                    yad vā tasyā nimittaṃ yat tad bhūtānāṃ bhaviṣyati ||
  74. 5,16.74sanniveśaviśiṣṭānām utpattiṃ yo gṛhādivat |                    sādhayec cetanādhiṣṭhāṃ dehānāṃ tasya cottaram ||
  75. 5,16.75kasya cid dhetumātratvaṃ yady adhiṣṭhātṛteṣyate |                    karmabhiḥ sarvajīvānāṃ tatsiddheḥ siddhasādhanam ||<468>
  76. 5,16.76icchāpūrvakapakṣe 'pi, tatpūrvatvena karmaṇām |                    icchānantarasiddhis tu dṛṣṭānte 'pi na vidyate ||
  77. 5,16.77anekāntaś ca hetus te taccharīrādinā bhavet |                    utpattimāṃś ca taddeho dehatvād asmadādivat ||
  78. 5,16.78atha tasyāpy adhiṣṭhānaṃ tenaivety avipakṣatā |                    aśarīro hy adhiṣṭhātā nātmā muktātmavad bhavet ||<469>
  79. 5,16.79kumbhakārādyadhiṣṭhānaṃ ghaṭādau yadi ceṣyate |                    neśvarādhiṣṭhitatvaṃ syād, asti cet sādhyahīnatā ||
  80. 5,16.80yathāsiddhe ca dṛṣṭānte bhaved dhetor viruddhatā |                    anīśvaravināśyādikartṛmattvaṃ prasajyate ||
  81. 5,16.81kulālavac ca naitasya vyāpāro yadi kalpate |                    acetanaḥ kathaṃ bhāvas tadicchām anurudhyate ||
  82. 5,16.82tasmān na paramāṇvāder ārambhaḥ syāt tadicchayā |<470>                    puruṣasya ca śuddhasya nāśuddhā vikṛtir bhavet ||
  83. 5,16.83svādhīnatvāc ca dharmādes tena kleśo na yujyate |                    tadvaśena pravṛttau vā vyatirekaḥ prasajyate ||
  84. 5,16.84svayaṃ ca śuddharūpatvād asattvāc cānyavastunaḥ |                    svapnādivadavidyāyāḥ pravṛttis tasya kiṃ kṛtā ||
  85. 5,16.85anyenopaplave 'bhīṣṭe dvaitavādaḥ prasajyate |                    svābhāvikīm avidyāṃ tu nocchettuṃ kaś cid arhati ||
  86. 5,16.86vilakṣaṇopapāte hi naśyet svābhāvikī kva cit |                    na tv ekātmābhyupāyānāṃ hetur asti vilakṣaṇaḥ ||<471>
  87. 5,16.87pumānakartā yeṣāṃ tu teṣām api guṇaiḥ kriyā |                    katham ādau bhavet, tatra karma tāvan na vidyate ||
  88. 5,16.88mithyājñānaṃ na trāsti rāgadveṣādayo 'pi vā |                    manovṛttir hi sarveṣāṃ na cotpannaṃ tadā manaḥ ||
  89. 5,16.89karmaṇāṃ śaktyavasthānāṃ yair uktā bandhahetutā |                    sā na yuktā na kāryaṃ hi śaktisthāt kāraṇād bhavet ||
  90. 5,16.90dadhiśaktir na hi kṣīre dādhikārambham arhati |                    dadhyārambhasya sā hetus tato 'nyā dādhikasya tu ||<472>
  91. 5,16.91kāraṇāc chaktyavasthāc ca yadi kāryaṃ prajāyate |                    bandhaḥ punaḥ prasajyeta phale datte 'pi karmaṇā ||
  92. 5,16.92śaktyavasthatvam eveṣṭaṃ vināśe 'pi hi karmaṇām |                    prāk cāpi śaktisadbhāvād anuṣṭhānaṃ vṛthā bhavet ||
  93. 5,16.93śaktyavasthaṃ ca rāgādi kiṃ neṣṭaṃ bandhakāraṇam |                    karmādattaphalatvāc cet, nāvyaktim api tad vrajet ||
  94. 5,16.94tacchaktyaprayogitvān na jñānaṃ mokṣakāraṇam |                    karmaśaktyā na hi jñānaṃ virodham upagacchati ||
  95. 5,16.95yady apy ajñānajanyatvaṃ karmaṇām avagamyate |                    rāgādivat tathāpy eṣāṃ na jñānena nirākriyā ||<473>
  96. 5,16.96karmakṣayo hi vijñānād ity etac cāpramāṇavat |                    phalasyālpasya vā dānaṃ rājaputrāparādhavat ||
  97. 5,16.97adyatve 'pi hi śaktisthaṃ yadi syāt karmakāraṇam |                    tataḥ pradhānakāle 'pi yujyate kāraṇābhidhā ||
  98. 5,16.98manovṛttir idānīṃ tu hetur nāsti ca sā tadā |                    manasāṃ saṅkarāc cāpi tadā syāt karmasaṅkaraḥ ||
  99. 5,16.99gasmān naiṣo 'dhikārākhyo bandhahetuḥ prakalpate |                    yogyatve 'py adhikārākhye viprayogo na yujyate ||<474>
  100. 5,16.100caitanyaṃ yogyatā puṃsaḥ prakṛtes tadanātmatā |                    bhoktṛbhogyatvayos te ca na tābhyām apagacchataḥ ||
  101. 5,16.101utpattau karmaṇāṃ ceṣṭam ajñānaṃ kāraṇaṃ yadi |                    tannāśāt syād anutpattis teṣāṃ na phalavarjanam ||
  102. 5,16.102jñānaṃ mokṣanimittaṃ ca gamyate nendriyādinā |                    na ca sāṅkhyādivijñānān mokṣo vedena codyate ||
  103. 5,16.103ātmā jñātavya ity etanmokṣārthaṃ na ca coditam |<475>                    karmapravṛttihetutvam ātmajñānasya lakṣyate ||
  104. 5,16.104vijñāte cāsya pārārthye yāpi nāma phalaśrutiḥ |                    sārthavādo bhaved eva na svargādeḥ phalāntaram ||
  105. 5,16.105sukhopabhogarūpaś ca yadi mokṣaḥ prakalpyate |                    svarga eva bhaved eṣa paryāyeṇa, kṣayo ca saḥ ||
  106. 5,16.106na hi kāraṇavat kiñ cid akṣayitvena gamyate |                    tasmāt karmakṣayād eva hetvabhāve na mucyate ||
  107. 5,16.107na hy abhāvātmakaṃ muktvā mokṣanityatvakāraṇam |                    na ca kriyāyāḥ kasyāś cid abhāvaḥ phalam iṣyate ||
  108. 5,16.108tatra jñātātmatattvānāṃ bhogāt pūrvakriyākṣaye |                    uttarapracayāsattvād deho notpadyate punaḥ ||<476>
  109. 5,16.109karmajanyopabhogārthaṃ śarīraṃ na pravartate |                    tadabhāve na kaś cid dhi hetus tatrāvatiṣṭhate ||
  110. 5,16.110mokṣārthī na pravarteta tatra kāmyaniṣiddhyoḥ |                    nityanaimittike kuryāt pratyavāyajihāsayā ||
  111. 5,16.111prārthyamānaṃ phalaṃ jñātaṃ na cānicchor bhaviṣyati |                    ātmajñe caitad astīti tajjñānam upayujyate ||<477>
  112. 5,16.112sargapralayavijñānaṃ samastajagadāśrayam |                    svaśarīravidāṃ puṃsāṃ nādhikyenopayujyate ||
  113. 5,16.113tasmād adyavad evātra sargapralayakalpanā |                    samastakṣayajanmabhyāṃ na sidhyatyapramāṇikā ||
  114. 5,16.114sarvajñavanniṣedhyā ca sraṣṭuḥ sadbhāvakalpanā |                    na ca dharmādṛte tasya bhavel lokād viśiṣṭhatā ||
  115. 5,16.115na cānanuṣṭhito dharmo nānuṣṭhānam ṛte mateḥ |                    na ca vedādṛte sā syād vedo na ca padādibhiḥ ||
  116. 5,16.116tasmāt prāg api sarve 'mī sraṣṭurāsan padādayaḥ |                    syāt tatpūrvakatā cāsya caitanyād asmadādivat ||<478>
  117. 5,16.117evaṃ ye yuktibhiḥ prāhus teṣāṃ durlabham uttaram |                    aneṣyo vyavahāro 'yam anādir vedavādibhiḥ ||
  118. 5,16.118pratyakṣādāv upakṣīṇe yo 'numānena ḍitthavat |                    sambandhitvān niyoktāraṃ gavādāv api kalpayet ||
  119. 5,16.119gavādiśabdasambandhaṃ sarvo 'nyasmāt prapadyate |                    madvat tadvyavahāritvāt tasyaitat pratisādhanam ||
  120. 5,16.120devadattādiśabde 'pi prasaktaivam anāditā |                    sambandhasya, balīyastvād dṛṣṭabādhān nivartate ||
  121. 5,16.121tatrāpi śaktinityatvam, niyogasya tv anityatā |                    tadgatāc cāpy anityatvāc chaktau bhrāntiḥ pravartate ||
  122. 5,16.122gavādiṣu tu na bhrāntir niyogānāditā yataḥ |                    yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt pūrvaṃ sambandhadarśanāt ||
  123. 5,16.123siddhaḥ sambandha ity evaṃ sambandhādir na vidyate |                    yadā cāptapraṇītatvāc chabdo 'rthaṃ pratipādayet ||
  124. 5,16.124na svaśaktyā tadāptatvaṃ mitau na smaryate katham |<479>                    yathā bauddhādayo yāvad buddhādyuktaṃ na jānate ||
  125. 5,16.125na tāvat pratipadyante bodhe vākyena saty api |                    samaye kathyamāne 'nyair asmaranto 'pi pāṇinim ||
  126. 5,16.126ādaicaḥ pratipadyante vṛddhiṃ kartuṃ smṛtir vṛthā |                    sūtrasthaḥ pāṇinis tatra svasaṃjñāṃ pratipādayet ||
  127. 5,16.127gauḥ sāsnādimatīty evaṃ vākyaṃ tv atra na vidyate |                    asambandhāc ca sarveṣām evaṃ kartum asambhavaḥ ||
  128. 5,16.128tasmān na pratipattiḥ syāt kathañ cit kartṛvarjitā |<480>                    dṛṣārthavyavahāratvād vṛddhyādau sambhaved api ||
  129. 5,16.129dharmāya niyamo 'trāpi na vinā pāṇiner bhavet |                    ākārānugamo yo hi vṛddhyā syād āśvalāyane ||
  130. 5,16.130nāsāv apāṇinīyatve sādhur ity avagamyate |                    dṛṣṭe bhavatu mā vā bhūt kartṛsampratipannatā ||
  131. 5,16.131vaidido vyavahāras tu na kartṛsmaraṇād ṛte |                    burgeṣu gavi gośabdaprayogo gamyate katham ||
  132. 5,16.132gatvā cet kena cid dṛṣṭaḥ, sambanddhā kiṃ na gacchati |                    īśvaratvād agatiś cāsya na kva cit pratibadhyate ||
  133. 5,16.133bahūnāṃ kāryataś cāpi saṅgānaṃ kena vāryate |<481>                    ekatra kathitaṃ cāpi lokenānyatra nīyate ||
  134. 5,16.134vṛddhyādiva, ato vyākhyā dvitīyaivātra śobhanā |                    kāṃś cit prasiddhasambandhān abhyupetya vaded yadi ||
  135. 5,16.135sambandhakaraṇam, tatra ke siddhā iti durvadam |                    na tāvad anya evāsan śabdā iti hi yuktimat ||
  136. 5,16.136viśeṣo 'dyatanānāṃ ca gavādīnāṃ na dṛśyate |                    śabdārthānāditāṃ muktvā sambandhānādikāraṇam ||
  137. 5,16.137na syād anyad, ato vede sambandhādir na vidyate |                    upāyarahitatvena sambandhakaraṇānumā ||
  138. 5,16.138anākhyānānumānaṃ tu dṛṣṭenaiva viruddhyate |<482>                    buddhānāṃ dṛśyamānā ca pratipattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||
  139. 5,16.139upāya iti taddhānirasiddhāvagatiṃ prati |                    hastasaṃjñādyupāyo hi siddho nādyakriyāsu naḥ ||
  140. 5,16.140na hy asau jñātasāmarthyo vinānyair vyavahartṛbhiḥ |                    śabdavṛddhābhidheyāṃś ca pratyakṣeṇātra paśyati ||
  141. 5,16.141śrotuś ca pratipannatvam anumānena ceṣṭayā |                    anyathā 'nupapattyā ca buddhyec chaktiṃ dvayāśritām |                    arthāpattyāvabuddhyante sambandhaṃ tripramāṇakam ||

Chapter 5,17 citrākṣepaparihāra CAP

  1. 5,17.1citrādiniṣphalatve 'pi yaduktaṃ sādhanadvayam |                    tatra hetor asiddhatvam ānantaryaṃ hy acoditam ||
  2. 5,17.2ānantaryaśrutiś cātra sāmārthyād api neṣyate |                    nāviśeṣā phalotpattiḥ karmaṇā nopapadyate ||
  3. 5,17.3karmaṇāṃ cāpi vaicitryād deśakālādyapekṣaṇāt |                    kasya cic cārddhabhuktatvāt karmānyat pratibadhyate ||
  4. 5,17.4tenānantaryaniṣpattiḥ phalasyehāpramāṇikā |                    pratyakṣādivisaṃvādo na śabde doṣamāsajet ||
  5. 5,17.5ānantaryavisaṃvādo nāviśeṣapravartinīm |                    codanāṃ bādhituṃ śaktaḥ sphuṭād viṣayabhedataḥ ||<484>
  6. 5,17.6yā tu mardanasādharmyād ānantaryā 'numā kṛtā |                    bādhyate 'nupalabdhyāsau samānaviṣayā yataḥ ||
  7. 5,17.7dṛṣṭārthasyāpi sevāder āyātam api satphalam |                    utpadyate cireṇaiva pratibandhena kena cit ||
  8. 5,17.8uptamātre na hi vrīhau phalam utpadyate kva cit |                    athāṅkuro 'pi tatra syāt, svargo 'py astīti gamyatām ||
  9. 5,17.9sthūlībhūtaś cireṇaiṣa bhogyatvaṃ pratipadyate |                    sarvasyotpadyamānasya kramaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sthitaḥ ||
  10. 5,17.10anantaraphalatvaṃ tu citrāder yadi sādhyate |                    tataḥ syāt siddhasādhyatvam anyadā na phalaṃ bhavet ||
  11. 5,17.11vyabhicārāc ca sevādeḥ paśvādeḥ sādhanāntaram |                    kim apy adṛṣṭam asty eva tatrānyanniṣpramāṇakam ||<485>
  12. 5,17.12īśvarecchādhikārādiśabdaliṅgādivarjanāt |                    kṛtaṃ kadā cic citrādiśabdena tv avagamyate ||
  13. 5,17.13nirnimittā na cotpattiḥ, na hi sarvāpramāṇatā |                    bodhayan na ca śabdo 'tra prāmāṇyād ativarttate ||
  14. 5,17.14yeṣāṃ tv iha phalāny eva citrādīnīti kalpanā |                    nirnimittaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ syād ihākṛtakarmaṇām ||
  15. 5,17.15citrādīnāṃ phalaṃ tāvat kṣīṇaṃ tatraiva janmani |                    na ca svargaphalasyeha kaś cid aṃśo 'nuvartate ||
  16. 5,17.16naiva hy anyaphalaṃ karma sādhayen naḥ phalāntaram |<486>                    gautamīye 'pi taccheṣas tasmāc citrādyapekṣayā ||
  17. 5,17.17svābhāvikatve siddhe ca karmānantarabhāvy api |                    phalaṃ kriyānimittatvaṃ na kathañ cit prapadyate ||
  18. 5,17.18tatra mlecchādivat sarve karmākṛtvāpi vaidikam |                    palaṃ labhanta ity evaṃ naṣṭā vedapramāṇatā ||
  19. 5,17.19anantaraṃ niyogena paśvādi ca bhaved yadi |                    pratyakṣaphalataiva syāt trivṛtpānavirekavat ||
  20. 5,17.20janmāntarānubhūtaṃ ca na smaryata itīdṛśam |                    na bhāṣyaṃ na ca sūtraṃ syād aprāpte śāstram arthavat ||
  21. 5,17.21tasmāt kālāviśeṣeṇa codanārtho yathā sthitaḥ |                    sa tathaivānugantavyo nādhiko niṣpramāṇakaḥ ||
  22. 5,17.22sarveṣāṃ karmavaiguṇyāt phalābhāvaṃ vadanti ye |                    ānantaryam upetyaiva te svābhāvikavādinaḥ ||
  23. 5,17.23svargasyāmuṣmikatvaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhādye sthāpayiṣyate |<487>                    paśvāder niyamābhāvo yogasiddhir itīha tu ||
  24. 5,17.24yadā kadā cid bhavad etad iṣyate phalaṃ hi paśvādi na sāmparāyikam |                    tathā sthitasyaiva hi tasya sādhanaṃ vidhīyate yo 'pi bhṛśaṃ tvarānvitaḥ ||
  25. 5,17.25sādhāraṇaṃ yat tu palaṃ bahūnāṃ svabhāvatas tādṛśaṃ eva ceṣṭam |                    sarvasya vā ''san na tayaiva kāmyaṃ vṛṣṭyādi tac caihikam eva yuktam ||
  26. 5,17.26kamipadam aviśiṣṭaṃ yady api śrūyate vā bhavati phalaviśeṣī nānyathā kāmyate hi |                    phalati yadi ni sarva tat kadā cit tadaiva dhruvam aparam abhuktaṃ karma śāstrīyamās te ||

Chapter 5,18 ātmavāda ATV

  1. 5,18.1sākṣād yady api sambandho nātmano yajñasādhanaiḥ |                    tathāpi lakṣaṇāvṛttyā śarīradvārako bhavet ||
  2. 5,18.2pratyakṣatvaṃ ca dehasthaṃ bhāktam ātmani kalpitam |                    ātmanaḥ svargayānaṃ vā śarīrasyopacaryyate ||
  3. 5,18.3nairātmyenātra cākṣiptāḥ sarvā eva hi codanāḥ |<489>                    sādhyasādhanasambandhas tadukto na hi siddhyati ||
  4. 5,18.4tā hi kartuḥ phalenāhuḥ sambandhaṃ kvāpi janmani |                    na ca vijñānamātratve bhoktṛkartṛtvasambhavaḥ ||
  5. 5,18.5śarīravinipātāc ca paraṃ nānyad yadeṣyate |                    adattaphalaiṣṭyādau tadā tadvacanaṃ mṛṣā ||
  6. 5,18.6tasmād vedapramāṇārtham ātmātra pratipādyate |                    yady api prakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ vyākhyāyetārthavādataḥ ||
  7. 5,18.7śarīrendriyabuddhibhyo vyatiriktatvam ātmanaḥ |                    nityatvaṃ ceṣyate, śeṣaṃ śarīrādi vinaśyate ||
  8. 5,18.8nityaḥ kartṛtvabhoktṛtve pratipanno 'pi san yadā |                    na karmaphalasambandhaṃ bhogakāle 'vabudhyate ||
  9. 5,18.9mayā yat tu kṛtaṃ karma tasyedaṃ bhujyate phalam |                    śubhāśubhaṃ mayaiveti tadā ko 'sya raso bhavet ||<490>
  10. 5,18.10aprāmṛśyamāne hi svakarmapratyaye phale |                    na viśeṣo bhavet kaś cit svaparātmopabhogayoḥ ||
  11. 5,18.11kurvann apy aśubhaṃ karma tenaivaṃ cintayen naraḥ |                    na smariṣyāmi bhoge 'ham iti naitad vivarjayet ||
  12. 5,18.12tatra nityatvapakṣe 'pi kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau |                    phalatas tulyarūpau ced vṛthā tatpratipādanam ||
  13. 5,18.13naiṣa doṣaḥ, na bhoge hi smṛtir na upayujyate |                    na pravṛtir nivṛttir vā bhogakāle smṛter bhavet ||
  14. 5,18.14tadaṅgaṃ yaḥ parāmarśas tadastitvaṃ ca mṛgyate |                    prāk pravṛttes tu so 'sty eva viduṣāṃ śāstrataḥ sphuṭaḥ ||
  15. 5,18.15paścād api ca śāstrajñā vimṛśanty eva ke cana |                    teṣām evādhikāraś ca mā bhūd aviduṣāṃ tu saḥ ||
  16. 5,18.16parāmarśaś ca sarvatra nāsti sarvapramāṇakaḥ |<491>                    na cānyenāparāmṛṣṭe syād anyasyāpramāṇatā ||
  17. 5,18.17nāvabudhyeta yas tv evaṃ mamāsmāt karmaṇaḥ phalam |                    bhaviṣyatīty avidvattvād daivād evātra na kriyā ||
  18. 5,18.18aparāmṛśyamāne 'pi svāpakāle sukhāśraye |                    sambhoge mṛduśayyādau prākpravṛttiś ca dṛśyate ||
  19. 5,18.19bhogakāle 'nusandadhyāt phalaṃ yadi tu kaś cana |                    rathādikarmavad yāge śāstraṃ syād aprakalpakam ||
  20. 5,18.20tava nityavibhutvābhyām ātmāno niṣkriyā yadi |                    sukhaduḥkhāvikāryāś ca kīdṛśo kartṛbhoktṛtā ||
  21. 5,18.21atha kartṛtvavelāyāṃ duḥkhādeś cāpi janmani |                    prāgrūpād anyathātvaṃ syān nityatāsya virudhyate ||<492>
  22. 5,18.22nānityaśabdavācyatvam ātmano vinivāryate |                    vikriyāmātravācitve na hy ucchedo 'sya tāvatā ||
  23. 5,18.23syātām atyantanāśe 'sya kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau |                    na tv avasthāntaraprāptau loke bālayuvādivat ||
  24. 5,18.24avasthāntarabhāvyetat phalaṃ mama śubhāśubham |                    iti jñātvānutiṣṭhaṃś ca vijahac ceṣṭate janaḥ ||
  25. 5,18.25anavasthāntaraprāptir dṛśyate na ca kasya cit |                    anucchedāt tu nānyatvaṃ bhoktur loko 'vagacchati ||
  26. 5,18.26sukhaduḥkhādyavasthāś ca gacchann api naro mama |                    caitanyadravyasattādirūpaṃ naiva vimuñcati ||
  27. 5,18.27duḥkhinaḥ sukhyavasthāyāṃ naśyeyuḥ sarva eva te |                    duḥkhitvaṃ cānuvarteta vināśe vikriyātmake ||
  28. 5,18.28tasmād ubhayahānena vyāvṛttyanugamātmakaḥ |                    puruṣo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ kuṇḍalādiṣu svarṇatvat ||<493>
  29. 5,18.29na ca kartṛtvabhoktṛtve puṃso 'vasthāsam āśrite |                    tenāvasthāvatas tattvāt karttaivāpnoti tatphalam ||
  30. 5,18.30na cāvasthāntarotpāde pūrvātyantaṃ vinaśyati |                    uttarānuguṇatvāt tu sāmānyātmani līyate ||
  31. 5,18.31svarūpeṇa hy avasthānām anyonyasya virodhitā |                    aviruddhas tu sarvāsu sāmānyātmā pravartate ||
  32. 5,18.32nairātmyavādapakṣe tu pūrvam evāvabudhyate |                    madvināśāt phalaṃ nasyānmatto 'nyasyātha vā bhavet ||
  33. 5,18.33iti naiva pravṛttiḥ syān na ca vedapramāṇatā |                    janmānare 'bhyupete 'pi jñānamātrātmavādinām ||
  34. 5,18.34jñānānāṃ kṣaṇikatvād dhi kartṛbhoktranyatā bhavet |                    niṣkriyatvāvibhutvābhyāṃ na ca dehāntarāśritiḥ ||<494>
  35. 5,18.35kartā ya eva santāno nanu bhoktā sa eva naḥ |                    vijñānakṣaṇabhedas tu tvadavasthāntaraiḥ samaḥ ||
  36. 5,18.36kartṛtvam eva duḥsādhaṃ dīrghakāleṣu karmasu |                    satsu jñānasahastreṣu kulakalpopamaṃ hi tat ||
  37. 5,18.37vyatirikto hi santāno yadi nābhyupagamyate |                    santāninām anityatvāt kartā kaś cin na labhyate ||
  38. 5,18.38bhoktur atyantabhedāc ca prasajyetākṛtāgamaḥ |                    kṛtanāśaṃ tu na brūmaḥ kṛtaṃ naiva hi kena cit ||
  39. 5,18.39santānānanyatāyāṃ tu vācoyuktyantareṇa te |                    tatra coktam, na cāvastu santānaḥ kartṛtāṃ vrajet ||
  40. 5,18.40santānakṣaṇikatve ca tad eva, akṣaṇikas tv atha |                    siddhāntahāniḥ, <495> evaṃ ca so 'pi dravyāntaraṃ bhavet ||
  41. 5,18.41ekā cāvyatiriktā ca santānibhyo 'tha santatiḥ |                    bhedābhedau prasaṅktavyau grāhyagrāhakayor yathā ||
  42. 5,18.42tasmād atyantabhedo vā kathañ cid vāpi bhinnatā |                    santānasyety ayaṃ cātmā syād vaiśeṣikasāṃkhyayoḥ ||
  43. 5,18.43santāno 'yaṃ sa eveti na tv abhedād vinā bhavet |                    vāyudopādisantāne vāyutvādir na bhidyate ||
  44. 5,18.44jñānatvenāpy abhinnatvaṃ śūnyavāde nirākṛtam |                    tathaiva karmabhir veṣṭā phalārthaṃ cittavāsanā ||
  45. 5,18.45na cātra vāsanākālaṃ kiñ cic cittam avasthitam |                    avastutvāc ca santānaḥ karmabhinaiva vāsyate ||<496>
  46. 5,18.46tatpāramparyajāte 'pi bhuñjāne karmaṇaḥ phalam |                    tādātmyena vinā spaṣṭau kṛtanāśākṛtāgamau ||
  47. 5,18.47santānāntarajebhyaś ca yo hetuphalabhāvataḥ |                    viśeṣaḥ so 'pi dussādhaḥ, parihāro na cānayoḥ ||
  48. 5,18.48tasminn asaty api brūyāḥ parihāraṃ tvam anyathā |                    samānapṛthivīvāsajñānatvādyaviśeṣataḥ ||
  49. 5,18.49samāna iti nāpy etadekatvānugamād vinā |                    tena yaccittajaṃ tasya santāna iti vo mṛṣā ||
  50. 5,18.50na hi yacchabdatacchabdau vartete bhinnavastuni |                    tenaikātmakataiṣṭavyā tatsantānātmavādibhiḥ ||<497>
  51. 5,18.51nanv anyatvaṃ vidanto 'pi putrādiphalasiddhaye |                    pravartante yathā tadvajjñānasantānino 'pi naḥ ||
  52. 5,18.52anyatve ca samāne 'pi yathā vaṃśāntarodbhavāḥ |                    na labhante phalaṃ tadvat santānāntarajāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ||
  53. 5,18.53na tāvad buddhir atraivam, api cātmaphalecchayā |                    putrādibharaṇe vṛttiḥ syāt tad apy atra nāsti te ||
  54. 5,18.54phalāntaram anuddiśya na ca putrādi bibhrati |                    vinaṣṭasya tu nātmīyasantānabharaṇāt phalam ||
  55. 5,18.55yas tv anenaiva mārgeṇa phalāntaram apīcchati |                    svasantānyantarair bhogyaṃ tatsantānāny upakārakam ||
  56. 5,18.56anavasthedṛśī tasya svopabhogād ṛte bhavet |                    naiva hy anyo 'pi santānī kaś cit tasyātmavanmataḥ ||<498>
  57. 5,18.57yāvad yāvac ca dūrasthe santānini phalaṃ bhavet |                    tāvat tāvac ca tannaśyet sutarāṃ viprakarṣataḥ ||
  58. 5,18.58bharaṇaṃ yadapatyānāṃ tiryagādiṣu dṛśyate |                    ajñānaṃ śaraṇaṃ tatra prājñānāṃ tu na yujyate ||
  59. 5,18.59dehāntare ca buddhīnāṃ sañcāro nopapadyate |                    pūrvadehād bahir bhāvo na ca tāsāṃ pratīyate ||
  60. 5,18.60vāyunā preryamāṇaṃ hi jvālādyanyatra sañcaret |                    buddheḥ kāraṇadeśāt tu preraṇaṃ nāsti kena cit ||
  61. 5,18.61amūrtatvāt svayaṃ nāsāvutplutyā 'nyatra gacchati |                    jīvaddehe 'pi tenāsyā gamanaṃ nopapadyate ||
  62. 5,18.62antarābhavadehas tu niṣiddho vindhyavāsinā |                    tadastitve pramāṇaṃ hi na kiñ cid avagamyate ||
  63. 5,18.63sahasā jāyate tac ca sahasaiva vinaśyati |                    sūkṣmarūpādiyuktaṃ cety utprekṣāmātram eva tat ||<499>
  64. 5,18.64saty api jñānasañcāras tatra syān niṣpramāṇakaḥ |                    tena cānyaśarīreṣu punarnikṣepakalpanā ||
  65. 5,18.65kalalādiṣu vijñānam astīty etac ca sāhasam |                    asañjātendriyatvād dhi na tatrārtho 'vagamyate ||
  66. 5,18.66na cārthāvagater anyad rūpaṃ jñānasya yujyate |                    mūrcchādāv api tenāsya sadbhāvo nopapadyate ||
  67. 5,18.67na cāpi śaktirūpeṇa tadā dhīr avatiṣṭhate |                    nirāśrayatvāc chaktīnāṃ sthitir na hy avakalpate ||
  68. 5,18.68yadi bhūtendriyādhārā jñānaśaktir bhavet tataḥ |                    tac caitanyaṃ prasajyeta na ca janmāntaraṃ bhavet ||
  69. 5,18.69pariṇāmavivekādyaiḥ śaktyabhivyaktyanugrahāt |                    tebhya eva bhaved buddhir na buddhyantarapūrvikā ||<500>
  70. 5,18.70tathaivottarakāle 'pi pūrvabuddher yad ucyate |                    buddhyantaraprasūtatvaṃ dṛṣṭānto 'tra na vidyate ||
  71. 5,18.71athādhāravinirmuktā śaktiḥ syāt kalalādiṣu |                    paścād vijñānasiddhyartham ātmā śaktyabhidho bhavet ||
  72. 5,18.72śaktyādhāraprakḷptau vā nātmano 'nyaḥ prakalpyate |                    jvālābudbudavad vṛttir na cādhārād dhiyām ||
  73. 5,18.73jñānaśaktisvabhāvo 'to nityaḥ sarvagataḥ pumān |                    dehāntarakṣamaḥ kalpyaḥ so 'gacchann eva yokṣyate ||<501>
  74. 5,18.74yajamānatvam apy ātmā sakriyatvāt prapadyate |                    na parispanda evaikaḥ kriyā naḥ kaṇabhojivat ||
  75. 5,18.75na ca svasamavetaiva kartṛbhiḥ kriyate kriyā |                    kriyā dhātvarthamātraṃ syād anyādhāre 'pi kartṛtā ||
  76. 5,18.76sattājñānādirūpāṇāṃ kartā tāvat svayaṃ pumān |                    yo 'pi bhūtaparispandas tatrādhiṣṭānato bhavet ||
  77. 5,18.77taduddeśapravṛtteś ca yā yā dehendriyaiḥ kriyā |                    kriyate puruṣeṇaiva sā sā sarvā kṛtocyate ||
  78. 5,18.78naiva hy eṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ syāt puruṣeṇāparigrahe |                    asvātantryād ato naiṣāṃ parispande 'pi kartṛtā ||<502>
  79. 5,18.79tatkarmopārjitaiś cetaiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu karmasu |                    kartṛtā yajamānānām ṛtvikparaśukarmavat ||
  80. 5,18.80yathā parikrayāmnānād ṛtvigdvārā kriyeṣyate |                    gamanādividhes tadvad bhūtadvāratvam āśritam ||
  81. 5,18.81krayo yathātmano nāsti gamanādi tathaiva hi |                    vidhīyate ca tenātra paradvārāsya kartṛtā ||
  82. 5,18.82yathā vā devadattasya cchedane kāṣṭhasaṃśrite |                    kartṛtvam evaṃ puṃsaḥ syāc charīragamanādiṣu ||
  83. 5,18.83vyāpārāntaratas tatra kartṛtvaṃ ced ihāpi naḥ |                    saṅkalpasattvavattvābhyāṃ pumāniṣṭaḥ prayojakaḥ ||
  84. 5,18.84sādhāraṇyena kartṛtvaṃ sattvavattvena karmasu |                    saṅkalpanaiḥ punarbhedāt pratikarmāsya kartṛtā ||<503>
  85. 5,18.85na ca sarvatra tulyatvaṃ syāt prayojakakarmaṇām |                    calanena hy asiṃ yoddhā prayuṅkte cchedanaṃ prati ||
  86. 5,18.86senāpatis tu vācaiva bhṛtyānāṃ viniyojakaḥ |                    rājā sannidhimātreṇa viniyuṅkte kadā cana ||
  87. 5,18.87tasmād acalato 'pi syāc calane kartṛtātmanaḥ |                    yathaivābhidyamānasya devadattasya bhettṛtā ||
  88. 5,18.88karmāntarair yadā dānaṃ svavyāpāraḥ sa eva vā |                    bhūtakriyāsu puṃsaḥ syāt, tāni bhūtāntaraiḥ punaḥ ||
