  89. 5,18.89tāni bhūtāntarebhyaś cety evamādir na vidyate |                    karmakṣayāt tv anātmīyaiḥ kṛtaṃ karma na limpati ||
  90. 5,18.90anvārambhaṇamānādāvaudumbaryādivarttini |                    svarūpāsambhavād yaṣṭuḥ śarīreṇaiva kartṛtā ||<504>
  91. 5,18.91tasmād yathākṛtau śāstraṃ pravṛttaṃ vyaktim āśrayet |                    tathā puṃsi pravṛttasya bhūtendriyasamāśrayaḥ ||
  92. 5,18.92parair abhigatān pūrvam ātmahetun nirasyati |                    nety etāvad avacchedyam, vidharmāṇa ime yataḥ ||
  93. 5,18.93 athāvasthāntaraṃ tatra tathā mṛtyur apīṣyatām |
  94. 5,18.94etāvan iha bhedaḥ syāc charīre dṛḍha eva yā |                    prāṇādyapagatis tatra nimittaṃ na pratīyate ||
  95. 5,18.95guṇo dravyavināśād vā vināśam upagacchati |                    guṇāntaropapātād vā tasmād utkṛtya nāśyate ||
  96. 5,18.96na tāvat tad dvayaṃ mṛtyau sarvasyaivopalabhyate |                    avinaṣṭaśarīrasya prāṇādiś cāpagacchati ||<505>
  97. 5,18.97tasmān na dehadharmatvaṃ prāṇāder iti gamyate |                    tasmin dṛṣṭe 'py asadbhāvāt sragvilepanagandhavat ||
  98. 5,18.98bahirvṛttitvam apy asti prāṇāder iti gamyate |                    parendriyaiḥ, sukhādis tu nāntaratvāt pratīyate ||
  99. 5,18.99prahṛṣṭavadanatvādiliṅgagamyaṃ sadaiva hi |                    antaḥsthiter na dṛṣṭiś cet, pāṭite 'py anupagrahāt ||
  100. 5,18.100antaḥśarīre rūpādi pāṭitasyopalabhyate |                    na sukhādiḥ, ago 'syāsau na manobuddhivad guṇaḥ ||
  101. 5,18.101guṇatvād āśritatvaṃ hi sukhādeḥ syād rasādivat |                    ya āśritaḥ sa ātmā, <506> iti bruvāṇasyaitaduttaram ||
  102. 5,18.102puṇānāṃ paratantratvāt guṇavān anumīyate |                    siddhe guṇatve tat tv asmān pratyasiddhaṃ sukhādiṣu ||
  103. 5,18.103bhedena kim upanyastā tulyanyāyecchayā smṛtiḥ |                    ubhayaṃ na hy adṛṣṭe 'rthe vāsanātaś ca siddhyati ||
  104. 5,18.104upalabdhimanāśritya smṛtyaivecchopajāyate |                    upalabdhisamāno 'syāḥ kartā naikāntato bhavet ||
  105. 5,18.105upalabdhyanusāreṇa smṛtyātmā punar iṣyate |                    samānas tena kartāsti tadarthaṃ punar ucyate ||
  106. 5,18.106tatrāpi tu samānāyāṃ santatau vāsanā yataḥ |                    tasmāt saty api bhinnatve smaraṇaṃ vyavatiṣṭate ||<507>
  107. 5,18.107hetuṣv evaṃ parokteṣu pratiṣiddheṣu samprati |                    ahampratyayavijñeyaḥ svayamātmopapādyate ||
  108. 5,18.108ahaṃ yāmīty ahaṃśabdaḥ śarīrārthaḥ prayujyate |                    gantṛtvāt tasya, na hy ātmā gamanaṃ pratipadyate ||
  109. 5,18.109smaraṇapratyabhijñāne bhavetāṃ vāsanāvaśāt |                    anyārthaviṣaye, jñātuḥ pratyabhijñā tu durlabhā ||
  110. 5,18.110ahaṃ vedmīty ahaṃ buddhir jñātāram adhigacchati |                    tatra syād jñātṛvijñānaṃ tadādhāro 'tha vā pumān ||
  111. 5,18.111kṛtaṃ bhūtendriyāṇāṃ ca caitanyapratiṣedhanam |                    samastavyastasaṅghātavivekapariṇāminām ||
  112. 5,18.112sāṅkhyādibhiḥ, <508> aśuddhatvāt saṅghātāt sanniveśataḥ |                    mṛtavac ca śarīratvād bhūtatvād bāhyabhūtavat ||
  113. 5,18.113cetanatve hi sarveṣāṃ na sambandhaḥ parasparam |                    samatvāt, ekacaitanye 'nyasyāṅgatvaṃ virudhyate ||
  114. 5,18.114saṅghātasanniveśau ca na staḥ pārārthyavarjitau |                    bhoktā ca cetanaḥ kaś cid astīty atrāviruddhatā ||
  115. 5,18.115yadi syād jñānamātraṃ ca kṣaṇikaṃ jñātṛ tatra vaḥ |                    na bhavet pratyabhijñānaṃ pūrvajñātari samprati ||
  116. 5,18.116jñātavān aham evedaṃ puredānīṃ ca vedmy aham |<509>                    tasya jñānakṣaṇaḥ ko nu viṣayaḥ parikalpyatām ||
  117. 5,18.117pūrvavṛtte hi viṣaye jñātavān iti sambhavet |                    jānāmīti na satyaṃ syān nedānīṃ vetty asau tataḥ ||
  118. 5,18.118yadīdānīntano grāhyo jānāmīty upapadyate |                    jñātavān ity ado 'satyaṃ naivājñāsīdayaṃ yataḥ ||
  119. 5,18.119ubhayagrāhyatāṃ tu dvayam apy anṛtaṃ bhavet |                    na hy etau jñātavantau vā jānīto vādhunā punaḥ ||
  120. 5,18.120santāno na ca tadgrāhyo dvairūpyasyāsambhavāt |                    jñātavān na hy asau pūrvam avastutvān na vādhunā ||
  121. 5,18.121sāmānyaṃ na ca kiñ cit te jñātṛ pūrvāparakṣaṇe |                    sādṛśyāt pratyabhijñā cen na syād asadṛśeṣu sā ||
  122. 5,18.122gām ahaṃ jñātavān pūrvam aśvaṃ jānāmy ahaṃ punaḥ |                    atha jñātṛtvasāmānyaṃ tat syād dehāntareṣv api ||
  123. 5,18.123tatra sarveṇa vijñāte bhaved aham iti smṛtiḥ |                    ekasantānaje cāpi sa iti syāt kṣaṇe matiḥ ||
  124. 5,18.124yathā dehāntarajñāne ghaṭādau vā bahiḥ sthite |<510>                    jñātari pratyabhijñāṃ ca vāsanā kartum arhati ||
  125. 5,18.125nātasmin sa iti jñānaṃ na hy asau bhrāntikāraṇam |                    na cāhampratyayo bhrāntir iṣṭo bādhakavarjanāt ||
  126. 5,18.126jñātur anyaś ca viṣayas tasya na syāt svabhāvataḥ |                    ahaṃ pratyayavijñeyo jñātā naḥ sarvadaiva hi ||
  127. 5,18.127guruḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśo vāham iti dehe 'pi yā matiḥ |                    bhrāntiḥ sā, bhedarūpaṃ hi guru me tad itīṣyate ||
  128. 5,18.128idaṃ mamedṛśaṃ cakṣurmano me bhrāntam ity api |                    indriyeṣv api bhedena vyavahāraś ca dṛśyate ||
  129. 5,18.129ajñātṛtvasya siddhatvād virodhād bhedavaty api |                    pratyāsattinimittas tu syād abhedamatir bhramaḥ ||<511>
  130. 5,18.130mamātmeti matibhedavyapadeśena yātmanaḥ |                    tatrāvasthātmanā bhedaṃ jñānasyāśritya kalpanā ||
  131. 5,18.131mametyetasya mukhyārtho nātmano 'nyaḥ pratīyate |                    tenāsau bhedahetuḥ syād, bhedaś ca jñānahetukaḥ ||
  132. 5,18.132ye cehājñātanānātvās teṣāṃ deheṣv ahaṃ matiḥ |                    tatrāpy ātmābhimānenety ahambuddhir dhruvātmani ||
  133. 5,18.133ye tu vijñātanānātvās te deheṣv anahaṃkṛtāḥ |                    jānāmy aham itīdaṃ tu jñānaṃ naiva nivarttate ||<512>
  134. 5,18.134tannivṛttau na teṣāṃ syād dhyānaṃ śiṣyopadeśane |                    pravṛttir dṛśyate sā ca, tenātmā taiḥ pratīyate ||
  135. 5,18.135śāstrādavardhavijñāte yady ahaṃ jñātavān iti |                    nāvagacchet tataḥ sarvaḥ pravartetāditaḥ punaḥ ||
  136. 5,18.136tenāsmāt pratyabhijñānāt sarvalokāvadhāritāt |                    nairātmyavādabādhaḥ syāt, ete ca pratihetavaḥ ||
  137. 5,18.137hyastanāhammatigrāhyo jñātādyāpy anuvarttate |                    ahaṃpratyayagamyatvād idānīntaboddhṛvat ||
  138. 5,18.138eṣa vā hyo bhavej jñātā jñātṛtvāt tat eva vā |                    hyastanajñātṛvat, teṣāṃ pratyayānāṃ ca sādhyatā ||
  139. 5,18.139ekasantānasambandhijñātrahampratyayatvataḥ |                    hyastanādyatanāḥ save tulyārthaś caikabuddhivat ||
  140. 5,18.140vedādevātmanāstitvaṃ yo nāma pratipadyate |                    virodhaṃ vātmanā brūyāt taṃ prati brāhmaṇābhidhā ||<513>
  141. 5,18.141anyathānupapatteś ca vidhinātmanyapekṣite |                    astitvadyotanād etair arthākṣiptasamarthanam ||
  142. 5,18.142śāntāyāṃ vācyaśaktāyām ātmā kena prakāśyate |                    ātmanaiva prakāśyo 'yam ātmā jyotir itīritam ||
  143. 5,18.143agrāhya iti sāmānyāt sarveṇeti pratīyate |                    ātmajyotiṣṭvavacanāt parair ity avatiṣṭhate ||
  144. 5,18.144arthād evārthabuddhir yā sā śuddhaivopamocyate |                    sādṛśyabodhanaṃ śabdair upamānāgamau punaḥ ||<514>
  145. 5,18.145ātmajñānāvinābhūtadṛṣṭaceṣṭānirūpaṇāt |                    pareṣām ātmavijñānam anumānād udāhṛtam ||
  146. 5,18.146sadasannāśyanāśātmaparikīrtanam ūḍhayā |                    coditaḥ pūrvapakṣo 'yam iti siddhāntam abravīt ||
  147. 5,18.147avināśī svarūpeṇa puruṣo yā tu nāśitā |                    mātrāṇāṃ sā 'dhikārāṇām, bhūtādīnām asaṃjñitā ||<515>
  148. 5,18.148ity āha nāsti kyanirākariṣṇur ātmāstitāṃ bhāṣyakṛdatra yuktyā |                    dṛḍhatvam etadviṣayaś ca bodhaḥ prayāti vedāntaniṣevaṇena ||

Chapter 6 śabdanityatādhikaraṇa SNA

  1. 6.1yady anityatvapakṣe 'pi śabdād artho 'vagamyate |                    anādir vyavahāraś ca nityatvaṃ kiṃ nu sādhyate ||
  2. 6.2satyam icchanti te 'py evaṃ nyāyas tatra parīkṣyate |                    na parābhyupagatyaiva prāmāṇyam avatiṣṭhate ||
  3. 6.3yadā hi kṣaṇikaḥ śabdo na śakto 'rthāvadhāraṇe |                    yuktyāvadhāryate tatra nirmalā vedadhīr bhavet ||<516>
  4. 6.4nirmūlair api vijñānair dṛṣṭārtheṣu bhaved gatiḥ |                    śrutimātrāśrayatvāt tu dharmo dauḥsthityam āśritaḥ ||
  5. 6.5anādivyavahāratvam ādimad vastusaṃśrayam |                    pratyākhyeyam, ghaṭatvādijātau vyaktibhramo hi saḥ ||
  6. 6.6sthite kūṭasthanityatve vyavahārasya nityatā |                    kūṭasthena vinaitena na tasyālambanaṃ bhavet ||
  7. 6.7prasiddhatvād ṛte sarvo vyavahāro hi neṣyate |                    tasmād vedapramāṇārthaṃ nityatvam iha sādhyate ||
  8. 6.8parasparāvinābhāvād anityakṛtakatvayoḥ |                    kāraṇaṃ dvayasiddhyarthaṃ kiñ cit kasya cid ucyate ||<517>
  9. 6.9nānādeśāvagamyatvād yugapat tulyabuddhibhiḥ |                    asmābhiḥ, kṛtakaḥ śabdo bhaved akṣaralekhyavat ||
  10. 6.10yaugapadyopalambhād vā bhedo bhedāc ca kāryatā |                    avibhutve hi yugapannaiko nānāvagamyate ||
  11. 6.11kārtyena cāvagamyatvād ekadeśe ghaṭādivat |                    śabdasyāvibhūtā, tasmād anyatāsya mukhāntare ||
  12. 6.12ekaḥ sann ekadeśastho yadaikena prayujyate |                    tadā vaktrantare na syād ekavaktṛmukhādivat ||<518>
  13. 6.13kāryatve syāt kriyābhedāt phalabhedaḥ pratikriyam |                    tenaikabuddhiḥ sādṛśyāt sphuṭe 'nyatve 'vakalpate ||
  14. 6.14nityatve tv ekabuddheḥ syān na kiñ cid bhrāntikāraṇam |                    kāmaṃ deśā iti nyāyāt tac caikatvaṃ viruddhyate ||
  15. 6.15na ca vyañjakabhedena deśabhedopalambhanam |                    pradīpair bhinnadeśasthair na bhinno vyajyate ghaṭaḥ ||
  16. 6.16vyomānavayavaṃ caiṣāṃ dhvanīnām āśrayo matam |<519>                    savyaṅgyānām ataḥ sarvair vyaktir ekatra te bhavet ||
  17. 6.17vastvantaravikāryatvāt smṛtisādṛśyasādhitāt |                    ikārāder anityatvaṃ dadhikṣīraguḍādivat ||
  18. 6.18hetuvṛddhyanusāritvāt kāryatāsya ghaṭādivat |                    na hi dīpasahasre 'pi vyañjake varddhate ghaṭaḥ ||
  19. 6.19anaikāntikatā tāvaddhetūnām iha kathyate |                    prayatnānantarā dṛṣṭir nitye 'pi na viruddhyate ||
  20. 6.20tasmāt tatraiva dṛṣṭatvād anyatrādṛṣṭakalpanā |<520>                    prāgūrdhvānupalabdho ced dhetutvena vivakṣite ||
  21. 6.21jātyaulūkyasya, sāṃkhyasya caitanyenātmavartinā |                    śākyasyāpi tv anaikāntaḥ kṣaṇikavyatirekibhiḥ ||
  22. 6.22pratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyānirodhavyom abhistribhiḥ |                    buddhipūrvaṃ vināśe hi pratisaṃkhyānirodhadhīḥ ||
  23. 6.23abuddhipūrvakas teṣāṃ nirodho 'pratisaṃkhyayā |                    tau ca dvāv apy anāśitvād iṣṭāvakṛtakāv api ||
  24. 6.24āhuḥ svabhāvasiddhaṃ hi te vināśam ahetukam |                    hetur yasya vināśo 'pi tasya dṛṣṭo 'ṅkurādivat ||
  25. 6.25vināśasya vināśas tu nāsti tasmād akṛtrimaḥ |<521>                    bhavati hy agnisambandhāt kāṣṭād aṅgārasantatiḥ ||
  26. 6.26mudgarādihatāc cāpi kapālaṃ jāyatte ghaṭāt |                    svābhāviko vināśas tu jātamātrapratiṣṭitaḥ ||
  27. 6.27sūkṣmaḥ sadṛśasantānadṛtter anupalakṣitaḥ |                    yadā vilakṣaṇo hetuḥ patet sadṛśasantatau ||
  28. 6.28vilakṣaṇena kāryeṇa sthūlo 'bhivyajyate tadā |                    tenāsadṛśasantāno hetoḥ sañjāyate yataḥ ||
  29. 6.29tenaivākriyamāṇo 'pi nāśo 'bhivyajyate sphūṭaḥ |                    sa mudgaraprahārādiprayatnānantarīyakaḥ ||
  30. 6.30yasmād akṛtako dṛṣṭo, hetuḥ syād vyabhicāryataḥ |                    ākāśam api nityaṃ sad yadā bhūmijalāvṛtam ||
  31. 6.31vyajyate tadapohena svananotsecanādibhiḥ |                    prayatnānantaraṃ jñānaṃ tadā tatrāpi dṛśyate ||
  32. 6.32tenānaikāntiko hetur yaduktaṃ tatra darśanāt |                    atha sthagitam apy etad asty evety anumīyate ||<522>
  33. 6.33tirohitānabhivyakteḥ śabdabuddhiprabandhavat |                    śabdasyaivānavasthānād iti hetuṃ vaded yadi ||
  34. 6.34asthānād ity ayaṃ hetus tadānaikāntiko bhavet |                    ākāśadhīprabandho hi tadā tasmin na tiṣṭati ||
  35. 6.35tirohitānabhivyakteḥ śabdabuddhiprabandhavat |                    śabdasyaivānavasthanād iti hetuṃ vaded yadi ||
  36. 6.36asiddha eva vaktavyas tato 'bhivyaktivādinā |                    tadvyāpārakṛtatve 'pi vyaṅgyair mūlodakādibhiḥ ||<523>
  37. 6.37kutakatve 'pi teṣāṃ hi notpattiḥ khananādinā |                    na cāccāraṇato 'nyāsti śabdasyotpādikā kriyā ||
  38. 6.38nibandharyasatīty evaṃ viśiṣṭe 'pi, tathaiva naḥ |                    abandhāḥ syur yaditeṣām abodho hetvabhāvataḥ ||
  39. 6.39vyañjakābhāvataḥ śabde 'py abodho badhirādivat |                    tasyaiva vā nibandhṛtve bhaved dhetor asiddhatā ||
  40. 6.40atha pūrvāparāsattvaṃ hitus tatrāpy asiddhatā |                    sann eva sādhānābhāvāc chabdo naivopalabhyate ||
  41. 6.41kṣaṇikaṃ sādhanaṃ cāsya buddhir apy anuvartate |                    meghāndhakāraśarvaryā vidyujjanitadṛṣṭivat ||<524>
  42. 6.42yathā ghaṭāder dīpādir abhivyañjaka iṣyate |                    cakṣuṣo'nugrahād evaṃ dhvaniḥ syāc chrītrasaṃskṛteḥ ||
  43. 6.43na ca paryanuyogo 'tra kenākāreṇa saṃskṛtiḥ |                    utpattāv api tulyatvāc chaktis tatrāpy atīndriyā ||<525>
  44. 6.44nityaṃ kāryānumeyā ca śaktiḥ kim anuyujyate |                    tadbhāvabhāvitāmātraṃ pramāṇaṃ tatra gamyate ||
  45. 6.45ato 'tīndriyayaivete śaktyā śaktim atīndriyām |                    indriyasyādadhānāḥ syuḥ śabdābhivyaktihetavaḥ ||
  46. 6.46vyañjako nānyajātiś cet, śrotraṃ śabdasya te katham |                    pārthivānāṃ ghaṭādīnāṃ pradopādiś ca taijasaḥ ||
  47. 6.47ātmādisamprayoge ca kāryaiḥ syāt tulyajātitā |                    jātir yā kā cid iṣṭā cet sā no 'trāpi bhaviṣyati ||
  48. 6.48upalabdhinimittāc ca nānyad vyañjakam ucyate |                    tasmād yathopalabdhatvāt sa jātivyañjako bhavet ||
  49. 6.49tathā tadavinābhāvād vijātīyo bhaviṣyati |<526>                    vāyavīyānabhijñatvāt tālvādisthābhimānataḥ ||
  50. 6.50anabhivyañjakatvārtham āhoparatayor api |                    vāyavīradhiyaivoktaṃ na nūnam iti cottaram ||
  51. 6.51abhighātavacas taḥ prāgevaṃ gūḍhadhiyāvubhau |                    yadi śabdam itīhāpi tredhābhivyaktisambhavaḥ ||
  52. 6.52sā hi syāc chabdasaṃskārādindriyasyobhayasya vā |                    tatra sarvaiḥ pratīyeta śabdaḥ saṃskriyate yadi ||
  53. 6.53nirbhāgasya vibhor na syād ekadeśe hi saṃskriyā |                    na cāsyādhārabhedena saṃskāraniyamo bhavet ||
  54. 6.54yataḥ śabdo nirādhāro vyomātmādivad eva ca |                    athāpy ākāśam ādhāras tatrānavayave 'sati ||
  55. 6.55na syāt pradeśasaṃskāraḥ, <527> kṛtsnaśabdamater api |                    na hi sāmastyarūpeṇa yāvad vyoma vyavasthitaḥ ||
  56. 6.56śaktyate sakalo boddhum ekadeśena saṃskṛtaḥ |                    ākāśaśrotrapakṣe ca vibhutvāt prāptitulyatā ||
  57. 6.57dūrabhāve 'pi śabdānām iti jñānaṃ prasajyate |                    śrotrasya caivam ekatvaṃ sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ bhavet ||
  58. 6.58tenaikaśrutivelāyāṃ śṛṇuyuḥ sarva eva te |                    tasyānavayavatvāc ca na dharmādharmasaṃskṛtaḥ ||
  59. 6.59nabhodeśo bhavec chrotraṃ vyavasthādvayasiddhayate |                    vaiśeṣikādisiddhānteṣv evaṃ tāvat prasajyate ||
  60. 6.60kāpile 'pi vibhutvena śrotrāder iyam eva dik |                    sakṛc ca saṃskṛtaṃ śrotraṃ sarvaśabdān prabodhayet ||
  61. 6.61ghaṭāyonmīlitaṃ cakṣuḥ paṭaṃ na hi na budhyate |<528>                    etad eva prasaṅktavyaṃ viṣayasyāpi saṃskṛtau ||
  62. 6.62samānadeśavartitvāt saṃskāro 'py aviśeṣataḥ |                    sthiravāyvapanītyā ca saṃskāro 'sya bhavan bhavet ||
  63. 6.63dṛṣṭaṃ vāvaraṇāpāye taddeśānyopalambhanam |                    saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtatve ca śabdaikatve na siddhyataḥ ||
  64. 6.64ekāvasthābhyupeto vā sarvair jñāyeta vā na vā |                    pratyekābhihitā doṣāḥ syur dvayor api saṃskṛtau ||
  65. 6.65tena prādeśikaṃ jñānaṃ na kṛtatvād vinā bhaved |                    uttaraṃ śrotrasaṃskārād bhāṣyakāreṇa varṇitam ||
  66. 6.66tadbhedāt śrutibhedaś ca pratiśrotṛ vyavasthitaḥ |                    nāvaśyaṃ śrotram ākāśam asmābhiś cābhyupeyate ||
  67. 6.67na cānavayavaṃ vyoma jainasāṃkhyaniṣedhataḥ |<529>                    tenākāśaikadeśo vā yad vā vastvantaraṃ bhavet ||
  68. 6.68kāryārthāpattigamyaṃ naḥ śrotraṃ pratinaraṃ sthiram |                    yady api vyāpi caikaṃ ca tathāpi dhvanisaṃskṛtiḥ ||
  69. 6.69adhiṣṭhāneṣu sā yasya tacchabdaṃ pratipatsyate |                    athāpīndriyasaṃskāraḥ so 'py adhiṣṭhānadeśataḥ ||
  70. 6.70śabdaṃ na śroṣyati śrotraṃ tenāsaṃskṛtaśaṣkuli |                    aprāptakarṇadeśatvād dhvaner na śrotrasaṃskriyā ||
  71. 6.71ato 'dhiṣṭhānabhedena saṃskāraniyamasthitiḥ |                    nanv ekasminn adhiṣṭhāne labdhasaṃskāram indriyam ||
  72. 6.72bodhakaṃ sarvadeheṣu syād ekendriyavādinaḥ |                    puṃsā dehapradeśeṣu vijñānotpattir iṣyate ||
  73. 6.73tena pradhānavaideśyād viguṇā sā tu saṃskṛtiḥ |<530>                    niṣpradeśo 'pi cātmā naḥ kārtsnyena ca vidann api ||
  74. 6.74śarīra eva gṛhṇātīty evam ukte na dṛṣyati |                    ekatve 'pi yathākāśaṃ dravyaiḥ sāvayavaiḥ pṛthak ||
  75. 6.75saṃsargabhedaṃ labhate saṃskārāsaṃskṛto tathā |                    vyomno 'navayavavyāptisadbhāve 'pi bhuviṣṭhitān ||
  76. 6.76dvyāśrayatvaṃ na saṃsargo ghaṭādīnanurudhyate |                    bādhiryādivyavasthānam anenaiva ca hetunā ||
  77. 6.77tadevābhogyam anyasya dharmādharmavaśīkṛtam |                    yathā tatra vasann eva svāmitvād avaropitaḥ ||
  78. 6.78na bhogaṃ labhate tadvadbadhiro 'nyatra śṛṇvati |<531>                    śrotraśabdāśrayāṇāṃ ca na nāmāvayavāḥ svayam ||
  79. 6.79na caikadeśavṛttitvaṃ tathāpy etan na duṣyati |                    vyañjakānāṃ hi vāyūnāṃ bhinnāvayavadeśatā ||
  80. 6.80jātibhedaś ca tenaiva saṃskāro vyavatiṣṭhate |                    anyārthaṃ prerito vāyur yathā'nyaṃ na karotivaḥ ||
  81. 6.81tathānyavarṇaṃ saṃskāraśakto nānyaṃ kariṣyati |                    anyais tālvādisaṃyogair varṇo nānyo yathaiva te ||
  82. 6.82tathā dhvanyantarākṣepo na dhvanyantarasāribhiḥ |                    tasmād utpattyabhivyaktyoḥ kāryārthāpattitaḥ samaḥ ||
  83. 6.83sāmarthyabhedaḥ sarvatra, <532> syāt prayatnavivakṣayoḥ |                    viṣayasyāpi saṃskāre tenaikasyaiva saṃskṛtiḥ ||
  84. 6.84naraiḥ sāmarthyabhedāc ca na sarvair avagamyate |                    yathaivotpadyamāno 'yaṃ na sarvair avagamyate ||
  85. 6.85digdeśādivibhāgena sarvān prati bhavann api |                    tathaiva yatsamīpasthair nādaiḥ syād yasya saṃskṛtiḥ ||
  86. 6.86tair eva śrūyate śabdo na dūrasthaiḥ kathañ cana |                    dvayasaṃskārapakṣe tu mṛṣā doṣadvaye vacaḥ ||
  87. 6.87yenānyataravaikalyāt sarvaiḥ sarvo na gṛhyate |                    sarvalokaprasiddhāṃ ca vivakṣānusṛtāṃ śrutim ||
  88. 6.88anugacchadibhir ekāntāt kāryo mārgaḥ parokṣakaiḥ |<533>                    tatra ye tāvad icchanti prāksaṃyogavibhāgataḥ ||
  89. 6.89śabda utpadyate tasmād anyas tatsadṛśaḥ punaḥ |                    tadanantaradeśe 'nyas tādṛganyas tataḥ paraḥ ||
  90. 6.90vīcītaraṅgavṛttyaivam antyaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate |                    adṛṣṭakalpanā tasmin pakṣe bahvī prasajyate ||
  91. 6.91śabdabhede na tāvan naḥ prajñābhedaḥ pravarttate |                    ārambhakatvaṃ śabdasya niṣkriyasyāpramāṇakam ||
  92. 6.92deśāntaragataṃ kārya nāmūrtasyābhighnataḥ |                    deśeyattānimittaṃ ca nārambhaniyamaṃ prati ||
  93. 6.93na ca diṅniyame hetur anuvātagates tathā |                    sadṛśaṃ vā sajātiṃ vā karotīti ca duṣkaram ||
  94. 6.94ārambhasarvadikkatve na ca hetuḥ pratīyate |<534>                    niranvayair vinaśyadbhir na cātyantāsatāṃ kriyā ||
  95. 6.95jñānasantānavaccaiṣāṃ santāno nāvakalpate |                    vegavatsakriyatvābhyāṃ taraṅgāṇāṃ tu yujyate ||
  96. 6.96kāryadeśāntarārambho yāvadvegaṃ ca tatkriyā |                    ārambhapratibandho 'sya na ca kuḍyādibhibhaṃvet ||
  97. 6.97na hy asūrttasya sadbhāvo sūrtamadhye vihanyate |                    na ca kuḍyādibhir vyoma nāśyate sāryate 'pi vā ||
  98. 6.98na tirodhīyate tasmāt kuḍyamadhye 'pi tad dhruvam |                    ākāśaṃ tatra na syāc cet kuḍyasthānaṃ virudhyate ||
  99. 6.99tan madhyāvayavānāṃ ca, na hi tiṣṭhati te ghane |                    athāvṛtyātmakadravyasaṃyogarahitaṃ nabhaḥ ||
  100. 6.100śabdotpādaṃ bibhartīti tatra nyāyo na kaś cana |<535>                    anyathāpy upapannatvāt nārthāpattyaitad iṣyate ||
  101. 6.101na pramāṇāntaraṃ ceyaṃ pramāṇadvayavādinām |                    sambandhānupalabdheś ca nānumānena kalpanā ||
  102. 6.102brūyāt sāmānyadṛṣṭaṃ ced, bhaved dhetor viruddhatā |                    sajātīyakaraḥ śabdo guṇatvāc cendriyādivat ||
  103. 6.103aśabdārambhakas tadvat syād adeśāntare tathā |                    yatra hy avayavā deśe paṭādīnāṃ vyavasthitāḥ ||
  104. 6.104tatraiva tadguṇāḥ sarve tadārabdho 'vayavy api |                    tadguṇāś cāpi taddeśās tenaiṣām ekadeśatā ||
  105. 6.105tadvadādyā pṛthagdeśāḥ śabdāḥ sarve bhavanti hi |                    śabdaṃ nārabhate śabdaḥ śabdatvād antyaśabdavat ||
  106. 6.106evaṃ vibhāgasaṃyogau tadbhāvād antyayogavat |                    jainakāpilanirdiṣṭaṃ śabdaśrotrādisarpaṇam ||
  107. 6.107sādhīyo 'smāt, <536> tad apy atra yuktyā naivāvatiṣṭhate |                    śabdasyāgamanaṃ tāvad adṛṣṭaṃ parikalpitam ||
  108. 6.108mūrtisparśādimattvaṃ ca teṣām abhibhavaḥ satām |                    tvagagrāhyatvam anye ca bhāgāḥ sūkṣmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||
  109. 6.109teṣām adṛśyamānānāṃ kathaṃ ca racanākramaḥ |                    kīdṛśād racanābhedād varṇabhedaś ca jāyate ||
  110. 6.110dravatvena vinā caiṣāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ kathyate katham |                    āgacchatāṃ ca viśleṣo na bhaved vāyunā katham ||
  111. 6.111laghavo 'vayavā hy ete nibaddhā na ca kena cit |                    vṛkṣādyabhihatānāṃ ca viśleṣo loṣṭavad bhavet ||
  112. 6.112ekaśrotrapraveśe ca nānyeṣāṃ syāt punaḥ śrutiḥ |                    na cāvāntaravarṇānāṃ nānātvasyāsti kāraṇam ||
  113. 6.113na caikasyaiva sarvāsu gamanaṃ dikṣu yujyate |<537>                    śrotrāgamanapakṣe ca, tan na, vṛttiś ca gacchati ||
  114. 6.114tadadṛṣṭadvayaṃ tasya, dūrasthena ca vikriyā |                    prāptiḥ sarvagatatvāc cet, tulyā dūragateṣv api ||
  115. 6.115vikriyāvikriye tatra sarvaiḥ syātāṃ na bhedataḥ |                    asambaddhavikāritvam apīṣṭaṃ tatra pūrvavat ||
  116. 6.116asambandhasamānatve nāsanno hi viśiṣyate |                    amūrtā śrotravṛttiś ca na mūrtena vihanyate ||
  117. 6.117tatra vyavahitaḥ śabdaḥ kimarthaṃ nopalabhyate |<538>                    śrtotrasya vikriyāyāṃ ca neyattāyā niyāmakam ||
  118. 6.118nānuvātādibhis tasya vṛtteś ca preraṇaṃ bhavet |                    anuvātaṃ vihanyeta, prativātaṃ ca sā vrajet ||
  119. 6.119tadgataṃ hy anuvātatvaṃ syān na śabdagataṃ tadā |                    yeṣāṃ tv aprāpta evāyaṃ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyate ||
  120. 6.120teṣām aprāptitulyatvaṃ dūravyavahitādiṣu |                    tatra dūrasamīpasthagrahaṇāgrahaṇe same ||
  121. 6.121syātāṃ na ca kramo nāpi tīvramandādisambhavaḥ |                    tasmāc chrotriyadṛṣṭāpi kalpaneyaṃ parīkṣyatām ||
  122. 6.122prayatnābhihato vāyuḥ koṣṭhyo yātītyasaṃśayam |                    sa saṃyogavibhāgau ca tālvāder anurudhyate ||
  123. 6.123vegavattvāc ca so 'vaśyaṃ yāvad vegaṃ pratiṣṭhate |                    tasyātmavayavānāṃ ca stimitena ca vāyunā ||
  124. 6.124saṃyogā viprayogāś ca jāyante gamanād dhruvam |<539>                    karṇavyomani sa prāptaḥ śaktiṃ śrotre niyacchati ||
  125. 6.125tadbhāve śabdabodhāc ca saṃskāro 'dṛṣṭa iṣyate |                    utpattiśaktivat so 'pīty adhikaṃ no na kiñ cana ||
  126. 6.126tathaiva tadviśeṣo 'pi viśiṣṭagrahaṇād bhavet |                    śabdotpatter niṣiddhatvād anyathānupapattitaḥ ||
  127. 6.127viśiṣṭasaṃskṛter janma dhvanibhyo 'dhyavasīyate |                    tadbhāvabhāvitā cātra śaktyastitvā'vavodhinī ||
  128. 6.128śrotraśaktivad eveṣṭā, buddhis tatra hi saṃhṛtā |<540>                    kuḍyādipratibandho 'pi yujyate mātariśvanaḥ ||
  129. 6.129śrotradeśābhighāte 'pi tena tīvrapravartinā |                    tasya ca kramavartitvāt kṣayi vegātmasaṃpadaḥ ||
  130. 6.130saṃskārakramatīvratvamandatādinimittatā |                    imam eva ca saṃskāraṃ śabdagrahaṇakāraṇam ||
  131. 6.131ke cit tu paṇḍitam manyāḥ śrotram ity abhimanvate |                    saṃjñāsañcāraṇāc caiṣāṃ bahumānaḥ svacetasi ||
  132. 6.132mudhaiṣāṃ bahumāno 'yaṃ vastvanutpādya kiñ cana |                    dhvanijanyād dhi saṃskārāc chrotraṃ nānyat pradarśitam ||
  133. 6.133taṃ muktvā śrotraśabdena kiṃ dṛṣṭam adhikaṃ ca taiḥ |                    evañ jātīyakān arthān phalena pratipāditān ||
  134. 6.134lokaḥ saṃskāraśabdena sāmānyenaiva jalpati |                    śrotraśabdo viśeṣeṇa tatrāvijñātasaṅgatiḥ ||
  135. 6.135siddhaṃ svārthaṃ parityajya nābhidhānena vartate |<541>                    ādāvaparibhāṣyatvaṃ bhāṣyakāro yadabravīt ||
  136. 6.136padārtheṣu bhavet teṣāṃ tadatikramaṇaṃ phalam |                    saṃskāravyatirikte ca sarvalokasya vastuni ||
  137. 6.137śrotraśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ san svāc chandyenāpanīyate |                    indriyāṇām abhivyaktir garbhasthasyaiva dehinaḥ ||
  138. 6.138prākkāryād āgamaiḥ siddhā tatpradveṣeṇa laṅghyate |                    na ca śabdārthasambandhaḥ kartuṃ yogyaḥ kathañ cana ||
  139. 6.139kṣaṇikaśrotrapakṣe ca so 'vaśyaṃ kṛtako bhavet |                    saṃskāre tulyam etac cet, na saṃskārāntarasthiteḥ ||
  140. 6.140saṃskāraśabdavācyā hi ke cid varṣaśatāny api |                    dhriyante tena tacchabdasambandho na vinaśyati ||<542>
  141. 6.141śrotraśabdaḥ punaḥ pūrva saṃskārād uttaratra tu |                    ekadeśanibaddhe hi sarvadārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥ ||
  142. 6.142śakyaṃ ca ghriyamāṇatvam indriyatvāt tvagāditvat |                    vaktuṃ śrotrasya tenātra kṣaṇikotpattyasambhavaḥ ||
  143. 6.143yadi ca dhvanisasamparkāc chrotram evopajāyate |                    badhirasyāpi tajjanma kimarthaṃ nopalabhyate ||
  144. 6.144yad yasya nāsti tat tasya sutarāṃ jananakṣamam |                    tasmād apekṣitaṃ śrotraṃ badhirasyāpi jāyatām ||
  145. 6.145saṃskāre 'py aviśiṣṭaṃ cet, nāsāv upahatendriye |                    śrotramācchāditaṃ doṣaiḥ saṃskartuṃ dhvanayo 'kṣamāḥ ||<543>
  146. 6.146utpadyamānapakṣe tu na kiñ cit pratibandhanam |                    śrotram ākāśadeśaṃ ca bhautikendriyavādinaḥ ||
  147. 6.147yamāhus tasya sadbhāvaḥ prāgdhvaneḥ kena vāryate |                    siddhasya ca padārthasya yānyataḥ kāryaṃ yogyatā ||
  148. 6.148saṃskāraśabdavācyatvāt sā yuktyā vāryate kayā |                    lokāgamaprasiddheṣu padārtheṣv anyathā vacaḥ ||
  149. 6.149tanmudhākhedakāri syād goviṣāṇāśanopamam |                    yadi tv avaśyaṃ kartavyastārkikoktiviparyayaḥ ||
  150. 6.150tato vedānusāreṇa kāryā dikśrotratāmatiḥ |                    diśaḥ śrotram iti hy etat pralayeṣv abhidhīyate ||
  151. 6.151tac ca prakṛtigāmitvavacanaṃ cakṣurādivat |                    sūryam asya tathā cakṣuruktaṃ gamayatād iti ||
  152. 6.152tejaḥ prakṛtivijñānaṃ tathā śrotraṃ digātmakam |<544>                    dik ca sarvaṃgataukā ca yāvad vyoma vyavasthitā ||
  153. 6.153karṇacchidraparicchannā śrtotram ākāśadeśavat |                    yāvāṃś ca kaṇabhugnyāyo nabhobhāgaprakalpane ||
  154. 6.154digbhāge tu samasto 'sau, āgamāt tu viśiṣyate |                    tasmād digdravyabhāgo yaḥ puṇyāpuṇyavaśīkṛtaḥ ||
  155. 6.155karṇacchidraparicchinnaḥ śrotraṃ saṃskriyate ca saḥ |                    tasmāt svato 'navasthānaṃ parastādity asiddhatā ||
  156. 6.156pratyayasyānavasthānaṃ vyomny api sthagite 'sti naḥ |                    na ca tasmin vināśitvaṃ dravye 'dravyātmake sati ||
  157. 6.157tatrānumānabuddhiś cet, śabde 'py astīti gamyatām |<545>                    karoter yac ca karmatvāt kṛtakatvam udāhṛtam ||
  158. 6.158arthas tāvadasiddho 'yam abhidhānam athocyate |                    tatrāpi vyabhicāritvaṃ tatkriyājanmavādinaḥ ||
  159. 6.159gomayādāvatajjanye 'py eṣa śabdo hi dṛśyate |                    yathā kathañ cid iṣṭaṃ cet kāryatvaṃ gomayādiṣu ||
  160. 6.160tathāpy ākāśamātratvaṃ kuruṣv ety atra dṛśyate |                    varaṇābhāvamātratvāt kāryam eveti cet, na tat ||
  161. 6.161bauddhānām api nābhāvaḥ svayaṃsiddho hi janyate |                    mṛdāṃ deśāntaraprāptir vyāpāraphalam atra hi ||
  162. 6.162anāvṛtyātmakaṃ vyoma nityam eva vyavasthitam |                    nityasya karaṇābhāvāt prayoge 'sminn athocyate ||
  163. 6.163bhrāntatvaṃ gauṇatā veti śabde 'py evaṃ bhaviṣyati |<546>                    prāgbhāgo yaḥ surāṣṭrāṇāṃ mālavānāṃ sa dakṣiṇaḥ ||
  164. 6.164prāgbhāgaḥ punar etaṣāṃ teṣām uttarataḥ sthitaḥ |                    tena sūryoditer deśau bhinnāv ubhayavāsinām ||
  165. 6.165dṛṣṭau saviturekatve 'py ato 'naikāntiko bhavet |                    paśyanty eke ca yaddeśāv udayās tamayau raveḥ ||
  166. 6.166tāvatyevābhimanyante parastāt tannivāsinaḥ |                    na ca bhinnā nirīkṣyante tena nādityabhinnatā ||
  167. 6.167madhyāhne sarvaṃ puṃsāṃ syād ekaṃ copari darśanam |                    yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmāt purataḥ savitekṣyate ||
  168. 6.168tadantarādhikātmā ca bhāti tenāgrataḥ sthitaḥ |                    viprakṛṣṭāntarāṇāṃ ca stokadeśe 'pi dṛśyate ||
  169. 6.169siddhabhinnāgradeśānāṃ dūradeśasamānatā |<547>                    tatrāpi viprakṛṣṭasya sannidhyadhyāsakāritā ||
  170. 6.170deśabhrāntir bhavet puṃsāṃ tattaddeśam apaśyatām |                    śabde tu kiṃnimittaiṣā, tatrāpi vyāpitākṛtā ||
  171. 6.171yo yo gṛhītaḥ sarvasmin deśe śabdo 'pi dṛśyate |                    na cāsyāvayavāḥ santi yena vartteta bhāgaśaḥ ||
  172. 6.172śabdo varttata ity evam, tatra sarvātmakaś ca saḥ |                    vyañjakadhvanyadhīnatvāt taddeśe tu sa gṛhyate ||<548>
  173. 6.173na ca dhvanīnāṃ sāmarthyaṃ vyāptuṃ vyoma nirantaram |                    tenāvicchinnarūpeṇa nāsau sarvatra gṛhyate ||
  174. 6.174dhvanīnāṃ bhinnadeśatvaṃ śrutis tatrānurudhyate |                    apūritāntarālatvād vicchedaś cāvasīyate ||
  175. 6.175teṣāṃ cālpakadeśatvāc chabdasyāvibhutāmatiḥ |                    gatimadvegavattvābhyāṃ te cāyānti yato yataḥ ||
  176. 6.176śrotā tatas tataḥ śabdamāyāntam iva manyate |                    sūryasya bhinnadeśatvaṃ nanv ekena na gṛhyate ||
  177. 6.177na nāma sarvathā tāvad dṛṣṭāsyānekadeśatā |                    saviśeṣaṇahetuś cet tathāpi vyabhicāritā ||
  178. 6.178dṛśyate bhinnadeśo 'yam ity eko 'pi hi buddhyate |<549>                    jalapātreṣu caikena nānekaḥ savitekṣyate ||
  179. 6.179yugapat, na ca bhedasya pramāṇaṃ tulyavedanāt |                    āhaikena nimittena pratipātraṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||
  180. 6.180bhinnāni pratibimbāni jāyante yugapanmama |                    atra brūmo yadā tāvajjale saureṇa tejasā ||
  181. 6.181sphuratā cākṣuṣaṃ tejaḥ pratisrotaḥ pravarttitam |                    svadeśa eva gṛhṇāti savitāram anekadhā ||
  182. 6.182bhinnamūrtiṃ yathā pātraṃ tadāsyānekatā kutaḥ |                    īṣannimīlite 'ṅgulyā yathā cakṣuṣi dṛśyate ||
  183. 6.183pṛthageko 'pi bhinnatvāc cakṣurvṛttes tathaiva naḥ |                    anye tu codayanty atra pratibimbodayaiṣiṇaḥ ||
  184. 6.184sa eva cet pratīyeta kasmān nopari dṛśyate |                    kūpādiṣu kuto 'dhastāt pratibimbekṣaṇaṃ bhavet ||
  185. 6.185prāṅmukho darpaṇaṃ paśyan syāc cet pratyaṅmukhaḥ katham |                    tatraiva bodhayed arthaṃ bahiryātaṃ yadindriyam ||
  186. 6.186tata etad bhaved evaṃ śarīre tat tu bodhakam |<550>                    apsūryadarśināṃ nityaṃ cakṣurdvedhā pravarttate ||
  187. 6.187ekamūrdhvamadhastāc ca tatrordhvāṃśaprakāśitam |                    adhiṣṭhānānṛjusthatvān nātmā sūryaṃ prapadyate ||
  188. 6.188pāramparyārpitaṃ santamavāgvṛttyā tu budhyate |                    ūrdhvavṛttes tadekatvādavāgiva ca manyate ||
  189. 6.189adhastād eva tenārkaḥ, sāntarālaḥ pratīyate |                    evaṃ prāgbhūtayā vṛttyā pratyagvṛttisamarpitam ||
  190. 6.190budhyamāno mukhaṃ bhrāntyā pratyagity avagacchati |                    anekadeśavṛttau vā saty api pratibimbake ||
  191. 6.191samānabuddhigamyatvān nānātvaṃ naiva vidyate |<551>                    vaktṛvaktrapradeśānāṃ bhinnatvād bhinnadeśatā ||
  192. 6.192śrotrāgamanapakṣe syāt taddeśe tv ekadeśatā |                    adhiṣṭhānābahirvṛtter anyasmin saty apīndriye ||
  193. 6.193taddeśāḥ karṇaśaṣkulyo gṛhyeran gamane sati |                    iyaṃ tu vaktranekatve śrotraikatve ca kalpanā ||
  194. 6.194vaktaryekatra bhinneṣu śrtotṛṣu syād viparyayaḥ |                    tatra hi śrotradeśānāṃ bhinnatvād bhinnadeśatā ||
  195. 6.195tadāgame tu vaktrekyādekadeśatvasambhavaḥ |<552>                    dhvanyāgatyā yadi bhrāntir itaratrāpi sā samā ||
  196. 6.196bhinnavyañjakatālvādideśabhedād bhaviṣyati |                    sūtreṇa yugapadbhāvaḥ śrotraikatvād udāhṛtaḥ ||
  197. 6.197atas tadanusāreṇa yady apītyādikīrtanam |                    deśabhedena bhinnatvam ity etac cānumānikam ||
  198. 6.198pratyakṣas tu sa eveti pratyayas tena bādhakaḥ |                    paryāyeṇa yathā caiko bhinnān deśān vrajann api ||
  199. 6.199devadatto na bhidyeta tathā śabdo na bhidyate |                    jñātaikatvo yathaivāsau dṛśyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||<553>
  200. 6.200na bhinnaḥ kālabhedena tathā śabdo na deśataḥ |                    paryāyād avirodhaś ced, vyāpitvād api dṛśyatām ||
  201. 6.201dṛṣṭasiddhau hi yo dharmaḥ sarvathā so 'bhyupeyate |                    varṇāntaravikāryatvād iti yoktā vināśitā ||
  202. 6.202ukte ca hetusiddhyartha sādṛśyasmaraṇe punaḥ |                    tatra smṛter asiddhatvam, na hy evaṃ pāṇiner vacaḥ ||
  203. 6.203ikārapariṇāmena yakāraḥ kriyatām iti |<554>                    siddhe śabdārthasambandhe tacchāstraṃ hi pravarttate ||
  204. 6.204prayoganiyamārthāya na caivaṃ siddhatā bhavet |                    bhinnaprasiddhayos tena dadhi dadhyeti śabdayoḥ ||
  205. 6.205ācakṣāṇena sādhutvaṃ dadhītyautsargikaḥ kṛtaḥ |                    anvākhyātuṃ svarūpeṇa dadhyaśabdaṃ ca veditum ||
  206. 6.206svaśāstre laghubodhārtham ekatvam iva darśitam |                    tatrāci parataḥ siddhaṃ dadhyaśabdaṃ nivarttayan ||
  207. 6.207dadhīti śāstrataḥ prāptaḥ so 'yaṃ tenaiva vāryate |                    ikprayogaprasaṅge tu yaṇ sādhur iti gamyate ||
  208. 6.208paramārthas tu naivāsmin vikāro 'bhūt kadā cana |                    kevalaṃ yat tu sādṛśyaṃ tadanaikāntikīkṛtam ||
  209. 6.209kunde dadhyavikāre 'pi tatsādṛśyaṃ hi dṛśyate |<555>                    nāsti sarvātmanā taccecchabde 'pi sthānamātrakam ||
  210. 6.210tenaitayor asiddhatvāt mūlahetor asiddhatā |                    kāraṇānuvidhāyitvaṃ yac cālpatvamahattvayoḥ ||
  211. 6.211tadasiddhaṃ na varṇo hi vardhate na padaṃ kva cit |                    varṇāntarajanau tāvat tatpadatvaṃ vihanyate ||
  212. 6.212apadaṃ hi bhaved etad yadi vā syāt padāntaram |                    varṇo 'navayavatvāt tu vṛddhihrāsau na gacchati ||
  213. 6.213vyomādivad ato 'siddhā vṛddhir asya svarūpataḥ |                    atha tādrūpyavijñānaṃ hetur ity abhidhīyate ||
  214. 6.214tathāpi vyabhicāritvaṃ śabdatve 'pi hi tanmatiḥ |                    vyaktyalpatvamahattve ca yad yathānuvidhīyate ||
  215. 6.215tathaivānuvidhānārthaṃ dhvanyalpatvamahattvayoḥ |                    vyaṅgyānāṃ caitadastīti loke 'py aikāntikaṃ na tat ||
  216. 6.216darpaṇālpamahattve 'pi dṛśyate 'nupatanmukham |                    na syād avyaṅgyatā tasya tatkriyājanyatāpi vā ||
  217. 6.217na cāsyoccāraṇādanyā vidyate janikā kriyā |<556>                    yathā mahatyāṃ khātāyāṃ mṛdi vyomni mahattvadhīḥ ||
  218. 6.218alpāyām alpadhīr evam atyantākṛtake sati |                    tenātraivaṃ paropādhiḥ śabdavṛddhau matibhramaḥ ||
  219. 6.219na casyūlatvasūkṣmatve lakṣyete śabdavṛttinī |                    buddhitīvratvamandatve mahattvālpatvakalpanā ||
  220. 6.220sā ca paṭvī bhavaty eva mahātejaḥprakāśite |                    mandaprakāśite mandā ghaṭādāv api sarvadā ||
  221. 6.221evaṃ dīrghādayaḥ sarve dhvanidharmā iti sthitam |                    nādo vāyuguṇas tadvān vāyur vā yadi kalpyate ||
  222. 6.222varṇānāṃ śrotragamyatvān na ca ye śrotragocarāḥ |                    tatrāvarṇātmakaḥ śabdaḥ śaṅkhādeḥ śrūyate katham ||
  223. 6.223dhvanīnāṃ śrotragamyatvaṃ tasmāt ke cit pracakṣate |<557>                    mārutapreritās te ca kurvanti śrotrasaṃskṛtim ||
  224. 6.224varṇavyaktau ca dṛṣṭatvāt teṣāṃ nādṛṣṭakalpanā |                    anye tu varṇayanty atra pūrvoktadhvanivādinaḥ ||
  225. 6.225marutām eva nānātvād ghoṣaśrutyupapādanam |                    tatra tālvādisaṃyogavibhāgaiḥ preritāḥ sphuṭam ||
  226. 6.226vyañjanti varṇam anye tu śabdatvaṃ sarvavarṇabhāk |                    varṇasarvagatatvāt tu nāpadyeta nirāśrayam ||
  227. 6.227na ca paryanuyogaḥ syāt kva varṇe vyaktir ity ayam |                    eta eva ca te pūrvam uktā bodhānuvarttinaḥ ||
  228. 6.228yeṣāṃ pracayanānātvād vṛttibhedaḥ pratīyate |<558>                    yad vā jātyantaraṃ santu sarvathā kāryahetukam ||
  229. 6.229tvatpakṣavad dhvanīnāṃ naḥ śaktibhedaprakalpanam |                    darśanasya parārthatvaṃ yadi nāma pratīyate ||
  230. 6.230śabdasya kim ihāyātaṃ yena nityo 'bhyupeyate |                    anityeṣv api dṛṣṭatvād dvīpajvālāghaṭādiṣu ||
  231. 6.231parārthadarśanatvasya dharmatve 'pi na hetutā |                    vinā sādharmyadṛṣṭāntād viruddho vā bhaved ayam ||
  232. 6.232nityānām aprayogitvam aṇūnām api daśyate |<559>                    arthapratyāyanaṃ caiṣa janmanaiva kariṣyati ||
  233. 6.233vināpi sthāsnurūpeṇa saṃyogādīn yathā kriyā |                    pūrvālocanam etasya bhūtasmṛtyā ca karmavat ||
  234. 6.234tasmān na viniyojyatvāt prāgastitvaṃ ghaṭādivat |                    prakāśitaṃ yathā cārthaṃ tejasā kena cit purā ||
  235. 6.235na vā bhūyopi buddhyante śabdād api tathā bhavet |                    darśanasya parārthatve yadasiddhyādi codyate ||
  236. 6.236tatkāṣṭhadahano vahnirabdāhārthaṃ niyujyate |                    anumānaprayoge hi vaktum ityādi yujyate ||
  237. 6.237arthāpattir iyaṃ coktā pakṣadharmādivarjitā |                    yadi nāśini nitye vā vināśiny eva vā bhavet ||
  238. 6.238śabde vācakasāmarthyam, tato dūṣaṇam ucyatām |                    phalavad vyavahārāṅgabhūtārthapratyayāṅgatā ||
  239. 6.239niṣphalatvena śabdasya yogyatvād avadhāryate |                    parīkṣyamāṇas tenāsya yuktyā nityavināśayoḥ ||<560>
  240. 6.240sa dharmo 'bhyupagantavyo yaḥ pradhānaṃ na bādhate |                    na hy aṅgāṅgānurodhena pradhānaphalabādhanam ||
  241. 6.241yujyate, nāśipakṣe ca tadekāntāt prasajyate |                    na hy adṛṣṭārthasambandhaḥ śabdo bhavati vācakaḥ ||
  242. 6.242tathā cet syād apūrvo 'pi sarvaḥ sarvaṃ prakāśayet |                    sambandhadarśanaṃ cāsya nānityasyopapadyate ||
  243. 6.243sambandhajñānasiddhiś ced dhruvaṃ kālāntarasthitiḥ |                    anyasmin jñātasambandhe na cānyo vācako bhavet ||
  244. 6.244gośabdejñātasambandhe nāśvaśabdo hi vācakaḥ |                    athānyo 'pi svabhāvena kaś cid evāvabodhakaḥ ||
  245. 6.245tatrānibandhane na syāt ko 'sāv iti viniścayaḥ |                    yataḥ pratyaya ity evaṃ vyavahāro 'vakalpate ||<561>
  246. 6.246śrotāṇāṃ syād apītthaṃ tu vaktāṇāṃ nāvakalpate |                    ajñātvā kam asau śabdam ādāv eva vivakṣati ||
  247. 6.247jānāti ced avaśyaṃ sa pūrvaṃ tenāvadhāritaḥ |                    tejaḥ pratyakṣaśeṣatvān na tattve 'pi prakāśakam ||
  248. 6.248sadṛśatvāt pratītiś cet, taddvāreṇāpy avācakaḥ |                    kasya caikasya sādṛśyāt kalpyatāṃ vācako 'paraḥ ||
  249. 6.249adṛṣṭasaṅgatitvena sarveṣāṃ tulyatā yataḥ |                    arthavān pūrvadṛṣṭaś cet, tasya tāvān kutaḥ kṣaṇaḥ ||
  250. 6.250dvistrir vānupalabdho hi nārthavān sampratīyate |<562>                    apratītānyaśabdānāṃ tatkāle 'sāv anarthakaḥ ||
  251. 6.251sa evānyaśrutīnāṃ syād arthavān iti vismayaḥ |                    athāsya vidyamānā 'pi kaiś cid artho na gamyate ||
  252. 6.252tattulyam uttarasyeti kiṃ sādṛśyena vācakaḥ |                    anarthakatvam asya syād arthānanyaśrutīn prati ||
  253. 6.253pūrvasminn api tatsattvāt sarvānarthakatā bhavet |                    arthavatsadṛśatvena yo vā śrutavatāṃ mataḥ ||
  254. 6.254mukhyo 'sāvaśrutīnāṃ syāt, tadekatve na yujyate |                    sambandhākaraṇe yuktis taduktam iti kathyate ||
  255. 6.255śabdānityatvapakṣe 'pi viśeṣeṇa sa duṣkaraḥ |<563>                    śabdaṃ tāvad anuccārya sambandhakaraṇaṃ kutaḥ ||
  256. 6.256na coccāritaṣṭasya sambandhena prayojanam |                    tenāsambaddhya naṣṭatvāt pūrvas tāvad anarthakaḥ ||
  257. 6.257uttaro 'kṛtasambandho vijñāyetārthavān katham |                    śabdoccāraṇasambandhakaraṇavyāvahārikāḥ ||
  258. 6.258kriyāḥ kramasvabhāvatvāt kaḥ kuryād yugapat kva cit |                    deśakālādibhedānāṃ puṃsā śabdāntaraśruteḥ ||
  259. 6.259pūrvaṃ kṛtrimasambandhe 'py ekaḥ śabdo na sidhyati |                    sambandhakathane 'py asya syād evaiṣā nirākṛtiḥ ||
  260. 6.260naṣṭāsadvarttamāneṣu nākhyānasya hi sambhavaḥ |                    arthavān kataraḥ śabdaḥ śroturvaktrā ca kathyatām ||
  261. 6.261yadā pūrvaśrutaṃ śabdaṃ nāsau śaknoti bhāṣitum |                    na tāvad arthavantaṃ sa bravīti sadṛśaṃ badet ||
  262. 6.262nārthavatsadṛśaḥ śabdaḥ śrotus tatropapadyate |                    arthavadgrahaṇābhāvāt, <564> na cāsāvarthavān svayam ||
  263. 6.263vaktuḥ śrotṛtvavelāyām etad eva prasajyate |                    evaṃ ca sarvavaktāṇāṃ na śabdaḥ kvacidarthavān ||
  264. 6.264bhaved yady api sambandhaḥ sargādau kasya cit kṛtaḥ |                    tasminn abuddhe naiva syād ekasmāt sadṛśe matiḥ ||
  265. 6.265atha tatkālajaiḥ pumbhis tasmin śabde 'vadhārite |                    pravṛtter anumīyeta tatsādṛśyaparamparā ||
  266. 6.266tatra sambandhamārgeṇa pūrvoktena prasajyate |                    smāryaṃ tanmūlasādṛśyaṃ tadadhīnārthaniścayāt ||
  267. 6.267vastuny utpattibhinne ca dūrādārabhya kalpitam |                    stokastokaviśeṣeṇa sādṛśyaṃ viprakṛṣyate ||
  268. 6.268svaravyañjanamātrādibhedāc chabde viśeṣataḥ |                    śālāmālā 'balāvelāśīletyādiprakalpanāt ||<565>
  269. 6.269sādṛśyāt pratipattau ca bhrāntijñānaṃ prasajyate |                    dhūme vṛṣṭe 'gnisambandhe bāṣpād iva kṛśānuṣīḥ ||
  270. 6.270evam astv iti cet brūyān naitadbādhakavarjanāt |                    tāvatā siddham iti cet, śabdābhedo 'pi sidhyati ||
  271. 6.271tathā bhinnam abhinnaṃ vā sādṛśyaṃ vyaktito bhavet |                    evam ekam anekaṃ vā nityaṃ vānityam eva vā ||
  272. 6.272bhinnatvaikatvanityatve jātir eva prakalpyate |                    abhedānityanānātve pūrvoktenaiva tulyatā ||
  273. 6.273vyaktyananyat tathaikaṃ ca sādṛśyaṃ nityam iṣyate |                    vyaktinityatvamāpannaṃ tathā saty asmadohitam ||
  274. 6.274na cāvayavasāmānyarūpā sadṛśatā tava |                    varṇābhede hi sā sidhyen na cābhedas tvayeṣyate ||<566>
  275. 6.275gośabdatvādigatvādi pūrvam eva nirākṛtam |                    varṇavyaktaya eva syur nityās tenāvabodhakāḥ ||
  276. 6.276gośabde 'vasthite 'smākaṃ tadaśaktijakāritā |                    gāvyāder api gobuddhir mūlaśabdānusāriṇī ||
  277. 6.277syāt sādṛśyanimittā ced gauraśabdād api dhruvam |                    tenāvyāvṛttir iṣṭātra gośabdād eva sā hi dhīḥ ||
  278. 6.278nanv ānupūrvyanityatvād anityo vācako bhavet |                    padaṃ vācakam iṣṭaṃ hi kramādhīnā ca tanmatiḥ ||
  279. 6.279varṇāḥ sarvagatatvād vo na svataḥ kramavṛttayaḥ |                    anityadhvanikāryatvāt kramasyāto vināśitā ||
  280. 6.280puruṣādhīnatā cāsya tadvivakṣāvaśād bhavet |                    varṇānāṃ nityatā tena niṣphalā paramāṇuvat ||
  281. 6.281yathā saty aṇunityatve ghaṭe tadracanātmake |                    na nityataivaṃ varṇeṣu nityeṣu padanāśitā ||<567>
  282. 6.282na ca kramād vinā varṇā vijñātāḥ pratipādakāḥ |                    kramasyaiva padatvaṃ vastasmādevaṃ prasajyate ||
  283. 6.283padaṃ varṇātiriktaṃ tu yeṣāṃ syāt kramavarjitam |                    teṣām evārthavatyeṣā śabdanityatvakalpanā ||
  284. 6.284na tāvad ānupūrvyasya padatvaṃ naḥ prasajyate |                    na hi vastvantarādhāram etad dṛṣṭaṃ prakāśakam ||
  285. 6.285dvaye saty api tenātra vijñeyo 'rthasya vācakaḥ |                    varṇāḥ kiṃ nu kramopetāḥ kiṃ nu varṇāśrayaḥ kramaḥ ||
  286. 6.286kramaḥ kramavatām aṅgam iti kiṃ yuktisādhyatā |                    dharmamātram asau teṣāṃ na vastvantaram iṣyate ||
  287. 6.287itthaṃ pratīyamānāḥ syur varṇās tenāvabodhakāḥ |                    na ca kramasya kāryatvaṃ pūrvasiddhaparigrahāt ||
  288. 6.288vaktā na hi kramaṃ kañ cid svātantryeṇa prapadyate |                    yathaivāsya parair uktis tathaivainaṃ vivakṣati ||
  289. 6.289paro 'py evam ataś cāsya, sambandhavadanityatā |<568>                    tenaivaṃ vyavahārāt syād akauṭasthye 'pi nityatā ||
  290. 6.290yatnataḥ pratiṣedhyā naḥ puruṣāṇāṃ svatantratā |                    varṇānām api nanv evam akauṭasthye 'pi setsyati ||
  291. 6.291nityeṣu satsu varṇeṣu vyavahārāt kramodayaḥ |                    ghaṭādiracanā yadvannityeṣu paramāṇuṣu ||
  292. 6.292tadabhāve hi nirmūlā racanā nāvadhāryate |                    aṇukalpāś ca varṇāṃśā na santīty upapāditam ||
  293. 6.293parair uktān bravīmīti vivakṣā cedṛśī dhruvam |                    tathā ca nityatāpattiḥ, <569> na cānyaccihnam asti vaḥ ||
  294. 6.294tajjātīyatvasādṛśye niṣiddhe, yat tu sambhavet |                    śabdatvena sajātitvaṃ tulyaṃ śabdāntareṣu tat ||
  295. 6.295jātyā yathā ghaṭādīnāṃ vyavahāropalakṣaṇam |                    tathaiva cānupūrvyāder jātidvāreṇa setsyati ||
  296. 6.296tālvādijātayas tāvat sarvapuṃsāṃ vyavasthitāḥ |                    vaktā tāvad dhvanīṃs tābhir upalakṣya nirasyati ||<570>
  297. 6.297teṣāṃ ca jātayo bhinnāḥ śabdābhivyaktihetavaḥ |                    yāvadvarṇaṃ pravartante vyaktayo vā tadanvitāḥ ||
  298. 6.298tatra tālvādisaṃyogavibhāgakramapūrvakam |                    dhvanīnām ānupūrvyaṃ syāj jātyā cobhayanityatā ||
  299. 6.299yathaiva bhramaṇādīnāṃ bhāgair jātyā ca lakṣitaiḥ |                    kramānuvṛttir evaṃ syāt tālvādidhvanivarṇabhāk ||
  300. 6.300vyaktīnām eva vā saukṣmyāj jātidharmāvadhāraṇam |                    tadvaśena ca varṇānāṃ vyāpitve 'pi kramagrahaḥ ||
  301. 6.301evaṃ dhvaniguṇān sarvān nityatvena vyavasthitān |                    varṇā anupatantaḥ syur arthabhedāvabodhinaḥ ||
  302. 6.302ānupūrvī ca varṇānāṃ hrasvadīrghaplutāś ca ye |                    kālasya pravibhāgās tair jāyante dhvanyupādhayaḥ ||<571>
  303. 6.303kālaś caiko vibhur nityaḥ, pravibhakto 'pi gamyate |                    varṇavat, sarvabhāveṣu vyajyate kena cit kva cit ||
  304. 6.304varṇeṣu vyajyamānasya tasya pratyāyanāṅgatā |                    anyatrāpi tu sadbhāvāt tatsvarūpasya nityatā ||
  305. 6.305tasmān na padadharmo 'sti vināśo kaś cid īdṛśaḥ |<572>                    tena nityaṃ padaṃ siddhaṃ varṇānityatvavādinām ||
  306. 6.306paradharme 'pi cāṅgatvam uktam aśvagajādivat |                    nityatāyāṃ ca sarveṣām arthapatteḥ pramāṇatā ||
  307. 6.307pade 'navayave cāpi vyañjakaiḥ kramavṛttibhiḥ |                    puruṣādhīnatāyāṃ ca na prāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate ||
  308. 6.308vākkyeṣu dṛṣṭam etac ca tannirbhāgatvavādinām |                    anyathānupapattyā tat sarvathā padanityatā ||
  309. 6.309parāthadarśanārthatvaṃ yenāyaṃ pratipadyate |                    sa dharmo hy anumānāya sambandhāpekṣitocyate ||<573>
  310. 6.310na sādhanaprayogo 'yaṃ sūtrakāreṇa racyate |                    vṛttikāreṇa cārthas tu yogyo dvābhyāṃ nirūpitaḥ ||
  311. 6.311atrocyate sthiraḥ śabdo dhūmagotvādijātivat |                    sambandhānubhvāpekṣasāmānyārthāvabodhanāt ||
  312. 6.312anyāpohanasārūpyajātiliṅgatvakalpane |                    viśeṣāṇām aliṅgatvāt sarvasāmānyanityatā ||
  313. 6.313svavākyādivirodho vā parārthatvena kathyate |                    pratijñoccāryate sarvā sādhyārthapratipattaye ||
  314. 6.314na cānityā bravīty eṣā svārtham ity upapāditam |                    tenārthapratyayāpannān nityatvān nāśabādhanam ||
  315. 6.315arthābhidhānasāmarthyam abhyupetya ca sādhayet |                    pūrvābhyupagatenāpi nāśitvaṃ bādhate paraḥ ||
  316. 6.316arthapratītisāmarthyaiḥ pratiśāstram upāśritaiḥ |                    āgamenāpi nāśitvaṃ bādhyate sarvavādinām ||<574>
  317. 6.317sarvalokaprasiddhyā ca bādhaḥ pūrvoktayā diśā |                    anumānavirodho 'pi prāguktenaiva hetunā ||
  318. 6.318pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatvaṃ saṅkhyābhāve 'bhidhāsyate |                    vaktavyaś caiṣa kaḥ śabdo nāśitvena prasādhyate ||
  319. 6.319triguṇaḥ paudgalo vā 'yam ākāśasyātha vā guṇaḥ |                    varṇād anyo 'tha nādātmā vāyurūpo 'rthavācakaḥ ||
  320. 6.320padavākyātmakaḥ sphoṭaḥ sārūpyānyanivarttane |                    eteṣām astv anityatvaṃ nāsmākaṃ teṣu nityatā ||
  321. 6.321aprasiddhaviśeṣyatvam āśrayāsiddhahetutā |                    athāsmad iṣṭaḥ pakṣaḥ syād dvayam etat samaṃ tava ||
  322. 6.322śabdamātram athocyeta śabdatvaṃ ca tathā sati |                    anityaṃ tac ca sarveṣāṃ nityam iṣṭaṃ viruddhyate ||
  323. 6.323yatkiñcid iha sāmānyaṃ nityaṃ sarveṇa kalpyate |<575>                    anityatve hi naitat syād vyaktiṣu kāsu cit ||
  324. 6.324vyaktayaḥ śabdaśabdena na śakyante ca bhāṣitum |                    tāsāṃ jātyatireke ca pūrvokte eva dūṣaṇe ||
  325. 6.325āśrayān atireke tu jātāv iva virodhitā |                    aprasiddhaviśeṣyatvaṃ syāt pareṣāṃ ca pūrvavat ||
  326. 6.326anityavaṃ ca nāśitvaṃ yady ātyantikam ucyate |                    tato 'smān prati pakṣaḥ syād aprasiddhaviśeṣaṇaḥ ||
  327. 6.327yathā kathañ cid iṣṭā ced anityavyapadeśyatā |                    anabhivyaktyavasthātaḥ sābhivyaktyātmaneṣyate ||
  328. 6.328aikāntikavikalpe ca vyatirekavināśayoḥ |                    pūrvābhyupagamenāpi virodhaḥ sāṃkhyajainayoḥ ||<576>
  329. 6.329pratyakṣaindriyakatvāder aulūkyānām asiddhatā |                    anekaśabdakalpyatvād ādyamadhyabhaveṣu ca ||
  330. 6.330antyaśabde 'pi pakṣe syād āśrayāsiddhatā mama |                    sarvaśabdeṣu sādhyeṣu hetur avyāpakas tava ||
  331. 6.331sāmānyair vyabhicāraś ca, jātimattve satīti cet |                    tathāpi, asiddham asmākaṃ tadvattvaṃ vyatiriktayā ||
  332. 6.332ananyayā tu tadvattā tavāsidhetyahetutā |                    athānuvṛttivyāvṛttihetunā yujyate matup ||
  333. 6.333tathāpy asty eva tadvattā teṣāṃ sāmānyabuddhitaḥ |<577>                    gotvādiṣv api sāmānyaṃ sāmānyam iti no matiḥ ||
  334. 6.334vyāvarttate viśeṣebhyaḥ seti śabdena tulyatā |                    nityatvaṃ cānugāmyeṣām anityebhyo nivarttitam ||
  335. 6.335athātra gauṇamithyātve syātām varṇeṣu te same |                    yogīndriyāvagamyaiś ca vyabhicāro 'ṇubhis tava ||
  336. 6.336nityānām api teṣāṃ hi pratyakṣatvādisambhavaḥ |                    atha syāt tannivṛttyartham asmadādiviśeṣaṇam ||
  337. 6.337ahaṃpratyayavijñeyair ātmabhirvyabhicāritā |                    liṅgaśabdādyabhāvena manassaṃyogahetukam ||
  338. 6.338pratyakṣaṃ caitadekāntāt sukhādāv iva kalpyate |                    bāhyendriyāvagamyatvam atha kuryād viśeṣaṇam ||
  339. 6.339tathāpi vyabhicāryeva jātīnāṃ jātimattayā |<578>                    ekārthasamavāyena jātir jātimatī hi vaḥ ||
  340. 6.340ādhāratvam athocyeta, nāmūrtā''dhīyate hy asau |                    samavāyaṃ yadi brūyāḥ, tvadīyaḥ so 'pi vāritaḥ ||
  341. 6.341abhedavṛttiṃ brūyāś cet, jātīnām api seṣyate |                    kleśaś ca nityavaidharmye kṛto bahuviśeṣaṇaiḥ ||
  342. 6.342svaśabdenaiva tāny uktvā tebhyo 'nyatvaṃ varaṃ kṛtam |                    evaṃ ca śakyate vaktaṃ nityatāpy ambarādivat ||
  343. 6.343tadbhinnā 'nityavṛkṣādivyatiriktatvahetukā |<579>                    kevalaindriyakatve 'pi sāṃkhyabauddhaprakalpite ||
  344. 6.344jātyā sādhitayedānīṃ vyabhicāraḥ pratīyate |                    asiddhe pakṣadharmatve yathaiva prativādinaḥ ||
  345. 6.345na hetur labhyate, tadvadanvayavyatirekayoḥ |                    tatra yady apy asiddhā syāj jātiḥ sādhanavādinaḥ ||
  346. 6.346tāvat tathāpy ahetutvaṃ yāvat sā na nirākṛtā |                    kāryā caindriyakatve 'pi kiṃ vastv iti nirūpaṇā ||
  347. 6.347vyaktyananyatvanānātvabhedābhedeṣu ca sphuṭā |                    tatrāsādhāraṇāsiddha sādhyahīnasapakṣatāḥ ||
  348. 6.348vikalpitānusāreṇa vaktavyā vādyapekṣayā |<580>                    viruddhāvyabhicāritvaṃ vakṣyamāṇaiś ca hetubhiḥ ||
  349. 6.349kevalākāśavarttitvād aulūkyasya vibhutvavat |                    tathā ca śrotragamyatvāc chabdatvavad iti sthitiḥ ||
  350. 6.350prāguktena vibhutvena vyomavac cāsya nityatā |                    sapakṣo 'pi vikalpyo 'tra śrutyarthe sādhyahīnatā ||
  351. 6.351vyaktilakṣaṇapakṣe 'pi jātyanyānanyakalpanā |                    anyatve dharmyasiddhir no 'nanyatve 'pi parān prati ||
  352. 6.352aviśeṣe 'pi nānityaṃ na nityaṃ vastu tanmama |                    aṃśo hy etasya jātyākhyo nityo dhvaṃsītaro mataḥ ||
  353. 6.353anityatā vikalpyātra, nāśaś cet sādhyahīnatā |                    mamānyathā tu bhavatām, ity eṣā dūṣaṇoktidik ||<581>
  354. 6.354sarveṇa śabdarūpaṃ ca vācakaṃ nityam iṣyate |                    tatsvarūpe vivādas tu varṇās tatra ca sādhitāḥ ||
  355. 6.355sambandhanityatāyāḥ kiṃ śabdādhikaraṇe 'bhidhā |                    tādarthyāc chabdacintāyāḥ saiva hy atrādhikāritī ||
  356. 6.356yad vā sambandhanityatvadvāreyaṃ śabdanityatā |                    sādhyate, na vinaṣṭe hi śabde tannityatā bhavet ||
  357. 6.357anityānāṃ hi nityātmā yaḥ sambandhaḥ pratīyate |                    āśrayāṇām anucchedān na kva cit sa virudhyate ||
  358. 6.358na cānucchedarūpeṇa gośabdānām iha sthitiḥ |                    na caiṣāṃ gamyate bhedas tenaikasyaiva nityatā ||
  359. 6.359kṛtrimatve ca sambandhas tatprayogāpavarjanāt |                    tadekavyaktiniṣṭhatvān naiva sārvatriko bhavet ||<582>
  360. 6.360pārthivadravyasattādilāṅgūlatvādisaṅkarāt |                    vinā prayogabhūyas tvaṃ na syād gotvāvadhāraṇā ||
  361. 6.361tasmād akṛtrimaḥ śabdo na kadā cid vinaṣyati |                    nityena nityasambandhād ākāśaparamāṇuvat ||
  362. 6.362yad vā sambandhanityatvaṃ sūtre 'smin naiva varṇyate |                    śabdanityatvamātre 'pi bhāṣyaṃ hy etasya yujyate ||
  363. 6.363sammugdhānekasāmānyaviṣayo hi sakṛcchrutaḥ |                    niṣkṛṣṭasvārthavācitvaṃ śabdo na pratipadyate ||
  364. 6.364bahubhiḥ śravaṇair eva prāṇitvādīni varjayet |                    śuklādigamanādīni sāsnālāṅgūlatādi ca ||
  365. 6.365śābaleyādikhaṇḍādivyaktīś ca svanibandhanāḥ |                    niṣkṛṣṭagotvavācitvaṃ cireṇa pratipadyate ||<583>
  366. 6.366tāvatkālaṃ sthiraṃ cainaṃ kaḥ paścān nāśayiṣyati |                    anapekṣatvasūtreṇa tac caitat sādhayiṣyate ||
  367. 6.367kriyāvatām abhede hi kriyāvṛttiṣu kṛtvasuc |                    tatprayogād dhruvaṃ tasya śabdasyāvarttate kriyā ||
  368. 6.368punaḥprayogavijñānaṃ na hi śabdāntare bhavet |                    tasyāṃ ca śabdasaṃkhyāyām aṣṭāv iti bhavecchrutiḥ ||
  369. 6.369bhuktavanto 'ṣṭakṛtvo 'dya brāhmaṇā iti dṛśyate |                    dravyabhede 'py anekāntaṃ matvā''ha kim ato yadi ||
  370. 6.370tasmāt tatparihārāya pramāṇāntaram ucyate |                    pratyabhijñānam etena prayogeṇopalakṣitam ||
  371. 6.371kṛtvasuc cāpi naivāyaṃ vyabhicārīti gamyate |                    yataḥ prayujyate caikabrāhmaṇatvavivakṣayā ||<584>
  372. 6.372pramāṇaṃ pratyabhijñānaṃ dṛḍhendriyatayocyate |                    itaro 'siddhatām āha sādṛśyād grāhyadūṣaṇāt ||
  373. 6.373nityaṃ sadṛśa eveti yatra rūḍhā matir bhavet |                    sa iti pratyabhijñānaṃ bhrāntis tatrāvakalpate ||
  374. 6.374iha nityaṃ sa eveti vijñānaṃ jāyate dṛḍham |                    tadāstitvādhikatvāc ca prāmāṇyaṃ tasya sādhitam ||
  375. 6.375nityaprasaṅgadvāreṇa spaṣṭayor apy anityayoḥ |                    pratyabhijñānasadbhāvād anaikāntikatocyate ||
  376. 6.376na pratyakṣe iti tv etadasambaddham ivottaram |                    yato nātra pareṇoktā pratyakṣatvena nityatā ||
  377. 6.377pratyakṣatvād ghaṭādīnāṃ mā prasāṅkṣīddhi nityatā |<585>                    atīndriyatvān mā bhuc ca vyomāder apy anityatā ||
  378. 6.378na ca nitye svarūpeṇa tenokte buddhikarmaṇī |                    yā tv anaikāntikatvoktiḥ sā tathaivāvatiṣṭhate ||
  379. 6.379na tayoḥ pratyabhijñānam etad eva kilocyate |                    pratyakṣatvaniṣedhena pratyakṣeṇa hi tad bhavet ||
  380. 6.380tena hetor abhāvo 'yaṃ vipakṣānujñayocyate |                    hetuṃ cāpy abhyanujñāya vipakṣo neti kathyate ||
  381. 6.381sādhyaṃ nityasvarūpaṃ ced etayoḥ pratyabhijñayā |                    tatrāsambaddhatā vācyā yoktā paṅktivane prati ||
  382. 6.382pratyabhijñānanityatve yāpy eṣānavadhāraṇā |                    anādarāya, na hy asmāt prakṛtaṃ mama duṣyati ||<586>
  383. 6.383vyaktirūpeṇa vā yena nāśitvaṃ buddhikarmaṇoḥ |                    na tatra pratyabhijñānaṃ, ghaṭabuddhau hi nāsya dhīḥ ||
  384. 6.384yena tu pratyabhijñānaṃ śaktijātyātmanānayoḥ |                    tena nityatvam eveṣṭaṃ kathañ cit sarvavādinām ||
  385. 6.385evaṃ tu pratyabhijñānaṃ vācoktaṃ kliṣṭayānayā |                    na ca śakyaṃ nirākartuṃ sarvalokaprasiddhitaḥ ||
  386. 6.386yena nāma pramāṇena grahaṇaṃ buddhikarmaṇoḥ |                    tenaiva pratyabhijñānān nityatvaṃ kiṃ na siddhyati ||
  387. 6.387vāṅmātrāt pratyabhijñānaṃ śakyaṃ śabde 'pabhāṣitum |<587>                    pratyabhijñānapekṣeṇa na pratyakṣeṇa kiñ cana ||
  388. 6.388rūpaśabdāvibhāgāc cety atraitat sādhayiṣyate |                    pratyakṣanityaṃ karmeti, tenaiṣātropavarṇanā ||
  389. 6.389nāsmābhiḥ pratyabhijñānaṃ nityasādhanam iṣyate |                    anityavādinas tv eṣā pratyakṣeṇa viruddhatā ||
  390. 6.390tenānaikāntiko nāyaṃ siddhāntāntaradūṣaṇam |                    dhīkarmasv api kiṃ naivam anityatvaṃ nivāryate ||
  391. 6.391taducyate vināśitvam anumānāt pratīyate |                    śabde pratyakṣagamye ca tena bādho balīyasā ||
  392. 6.392dhīkarmaṃ pratyabhijñānān nityatā tvānumānikī |                    tādṛśī nāśitāpīti na syāt tatra balābalam ||
  393. 6.393na hi te iti tenāha, yad vā hetor viśeṣaṇam |                    pratyakṣam, <588> śrautratā ceyaṃ hetuḥ śabdatvavat kṛtaḥ ||
  394. 6.394yatkarmātīndriyādhāraṃ tadapratyakṣam ucyate |                    apratyakṣeti buddhiś ca śūnyavāde nirūpitā ||
  395. 6.395pratyakṣadravyavarttinyo dṛśyante yoḥ punaḥ kriyāḥ |                    tāsāṃ varṇavad eveṣṭaṃ nityatvaṃ pratyabhijñayā ||
  396. 6.396vyañjakābhāvataś cāsāṃ santatānupalabdhitā |                    yad evotpādakaṃ vaḥ syāt tad eva vyañjakaṃ mama ||
  397. 6.397tava śabdatvakartṛtve nitye api satī yathā |                    na nityam upalabhyete tathā me buddhikarmaṇī ||<589>
  398. 6.398yathā vā śaktisadbhāve kutaś cit kāraṇād ṛte |                    na kāryāṇy upajāyante tathābhivyaktir iṣyatām ||
  399. 6.399vyaktibhyo 'nyatayā tāvat karma kleśena kalpyate |                    punarjātisahasrāṇāṃ tadbhede kliṣṭakalpanā ||
  400. 6.400tata ekatvanityatvapratyekasamavāyitāḥ |                    vṛttiś ca viprakīrṇeṣu karmabhāgeṣu nāśiṣu ||
  401. 6.401ekatvāc calanādīnāṃ tasmād ekātmikā matiḥ |                    prayatnāśrayanānātvād buddhibhedaḥ pravarttate ||
  402. 6.402naiva hy atrāpi vicchinnāḥ śābaleyādipiṇḍavat |                    karmavyaktīr vijānīmaḥ kalpayema dvayaṃ yataḥ ||
  403. 6.403śīghramandādibhede 'pi syāt prayatnādibhedataḥ |                    vyaktidvāro yathā jāteḥ, vyakter vā janane yathā ||<590>
  404. 6.404buddhīnām api caitanyasvābhāvyāt puruṣasya naḥ |                    nityatvam ekatā ceṣṭā, bhedas tu viṣayāśrayaḥ ||
  405. 6.405svarūpeṇa yathā vahnir nityaṃ dahanakarmakaḥ |                    upanītaṃ dahatyarthaṃ dārhya nānyanna cānyathā ||
  406. 6.406yathā vā darpaṇaḥ svaccho yathā ca sphaṭiko 'malaḥ |                    yadyannidhīyate yogyaṃ tacchāyāṃ pratipadyate ||
  407. 6.407tathaiva nityacaitanyāḥ pumāṃso dehavṛttayaḥ |                    gṛhṇanti karaṇānītān rūpādīn, dhīr asau matā ||
  408. 6.408tenopanetṛsambandhabhaṅgitvād bhaṅgino matiḥ |<591>                    nanityaṃ dāhako vahnir dāhyāsannidhinā yathā ||
  409. 6.409tatra bodhātmakatvena pratyabhijñāyate matiḥ |                    ghaṭahastyādibuddhitvaṃ tadbhedāl lokasammatam ||
  410. 6.410saiveti nocyate buddhir arthabhedānusāribhiḥ |                    na cāsyāḥ pratyabhijñānam arthabhede 'nupāśrite ||
  411. 6.411etanmanasi kṛtvā''ha nitye eveti bhāṣyakṛt |                    etayaiva diśā vācyā śuklāder api nityatā ||
  412. 6.412saṃsargamātrabhedena syāt tatrāpi hi bhedadhīḥ |                    svarūpaṃ tu tad eveti ko jātiṃ kathayiṣyati ||<592>
  413. 6.413kva cid dravyeṇa saṃsargaḥ kva cin na syād guṇāntaraiḥ |                    śuklādes tena bhinnatvaṃ siddhaṃ bhāsuradhūsaraiḥ ||
  414. 6.414jvālādeḥ kṣaṇikatve 'pi pratyabhijñeti cet, na tat |                    tatrāpi pratyabhijñeyaṃ sāmānyaṃ nityam eva naḥ ||
  415. 6.415bhedabuddhis tu yatrāṃśe syāt kena cid upādhinā |                    tatra naḥ pratyabhijñānaṃ bhedabuddhyaiva vāritam ||
  416. 6.416hy astanoccāritas tasmād gośabdo 'dyāpi vidyate |                    gośabdajñānagamyatvād yathokto 'dyaiṣa gaur iti ||
  417. 6.417hyo vāsīd eṣa gośabdaḥ pūrvoktenaiva hetunā |                    yad vā gotvābhidhāyitvaṃ vācyo hetur dvayor api ||
  418. 6.418gośabdabuddhyā hy astanyā gośabdo 'yaṃ prakāśitaḥ |<593>                    gośabdaviṣayatvena yathaivādyaprasūtayā ||
  419. 6.419iyaṃ vā taṃ vijānāti taddhetoḥ pūrvabuddhivat |                    ubhe vāpy ekaviṣaye bhavetām ekabuddhivat ||
  420. 6.420deśakālādibhinnā vā samastā gotvabuddhayaḥ |                    ekagośabdajanyāḥ syur godhītvād ekabuddhivat ||
  421. 6.421gośabdabuddhayo 'py evam ekagośabdagocarāḥ |                    gośabdaviṣayatvena kalpyantām ekabuddhivat ||
  422. 6.422gośabdatvaniṣedhāc ca nātra syāt siddhasādhyatā |                    ghaṭāder ekatāpattau jātyeṣṭaṃ siddhasādhanam ||
  423. 6.423vyaktīnām ekatārpattiṃ kuryāc ced anayā diśā |                    tasya dṛṣṭaviruddhatvaṃ vācyaṃ sarvapramāṇakam ||
  424. 6.424ye 'pi sthūlavināśānām anyathānupapattitaḥ |                    kalpayantyantarā sūkṣmaṃ vināśitvaṃ pratikṣaṇam ||
  425. 6.425te 'pi kṣaṇikanāśitvād adhikāṃ sthūlanāśitām |                    śabdānām avijānanto na śaktā nāśisādhane ||
  426. 6.426kṣaṇabhaṅgo ghaṭādīnāṃ vāryas tair eva sādhanaiḥ |<594>                    tathaiva pratyabhijñānād, yāvad dṛṣṭaṃ na bādhate ||
  427. 6.427sādhanaṃ tu bruvāṇasya dīpajvālādidarśanāt |                    pūrvoktenaiva māgreṇa pratyakṣādiviruddhatā ||
  428. 6.428pūrvakṣaṇavināśe ca kalpyamāne niranvaye |                    uttarasyānimittatvād utpattir nopapadyate ||
  429. 6.429atyantāsann asau tasminn tāvad vyāpṛtikṣamaḥ |                    svayaṃ cābhāvadaṣṭatvāt kasmin kāle kariṣyate ||
  430. 6.430nāśotpādasamatve 'pi nairapekṣyāt parasparam |                    na kāryakāraṇatve staḥ, tadvyāpārānanugrahāt ||
  431. 6.431na hy alabdhātmakaṃ vastu parāṅgatvāya kalpte |                    na vinaṣṭaṃ, na ca sthānaṃ tasya kāryakṛtikṣamam ||<595>
  432. 6.432jāyamānaṃ ca gandhādi ghaṭarūpe vinaśyati |                    tatkāryaṃ neṣyate tadvat tathā rūpāntarāṇy api ||
  433. 6.433tasmāt prākkāryaniṣpatter vyāpāro yatra dṛśyate |                    tad eva kāraṇaṃ tasya na tvānantaryamātrakam ||
  434. 6.434jvālāder api nāśitvaṃ naiva siddhaṃ pratikṣaṇam |                    laghavo 'vayavās tatra yānti deśāntaraṃ laghu ||
  435. 6.435prabhūtaṃ varttideśe hi tejastiṣṭhati piṇḍitam |                    tatra yāvad vrajaty ūrdhvaṃ tāvajjvāleti gamyate ||
  436. 6.436tato 'pi yadatikramya yāti tat syāt prabhātmakam |<596>                    tataḥ paraṃ tu yad yāti tat saukṣmyān nāvadhāryate ||
  437. 6.437uttarāvayavai ruddhe mārge pūrve na yānti ca |                    yathottare vimuñcanti pūrve yānti tathā tathā ||
  438. 6.438saṃkrāntāv api tenaiṣāṃ tṛṇādau vṛddhyasambhavaḥ |                    śabde vṛddhyādyabhāvo 'pi dhvaniśaighryeṇa jāyate ||
  439. 6.439śarīre yauvanādyāptiḥ pariṇāmāc ca setsyati |                    tathā hi sanniveśādi pratyabhijñāyate janaiḥ ||
  440. 6.440tatrānyānanyavṛttīnām anekāntasvabhāvataḥ |                    utpattisthitināśānāṃ virodhaḥ prāṅnirākṛtaḥ ||<597>
  441. 6.441ekasantānasambandhāt pratyabhijñānakalpanā |                    jñānasantatimārgeṇa vāryānyatvādyasambhavāt ||
  442. 6.442evaṃ sthitasya śabdasya śrutikālāt kṣaṇāntare |                    sambhāvyate vināśitvaṃ na bhūyo 'nyena hetunā ||
  443. 6.443yathā śastrādibhir bhedāj jarayā vā paṭādayaḥ |                    naṅkṣyantītyavagamyante naivaṃ śabde 'sti kāraṇam ||
  444. 6.444śabdo yathā paudgaliko niṣiddhaḥ, syād vāyavīyasya sa eva mārgaḥ |                    tasmād anirdhāritahetumārgaḥ sarvatra sākṣād bhavatīti nityaḥ ||

Chapter 7 vākyādhikaraṇa VAA

  1. 7.1padārthapadasambandhanityatve sādhite 'pi vaḥ |                    naiva vedapramāṇatvaṃ vākyārthaṃ prati sidhyati ||<599>
  2. 7.2padāni gamayeyus taṃ pratyekaṃ saṃhatāni vā |                    vyatirikto 'tha vā śabdaḥ, padārthā vā 'pi pūrvavat ||
  3. 7.3tat pramāṇaṃ smṛtīnāṃ ca tathā sambandhataddhiyām |                    pratyekaṃ saṃhatatvena tadvad eva vikalpanam ||
  4. 7.4adṛṣṭasaṅgatitvena sarveṣām animittatā |                    anyaḥ pratīto na hy anyaṃ gamayiṣyaty asaṅgatam ||
  5. 7.5apratītaś ca sambandho nāpy asattvād viśiṣyate |                    na cā'vijñāyamānasya sadbhāvo 'pi pramāṇavān ||
  6. 7.6vākyavākyārthayor nāpi vastutvam upapadyate |                    spaṣṭaṃ padatadarthābhyām anyā'nanyā'nirūpaṇāt ||
  7. 7.7na tāvad avagamyete kaiś cit tadvyatirekataḥ |                    yaugapadyāgṛhīteś ca samudāyau na sidhyataḥ ||<600>
  8. 7.8na sattāyaugapadyasya vyavahārāṅgateṣyate |                    arvanityatayā mā bhūd viśeṣānavadhāraṇam ||
  9. 7.9jñānānāṃ kramavarttitvād yaugapadye 'py asambhavaḥ |                    ena tatsamudāyo 'pi na vākyārthaḥ pratīyate ||
  10. 7.10sambandhapūrvakatvaṃ ca vākyavākyārthayoḥ sthitam |                    svatantreṣu hi vākyatvaṃ kadā cin nopalakṣyate ||
  11. 7.11sambandhaś cānapekṣatvāt kasya cin nāvakalpate |                    padāni tāvad varṇā vā svarūpair na kadācana ||
  12. 7.12anarthakeṣv adṛṣṭatvād apekṣante parasparam |                    na cānuccāritaḥ śabdaḥ śaknoty anyam apekṣitum ||
  13. 7.13yaugapadyaṃ tu nāsty eva na coccārya tirohitaḥ |                    apekṣaṇe 'pi sambandho naiva kaś cit pratīyate ||
  14. 7.14kāryakāraṇasaṃyogasamavāyādilakṣaṇaḥ |<601>                    ekārthasamavāye 'pi sarveṣāṃ vyomni tulyatā ||
  15. 7.15tatroktānuktayogyāder na viśeṣyeṇa saṅgatiḥ |                    ekakāryaniyogo 'pi vyaṅgye janye 'tha vā bhavet ||
  16. 7.16vyaṅgyās tāvat pṛthagbhūtāḥ padārthāḥ padabhedataḥ |                    tathā tadviṣayāpy etair buddhir naikāpi jāyate ||
  17. 7.17yā tu svaviṣayā buddhiḥ pratiśabdam asāv api |                    na caikajñānajananaṃ bhinnais taiḥ kramavarttibhiḥ ||
  18. 7.18na cāvayavaśo bodhād aikyaṃ vākyatadarthayoḥ |                    na cāvayavabuddhīnāṃ bhrāntitvaṃ bādhakād ṛte ||
  19. 7.19ekanirbhāgatābuddher asatyāḥ satyatā katham |                    anurāgavyavacchedau buddhīnāṃ na ca siddhyataḥ ||
  20. 7.20kṣaṇikatvād ato 'rthatvaṃ neṣṭaṃ saṃsargabhedayoḥ |<602>                    yadi dhriyata gobuddhiḥ śuklabuddhijanikṣaṇe ||
  21. 7.21tato 'nyābhyo nivartteta saṃsṛjyeta tathānayā |                    saṃsargo na ca buddhīnāṃ saṃyogāder asambhavāt ||
  22. 7.22ekātmavṛttitā tulyā ghaṭahastyādidhīṣv api |                    tathā nirantarotpattiḥ, nākāṅkṣā vātra śabdavat ||
  23. 7.23kṣaṇikā 'yugapadbhāve kā buddhiḥ kām apekṣate |                    ata eva viśiṣṭā dhīs tābhir naikopajanyate ||
  24. 7.24yataḥ kalpyeta sarvāsāṃ saṃsargas tadapekṣayā |                    na ca saṃsargavicchedanirbhāso 'ntaḥ prakalpitaḥ ||
  25. 7.25bāhyābhāso 'rtharūpeṇa pramāṇaṃ svapnavad bhavet |<603>                    na ca kālatrayopetabāhyārthāsambhave sati ||
  26. 7.26pravartetāpi vijñānaṃ na cāsmin bāhyasambhavaḥ |                    anutpanne 'pi tenāsminn utpannaparikalpanā ||
  27. 7.27arthasaṃsargadṛṣṭyā vā saṃsargo 'tra prakalpyate |                    buddhyor na tāvad evaṃ syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatā ||
  28. 7.28tathaiva śabdatadbuddhyor viśeṣotpattyasambhavāt |                    tāvān eva hi gośabdaḥ śuklaśabde 'pi kīrtite ||
  29. 7.29pūrvasattve 'pi tāvattā tasyaivaṃ taddhiyor api |                    viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatvaṃ na syāc chuklatvagotvayoḥ ||
  30. 7.30na tayor anurāgo hi nā'vacchedaḥ parasparam |<604>                    gotvena na hi śuklatvaṃ gotvaṃ vā tena rajyate ||
  31. 7.31anyonyātmany asadbhāvād vyaktyaṅgatvād dvayor api |                    vyaktiś ced anurajyeta tābhyāṃ tatrāpi śabdayoḥ ||
  32. 7.32na parasparasambandhaḥ syād atadgocarau hi tau |                    śabdair anucyamāne hi saty apy ekāśraye 'rthataḥ ||
  33. 7.33śabdānāṃ naiva sambandhaḥ pṛthivīsthagavāśvavat |                    ekārthasamavāye 'pi rūpāder naiva saṅgatiḥ ||
  34. 7.34na caikavyaktivṛttitve pramāṇaṃ gotvaśuklayoḥ |                    sambandhād etayos tatra syād ekavyaktikalpanā ||
  35. 7.35tadekatvāc ca sambandha evam anyonyasaṃśrayam |<605>                    na cātra padam asty anyad yenaikavyaktidhīr bhavet ||
  36. 7.36na cā'syāḥ padavācyatvaṃ, vācyate 'pi na caikatā |                    gamyamānasya caikatvāt sambandho yadi kalpyate ||
  37. 7.37pārthivatvādyabhedena kiṃ na syād ghaṭavṛkṣayoḥ |                    śuklaśrutyā na gotvādiḥ kṛṣṇādibhyo nivarttyate ||
  38. 7.38svabhāvato 'vabodhaś ca tadvaśān nā'pasarpati |<606>                    kṛṣṇādyapohanaṃ vācyaṃ śuklaśabdasya yady api ||
  39. 7.39tathāpi gogatatve 'sya pramāṇaṃ naiva sannidhiḥ |                    tadviṣaya eveti yāvacchabdena nocyate ||
  40. 7.40tāvat sarvam aśābdaṃ syāt svātantryeṇā'dhyavasyataḥ |                    sannidher anumīyeta tādṛśaṃ vacanaṃ yadi ||
  41. 7.41punaḥ saṇṇidhyadhīnaiva tasyaitadviṣayā'rthatā |                    tatrāpi śabdakḷptiś ced anavasthā bhaved iyam ||
  42. 7.42ṣaṭpramāṇā'tiriktatvāt tasmāt sannidhyanāśrayaḥ |                    sambandhakāraṇaṃ nāpi ṣaṣṭhī gavyupalabhyate ||
  43. 7.43satyām api tu sambandhaḥ śrautas tāvan nirākṛtaḥ |<607>                    gamyamānasya cārthasya naiva dṛṣṭaṃ viśeṣaṇam ||
  44. 7.44śabdāntarair vibhaktyā vā dhūmo 'yaṃ jvalatītivat |                    saṃsarge cāpi bhede vā vākyārthe parikalpite ||
  45. 7.45tasya yāvat padārthatvān naikavākyatvasambhavaḥ |                    padārthavyatirekaś ca nāsti saṃsargabhedayoḥ ||
  46. 7.46na ca vastvantarā''rambhaḥ padārthais tadanugrahāt |                    na hi jātiguṇaiḥ kiṃ cit kāryamāraśyate bahiḥ ||
  47. 7.47tadabhāve 'vabodhaś ca jāto 'pi svapnavanmṛṣā |                    satām eva viśeṣāṇāṃ saṃnidher yo 'pi manyate ||
  48. 7.48vākyārthatvam abhivyaktau tasyāpi tadanekatā |                    prāksattve ca kutas teṣāṃ pramāṇaṃ pratyayair vinā ||
  49. 7.49na caiṣāṃ vastusattvaṃ ca tatpade 'stitvakāraṇaṃ |<608>                    evam ādyā'ntyasarveṣāṃ pṛthaksaṃghātakalpane ||
  50. 7.50anyonyā'nugrahā'bhāvāt padānāṃ nāsti vākyatā |                    ādyaṃ yadi padaṃ sarvaiḥ saṃskriyeta viśeṣataḥ ||
  51. 7.51tatas tad eva vākyaṃ syād anyaś ca dyotako gaṇaḥ |                    evam antyeṣu sarveṣu pṛthagbhūteṣv avasthitam ||
  52. 7.52svatantreṣu hi vākyatvaṃ kathacinnopalakṣitam |                    sphoṭajātiniṣedhaś ca syāt padasphoṭajātivat ||
  53. 7.53vāryaḥ padakramo vākyaṃ yathā varṇakramaḥ padam |                    buddhyā na copasaṃhartuḥ kramo niṣkṛṣya śakyate ||
  54. 7.54padāny eva hi tadvanti vartante śrotrabuddhivat |<609>                    tāvatsv eva padeṣv anyaḥ kramo 'nyaś ca pratīyate ||
  55. 7.55tatra yāvat kramaṃ bhedo vākyārthasya prasajyate |                    padāntarasya pārārthyādākhyātaṃ yo 'pi manyate ||
  56. 7.56vākyaṃ prādhānyayogena vākyārthaṃ cāpi bhāvanām |                    tatrāpi na bahirvastu kriyākārakasaṅgatiḥ ||
  57. 7.57na kārakāṇām anyonyaṃ na kriyāṇāṃ pratīyate |                    ukhāyāmodanaṃ kāṣṭhair devadattaḥ paced iti ||
  58. 7.58dravyāṇāṃ tāvad etasmin na sambandhaḥ parasparam |                    atyantabhedaniṣpannaṣaṣṭhyabhāvānapekṣaṇaiḥ ||
  59. 7.59tṛtīyādyapahāreṇa sannidher api bādhanāt |                    kāṣṭhādīnāṃ ca sambandhaḥ kriyayā na svarūpataḥ ||
  60. 7.60ārdrādidharmakaiḥ pākas taiḥ kṛto na hi dṛśyate |<610>                    śaktiḥ kāraṇam iṣṭhā ced, amūrtā sāpi niṣkriyā ||
  61. 7.61śaktair api ca taiḥ pākas tiṣṭhadbhir naiva sādhyate |                    jvalanādimukhenātha teṣāṃ pākena saṅgatiḥ ||
  62. 7.62tathāpi karmaṇā kramaṃ na sādhyam iti durbham |                    bhinnārthasamavetatvān na ca sambandhasambhavaḥ ||
  63. 7.63na cānyakārakotpādye kārakaṃ kārakāntaram |                    jvalanādīni kurvanti na ca syuḥ pākasādhanam ||
  64. 7.64apākasādhanānāṃ ca kutas tenaikavācyatā |                    jvalanādigatā pāke śaktiś ced upacaryate ||
  65. 7.65kartṛtvāt tatra kāṣṭhādeḥ karaṇatvādi ca durlabham |<611>                    mukhyaṃ kārakavaicitryam alabdhaṃ jvalanādiṣu ||
  66. 7.66kathaṃ tu pākavelāyām upacāreṇa labhyate |                    svavyāpāre ca kāṣṭhādeḥ karaṇatvādyasambhavaḥ ||
  67. 7.67viklidyanti jvalantīti bibhratīti ca darśanāt |                    na caiṣāṃ pākavelāyāṃ vyāpārāntaram iṣyate ||
  68. 7.68ekaprayogavat, tena kartṛtaiva prasajyate |                    pacinā cānupātteṣu jvalanādiṣv asaṅgatiḥ ||
  69. 7.69na hi sadbhāvamātreṇa tāni sambandhakāraṇam |                    na ca śabdāntarair eṣām upādānamataḥ paciḥ ||
  70. 7.70devadattakriyāvācī na syāt kāṣṭhādisaṅgataḥ |                    sarvavyāpāravācī cet pacir iṣṭas tathā sati ||
  71. 7.71kartṛtvam eva kāṣṭāder āpannaṃ devadattavat |                    dhātunoktakriye nityaṃ kārake kartṛteṣyate ||<612>
  72. 7.72sarveṣāṃ bhāvanāsāmye na hy anyat kartṛlakṣaṇam |                    kāṣṭhādīni pacantīti vivakṣā yā ca dṛśyate ||
  73. 7.73sāpi naivopapadyeta yady anyat kartṛlakṣaṇam |                    ekadhātugṛhītānāṃ na cāsty aṅgapradhānatā ||
  74. 7.74na kārakaṃ tataḥ karttā prādhānyābhihitakriyam |                    ataḥ samapradhānānām abhidhā sadasattvayoḥ ||
  75. 7.75kva cit kārakavaicitryaṃ kva cid aikyaṃ na yujyate |                    pratyayenāpi naivātra jvalanādiparigrahaḥ ||
  76. 7.76kartṛmātraṃ tv asau brūyād atha vā tadgatā kriyām |                    tasmān na pacatīty atra kāṣṭhāder asti saṅgatiḥ ||
  77. 7.77sarvatra na ca dhātvarthaḥ pratyayārthena yujyate |<613>                    bhāvanā pratyayārtho hi dhātvarthānāṃ ca tāṃ prati ||
  78. 7.78sādhyasādhanayogyānām upādānaṃ ca dhātubhiḥ |                    sādhyatvaṃ pākam ity evaṃ pākenaiva ca sādhanam ||
  79. 7.79pac ity etena rūpeṇa naiko 'py aṃśaḥ pratīyate |                    vidhibhāvanayoś caikapratyayagrāhyatākṛtaḥ ||
  80. 7.80dhātvarthāt prathamaṃ tāvat sambandho 'dhyavasīyate |                    vidhāv avasite tatra kevale bhāvanātmani ||
  81. 7.81paścāt sambadhyamāno 'pi na dhātvartho vidhīyate |                    vidhyahīnapravṛtteś ca na sa kāryaḥ śruto 'pi san ||
  82. 7.82evaṃ kārakavidhyantavidhānasyāpy asambhavaḥ |                    vidhyantatvaṃ prayājāder niṣedhavyam asaṅgatam ||<614>
  83. 7.83asambaddhatvam eteṣāṃ vācyaṃ śuklagavādivat |                    tatrārthalakṣaṇā kā cit sambhaved api saṅgatiḥ ||
  84. 7.84vākyair eva tv asambaddhaiḥ sambandho na prakalpyate |                    ato 'nyonyāśrayatvaṃ syād ekamūlāprasiddhitaḥ ||
  85. 7.85evam aṃśatrayāsattvāj jāto nirviṣayo vidhiḥ |                    dhātvarthakārakāṇāṃ tu sākṣān naivaiṣa sidhyati ||
  86. 7.86vidher bhāvanayā rodhāt kartus teṣv apravartanāt |                    kriyākārakasambandhamūlatvāt sarvasaṅgatiḥ ||
  87. 7.87niṣedhyā tanniṣedhena svasvāmipitṛbandhuṣu |                    upasarganipātānāṃ kena cin na ca saṅgatiḥ ||
  88. 7.88parasparaṃ tv asiddhaiva svātantryeṇa ca nāmabhiḥ |<615>                    kriyāviśeṣaṇatvāc ca vinā naivopasargatā ||
  89. 7.89vākyārtho 'sattvabhūtatvād etair na ca viśiṣyate |                    kriyādvārā'tha kalpyeta sāpi nākārakātmanaḥ ||
  90. 7.90asattvabhūm arthaṃ ca nādhyavasyati kārakam |                    viśeṣaṇatvam apy eṣāṃ naivārthānanurañjanāt ||
  91. 7.91ānarthakyānyavācitvaviparotaprasādhanāt |                    pralambate 'yam ityādau teṣāṃ kaś cid arthakaḥ ||
  92. 7.92prāsādādiṣu cānyo 'rtho viparītaḥ pratiṣṭhate |                    yena svārthāvirodhena viśeṣa upajanyate ||
  93. 7.93viśeṣaṇaṃ tadeveṣṭaṃ na tu yat svārthanāśakam |                    ābhimukhyordhvagatyādiviśeṣo yo 'vagamyate ||
  94. 7.94tasyāpi kartṛdharmatvān na dhātvarthāṅgateṣyate |                    kartrā ca saha sambandho nopasargasya vidyate ||
  95. 7.95aṃśatrayātiriktatvān nāpi bhāvanayā saha |                    pratiṣedhavikalpādeḥ sambandhaś ca virudhyate ||<616>
  96. 7.96anyarūpaparicchedād vāhyavastvarthavādinām |                    svaśruteḥ prathamaṃ vastu sadbhāvena nirūpitam ||
  97. 7.97kathaṃ nañādibhiḥ paścād abhāvam upanīyate |                    virodhaś ca tayoḥ śrutyor asti nāstīti śabdavat ||
  98. 7.98vikalpe punarekasya śabdasyaiṣā virodhitā |                    gavādivac ca naiteṣāṃ svatantrārthāvadhāraṇam ||
  99. 7.99yena tatpūrvakaṃ santaṃ vākyārthaṃ yāyurātmanā |                    samudāye 'py asiddhatvāt yena vakṣyaty ahetutām ||
  100. 7.100gamyate cet yato 'vocat pratyekāśaktisiddhaye |                    asambandhāt padārthānām iti pūrvoktayā diśā ||
  101. 7.101sann apy ajñāyamānatvād asann ity abhidhīyate |<617>                    aikaikaśye padārthānāṃ vākyārthe vyabhicāritā ||
  102. 7.102prāgasiddheḥ samastānām asādhāraṇaduṣṭatā |                    padārthān eva vākyārthaṃ yaḥ sāmastyena manyate ||
  103. 7.103gaur aśvaḥ puruṣo hastīty atrāpy asya prasajyate |                    vyastasya yo 'rthaḥ śabdasya na sāmastye jahāti tam ||
  104. 7.104taṃ cojjhati na viśrambhaḥ padārthaṃ prati labhyate |                    tatra dvitrādisāmānyavijñānaṃ kevalaṃ bhavet ||
  105. 7.105anekaśabdavijñānān na viśeṣāvadhāraṇam |<618>                    padārthasaṅgate 'rthe ced vākyaṃ sākṣāt pravarttate ||
  106. 7.106padārthasaṃvidas tatra na syād dṛṣṭopakāritā |                    tenājñātapadārtho 'pi budhyetaiva svabhāvataḥ ||
  107. 7.107tān vānurudhyamānasya kāraṇaṃ syusta eva te |                    tatra coktam, ato nāsti vākyadhīmūlasambhavaḥ ||
  108. 7.108tataś cārthād bhavel loke, vedārthas tv apramāṇakaḥ |                    samayāt puruṣāṇāṃ vā guṇavṛddhyādivanmataḥ ||
  109. 7.109niṣkāraṇo 'pi sannartho yājñikaiḥ paribhāṣitaḥ |                    tatra coktaṃ kathāvat tu saṅghātāt pauruṣeyatā ||<619>
  110. 7.110na cāptaḥ puruṣo 'trāsti, tena vedāpramāṇatā |                    atrābhidhīyate, yady apy asti mūlāntaraṃ na naḥ ||
  111. 7.111padārthānāṃ tu mūlatvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tadbhāvabhāvataḥ |                    satyaṃ na vācakaṃ vākyaṃ vākyārthasyopapadyate ||
  112. 7.112anyathāpy upapannatvāc chaktis tatrāpramāṇikā |                    pada eva hi varṇānāṃ śaktiḥ kleśena kalpitā ||
  113. 7.113tirobhāvād iha tv eṣāṃ bhavet kleśatareṇa sā |                    bahavaś cānusandheyā varṇāś ciratirohitāḥ ||
  114. 7.114padārtheṣūpayuktānāṃ punarvyāpārakalpanā |<620>                    padārthānāṃ ca sāmarthyaṃ gamyamānam apahnutam ||
  115. 7.115ānantaryād dhi vākyārthas taddhetutvaṃ na muñcati |                    ekayaiva hi saṃskṛtyā kathaṃ kāryadvayaṃ bhavet ||
  116. 7.116na caiṣāṃ pūrvasaṃskārād anyo 'stīti pratīyate |                    na cānyavarṇavelāyāṃ teṣv ālocanasambhavaḥ ||
  117. 7.117padatadvācyasambandhabuddhivyavadhibādhanāt |                    pratyakṣasmṛtirūpāto na teṣv ekāsti vākyadhīḥ ||
  118. 7.118tasmāc ca vākyanirbhāsā vākyaṃ sā dhīr na kalpate |                    vākyam ity anayā buddhyā na cātmāṃśaḥ pratīyate ||
  119. 7.119na ca vākyārthabuddhyedaṃ śūnyavāde nirūpitam |<621>                    vākyavākyārthyor aikye bāhyābhyantaravādinām ||
