  120. 7.120vicchinnabhāgabuddhīnāṃ mṛṣātvaṃ niṣpramāṇakam |                    kalpyamāne 'pi naivaṃ ca vastubuddhir nivarttate ||
  121. 7.121teṣv eva ca padārtheṣu prakḷptastokaśaktiṣu |                    āvāpodvāparacanābhedād vākyeṣv anantā ||
  122. 7.122stokaśaktyupapanne 'rthe bahuśaktyapramāṇatā |                    vākyatacchaktyanantatve nārthāpattis tato bhavet ||
  123. 7.123na cāvayavabuddhīnāṃ sādṛśyād bhrāntikalpanā |                    na prasiddhāḥ pṛthagbhūtā mukhyā hy avayavāḥ kva cit ||
  124. 7.124nāvayavyantare yasmāt sarvavākyeṣv abhāgatā |                    satām avayavānāṃ hi syād vā sadṛśatā na vā ||<622>
  125. 7.125sādṛśyaṃ narasiṃhādau yuktaṃ jātyantare sati |                    tatra hy avayavāḥ siddhāḥ prāksaṃyogavibhāginaḥ ||
  126. 7.126pāṇyādayo hi vicchinnā dṛśyante nṛśarīrataḥ |                    deheṣu ca pṛthagbuddhis teṣu sarveṣu jāyate ||
  127. 7.127tatra tatsadṛśatvād vā tatsāmānyena vaikatā |                    hastādiṣūpapanneti pratyabhijñānasambhavaḥ ||
  128. 7.128tadvad atrāpi sādṛśyaṃ yadi nāmāvadhāryate |                    siddhe 'vayavasatyatve mṛṣā nirbhāgakalpanā ||
  129. 7.129asatā yat tu sādṛśyam asataḥ parikalpyate |                    dhruvaṃ śaśaviṣāṇena kharaśṛṅgasya tad bhavet ||
  130. 7.130athāsattvena sādṛśyam atrāpy astīti manyate |                    sarvatraivaṃ samānatvāt kaś cin nāsadṛśo bhavet ||
  131. 7.131bhāgaś citre 'pi dṛṣṇādir dṛṣṭa eva sadṛktayā |<623>                    ekadeśaś ca madye 'pi samyaktiktaraseṣu ca ||
  132. 7.132citrabuddhes tu naivāsti pratītir bhāgaśo mama |                    ākārābhāvataḥ, artho 'tra citraḥ sāvayavaḥ sa ca ||
  133. 7.133tasmān na padavarṇānām asattvāt sadṛśī gatiḥ |                    vākyasyāpi na sādṛśyaṃ tatrāvayavavarjanāt ||
  134. 7.134syād varṇapadaniṣkṛṣṭir na ca vākyasadṛktayā |                    tena na syād apoddhāras teṣām ālambanād ṛte ||<624>
  135. 7.135na ca vyañjakabhedo 'pi padavarṇādṛte 'sti te |                    sūkṣmatvād, aṇukalpānāṃ dhvanīnāṃ parikalpanāt ||
  136. 7.136na ca kāryāntarārambhas tais tādṛgupapadyate |                    tenāṇumātraśabdāṃśagṛhītiḥ kevalā bhavet ||
  137. 7.137sator api ca nādānāṃ pṛthaktvakramavattvayoḥ |                    vyaṅgyābhāvena naivaiṣām abhivyaktiḥ prasidhyati ||
  138. 7.138kṛtsnasya yaugapadyena bhaved vāvagatir na vā |                    naiva prāksakalād vākyād grāhyaṃ kiñ cit tavāsti hi ||
  139. 7.139tad eva sakalaṃ vākyaṃ nyūnam anyadapekṣya ca |                    tadviruddham, <625> na cābhinne nyūnasākalyakalpanā ||
  140. 7.140pṛthakprasiddhasadbhāvaṃ tripadaṃ ca catuṣpade |                    nāstīti yadi kalpyeta vṛkṣo na syāt tadā vane ||
  141. 7.141pṛthakprasiddhyamithyātvāt syād vākyāntaratā yadi |                    vākyāc chabdāntaratvaṃ syāt tathaiva padavarṇayoḥ ||
  142. 7.142tasmād yathā mahāvākye laghūnām anirākriyā |                    tathaiva padavarṇānāṃ nāsattvaṃ vākyabuddhiṣu ||
  143. 7.143kevalasyāprayogāc cet, mahadarthe laghor api |                    alpārthe tatprayuktaṃ cet svārthe tadvat padāni naḥ ||<626>
  144. 7.144yady api vyavahāraṅgaṃ na pūrṇaṃ padavarṇayoḥ |                    tathāpy asty eva sadbhāvas tanmātre prayuyukṣite ||
  145. 7.145padārthamātram eveṣṭaṃ viśeṣe 'vagate kva cit |                    padaṃ prayuñjate ke cid varṇaṃ vārthasamanvitam ||
  146. 7.146granthādhyayanavelāyāṃ svarūpeṇāvadhāraṇam |                    pradhānaṃ padavarṇānāṃ vicchinnānām upāśritam ||
  147. 7.147tadā prasiddhasattvānāṃ cottaratrāsti sādhanam |                    na hi vākyārthabuddhyaiṣāṃ rūpaṃ kiñ cid viruddhyate ||
  148. 7.148yady apy eṣāṃ na sāmarthyaṃ kevalānāṃ tadudgame |                    aviruddhas tu sadbhāvaḥ kāryāśaktarathāṅgavat ||
  149. 7.149kevalasyāprayogitvaṃ tenānaikāntikīkṛtam |                    kāryād ṛte 'pi dṛṣṭir yā, <627> sā śabde 'py upapāditā ||
  150. 7.150sadbhāve padavarṇānāṃ bhedo yaḥ paramāṇuvat |                    sarvābhāvas tataś ceti seyaṃ bālabibhīṣikā ||
  151. 7.151yathā tantvādayaḥ siddhāḥ paramāṇuṣu satsv api |                    tathā satsv api bhāgeṣu na varṇādi virotsyate ||
  152. 7.152kiñ cit sāvayavaṃ dṛṣṭvā na ca sarvaṃ prasajyate |                    ghaṭasāvayavatve 'pi na bhāgaḥ paramāṇuṣu ||
  153. 7.153tad atra padavarṇānāṃ bhedaṃ pratyakṣasādhitam |                    varṇāṃśānupapattyā kaḥ śaknuyādapabādhitum ||<628>
  154. 7.154asattve ye ca dṛṣṭāntāḥ prakṛtipratyayādayaḥ |                    asiddhās te, yato loke tatsadbhāvaḥ pratīyate ||
  155. 7.155naiva hi prakriyāmātraṃ śāstrataḥ parikalpyate |                    pratyakṣaṃ hy eva tadrūpaṃ vācyam apy anyavācyavat ||
  156. 7.156krameṇa hi pratīyete prakṛtipratyayau pade |                    tadāgame tadartho 'pi svasaṃvedyaḥ krameṇa naḥ ||
  157. 7.157anvayavyatirekābhyām apy artho gamyate tayoḥ |                    amādyupajanāpāye vṛkṣārtho hy anugamyate ||
  158. 7.158vṛkṣaṃ vṛkṣeṇa cety atra vṛkṣatvaṃ tāvad eva hi |                    karmatvaṃ hīyate pūrvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca jāyate ||
  159. 7.159tathā vṛkṣaṃ ghaṭaṃ ceti karmatvam anugamyate |                    vṛkṣatvaṃ hīyate 'nyā ca ghaṭadhīrupajāyate ||
  160. 7.160tatra yo 'nveti yaṃ śabdam arthas tasya bhaved asau |                    anyathānupapattyā hi śaktis tatrāvatiṣṭhate ||<629>
  161. 7.161yat kūpayūpasūpādau samāne 'py upabandhane |                    nāsty arthānugamaḥ kaś cit tan na śabdo 'parādhyati ||
  162. 7.162nānvayavyatirekābhyām apūrvārthāvadhāraṇam |                    saṃsṛṣṭe 'vagate 'rthe hi tābhyāṃ śaktir niyamyate ||
  163. 7.163tenānekātmakāc chabdād anekārthāvabodhane |                    siddhe yadāgame yo 'rthaḥ sa tasyaivāvadhāryate ||
  164. 7.164evaṃ pipīlikāpaṅkte reṇucakrānvaye sati |                    gajāśvopajanāpāye 'py atādarthyam aśaktitaḥ ||<630>
  165. 7.165asty eva ca gajāśveṣu sāmānyaṃ reṇukāraṇam |                    dṛḍhaprāṇiviśeṣatvaṃ samastavyastalakṣitam ||
  166. 7.166dṛṣṭā pipīlikāpaṅktiḥ kevalā reṇuvarjitā |                    hastyādyanvayinī tena na hetutvaṃ prapadyate ||
  167. 7.167prakṛtipratyayādīnāṃ kevalāviniyogataḥ |                    yathaivārthā na dṛśyante tathā cānartham apy adaḥ ||
  168. 7.168nāmākhyātādisākalyavaikalyānugame sati |                    tadarthāsambhavo dṛṣṭaḥ padavākyāntarāśrayaḥ ||
  169. 7.169viprāśvaḥ pacate yātaṃ rājahastinyagāditi |                    tathānyarūpam anyādṛk rājñā dadhy atra gām iti ||
  170. 7.170vipraśabdau kva cid dṛṣṭānupasargārthavācinau |                    samudāyas tathānyatra brāhmaṇatvāvabodhakaḥ ||
  171. 7.171aśva ity api nāmedam ākhyātaṃ luṅi cedṛśam |                    ākhyātaṃ pacateśabdaḥ paca te iti vā dvayam ||<631>
  172. 7.172strīdvitvaṃ puṃbahutvaṃ vā te ṣaṣṭhyartha caturthyatha |                    pacate iti sarvaṃ vā caturthyantaṃ śatuḥ padam ||
  173. 7.173yātaṃ loṇmadhyamadvitvamayātaṃ laṅi vā bhvet |                    kartṛniṣṭhādvitīyāntaṃ prathamāntaṃ napuṃsakam ||
  174. 7.174rājahastī samāso vā rājaloṇmadhyamo 'pi vā |                    hastinītyatha saptamyāmatha strīpratyayāntaram ||
  175. 7.175agāditi luṅantaṃ syādago vā pañcamīparaḥ |                    tānattītyatha vāpy evaṃ kvibanto 'yaṃ samāsabhāk ||
  176. 7.176evamarthavikalpena bhede 'rtho nāvatiṣṭhate |                    nirbhāge vācake vākye samastādasti nirṇyaḥ ||
  177. 7.177tasmān na yo yam anveti sarvadā tena so 'rthavān |                    anarthakatvavijñānāt tadrūpe 'pi padāntare ||
  178. 7.178tathā rājārthavān dṛṣṭo rājñety atra ca nāsty asau |                    dadhi gaur iti nāpīmau vidmo dadhy atra gāmiti ||
  179. 7.179anyasmiñ jñātasambandhe niṣiddho 'nyaś ca vācakaḥ |<632>                    na ca sarvavikārāṇām ānantyāt saṅgatīkṣaṇam ||
  180. 7.180tasmād anarthakair eva vinā jātiguṇānvayāt |                    prakṛtipratyayādyantapadabhāgavivarjitaiḥ ||
  181. 7.181vākyair eva viśiṣṭho 'rthaḥ svatantraiḥ pratipādyate |                    bhāgaśaḥ kathitopāyair aśvakarṇājakarṇavat ||
  182. 7.182atra brūmaḥ padātmā na sarveṣv eteṣu bhidyate |                    kena cid dhaddharmabhedena jarā rājetivat kramāt ||
  183. 7.183padāvadhāraṇopāyān bahūnicchanti sūrayaḥ |                    kramanyūnātiriktatvasvaravākyasmṛtiśrutīḥ ||<633>
  184. 7.184śeṣān arthān paricchidya svarūpair vākyagocarān |                    tatsambandhānurūpārthavācitvenānyanirṇayaḥ ||
  185. 7.185tatrāvadhṛtanāmārthair ākhyātāpekṣaṇena tat |                    ākhyāte sati nāmatvaṃ bhaved ubhayasambhave ||
  186. 7.186yathā ca puruṣākāre samāne 'py avagamyate |                    smaraṇād brāhmaṇatvādi prakṛtipratyayānvayāt ||
  187. 7.187tathānvākhyānabhedena prakṛtipratyayādibhiḥ |                    nāmākhyātavyavasthānaṃ smaraṇenopalakṣyate ||
  188. 7.188aprāptasmṛtyupāyānāṃ viveko 'yaṃ na jāyate |                    ajñāte pitṛsaṃbandhe tulyo 'sau brāhmaṇādiṣu ||
  189. 7.189tathā śrutyaiva sandigdhaṃ kiñ cin nirṇīyate padam |                    sāmānādhikaraṇyena prasiddhākhyātanāmabhiḥ ||<634>
  190. 7.190nanv ayaṃ na vibhāgaḥ syāt padajātimanicchataḥ |                    nāmākhyātamatigrāhyāḥ kathaṃ varṇāsta eva te ||
  191. 7.191kena vā neṣyate jātiḥ padajātacatuṣṭaye |                    suptiṅkṛttaddhitāḥ santi tathā dhātvādijātayaḥ ||
  192. 7.192padaikye 'py aviruddheyam atyantānatirekiṇī |                    varṇā eveti cagranthe niṣiddhātyantabhinnatā ||
  193. 7.193bhramaṇatvādivac cāsau vyajyate kramavarttibhiḥ |                    antyavarṇe 'tha vā vyaktiḥ pūrvasaṃskṛtyapekṣiṇi ||
  194. 7.194yad vā yenaiva dharmeṇa vyaṅktuṃ jātyantaraṃ kṣamāḥ |                    varṇāḥ svarūpasāmye 'pi tenākhyātādibuddhiṣu ||<635>
  195. 7.195vanapaṅktyādivac caiṣu samudāyeṣv asatsv api |                    bhinnākhyātādisāmānyavyavahāro bhaviṣyati ||
  196. 7.196dhātupratyayatadvācyasāmānyānām iyaṃ gatiḥ |                    taddhitākhyātakṛdrūpaṃ nityaṃ hi smaryate janaiḥ ||
  197. 7.197na cānvākhyānamātreṇa kalpitaṃ tacchabādivat |                    prayujyate hi yadrūpaṃ tadupāye na tiṣṭhati ||<636>
  198. 7.198avadhyagrahaṇaṃ yat tu prakṛtipratyayau prati |                    anvākhyānavisaṃvādād ity etac ca na duṣyati ||
  199. 7.199tatra hy āptanaroktīnāṃ prāmāṇyam upapadyate |                    yad vā tulyabalatvena vikalpena matāntaram ||
  200. 7.200prakṛtiḥ pratyayāṃśo vā kaś cit tāvan na bhidyate |                    śiṣṭe vikaraṇādau tu yatheṣṭāṅgāṅgikalpanā ||
  201. 7.201dhūmādāv api vahnyaṃśo kaś cid aṃśo 'numāpakaḥ |                    anyaḥ sādhāraṇo yadvat tadvad atra bhaviṣyati ||
  202. 7.202yathā ca nityarūpatvān na tatrāṃśāntaroddhṛtiḥ |                    tathātrāgamako 'py aṃśo nityatve na vyavasthitaḥ ||
  203. 7.203yatra pratyayalopena prakṛtiḥ syāt kvibantabat |                    śuddhaḥ prakṛtilopena pratyayo vādhunādivat ||
  204. 7.204tanmātrasya dviśaktitvaṃ tatra śabdasvabhāvataḥ |                    vākyārthe taddhitāntādipadasāmarthyabhedavat ||
  205. 7.205ekadeśānumānena ke cid āhur dvayārthatām |                    apare 'rthaikadeśena bruvate 'nyārthalakṣaṇām ||<637>
  206. 7.206tattvayuktaṃ yato nāsti lakṣaṇārūpatā mateḥ |                    mukhyatvenaiva buddhir naḥ kvibantādiṣu jāyate ||
  207. 7.207lakṣaṇādipravṛttiś ca na śāstreṇānugamyate |                    tatsaṅkare ca tenaiva vācyavācakanirṇayaḥ ||
  208. 7.208na ca tena sahaitasya vijñātā sahavācitā |                    lokaprayuktaśabdārtho nopāyatvāc ca mucyate ||
  209. 7.209ākhyātapratyayenāpi sahāsāv upalakṣitaḥ |                    kāmaṃ tadīyam apy arthaṃ gamayed anumānataḥ ||<638>
  210. 7.210tāvatyaṃśe na kalpyau ca prakṛtipratyayau punaḥ |                    sa evārthadviśaktitve varaṃ kleśaḥ samāśritaḥ ||
  211. 7.211nirjñātaparimāṇasya smaraṇānugamād vinā |                    nānātvaṃ kalpayitvāsya kaḥ śaktiṃ kalpayiṣyati ||
  212. 7.212dadhyatreti yadanyādṛkpadaṃ pūrvāvadhāritāt |                    ke cid āhus tad evedam ajānantaryadūṣitam ||
  213. 7.213pratyabhijñāyate tad dhi sa cārthaḥ sampratīyate |                    ikāre tu yavijñānamakāraparasaṃhite ||
  214. 7.214atha vātmīyasiddhāntād yakāratve 'sya saty api |                    dadhivācyārthaṃ sāmarthyaṃ lakṣaṇād avagamyate ||
  215. 7.215tathā hy aśrutadadhyatro lakṣaṇānugamād vinā |                    vyutpannadadhiśabdo 'pi dadhyatreti na buddhyate ||<639>
  216. 7.216vikārānantyato yas tu sambandhajñaptyasambhavaḥ |                    lakṣaṇāt tadvidukter vā nātikleśo bhaviṣyati ||
  217. 7.217kiyat padam iti jñānaṃ yat tu tatra na jāyate |                    svarāntaṃ vyañjanāntaṃ vā na cājñāte 'rthanirṇayaḥ ||
  218. 7.218taducyate padacchede tadapabhraṃśatāṃ vrajet |                    saṃhitāviṣaye cāsya smaryate sādhuśabdatā ||
  219. 7.219etasmiṃs tu pratīmo 'rtham agṛhītāvadhāv api |                    tena saty api vicchede pade bhedo 'rthabhedataḥ ||
  220. 7.220jñāyate cāvadhis tatra vyañjanānto na tūcyate |                    dadhiśabdāvabodhyatvān nityaṃ nityasamāsavat ||
  221. 7.221etena rājarājñādiśabdānāṃ dattam uttaram |<640>                    kiñ cid aṃśasamānaṃ hi tadarthaṃ tatpadāntaram ||
  222. 7.222yat tu brāhmaṇavastrādau brāhmaṇārtho na gamyate |                    avadhyantaratas tatra tatpadāntarajṛmbhitam ||
  223. 7.223utsargasyāpavādena bādhaḥ kasya na sammataḥ |                    tad brāhmapadam utsṛṣṭaṃ bādhyate 'nyāvadhau pade ||
  224. 7.224tattvenāvadhim utkṛṣya yady ucyeta padāntaram |                    kena svārtho 'sya vāryeta devadattādiśabdavat ||
  225. 7.225evam evāśvakarṇādau samudāyaprasiddhitaḥ |                    vāryate 'vayavasyārtho vṛkṣādyarthāvadhāraṇāt ||
  226. 7.226arthaprakaraṇādhīnabādhitasvārthayor api |                    samastavyastayor bhūyaḥ sa evārthaḥ pratīyate ||<641>
  227. 7.227gośuklādipadānāṃ tu samastavyastabhāvinām |                    svārthahānir na dṛṣṭeti kvānarthakyaṃ bhaviṣyati ||
  228. 7.228padārthānugataś caiṣa vādyārtho gamyate sadā |                    na viśiṣṭārthatā tasmād vākyasvātantryasādhinī ||
  229. 7.229na vimuñcanti sāmarthyaṃ vākyārtheṣu padāni naḥ |                    tanmātrāvasiteṣv eṣu padārthebhyaḥ sa gamyate ||
  230. 7.230aśābde cāpi vākyārthai na padārtheṣv aśābdatā |                    vākyārthasyeva naiteṣāṃ nimittāntarasambhavaḥ ||
  231. 7.231sambaddham eva caite 'rthaṃ gamayantyavinābhuvam |                    sāmānyaṃ svaviśeṣeṇa vinā na hy upapadyate ||<642>
  232. 7.232na cānumānam eṣā dhīs tanmātreṇa prasajyate |                    pratijñārthaikadeśatvāt padārthānāṃ hy aliṅgatā ||
  233. 7.233padārthair anurakto 'sau vākyārthaḥ sampratīyate |                    nātmanā gamayantyenaṃ vinā, dhūmo 'gnimattvavat ||
  234. 7.234pakṣadharmatvam eteṣāṃ vākyārthe na ca gamyate |                    na hi deśādivat pūrvaṃ niṣpannaḥ sa pratīyate ||
  235. 7.235asattvabhūtamenaṃ hi pratipadyāmahe tataḥ |                    kriyākārakasaṃsargaviśiṣṭaḥ prāgasau kutaḥ ||
  236. 7.236dharmiṇy anavabuddhe ca na taddharmāvadhāraṇam |                    na ca prāgbodhakaṃ kiñ cid vākyārthasyopapadyate ||
  237. 7.237avabuddhe tu vākyārthe yadi taddharmatā bhavet |                    vijñāte 'rthe tataḥ kiṃ nu prameyam avaśiṣyate ||
  238. 7.238anvayaś ca padārthānāṃ na vākyārthair apekṣyate |<643>                    sarvasminn eva sujñāno bhūtabhāvitirohite ||
  239. 7.239anyavākyārthasambandhajñānāc cānyo na gamyate |                    anyatvāc ca padārthānām, te cen nānyārthadhīr bhavet ||
  240. 7.240sāmānyadṛṣṭakḷptau vā labhyate na viśeṣadhīḥ |                    vākyārthāvagatiḥ sarvā tv asādhāraṇagocarā ||
  241. 7.241asambandhapratīteś ca prāmāṇyam upapāditam |                    sarvalokaprasiddhā ca pratipattir iha sphuṭā ||
  242. 7.242yatra kva cana vijñātān padārthān pratipadya hi |                    dūradeśādivār tāsu nāptokte dhīr vihanyate ||
  243. 7.243āptavādāvisaṃvādād atra ced anumānatā |<644>                    nirṇayas tāvatā sidhyed buddhyutpattir na tatkṛtā ||
  244. 7.244anyad eva hi satyatvam āptavādatvahetukam |                    vākyārthaś cānya eveti jñātaḥ pūrvataraṃ tataḥ ||
  245. 7.245tatra ced āptavādena satyatvam anumīyate |                    vākyārthapratyayasyātra kathaṃ syād anumānatā ||
  246. 7.246janma tulyaṃ hi buddhīnām āptānāptagirāṃ śrutau |                    janmādhikopayogī ca nānumāyās trilakṣaṇaḥ ||
  247. 7.247śabdaprāmāṇyanirṇītyai padārthebhyo yatheṣyate |                    atyantādṛṣṭavākyārthapratipattis tathocyate ||<645>
  248. 7.248bhāvanāvacanas tāvat tāṃ smārayati lokavat |                    anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ pratyayārthas tu seṣyate ||
  249. 7.249kaiś cit, anyais tu dhātvarthas tatsāmīpyopakārataḥ |                    aparaiḥ samudāyārthas tata eva hi gamyate ||
  250. 7.250pākādau yan na dṛṣṭāsau bhavatyādau tathaiva ca |                    vivekaphalamandatvāt pacatyādau yatheṣṭatā ||
  251. 7.251sā sādhyasādhanopāyasāmānyārthāvadhāraṇāt |                    anyalabhyaṃ viśeṣāṃśaṃ yaṃ kañ cid abhikāṅkṣati ||
  252. 7.252kāmāvagatasādhyatvaḥ svargaḥ kāṅkṣati bhāvanām |                    tatra sannidhiyogyatvāt sambandhaḥ kalpyate tayoḥ ||
  253. 7.253tataḥ sā kḷptasambandhā sādhanāṃśam apekṣate |<646>                    dhātvarthāsādhanaṃ kiñ cin nānuṣṭhānaṃ hi siddhyati ||
  254. 7.254dhātuvācyaś ca yāgādir atṛtīyāparo 'pi san |                    svabhāvād bhāvanāsaktaḥ sādhyaṃ kiñ cid apekṣate ||
  255. 7.255pratyāsattinimitto 'yaṃ sambandhaḥ kalpyate 'nayoḥ |                    taṃ ca vispaṣṭam ākhyātuṃ yāgeneti prayujyate ||
  256. 7.256yathaupagavaśabdārthaṃ tasyāpatyam itīdṛśāt |                    kathayanti na caitasmin ṣaṣṭhyantopagusamabhavaḥ ||
  257. 7.257na kevalaṃ tṛtīyaiva karaṇatvaṃ niyacchati |                    pramāṇāntaragamye 'pi na kiñ cid viruṇaddhi sā ||
  258. 7.258prajñātakaraṇatve vā dhātau saty api neṣyate |                    aprātipadikatvena tṛtīyā yāgaśabdavat ||<647>
  259. 7.259ato yā śabdasāmarthyalabhyā karaṇatā yajeḥ |                    kevalasyāprayogitvāt sā yāgeneti kathyate ||
  260. 7.260tathotpannakathaṃbhāvā bhāvanopāyamātrake |                    upāyo 'pi ca kartavyamātrākāṅkṣī niyamyate ||
  261. 7.261yogyatvasannidhānābhyām anyathānupapattitaḥ |                    sa ca svavākyalabhyo vā vākyāntaragato 'pi vā ||
  262. 7.262prakṛtipratyayau yadvadapekṣete parasparam |                    padaṃ padāntaraṃ yadvad vākyaṃ vākyāntaraṃ tathā ||
  263. 7.263karaṇaiḥ sādhyate kiñ cin nopāyarahitaiḥ phalam |                    prayājādividhānaṃ ca na ca syān niṣprayojanam ||
  264. 7.264prayojanāntarāt tatra pratyāsatter apekṣitaḥ |                    phalavadbhāvanāṃśasthakaraṇānugraho varam ||
  265. 7.265ekabhāvanayopāttās trayo 'py aṃśāḥ parasparam |                    upakāryopakāritvaṃ paścādanubhavanti te ||<648>
  266. 7.266bhāvanāpekṣamāṇā hi sādhanaṃ kiṃ phalasya me |                    sādhanānugraḥ ko vetyanusyūtam apekṣate ||
  267. 7.267ākāṅkṣaivam avicchedasiddhā śuklagavādiṣu |                    ekakriyāgṛhīteṣu sambandhaś ca parasparam ||
  268. 7.268dravyadvāreṇa caiteṣāṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatā |                    itaropakṛtadravyavarttitvāt tatra karmaṇi ||
  269. 7.269dravyāntaram anicchantyā kriyayā ca parigrahāt |                    ekadravyāśrayaprāptir iti nānyonyasaṃśrayam ||
  270. 7.270parasparānurāgaś ca sutarām upakārakaḥ |<649>                    arthāc cānyavyavacchedaḥ, sambandho 'to na duṣyati ||
  271. 7.271tatrānaikāntikānekavākyārthopaplave sati |                    anyonyātmavyavacchedād ekatra sthāpyate matiḥ ||
  272. 7.272ato 'nvayātirekābhyām anumā neyam iṣyate |                    ekārthaikāntikatvaṃ tadanyathaivātra labhyate ||
  273. 7.273evaṃ padārthavākyārthasaṅghātair upakalpitām |                    viśiṣṭāṃ bhāvanāṃ prāpya vṛttir vidhiniṣedhayoḥ ||
  274. 7.274yady apy anyair asaṃspṛṣṭāṃ vidhiḥ spṛśati bhāvanām |                    tathāpy aśaktito nāsau tanmātre paryavasyati ||<650>
  275. 7.275anuṣṭheye hi viṣaye vidhiḥ puṃsāṃ pravartakaḥ |                    aṃśatrayeṇa cāpūrṇāṃ nānutiṣṭhati bhāvanām ||
  276. 7.276tasmāt prakrāntarūpo 'pi vidhis tāvat pratīkṣate |                    yāvad yogyatvam āpannā bhāvanānyānapekṣiṇī ||
  277. 7.277upasarganipātānāṃ prayoganiyame sati |                    arthas tadāgamanyāyāt syāt samāsapadeṣv iva ||
  278. 7.278vācakadyotakatvaṃ tu nātīvātropayujyate |                    tadbhāvād vācakatvaṃ vā parasyānugrahī 'stu vā ||
  279. 7.279īṣadarthādayas tāvat sākṣān nāmnaiva saṅgatāḥ |                    aprayuktakriyādvārā viśeṣādhānato 'pare ||
  280. 7.280āpiṅgaḥ pravayāś ceti dvayasyaitannidarśanam |<651>                    kva cit prakṛṣṭatādīnāṃ bhāvanopanipātinām ||
  281. 7.281itikartavyatātvena pratipattiparigrahau |                    ekārthasamavāyitvāt kartṛdharmo 'pi bhāvanām ||
  282. 7.282gamiṣyati, na kartṛṇāṃ svarūpe sa hi kīrtyate |                    ye tv anyārthaṃ viruddhārthadhātuśaktyavalopinaḥ ||
  283. 7.283teṣāṃ tadaṅgataiveṣṭā dhātubhāgasamā hi te |                    praśabdenopasṛṣṭasya tiṣṭhater gatiśaktatā ||
  284. 7.284na hi praśabdavelāyāṃ gamane jāyate matiḥ |                    sāmānyataḥ kriyāśaktiḥ kḷptā dhātoḥ puraiva tu ||
  285. 7.285viśeṣa eva tatra syād itarasya dvaye punaḥ |                    yā ca śaktyantarodbhūtir iyam eva viśeṣyatā ||<652>
  286. 7.286na sāmānyāparityāgī kevalo 'nyair viśeṣyate |                    ukter viśeṣaṇaṃ kiñ cid ucyamānaviśeṣaṇam ||
  287. 7.287tena śaktyapavādo 'yaṃ bhaved arthāpavādavat |                    tathaiva jvalanādīnāṃ pākasambandhiteṣyate ||
  288. 7.288itikartavyatāṃśatvāt pāke vā tatphale 'pi vā |                    odane sādhyamāne hi pākaḥ karaṇam iṣyate ||
  289. 7.289akṛtaḥ so 'pi nāstīti punaḥ karaṇavāñchanam |                    karaṇaṃ jvalanādīni tasya kāṣṭhādi vā tathā ||<653>
  290. 7.290itikarttavyatākāṅkṣā yāvatkaraṇasaṃśrayā |                    itikarttavyatāpy anyadapekṣya karaṇaṃ bhavet ||
  291. 7.291jvalanādinimittā 'taḥ kāṣṭhādeḥ pākasaṅgatiḥ |                    karmaṇaḥ karmasādhyatvaṃ nāsmatpakṣe viruddhyate ||
  292. 7.292anātmasamavetasya nimittaṃ karma hīṣyate |                    jvalanādisvarūpaṃ ca na kāṣṭhādibharīpsitam ||
  293. 7.293pākaprayojitānāṃ hi tadvṛttir nāntarīyakī |                    kartṛtve 'pi ca kāṣṭhādeḥ pāke syāt karaṇāditā ||<654>
  294. 7.294āvibhūtānyaśaktitvād ekatve cāpy apekṣayā |                    jvalanādiṣu sarveṣāṃ svātantryāt kartṛteṣyate ||
  295. 7.295tatsvātantryāvagatyaiva prayuṅkte hi prayojakaḥ |                    niyuktānāṃ tu tenaiṣāṃ karaṇatvādivācyatā ||
  296. 7.296udbhūtadevadattādivyāpārābhibhavād bhavet |                    yatra tv abhibhavas teṣāṃ naikenāpi vivakṣyate ||
  297. 7.297kāṣṭhādīni pacantīti prayogas tatra jāyate |                    ekaśabdagṛhīte 'pi guṇaprādhānyam iṣyate ||
  298. 7.298ākhyātapratyayopāttabhāvanākartṛsaṃkhyavat |<655>                    tasmād yasya vivakṣyeta pradhānaṃ dhātubhiḥ kriyā ||
  299. 7.299sa kartā guṇabhūtānyavyāpāre karaṇāditā |                    itikartavyatāṃśena sarveṣāṃ tena saṅgatiḥ ||
  300. 7.300avāntarakriyāyogāt pradhānakriyayā saha |                    vikalpapratiṣedhāder virodho na ca vastunā ||
  301. 7.301abhāvam eva nañ prāha vartamānādikālikam |                    nāmadhātvarthayogī ca niṣedho 'nyārthabhāg bhavet ||
  302. 7.302tatra vastvantaronmuktaṃ vastv evānuguṇaṃ ca tat |                    ākhyātapratyayair yoge nivṛttyarthaḥ pratīyate ||
  303. 7.303tatra cājñātasandigdhaviparītārthavāraṇam |<656>                    asti nāstīti sandehe pākṣikāstitvabodhanam ||
  304. 7.304nivartyate nañā, yad vā nāstitaivocyate satī |                    avyutpannasya tatraiva jāyate nāstitāmatiḥ ||
  305. 7.305astitvamāninaḥ saiva vāryate viparītadhīḥ |                    apūrvābhāvavijñānavirodhāt svayam eva tu ||
  306. 7.306nivartate 'stitābuddhir mṛgatṛṣṇādibuddhivat |                    tac caitadaniṣedhe 'pi sthāṇvādāv īdṛg eva naḥ ||
  307. 7.307tatrāpy ajñātasandigdhaviparītārthabādhanāt |                    abhāvasya ca vastutve purastāt pratipāmite ||
  308. 7.308ghaṭāditulyatā tasya, pratiṣedho na cāpy ayam |                    vidhāyakairasaṃyukto na hi nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ ||
  309. 7.309abhāvakathanaṃ hy etan nāvaśyaṃ prāptipūrvakam |<657>                    na ca śabdena sadbhāvas tasya cārthasya bodhitaḥ ||
  310. 7.310astitvādyanapekṣaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ tena gamyate |                    astiśabdaprayogo 'pi tenaivātropapadyate ||
  311. 7.311jāter astitvanāsitve na ca kaś cid vivakṣati |                    nityatvāl lakṣyamāṇāyā vyaktes te hi viśeṣaṇe ||
  312. 7.312tenātra na virodhitvaṃ śrutyā pūrvoktayā nañaḥ |                    yatrāpy astīty upādāya prayujyeran nañādayaḥ ||
  313. 7.313tatra tasyāpavādatvāt pūrvajñānopamardanam |                    astitvaṃ vā sad evātra smaryate pūrvalakṣitam ||
  314. 7.314abhāvottarakālaṃ syād viśeṣe tadvivakṣite |<658>                    vidhinā yujyate yatra na hanyān na pibediti ||
  315. 7.315tatrābhāvārthatā naiva svayaṃ so ruṇaddhi hi |                    anyathaiva pravarttante bhāvābhāvadhiyo 'parāḥ ||
  316. 7.316vyavasthitabahirvastuparicchedaphalātmikāḥ |                    anyathānāgatotpādyabhāvapreraṇavārikā ||
  317. 7.317antaḥsaṅkalpamūlātmā vṛttir vidhiniṣedhayoḥ |<659>                    vikalpo 'py anayor eva viṣayeṣu pravarttate ||
  318. 7.318prāpteṣu pratiṣedhārtham aprāpteṣu vidhitsayā |                    yugapac ca viruddhārthapratipatter asambhavaḥ ||
  319. 7.319paryāyeṇa kadā cit tu kā cid vṛttir bhaviṣyati |                    prāptāprāptavikalpas tu naiveṣṭo lokavedayoḥ ||
  320. 7.320na vikalpārthavācī tu vāśabdo viṣayāntare |                    sthāṇur vā puruṣo veti yāti tiṣṭhati vety ayam ||
  321. 7.321sandehakathanārthaḥ syān na hi vastu vikalpate |<660>                    viṣaye bāhya evaivaṃ pratiṣedhādisambhavaḥ ||
  322. 7.322na hi tatsambhavaḥ kaś cid jñāne svarasabhaṅgini |                    jñānaṃ yat tāvad utpannaṃ nānutpanaṃ tad iṣyate ||
  323. 7.323vināśe 'pi samānatvaṃ satyamithyāvabodhayoḥ |                    bāhyārthavādinas tvarthe yajjñānaṃ jāyate 'nyathā ||
  324. 7.324tanmithyātvopasaṃkhyānāt pūrvabadhādisambhavaḥ |                    tatrāpi tu na tadrūpaṃ bādhyate na ca bodhyate ||
  325. 7.325arthajñānādirūpāt tu phalato viprayujyate |                    pratibhānekadhā puṃsāṃ yady apy artheṣu jāyate ||
  326. 7.326tathāpi bāhya evārthas tasya vākyasya ceṣyate |<661>                    vākyaprayojanatvena janyatvenātha vā yadi ||
  327. 7.327ucyate pratibhāpy artho na naḥ kiñ cid virudhyate |                    śabdādyutthāpitair jñānair ātmāṃśagrahaṇākṣamaiḥ ||
  328. 7.328yad bāhyamāpyate vastu sa tvarthaḥ pāramārthikaḥ |                    pratyakṣavyatiriktaṃ tu vijñānam upavarṇitam ||
  329. 7.329trikālaviṣayaṃ yasmād asannidhiradūṣaṇam |                    anekākāratā yāpi śūrabhīrudhiyaṃ prati ||
  330. 7.330vāsanānugrahāt soktā kuṇapādimater iva |                    bhāvanaiva ca vākyārthaḥ, sarvatrākhyātavattayā ||
  331. 7.331anekaguṇajātyādikārakārthānurañjitā |<662>                    ekayaiva tu buddhyāsau gṛhyate citrarūpayā ||
  332. 7.332padārthā''hitasaṃskāracitrapiṇḍaprasūtayā |                    padārthapadabuddhīnāṃ saṃsargas tadapekṣayā ||
  333. 7.333padavyavadhinā caiṣāṃ nāsaṃsargo bhaviṣyati |                    tulyakakṣo hy asambandhī vyavadhāteti kīrtyate ||
  334. 7.334aṅgatvāt tu padair na syād aṅgivyavadhikalpanā |                    ekasmiṃś ca gṛhīte 'rthe sopāyo 'nyo 'py apekṣyate ||
  335. 7.335apekṣyā ca sarvo 'sau sambandhaṃ pratipadyate |                    padānām api sambandha evaṃ vākyeṣu sidhyati ||<663>
  336. 7.336padārthapūrvakas tasmād vākyārtho 'yam avasthitaḥ |                    artharūpam ivāpannaṃ vākyaṃ vākyasya vākyasya gocaraḥ ||
  337. 7.337neṣyate na hy abhedena vṛttir astīti sādhitam |                    prasaṅgikādi yat kāryaṃ padārthopanibandhanam ||
  338. 7.338ākāṅkṣāviditapraśnau yau ca dṛṣṭau pikādiṣu |                    asatyaṃ tad, apoddhṛtya na caivaṃ kalpyiṣyati ||
  339. 7.339śaśaśṛṅgādyapoddhṛtya vākyārtho na hi dṛśyate |                    asatyair gamyamāne 'rthe satyatā nety udāhṛtam ||
  340. 7.340svarūpeṇāsato dṛṣṭaṃ nopāyatvaṃ hi kasya cit |                    avācakatvaṃ vākyasya tadbhūtānām itīritam ||<664>
  341. 7.341hetuḥ syāt tannimittatm, mūlaṃ vārthasya kathyate |                    padārthamūlako hy eṣa na bhrāntir iti gamyatām ||
  342. 7.342sākṣād yady api kurvanti padārthapratipādanam |                    varṇās tathāpi naitasmin paryavasyanti niṣphale ||
  343. 7.343vākyārthamitaye teṣāṃ pravṛttau nāntarīyakam |                    pāke jvāleva kāṣṭhānāṃ padārthapratipādanam ||
  344. 7.344prayojanatayā caiṣām artham icchanti bhāvanām |                    kriyārtheneti tenāha samāmnāyaprayojanam ||
  345. 7.345śuklo gaur iti vākyārthavākyayor yadudāhṛtam |                    sambandhakathanārthaṃ tan na jñeyaṃ pāramārthikam ||
  346. 7.346na hi prayojanāpetaṃ vākyam uccāryate kva cit |<665>                    prayojanakṣamaṃ nāpi padam ākhyātavarjitam ||
  347. 7.347gaur aśva iti vā śrutyā yad gotvādyavabodhitam |                    viśeṣe yadi tan na syāt tatra syāc chrutibādhanam ||
  348. 7.348jātivyaktī gṛhītvaiva vayaṃ tu śrutilakṣite |                    kṛṣṇādi yadi muñcāmaḥ kā śrutis tatra bādhyate ||
  349. 7.349lakṣaṇāto 'pi parato yaḥ sandehaḥ pravarttate |                    kā nāma pīḍyate tatra śuklaśrutyā nivartate ||
  350. 7.350agṛhṇatas tu śuklatvaṃ śrutis te bādhyatetarām |                    asya vākyam asambaddhaṃ sarvam evāprayojanam ||
  351. 7.351vākyārtho 'pīti bhāṣyeṇa solluṇṭham abhidhīyate |                    na sarvatrety anenāpi kva cit sā nety avocata ||<666>
  352. 7.352prakṛtyarthānuraktāyāṃ buddhau nipatatā dhruvam |                    karmādīnāṃ viśeṣyatvam iti kā vā śrutir bhavet ||
  353. 7.353prakṛtipratyayau nāpi prayujyete ca kevalau |                    yena yuṣmadabhipretā śrutir labhyeta karhi cit ||
  354. 7.354yatrāpi nāma dṛśyete devalāvadhunādivavat |                    tatrāpy anyārthasaṃyuktāv iti pūrvaṃ nirūpitam ||
  355. 7.355ayam eva viśeṣaś ca kathyate padavākyayoḥ |                    arthavadbhāgatulyatve prakṛtipratyayārthataḥ ||
  356. 7.356dṛṣṭā yathā hi sākāṅkṣāḥ padārthāḥ kevalāḥ kva cit |                    svātantryeṇa gṛhītāś ca viśīṣṭārthāvabodhakāḥ ||
  357. 7.357prakṛtipratyayau naivaṃ kadā cid api lakṣitau |                    prakṛtyarthānurakto hi pratyayārthaḥ sadeṣyate ||<667>
  358. 7.358paśyataḥ śvetimārūpaṃ hreṣāśabdaṃ ca śṛṇvataḥ |                    khuranikṣepaśabdaṃ ca śveto 'śvo dhāvatīti dhīḥ ||
  359. 7.359dṛṣṭā vākyavinirmuktā na padārthair vinā kva cit |                    mānasād ity ato nāsya vākyāgrahaṇam uttaram ||
  360. 7.360mānasenāparādhena padārthān ye na gṛhṇate |                    te tadvākyaṃ gṛhītvāpi nārthaṃ gṛhṇanti karhi cit ||
  361. 7.361vākyena tena nocyeta vākyārtho 'nyair nirūpaṇāt |                    tacchrutāv apy abodhād vā palāśeneva vṛkṣatā ||
  362. 7.362varṇā vā na bruvantyenaṃ tatsambandhyarthabodhanāt |                    sattve 'py agamakatvād vā vṛkṣatvam iva śiṃśapā ||
  363. 7.363padārthā gamayantyetaṃ pratyekaṃ saṃśaye sati |                    sāmastye nirṇayotpādāt sthāṇumūrddhasthakākavat ||<668>
  364. 7.364tadabhāvāpratīter vā tadgamyo 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati |                    śrotrābhāvāpratīter hi śrautraṃ śabdaṃ pracakṣate ||
  365. 7.365sambandhākaraṇanyāyād vaktavyā vākyanityatā |                    saṅghātatvasya vaktavyam īdṛśaṃ pratisādhanam ||
  366. 7.366vedasyādhyayanaṃ sarva gurvadhyayanapūrvakam |                    vedādhyayanavācyatvād adhunādhyayanaṃ yathā ||
  367. 7.367bhārate 'pi bhaved evaṃ kartṛsmṛtyā tu bādhyate |                    vede 'pi tatsmṛtir yā tu sārthavādanibandhanā ||
  368. 7.368pāramparyeṇa kartāraṃ nādhyetāraḥ smaranti hi |                    teṣāmanevamātmatvād bhrāntiḥ seti ca vakṣyate ||
  369. 7.369teṣu ca dhriyamāṇeṣu na mūlāntarakalpanā |<669>                    tathā hy adyatanasyāpi te kurvantīdṛśīṃ matim ||

Chapter 8 vedapauruṣeyatādhikaraṇa VPA

  1. 8.1vacanāntarasādharmyāt kartuḥ sāmānyasamplave |                    samākhyayā viśeṣo 'yaṃ kaṭhādiravadhāryate ||<670>
  2. 8.2anapekṣatvasūtre yā rūpāt kṛtakatoditā |                    vede sā dṛśyate spaṣṭā kṛtakārthābhidhāyini ||
  3. 8.3smṛtiprayojanābhāvāt kartṛmātre 'napekṣite |                    sāmānyasiddhyapekṣatvān na samākhyā niyāmikā ||
  4. 8.4anyathāpy upapannatvād iyaṃ pravacanādinā |                    na śaktā kartṛmūlāya, prokte ca smaraṇaṃ sthitam ||
  5. 8.5śrutyāder durbalā cāsau na śaktā tāni bādhitum |                    aṅgabhūyāṃsamekeyaṃ śabdarāśiṃ na bādhate ||
  6. 8.6kāmaṃ vā nirnimitteyaṃ śākhām ekāṃ vadiṣyati |                    śrutisāmānyamātraṃ hi nātra daṇḍena vāyate ||
  7. 8.7sati sādhāraṇatve vā sambhavena viśeṣaṇam |                    yathā vairūpasāmeti sattayaiva pratīyate ||<671>
  8. 8.8avyāsaṅgi ca sarveṣu pravaktṛtvaṃ kaṭhādiṣu |                    tenaikavyapadeśyatvaṃ lakṣyate ḍitthamātṛvat ||
  9. 8.9anyais tulye 'pi sambandhe yat tair na vyapadiśyatem |                    na hy eṣa kartṛsaṃskāraḥ pārārthye caika iṣyate ||
  10. 8.10vidyamānanimittaṃ ca kathyate, nāsataḥ kriyā |                    sādhāraṇaṃ ca tīrthādi kena cid vyapadiśyate ||
  11. 8.11yadi cāpauruṣeyyeṣā nānityapratipādinī |                    pauruṣeyyās tu satyatvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate ||<672>
  12. 8.12nityam eva nimittaṃ vā kaṭhatvaṃ jātir asti naḥ |                    kāṭhakādipravṛttyarthaṃ vyāvṛttaṃ caraṇāntarāt ||
  13. 8.13anityārthābhidhāyitvaṃ svayam evaiṣa muñcati |                    nityānityavikalpena vedastādarthyavarjanāt ||
  14. 8.14nityasya nitya evārthaḥ kṛtakasyāpramāṇatā |                    unmattavacanatvaṃ tu pūrvam eva nirākṛtam ||
  15. 8.15iti pramāṇatvam idaṃ prasiddhaṃ yuktyeha dharmaṃ prati codanāyāḥ |                    ataḥ paraṃ tu pravibhajya vedaṃ tredhā tato vakṣyati yasya yo 'rthaḥ ||
